from pathlib import Path; import json
from sym_normalize import normalize
DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
for tf in ["1m","3m","5m","15m","30m"]:
  d=C/tf
  if d.exists():
    for p in d.glob("*.json"):
      n=normalize(p.stem)
      if n!=p.stem: (p.parent/n).with_suffix(".json").write_text(p.read_text()); p.unlink()
f=DATA/"top.json"
if f.exists():
  t=json.loads(f.read_text()); t["symbols"]=[normalize(s) for s in (t.get("symbols") or [])]
  f.write_text(json.dumps(t))
print("OK: fix_names")

Path: /opt/scalp/tools/ws_writer_supervisor.sh
Size: 619
MTime: 2025-09-27 13:07:10.758066784 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data}"
SYMBOL="${SYMBOL:-BTCUSDT}"
PY="/opt/scalp/tools/ws_candle_futures_writer.py"
LOG="$DATA/logs/ws_writer.log"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$LOG")"

i=0
while :; do
  ts="$(date -u '+%F %T')"
  echo "[$ts] start ws writer for $SYMBOL" | tee -a "$LOG"
  if python3 -u "$PY" 2>>"$LOG"; then
    echo "[$ts] ws exited cleanly" | tee -a "$LOG"
    sleep 1
  else
    rc=$?
    backoff=$(( 1<<i )); [[ $backoff -gt 60 ]] && backoff=60
    echo "[$ts] ws crashed rc=$rc; retry in ${backoff}s" | tee -a "$LOG"
    (( i<6 )) && ((i++))
    sleep "$backoff"
  fi
done
----- FILE END -----

MTime: 2025-09-27 06:28:54.045180043 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Remplit localement jusqu'à N barres mini en dupliquant la dernière barre.
# Utile pour déboguer quand le fetch réel est partiel.
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data"))

# Minima par TF selon A puis B
MINB = {
    "1m": int(os.environ.get("MIN_1M", 60)),   # B
    "3m": int(os.environ.get("MIN_3M", 40)),   # B
    "5m": int(os.environ.get("MIN_5M", 40)),   # A
    "15m": int(os.environ.get("MIN_15M", 40)), # A
    "30m": int(os.environ.get("MIN_30M", 40)), # A
}

STEP = {"1m":60, "3m":180, "5m":300, "15m":900, "30m":1800}

def load_arr(p: Path):
    try:
        return json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
    except:
        return []

def save_arr(p: Path, arr):
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(arr, ensure_ascii=False))

def to_list(bar):
    # Accept dict {"t","o","h","l","c","v"} or list [ts,o,h,l,c,v]
    if isinstance(bar, (list, tuple)) and len(bar) >= 6:
        return [int(bar[0]), float(bar[1]), float(bar[2]), float(bar[3]), float(bar[4]), float(bar[5])]
    if isinstance(bar, dict):
        ts = int(bar.get("t") or bar.get("time") or bar.get("T") or 0)
        c = float(bar.get("c") or bar.get("close") or bar.get("C") or 0.0)
        o = float(bar.get("o") or bar.get("open")  or c)
        h = float(bar.get("h") or bar.get("high")  or max(o, c))
        l = float(bar.get("l") or bar.get("low")   or min(o, c))
        v = float(bar.get("v") or bar.get("volume") or 0.0)
        return [ts, o, h, l, c, v]
    return None

def fill(symbol: str, tf: str):
    f = DATA / "candles" / tf / f"{symbol}.json"
    arr = load_arr(f)
    arr = [x for x in (to_list(x) for x in arr) if x]
    if not arr:
        # crée 1 barre plate "now - N*step"
        n = MINB.get(tf, 0)
        if n <= 0:
            return
        now = int(time.time() // STEP[tf] * STEP[tf])
        first_ts = now - (n-1)*STEP[tf]
        base = [first_ts, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 0.0]
        arr = [ [first_ts + i*STEP[tf]] + base[1:] for i in range(n) ]
    need = MINB.get(tf, 0) - len(arr)
    if need > 0:
        last = arr[-1][:]
        for _ in range(need):
            last = [last[0] + STEP[tf]] + last[1:]
            arr.append(last[:])
    save_arr(f, arr)

def main():
    import argparse
    p = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    p.add_argument("--symbol", required=True)
    p.add_argument("--tfs", required=True)  # ex: 5m,15m,30m
    args = p.parse_args()
    for tf in [t.strip() for t in args.tfs.split(",") if t.strip()]:
        fill(args.symbol, tf)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math
from pathlib import Path
from time import time

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data"))
CAND = DATA / "candles"
DEBUG_DIR = DATA / "debug" / "bridge"
DEBUG_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# Garde-fous (modifiables par env)
ENTRY_FROM_HOLD = int(os.environ.get("ENTRY_FROM_HOLD", "0"))
MIN_STRENGTH    = float(os.environ.get("MIN_STRENGTH", "7"))
PB_TH           = float(os.environ.get("PB_TH", "0.65"))
PS_TH           = float(os.environ.get("PS_TH", "0.65"))
ATR_PER         = int(os.environ.get("ATR_PER", "14"))
ATR_MIN_PCT     = float(os.environ.get("ATR_MIN_PCT", "0.10"))   # % mini en 1m
EMA_VETO        = int(os.environ.get("EMA_VETO", "0"))           # 0=off
COOLDOWN_S      = int(os.environ.get("COOLDOWN_S", "120"))
RISK_PCT        = float(os.environ.get("RISK_PCT", "0.01"))
LEVERAGE        = float(os.environ.get("LEVERAGE", "5"))
SLxATR          = float(os.environ.get("SLxATR", "1.0"))
TpxATR          = float(os.environ.get("TpxATR", "1.5"))
FORCE_ENTRY     = int(os.environ.get("FORCE_ENTRY", "0"))

SIG = DATA / "signals.json"
POS = DATA / "paper" / "positions.json"
BAL = DATA / "paper" / "balance.json"

def jload(p: Path, dflt):
    try:
        return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception:
        return dflt

def dump_json(p: Path, obj):
    p.write_text(json.dumps(obj, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))

def last_closed_1m(sym: str):
    """Retourne close de la dernière bougie 1m **clôturée**.
    Règle simple: on prend l'avant-dernière ligne."""
    f = CAND / "1m" / f"{sym}.json"
    try:
        rows = json.loads(f.read_text())
        if len(rows) >= 2:
            return float(rows[-2][4])  # close
    except Exception:
        pass
    return None

def atr_1m_pct(sym: str, n=ATR_PER):
    f = CAND / "1m" / f"{sym}.json"
    try:
        rows = json.loads(f.read_text())
        rows = rows[-(n+1):]
        if len(rows) < n+1: 
            return None
        trs = []
        prev_close = float(rows[0][4])
        for r in rows[1:]:
            h,l,c = float(r[1]), float(r[2]), float(r[4])
            tr = max(h-l, abs(h-prev_close), abs(l-prev_close))
            trs.append(tr); prev_close = c
        atr = sum(trs)/len(trs)
        last_close = float(rows[-1][4])
        return 100.0*atr/last_close
    except Exception:
        return None

def ema(series, span):
    k = 2/(span+1)
    e = series[0]
    for x in series[1:]:
        e = x*k + e*(1-k)
    return e

def ema_veto(side: str, sym: str):
    if not EMA_VETO: 
        return False
    f = CAND / "5m" / f"{sym}.json"
    try:
        rows = json.loads(f.read_text())
        closes = [float(r[4]) for r in rows][-50:]
        if len(closes) < 22: 
            return False
        e9  = ema(closes, 9)
        e21 = ema(closes, 21)
        return (side=="buy"  and e9<e21) or (side=="sell" and e9>e21)
    except Exception:
        return False

def cooldown_block(sym: str):
    """Anti double entrée: refuse si position 'open' existe récente."""
    pos = jload(POS, [])
    now = time()
    for p in pos:
        if p.get("symbol")==sym and str(p.get("status","")).lower().startswith("open"):
            # si la position a été ouverte il y a moins de COOLDOWN_S on bloque
            ts = p.get("ts_open") or 0
            try:
                if now - float(ts) < COOLDOWN_S: 
                    return True
            except Exception:
                return True
    return False

def decide(sig: dict):
    sym  = sig.get("symbol") or sig.get("sym") or sig.get("coin")
    ctx  = (sig.get("ctx") or sig.get("context") or "").lower()
    act  = (sig.get("action") or "").lower()
    side = (sig.get("side") or "").lower()

    # mapping context -> side si besoin
    if side not in ("buy","sell"):
        if ctx=="buy" or ctx=="bullish": side="buy"
        elif ctx=="sell" or ctx=="bearish": side="sell"
        else: side="none"

    strength = float(sig.get("strength") or sig.get("str") or 0)
    pb = float(sig.get("pb", 0)); ps = float(sig.get("ps", 0))

    # filtre A/B pour convertir hold->enter
    will_enter = act in ("enter_long","enter_short")
    if not will_enter and ENTRY_FROM_HOLD:
        if act in ("hold_long","hold_short"):
            will_enter = True
            side = "buy" if "long" in act else "sell"

    # gardes-fous
    reason = []
    if not will_enter and not FORCE_ENTRY:
        return "gate_action_none", None

    if not FORCE_ENTRY:
        if strength < MIN_STRENGTH or (pb < PB_TH and ps < PS_TH):
            return "gate_strength_pb_ps", None

        atrp = atr_1m_pct(sym)
        if atrp is None or atrp < ATR_MIN_PCT:
            return "gate_atr_too_small", None

        if ema_veto(side, sym):
            return "gate_ema_veto", None

        if cooldown_block(sym):
            return "gate_cooldown", None

    # prix d'entrée
    px = last_closed_1m(sym)
    if px is None:
        if FORCE_ENTRY:
            return "skip_no_price_force", {"sym":sym, "side":side, "action":"hold_"+("long" if side=="buy" else "short"),
                                           "price": None, "sl": None, "tp": None, "size": 0, "margin": 0}
        return "gate_no_px_or_atr", None

    # ATR pour SL/TP (recalc au besoin)
    atrp = atr_1m_pct(sym) or 0.0
    atr_abs = px * (atrp/100.0)
    sl = px - SLxATR*atr_abs if side=="buy" else px + SLxATR*atr_abs
    tp = px + TpxATR*atr_abs if side=="buy" else px - TpxATR*atr_abs

    # sizing risque fixe
    bal = float(jload(BAL, {"cash":200}).get("cash", 200))
    risk_amt = max(0.0, bal*RISK_PCT)
    stop_dist = abs(px - sl)
    qty = 0.0 if stop_dist<=0 else risk_amt/stop_dist
    # marge
    notionnel = qty*px
    margin = notionnel/LEVERAGE if LEVERAGE>0 else notionnel

    # arrondis simples
    def rnd(x, step): 
        try: 
            return math.floor(x/step)*step
        except Exception:
            return x
    qty = rnd(qty, 1e-3)
    px  = round(px, 6); sl = round(sl, 6); tp = round(tp, 6)
    margin = round(margin, 2)

    out = {"sym": sym, "side": side, "action": "enter_"+("long" if side=="buy" else "short"),
           "price": px, "sl": sl, "tp": tp, "size": qty, "margin": margin}

    # log par coin
    log = {
        "ctx": ctx, "str": strength, "pb": pb, "ps": ps, "atr%": atrp,
        "side": side, "px": px, "sl": sl, "tp": tp, "qty": qty, "margin": margin
    }
    (DEBUG_DIR/f"{sym}.log").write_text(json.dumps(log, indent=2))
    return "ENTRY", out

def main():
    sigs = jload(SIG, [])
    items = []
    gates = {"ENTRY":0, "gate_strength_pb_ps":0, "gate_atr_too_small":0,
             "gate_ema_veto":0, "gate_cooldown":0, "gate_no_px_or_atr":0,
             "gate_action_none":0, "skip_no_price_force":0}
    for s in sigs:
        decision, out = decide(s)
        gates[decision] = gates.get(decision,0)+1
        if out: 
            items.append(out)
        else:
            # garder le signal original si pas d'entrée, mais renseigner champs par défaut
            s.setdefault("price", None); s.setdefault("sl", None)
            s.setdefault("tp", None);    s.setdefault("size", 0)
            s.setdefault("margin", 0)
            items.append({"sym": s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym") or s.get("coin"),
                          "side": s.get("side") or "none",
                          "action": s.get("action") or "none",
                          "price": s.get("price"), "sl": s.get("sl"),
                          "tp": s.get("tp"), "size": s.get("size"), "margin": s.get("margin")})

    dump_json(SIG, items)

    # petite synthèse stdout
    print(f"[bridge] wrote {SIG} items={len(items)}",
          *[f"{k}={v}" for k,v in gates.items() if v], sep=" ")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import os, json, time, math, traceback
from pathlib import Path
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
CAND.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
(CAND/"1m").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
(CAND/"3m").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
(CAND/"5m").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

TOP = json.loads((DATA/"top.json").read_text())
A   = json.loads((DATA/"analyse_A_out.json").read_text()) if (DATA/"analyse_A_out.json").exists() else {}

# --- Sélection: seulement ctx != "none" ---
symbols = [s for s in (TOP.get("symbols") or []) if (A.get(s,{}).get("ctx") or "none") != "none"]

# --- Exchange ccxt ---
import ccxt
EXCHANGE = os.getenv("EXCHANGE", TOP.get("exchange") or "xt").lower()
def build_ex():
    klass = getattr(ccxt, EXCHANGE)
    return klass({"enableRateLimit": True, "timeout": 20000})

ex = build_ex()

# --- Utilitaires OHLCV ---
def fetch_ohlcv(sym, tf, limit=600):
    # returns list[[ts,open,high,low,close,vol], ...], ts ms
    try:
        return ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym.replace("_","/"), timeframe=tf, limit=limit) or []
    except Exception:
        return []

def save_json(p, arr):
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(arr))

def last_complete(arr, tf_sec):
    if not arr: return []
    now = int(time.time()*1000)
    return arr[:-1] if now - arr[-1][0] < tf_sec*1000 else arr

def resample_3m_from_1m(arr1):
    out=[]
    bucket=None
    for k in arr1:
        ts,o,h,l,c,v = k
        # début de bucket 3m aligné
        b = ts - (ts % (3*60*1000))
        if (bucket is None) or (b!=bucket[0]):
            # push précédent
            if bucket is not None: out.append(bucket)
            bucket = [b,o,h,l,c,v]
        else:
            bucket[2] = max(bucket[2], h)
            bucket[3] = min(bucket[3], l)
            bucket[4] = c
            bucket[5] += v
    if bucket is not None: out.append(bucket)
    return out

# --- Worker par symbole ---
RATE_MS = int(os.getenv("FETCH_RATE_MS", "220"))
def work(sym):
    t0=time.time()
    try:
        m1 = fetch_ohlcv(sym, "1m", 900)
        m5 = fetch_ohlcv(sym, "5m", 600)
        m1 = last_complete(m1, 60)
        m5 = last_complete(m5, 300)
        m3 = resample_3m_from_1m(m1)
        save_json(CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json", m1)
        save_json(CAND/"5m"/f"{sym}.json", m5)
        save_json(CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.json", m3)
        ok = (len(m1)>0 and len(m3)>0 and len(m5)>0)
        dt = int((time.time()-t0)*1000)
        return (sym, ok, dt, len(m1), len(m3), len(m5))
    except Exception as e:
        return (sym, False, -1, 0, 0, 0)
    finally:
        # petit rate-limit inter-threads
        time.sleep(RATE_MS/1000.0)

WORKERS = int(os.getenv("FETCH_WORKERS", "8"))
results=[]
with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS) as pool:
    futs=[pool.submit(work, s) for s in symbols]
    for f in as_completed(futs):
        results.append(f.result())

# Log court sur stdout
for sym,ok,dt,n1,n3,n5 in sorted(results):
    print(f"{sym:12s} ok={int(ok)}  {dt:4d}ms  1m={n1:4d} 3m={n3:4d} 5m={n5:4d}")
print(f"done ctx-syms={len(symbols)}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math, time, asyncio, statistics as stats
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# --------- Params ---------
EX="bitget"; QUOTE="USDT"
TOP_N = int(os.getenv("TOP_N","30"))
SHORTLIST_K = int(os.getenv("SHORTLIST_K","80"))
MIN_QV = float(os.getenv("MIN_QV","1000000"))
MAX_SP = float(os.getenv("MAX_SP_BPS","60"))   # 0.60%
USE_DEPTH = os.getenv("USE_DEPTH","0")=="1"
MIN_DEPTH = float(os.getenv("MIN_DEPTH_USD","200000"))
BAND_BPS = int(os.getenv("DEPTH_BAND_BPS","50"))  # ±0.5%

# pondérations
W_VOL24 = 0.30
W_TURN  = 0.30
W_VOLA  = 0.20
W_DEPTH = 0.15
W_SP    = -0.05

# exécution
WORKERS = int(os.getenv("TOP_WORKERS","8"))
RATE_LIMIT_MS = int(os.getenv("TOP_RATE_LIMIT_MS","220"))
FUT = {"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}

BAD_KW=("UP","DOWN","BULL","BEAR","3L","3S","5L","5S")
BAD_BASES={"USDT","USDC","FDUSD","TUSD","DAI","EUR","TRY","USD"}

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
TOP=DATA/"top.json"; RANK=DATA/"top_ranked.json"

def now_iso(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")
def clamp(x,a,b): return a if x<a else b if x>b else x
def winsor(vals, p=0.01):
    if not vals: return vals
    s=sorted(vals); n=len(s)
    lo=s[max(0,int(n*p)-1)]; hi=s[min(n-1,int(n*(1-p)))]
    return [min(max(v,lo),hi) for v in vals]
def rnorm(d):
    if not d: return {}
    it=sorted(d.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1]); n=max(1,len(it)-1)
    return {k:i/n for i,(k,_) in enumerate(it)}
def ema(vals, p):
    if not vals: return 0.0
    a=2/(p+1); e=float(vals[0])
    for v in vals[1:]: e=a*float(v)+(1-a)*e
    return float(e)

# ---------- async throttle ----------
_executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS)
_sem = asyncio.Semaphore(max(1, 1000//RATE_LIMIT_MS))
async def throttled(loop, fn, *a, **k):
    async with _sem:
        t0=time.time()
        try: res = await loop.run_in_executor(_executor, lambda: fn(*a, **k))
        except Exception: res=None
        dt=time.time()-t0
        sl=max(0.0, RATE_LIMIT_MS/1000 - dt)
        if sl: await asyncio.sleep(sl)
        return res

def load_seed():
    try:
        j=json.loads(TOP.read_text()); s=j.get("symbols") or []
        out=[x for x in s if isinstance(x,str)]
        return out if out else ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","BNBUSDT"]
    except:
        return ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","BNBUSDT"]

def main():
    import ccxt
    seeds = load_seed()

    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    mkts=[m for m in ex.markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE and m.get("active") is not False]
    symbols=[m["symbol"] for m in mkts]
    bases={m["symbol"]: m["base"] for m in mkts}

    # ---- 1) bulk tickers
    tickers={}
    try: tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols, {**FUT})
    except Exception:
        for s in symbols:
            try: tickers[s]=ex.fetch_ticker(s,{**FUT})
            except Exception: tickers[s]={}

    pool=[]
    for s in symbols:
        b=bases[s]
        if any(k in b for k in BAD_KW): continue
        if b in BAD_BASES: continue
        t=tickers.get(s,{})
        # volume quote avec fallback "info"
        qv = t.get("quoteVolume")
        if not qv:
            info=t.get("info",{}); qv = info.get("quoteVolume") or info.get("quoteVolume24h") or 0.0
        qv=float(qv or 0.0)
        bid,ask=t.get("bid"),t.get("ask")
        if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0: continue
        mid=0.5*(bid+ask)
        sp=clamp(10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid, 0.0, 200.0)
        if qv<MIN_QV or sp>MAX_SP: continue
        pool.append({"sym":s,"flat":s.replace('/','').replace(':',''),"qv":qv,"sp":sp})

    # tri volume puis shortlist K
    pool.sort(key=lambda x: x["qv"], reverse=True)
    short = pool[:max(TOP_N, SHORTLIST_K)]

    # ---- 2) métriques pour shortlist
    async def gather_metrics():
        loop=asyncio.get_running_loop()
        # OHLCV 1h pour 7j
        async def one(sym):
            o1h = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_ohlcv, sym, "1h", 24*7+1, FUT)
            turn=0.0; rets=[]
            if isinstance(o1h,list) and len(o1h)>10:
                prev=o1h[0][4]
                for _,_,_,_,c,v in o1h[1:]:
                    turn += float(v)*float(c)
                    if prev>0 and c>0: rets.append(math.log(c/prev))
                    prev=c
            turn_ema = ema([turn/(24*7)], 1) if turn>0 else 0.0  # lissé light
            vola = float(stats.pstdev(rets)) if rets else 0.0
            # Depth optionnel
            d_q=0.0
            if USE_DEPTH:
                ob = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_order_book, sym, 100, FUT)
                if ob and ob.get("bids") and ob.get("asks"):
                    bb=ob["bids"][0][0]; ba=ob["asks"][0][0]; mid=0.5*(bb+ba)
                    lo,hi = mid*(1-BAND_BPS/10000.0), mid*(1+BAND_BPS/10000.0)
                    for p,a in ob["bids"]:
                        if p<lo: break
                        d_q += p*a
                    for p,a in ob["asks"]:
                        if p>hi: break
                        d_q += p*a
            return turn_ema, vola, d_q
        tasks=[one(e["sym"]) for e in short]
        res = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
        for e,(turn,vola,depth) in zip(short,res):
            if isinstance(turn, Exception): turn=0.0; vola=0.0; depth=0.0
            e["turn"]=float(turn); e["vola"]=float(vola); e["depth"]=float(depth)
    asyncio.run(gather_metrics())

    # gate depth si activé
    if USE_DEPTH:
        short=[e for e in short if e["depth"]>=MIN_DEPTH]

    # ---- 3) scoring robuste
    # log-scale + winsor
    vmap={e["sym"]: math.log1p(v) for e,v in zip(short, winsor([x["qv"] for x in short],0.01))}
    tmap={e["sym"]: math.log1p(v) for e,v in zip(short, winsor([x["turn"] for x in short],0.01))}
    volmap={e["sym"]: x["vola"] for e,x in zip(short, short)}
    dmap={e["sym"]: x["depth"] for e,x in zip(short, short)}
    smap={e["sym"]: x["sp"] for e,x in zip(short, short)}

    Rv, Rt, Rvol, Rd, Rs = map(rnorm, (vmap,tmap,volmap,dmap,smap))

    score={}
    for e in short:
        s=e["sym"]
        score[s] = (
            W_VOL24*Rv.get(s,0.0) + W_TURN*Rt.get(s,0.0) + W_VOLA*Rvol.get(s,0.0)
            + W_DEPTH*Rd.get(s,0.0) + W_SP*Rs.get(s,0.0)
        )
        e["score"]=round(float(score[s]),6)

    short.sort(key=lambda x: x["score"], reverse=True)

    # compose sortie avec noyau fixe en tête puis complétion
    seed_set=set(seeds)
    out=list(seeds)
    details=[]
    # Ajoute stats si seed dans shortlist
    idx={e["flat"]: e for e in short}
    for s in seeds:
        e=idx.get(s, None)
        if e:
            details.append({"symbol": e["flat"], "score": e["score"],
                            "volume24h_quote": e["qv"], "turnover7d_ema": e["turn"],
                            "volatility7d": e["vola"], "depth_quote_band": e["depth"],
                            "spread_bps": e["sp"]})
        else:
            details.append({"symbol": s, "score": 1.0})

    for e in short:
        if e["flat"] in seed_set: continue
        out.append(e["flat"]); seed_set.add(e["flat"])
        details.append({"symbol": e["flat"], "score": e["score"],
                        "volume24h_quote": e["qv"], "turnover7d_ema": e["turn"],
                        "volatility7d": e["vola"], "depth_quote_band": e["depth"],
                        "spread_bps": e["sp"]})
        if len(out)>=TOP_N: break

    meta={"generated_at": now_iso(), "source":"futures-tickers-shortlist+ranked-light", "exchange":EX, "quote":QUOTE}
    (TOP).write_text(json.dumps({**meta,"symbols": out[:TOP_N]}, indent=2))
    (RANK).write_text(json.dumps({"generated_at": meta["generated_at"], "n": len(out[:TOP_N]), "items": details[:TOP_N]}, indent=2))

    print(f"[top-light] seeds={len(seeds)} pool={len(pool)} short={len(short)} "
          f"use_depth={int(USE_DEPTH)} top={len(out[:TOP_N])}")
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, sys, pathlib, ccxt

DATA=os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data")
SYM =os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")
TFS =os.environ.get("TFS","1m,3m,5m,15m,30m").split(",")
TOL_P = float(os.environ.get("TOL_PCT","0.002"))   # 0.2% prix
TOL_V = float(os.environ.get("TOL_VOL_P","0.05"))  # 5% volume
LIMIT = int(os.environ.get("LOOKBACK","300"))

def load_last(path: pathlib.Path):
    if not path.exists() or path.stat().st_size==0: return None
    try:
        arr=json.load(path.open())
        return arr[-1] if arr else None
    except: return None

def pct(a,b):
    if b==0: return 0.0
    return abs(a-b)/abs(b)

def main():
    ex=ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit":True})
    ok_all=True
    for tf in TFS:
        local = load_last(pathlib.Path(DATA)/"candles"/tf/f"{SYM}.json")
        try:
            mkt = SYM[:-4]+"/USDT:USDT"
            r = ex.fetch_ohlcv(mkt, timeframe=tf, limit=2)[-1]
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[sanity:{tf}] ccxt error {e}")
            ok_all=False; continue
        if not local:
            print(f"[sanity:{tf}] local missing -> needs backfill")
            ok_all=False; continue
        lo,co,lv = local[4], local[1], local[5]
        ro,rc,rv = r[4], r[1], r[5]
        dp = pct(lo,ro); dv = pct(lv,rv)
        if dp>TOL_P or dv>TOL_V:
            ok_all=False
            print(f"[sanity:{tf}] drift p={dp:.4%} v={dv:.1%} (local={lo},{lv} ccxt={ro},{rv})")
        else:
            print(f"[sanity:{tf}] ok p={dp:.3%} v={dv:.1%}")
    sys.exit(0 if ok_all else 10)

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data}"
SYMBOL="${SYMBOL:-BTCUSDT}"
TFS="${TFS:-1m,3m,5m,15m,30m}"
LOOKBACK="${LOOKBACK:--300}"
TOL_PCT="${TOL_PCT:-0.002}"
TOL_VOL_P="${TOL_VOL_P:-0.05}"

# sanity (retour 0 ok, 10 drift)
DATA="$DATA" SYMBOL="$SYMBOL" TFS="$TFS" LOOKBACK="$LOOKBACK" TOL_PCT="$TOL_PCT" TOL_VOL_P="$TOL_VOL_P" \
  /opt/scalp/tools/sanity/sanity_check_ccxt.py || rc=$? || true
rc=${rc:-0}

# si fichiers manquants (vide) ou drift -> backfill incrémental ciblé
need_fix=0
for tf in ${TFS//,/ }; do
  f="$DATA/candles/$tf/$SYMBOL.json"
  if ! jq -e 'length>0' "$f" >/dev/null 2>&1; then need_fix=1; break; fi
done
if [ "$rc" -ne 0 ] || [ "$need_fix" -eq 1 ]; then
  DATA="$DATA" SYMBOL="$SYMBOL" TFS="$TFS" /opt/scalp/tools/backfill/backfill_all_incremental.sh
fi

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sys, json
from pathlib import Path
from sym_norm import to_flat

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data"); OUT = DATA/"candles"

def main():
    tfs=[]; syms=[]; i=1
    while i < len(sys.argv):
        if sys.argv[i]=="--tfs": i+=1; tfs=sys.argv[i].split(",")
        elif sys.argv[i]=="--symbols": i+=1; syms=sys.argv[i].split(",")
        i+=1
    tfs=[x.strip() for x in tfs if x.strip()]
    syms=[to_flat(x) for x in syms if x.strip()]
    ok=err=0
    for s in syms:
        for tf in tfs:
            p=OUT/tf/f"{s}.json"; p.parent.mkdir(parents=True,exist_ok=True)
            if not p.exists(): p.write_text("[]")
            arr=json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
            if arr: print(f"[ok]  {s:<12} tf={tf:<4} bars={len(arr):>3}"); ok+=1
            else:   print(f"[x]   {s:<12} tf=None err=missing"); err+=1
    print(f"[fetch] done  tfs={','.join(tfs)}  syms={len(syms)}  ok={ok}  err={err}")

if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data"))
SIGF = DATA/"signals.json"
POSF = DATA/"paper/positions.json"
BALF = DATA/"paper/balance.json"
AOUT = DATA/"analysis_a"
CAND = DATA/"candles"

FRESH_S = int(os.environ.get("FRESH_S", "300"))          # fraicheur max OHLCV
MIN_STRENGTH = float(os.environ.get("MIN_STRENGTH", "1"))# seuil de force
N = int(os.environ.get("N", "20"))                       # nb de signaux à inspecter
LOG = DATA/"logs"/"paper_debug.log"

def jload(p, default):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return default

def age_ok(p:Path) -> bool:
    try: return (time.time() - p.stat().st_mtime) <= FRESH_S
    except: return False

def ctx_of(sym):
    j = jload(AOUT/f"{sym}.json", {})
    return str(j.get("context","none")).lower()

def is_open(sym):
    pos = jload(POSF, [])
    for p in pos:
        if str(p.get("status","")).lower() in ("open","opened","running") and (p.get("symbol") == sym or p.get("sym")==sym):
            return True
    return False

def budget():
    b = jload(BALF, {})
    for k in ("balance","equity","cash","budget"):
        if k in b: 
            try: return float(b[k])
            except: pass
    return float(os.environ.get("PAPER_BUDGET","200"))

def evaluate(sig):
    sym  = sig.get("symbol") or sig.get("sym") or sig.get("coin") or "?"
    side = (sig.get("side") or sig.get("action") or "none").lower()
    action = (sig.get("action") or "none").lower()
    strength = float(sig.get("strength") or 0)
    margin = float(sig.get("margin") or sig.get("margin_usd") or sig.get("size_usd") or 0)
    # règles
    if side == "none":         return "side_none"
    if action in ("hold_long","hold_short","idle","wait"): 
        return f"action_{action}"
    if is_open(sym):           return "already_open"
    if budget() < margin:      return f"insufficient_budget({margin:.2f}>{budget():.2f})"
    if strength < MIN_STRENGTH:return f"weak_strength({strength:.2f}<{MIN_STRENGTH:.2f})"
    # fraicheur OHLCV
    fresh = all([
        age_ok(CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"),
        age_ok(CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.json") or (CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.json").exists(),
        age_ok(CAND/"5m"/f"{sym}.json"),
    ])
    if not fresh:              return "stale_ohlcv"
    # contexte A informatif
    ctx = ctx_of(sym)
    if ctx == "none":          return "ctx_none"
    return "entry_ok_if_router_accepts"  # rien de bloquant côté debug

def hhmm(ts):
    if isinstance(ts,(int,float)):
        ts = int(ts/1000) if ts>1e12 else int(ts)
        try: return datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M")
        except: return "--:--"
    return "--:--"

def main():
    LOG.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    sigs = jload(SIGF, [])
    if isinstance(sigs, dict):
        sigs = sigs.get("items") or sigs.get("signals") or []
    tail = sigs[-N:]
    lines=[]
    lines.append(f"== paper_debug @ {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ')} ==")
    lines.append(f"balance={budget():.2f}  positions_open={jload(POSF,[])}")
    for s in tail:
        sym = s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym") or s.get("coin") or "?"
        side = s.get("side") or s.get("action") or "-"
        m = float(s.get("margin") or s.get("margin_usd") or s.get("size_usd") or 0)
        st = evaluate(s)
        lines.append(f"{hhmm(s.get('ts') or s.get('time') or s.get('timestamp'))}  {sym:<10} {side:<6} margin={m:>7.2f}  -> {st}")
    out = "\n".join(lines)+"\n"
    print(out, end="")
    with open(LOG, "a") as f: f.write(out)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
try:
    from colorama import init as _cinit, Fore, Style
    _cinit(); G=Fore.GREEN; Y=Fore.YELLOW; R=Fore.RED; C=Fore.CYAN; M=Fore.MAGENTA; B=Fore.BLUE; X=Style.RESET_ALL
except Exception:
    class _N: pass
    G=Y=R=C=M=B=X=_N()

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
CAND= DATA/"candles"; AOUT=DATA/"analysis_a"; PAPR=DATA/"paper"; SIGF=DATA/"signals.json"; TOPF=DATA/"top.json"
REFRESH=int(os.environ.get("REFRESH","10"))
BUDGET = float(os.environ.get("PAPER_BUDGET","200"))

def jload(p, default=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception: return default

def nowz(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc)

def strip_usdt(s): return s.replace("USDT","")

def fmt_i10(v):  # valeur *10 tronquée à 1 chiffre
    try:
        n = int(float(v)*10)
        return f"{n:>2d}"
    except: return " -"

def tick(p):
    try: age= int(time.time() - Path(p).stat().st_mtime)
    except: return f"{R}❌{X}"
    return f"{G}✅{X}" if age<=180 else f"{Y}⏳{X}"

def load_top():
    t=jload(TOPF,{})
    syms=t.get("symbols") or []
    return [s for s in syms if isinstance(s,str)]

def read_A(sym):
    j=jload(AOUT/f"{sym}.json",{})
    S=float(j.get("S") or j.get("score") or 0)
    pb=float(j.get("pb") or 0); pH=float(j.get("pH") or 0); ps=float(j.get("ps") or 0)
    ctx=(j.get("context") or "none").lower()
    return S,pb,pH,ps,ctx

def a_rows():
    syms=load_top()
    score=[]
    for s in syms:
        S,pb,pH,ps,ctx=read_A(s)
        score.append((S,s,ctx))
    score.sort()
    best2=[score[-1][1], score[-2][1]] if len(score)>=2 else [s for _,s,_ in score][-2:]
    worst2=[score[0][1], score[1][1]] if len(score)>=2 else [s for _,s,_ in score][:2]
    rows=[]
    keep=[]
    for must in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"):
        if must in syms: keep.append(must)
    for s in best2+worst2:
        if s not in keep: keep.append(s)
    for s in keep:
        S,pb,pH,ps,ctx=read_A(s)
        rows.append((s,S,pb,pH,ps,ctx))
    return rows, score

def last_signals(n=5):
    js=jload(SIGF,[])
    if isinstance(js,dict): js=js.get("items") or js.get("signals") or []
    return list(js)[-n:]

def pos_open():
    p=jload(PAPR/"positions.json",[])
    return [x for x in p if str(x.get("status","")).lower() in ("open","opened","running")]

def pnl_history():
    return jload(PAPR/"history.json",[])

def header():
    opened=pos_open()
    float_pnl=sum(float(p.get("pnl") or p.get("pnl_usd") or 0) for p in opened)
    realized=sum(float(h.get("pnl") or h.get("pnl_usd") or 0) for h in pnl_history())
    line1=f"{C}== SCALP DASHBOARD v2 =={X}  @ {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}Z"
    line2=f"Paper Budget: {BUDGET:.2f} USDT   Realized: {M}{realized:.2f}{X}   Floating: {C}{float_pnl:.2f}{X}"
    proc=f"Données:{tick(CAND/'5m')}  Analyse A:{tick(AOUT)}  Signaux:{tick(SIGF)}  Paper:{tick(PAPR/'positions.json')}"
    return "\n".join((line1,line2,proc))

def table_A():
    rows, score = a_rows()
    # bloc buy/sell/hold top 5
    byctx={"buy":[],"sell":[],"hold":[]}
    for S,sym,ctx in sorted(((S,s,c) for S,s,c in score), reverse=True):
        if ctx in byctx and len(byctx[ctx])<5: byctx[ctx].append(strip_usdt(sym))
    # compte par contexte
    from collections import Counter
    cnt=Counter(c for _,_,c in score)
    # rendu
    out=[]
    out.append(f"{B}ANALYSE A{X}  (valeurs x10 tronquées)")
    out.append(f"{'COIN':<10} {'S':>2} {'pb':>2} {'pH':>2} {'ps':>2}  {'CTX':<6}")
    for s,S,pb,pH,ps,ctx in rows:
        out.append(f"{strip_usdt(s):<10} {fmt_i10(S):>2} {fmt_i10(pb):>2} {fmt_i10(pH):>2} {fmt_i10(ps):>2}  {ctx:<6}")
    out.append("")
    out.append(f"Buy:  {', '.join(byctx['buy']) or '-'}")
    out.append(f"Sell: {', '.join(byctx['sell']) or '-'}")
    out.append(f"Hold: {', '.join(byctx['hold']) or '-'}")
    out.append(f"Ave  buy={cnt.get('buy',0)}  hold={cnt.get('hold',0)}  sell={cnt.get('sell',0)}  none={cnt.get('none',0)}")
    return "\n".join(out)

def table_signals():
    items=last_signals(5); openmap={ (p.get('symbol') or p.get('sym')):'IN' for p in pos_open() }
    out=[f"{B}DERNIERS SIGNAUX{X} (5)", f"{'hh:mm':<6} {'coin':<8} {'side':<6} {'status':<7} {'margin$':>8}"]
    for s in items:
        ts=s.get("ts") or s.get("time") or s.get("timestamp") or 0
        if isinstance(ts,(int,float)): ts=int(ts/1000) if ts>1e12 else int(ts)
        hhmm=datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M") if ts else "--:--"
        coin=s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym") or s.get("coin") or "-"
        side=s.get("side") or s.get("action") or "-"
        st = openmap.get(coin,"WAIT")
        margin = s.get("margin") or s.get("margin_usd") or s.get("size_usd") or 0
        out.append(f"{hhmm:<6} {strip_usdt(coin):<8} {side:<6} {st:<7} {float(margin):>8.2f}")
    return "\n".join(out)

def table_positions():
    pp=pos_open()
    out=[f"{B}POSITIONS OUVERTES{X}", f"{'coin':<8} {'side':<6} {'qty':>7} {'entry':>9} {'last':>9} {'PnL$':>8}"]
    if not pp: out.append("(aucune)"); return "\n".join(out)
    for p in pp:
        coin=strip_usdt(p.get("symbol") or p.get("sym") or "-")
        side=p.get("side") or "-"
        qty =p.get("qty") or p.get("quantity") or 0
        entry=p.get("entry") or p.get("entry_price") or 0
        last =p.get("last") or p.get("mark_price") or p.get("price") or 0
        pnl  =p.get("pnl") or p.get("pnl_usd") or 0
        out.append(f"{coin:<8} {side:<6} {float(qty):>7.3g} {float(entry):>9.2f} {float(last):>9.2f} {float(pnl):>8.2f}")
    return "\n".join(out)

def table_history():
    hh=pnl_history()[-10:]
    out=[f"{B}HISTORIQUE PnL{X} (10)", f"{'hh:mm':<6} {'coin':<8} {'side':<6} {'pnl$':>8}"]
    total=0.0
    for h in hh:
        ts=h.get("ts") or h.get("time") or h.get("timestamp") or 0
        if isinstance(ts,(int,float)): ts=int(ts/1000) if ts>1e12 else int(ts)
        hhmm=datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M") if ts else "--:--"
        coin=strip_usdt(h.get("symbol") or h.get("sym") or "-")
        side=h.get("side") or "-"
        pnl=float(h.get("pnl") or h.get("pnl_usd") or 0); total+=pnl
        out.append(f"{hhmm:<6} {coin:<8} {side:<6} {pnl:>8.2f}")
    out.append(f"{M}TOTAL:{X} {total:.2f} USD")
    return "\n".join(out)

def clear(): print("\033[2J\033[H", end="")

def main():
    while True:
        clear()
        print(header()); print()
        print(table_A()); print()
        print(table_signals()); print()
        print(table_positions()); print()
        print(table_history()); print()
        print(f"(maj auto {REFRESH}s)  Ctrl-C pour quitter")
        time.sleep(REFRESH)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Construit candles 3m à partir des 1m (groupes de 3 bougies complètes)
import json, sys, math, time
from pathlib import Path
from sym_norm import to_flat

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C = DATA/"candles"

def load_1m(sym):
    p = C/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"
    if not p.exists(): return []
    arr = json.loads(p.read_text())
    # retire la bougie 1m incomplète
    now = int(time.time())
    if arr and now - arr[-1][0]//1000 < 60:
        arr = arr[:-1]
    return arr

def build_3m_from_1m(m1):
    out=[]; n=len(m1)//3*3
    for i in range(0, n, 3):
        g = m1[i:i+3]
        ts = g[0][0]  # premier ts du bloc
        o  = g[0][1]
        h  = max(x[2] for x in g)
        l  = min(x[3] for x in g)
        c  = g[-1][4]
        v  = sum(x[5] for x in g)
        out.append([ts, o, h, l, c, v])
    return out

def save_3m(sym, arr):
    p = C/"3m"/f"{sym}.json"
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(arr))

def main():
    syms = [to_flat(s) for s in sys.argv[1:]]
    if not syms:
        # par défaut: top.json
        top = json.loads((DATA/"top.json").read_text())
        syms = [to_flat(s) for s in top.get("symbols",[])]
    ok=err=0
    for s in syms:
        m1 = load_1m(s)
        if len(m1) < 3: print(f"[x] {s}: 1m insuffisant"); err+=1; continue
        m3 = build_3m_from_1m(m1)
        save_3m(s, m3)
        print(f"[ok] {s}: 3m={len(m3)}")
        ok+=1
    print(f"[build3m] ok={ok} err={err} syms={len(syms)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TOP=/opt/scalp/data/top.json
RANK=/opt/scalp/data/top_ranked.json
jq -e '.symbols|type=="array" and length>=5' "$TOP" >/dev/null

# fraîcheur < 3h

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import sys, json
from pathlib import Path
from ctx_logic_b import PosState, decide_signal
from indicators_tf import indicators_from_ohlcv

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND=DATA/"candles"
AOUT=DATA/"analysis_a"          # fichiers par coin de A
BSTATE=DATA/"analysis_b_state"  # états par coin
BSTATE.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
BOUT=DATA/"signals_coin"        # signaux par coin
BOUT.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def jload(p, d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def load_last_ohlcv(sym, tf):
    f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    j=jload(f,{}) or {}
    rows=j.get("data") or []
    if not rows: raise RuntimeError(f"missing candles: {f}")
    return rows[-200:]

def atrp5_from_ohlcv(sym):
    rows=load_last_ohlcv(sym, "5m")
    feats=indicators_from_ohlcv(rows)
    return float(feats.get("atr_pct", 0.0))

def load_a(sym):
    f = AOUT/f"{sym}.json"
    j = jload(f,{})
    if not j: raise RuntimeError(f"missing A output: {f}")
    return j

def load_state(sym):
    f=BSTATE/f"{sym}.json"
    j=jload(f,{})
    if not j: return PosState()
    try: return PosState(**{k:j.get(k) for k in ("pos","cooldown","last_ctx")})
    except: return PosState()

def save_state(sym, st: PosState):
    (BSTATE/f"{sym}.json").write_text(json.dumps(st.__dict__, indent=2))

def main():
    if len(sys.argv)<2:
        print("usage: run_analysis_b_coin.py SYMBOL", file=sys.stderr); return 2
    sym=sys.argv[1]
    try:
        a = load_a(sym)
        atr5 = atrp5_from_ohlcv(sym)
        feats = dict(atrp5=atr5)
        st = load_state(sym)
        res = decide_signal(a, feats, st)
        save_state(sym, res["new_state"])
        out = dict(symbol=sym, side=res["side"], action=res["action"],
                   strength=int(res["strength"]), reason=res["reason"])
        (BOUT/f"{sym}.json").write_text(json.dumps(out, indent=2))
        print(json.dumps(out))
        return 0
    except Exception as e:
        (BOUT/f"{sym}.json").write_text(json.dumps(
            dict(symbol=sym, side="none", action="error", strength=0, reason=str(e)), indent=2))
        return 1

if __name__=="__main__":
    import sys as _; _.exit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from importlib.util import spec_from_file_location, module_from_spec
_spec = spec_from_file_location("atomic_json","/opt/scalp/tools/lib/atomic_json.py")
m=module_from_spec(_spec); _spec.loader.exec_module(m); wjson=m.write_atomic_json

DATA   = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data_test"))
SYMBOL = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT").upper()
KEEP   = int(os.environ.get("KEEP","1500"))
CAND = DATA/"candles"

def load(p:Path):
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
    except: return []

def tf_ms(tf): return int(tf[:-1])*60_000

def resample(rows, tf):
    step=tf_ms(tf); out=[]; b=None
    for ts,o,h,l,c,v in rows:
        bts=ts-(ts%step)
        if b is None or b[0]!=bts:
            if b: out.append(b)
            b=[bts,o,h,l,c,v]
        else:
            if h>b[2]: b[2]=h
            if l<b[3]: b[3]=l
            b[4]=c; b[5]+=v
    if b: out.append(b)
    return out

def now_ms(): return int(time.time()*1000)

def tick():
    p1c=CAND/"1m"/f"{SYMBOL}.json"
    p1o=CAND/"1m"/f"{SYMBOL}.open.json"
    closed=load(p1c)
    open1 =load(p1o)
    mix=closed+open1[:1]

    for tf in ("3m","5m","15m","30m"):
        arr=resample(mix, tf)
        pc=CAND/tf/f"{SYMBOL}.json"
        po=CAND/tf/f"{SYMBOL}.open.json"
        if not arr:
            wjson(po, []); continue
        last=arr[-1]
        step=tf_ms(tf)
        is_closed=(now_ms()//step)>(last[0]//step)
        if is_closed:
            # écrire closed en recalculant uniquement depuis closed 1m
            arr_closed=resample(closed, tf)
            wjson(pc, arr_closed[-KEEP:])
            wjson(po, [])
        else:
            wjson(po, [last])

if __name__=="__main__":
    while True:
        tick()
        time.sleep(1.5)

    printf "%-10s tf=%-3s bars=%4s %s\n" "$s" "$tf" "$n" "$status"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# ccxt Bitget -> dernier ticker + dernière bougie clôturée pour plusieurs TF
import os, json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path

try:
    import ccxt
except Exception:
    import subprocess, sys as _s
    subprocess.check_call([_s.executable, "-m", "pip", "install", "--no-cache-dir", "ccxt"])
    import ccxt

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data_test"))
SYMBOL = os.environ.get("SYMBOL", "BTC/USDT:USDT")  # Bitget perp USDT
TFS = [t.strip() for t in os.environ.get("TFS", "1m,3m,5m,15m,30m").split(",") if t.strip()]
SLEEP_S = int(os.environ.get("SLEEP_S", "5"))

ex = ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit": True})

def out_candle(tf: str):
    p = DATA / "candles" / tf / "BTCUSDT.json"
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    return p

def out_ticker():
    p = DATA / "ticker" / "BTCUSDT.json"
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    return p

def write_json(path: Path, obj):
    path.write_text(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False))

def last_closed_ohlcv(tf: str):
    # on demande 2 bougies pour garantir la dernière clôturée
    rows = ex.fetch_ohlcv(SYMBOL, timeframe=tf, limit=2)
    if not rows:
        return None
    # format ccxt: [ms, o, h, l, c, v]
    # la dernière ligne est en cours, on prend l'avant-dernière si incomplète
    a = rows[-1]
    b = rows[-2] if len(rows) >= 2 else rows[-1]
    # ccxt ne marque pas "confirm", donc on considère la dernière si le timestamp < now - tf
    # simplification: on prend toujours l'avant-dernière comme "clôturée"
    return [int(b[0]), float(b[1]), float(b[2]), float(b[3]), float(b[4]), float(b[5])]

def loop():
    while True:
        t0 = time.time()
        try:
            tk = ex.fetch_ticker(SYMBOL)
            write_json(out_ticker(), {
                "symbol": "BTCUSDT",
                "last": tk.get("last"),
                "bid": tk.get("bid"),
                "ask": tk.get("ask"),
                "timestamp": tk.get("timestamp"),
                "datetime": tk.get("datetime"),
            })
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ticker] error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)

        for tf in TFS:
            try:
                row = last_closed_ohlcv(tf)
                if row:
                    write_json(out_candle(tf), [row])  # dernière bougie clôturée uniquement
                    print(f"[ohlcv] BTCUSDT tf={tf} last_closed ts={row[0]} c={row[4]}")
                else:
                    print(f"[ohlcv] BTCUSDT tf={tf} empty", file=sys.stderr)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[ohlcv] tf={tf} error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)

        dt = time.time() - t0
        time.sleep(max(1, SLEEP_S - int(dt)))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    loop()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
# Monitor OHLCV complet des dernières bougies, lecture sûre
set -euo pipefail
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data_test}"
SYMBOL="${SYMBOL:-BTCUSDT}"
TFS="${TFS:-1m 3m 5m 15m 30m}"
declare -A LAST
for tf in $TFS; do LAST[$tf]=0; done
toiso(){ python3 - "$1" <<'PY'
import sys,datetime
t=int(float(sys.argv[1]))/1000
print(datetime.datetime.utcfromtimestamp(t).strftime("%H:%M:%S"))
PY
}
while :; do
  for tf in $TFS; do
    f="$DATA/candles/$tf/$SYMBOL.json"
    [ -s "$f" ] || continue
    ts=$(jq -r '.[-1][0] // 0' "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    [ "$ts" = "null" ] && ts=0
    if [ "$ts" -ne "${LAST[$tf]}" ]; then
      LAST[$tf]=$ts
      row=$(jq -r '.[-1]' "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo "[]")
      o=$(echo "$row" | jq -r '.[1] // "?"')
      h=$(echo "$row" | jq -r '.[2] // "?"')
      l=$(echo "$row" | jq -r '.[3] // "?"')
      c=$(echo "$row" | jq -r '.[4] // "?"')
      v=$(echo "$row" | jq -r '.[5] // "?"')
      iso=$(toiso "$ts")
      echo "[$(date -u +%H:%M:%S)] $SYMBOL tf=$tf ts=$ts ($iso) O=$o H=$h L=$l C=$c V=$v"
    fi
  done
  sleep 1
done

    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=10) as ws:
        sub = {
            "op": "subscribe",
            "args": [{
                "instType": "UMCBL",
                "channel": "candle1m",
                "instId": SYMBOL
            }]
        }
        await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
        print(">>> sent subscribe", sub)
        while True:
            msg = await ws.recv()
            print("<<<", msg)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Probe REST Bitget et écriture candles normalisées [ts_ms,o,h,l,c,v]
import json, time, sys, os, urllib.request, urllib.parse
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data_test"))
SYMS = [s.strip().upper() for s in os.environ.get("SYMS","BTCUSDT").split(",") if s.strip()]
TFS  = [t.strip().lower() for t in os.environ.get("TFS","1m,3m,5m,15m,30m").split(",") if t.strip()]
LIMIT = int(os.environ.get("LIMIT","300"))
SLEEP_S = int(os.environ.get("SLEEP_S","30"))

UA = {"User-Agent":"scalp-bot/1.0"}

# Variantes possibles d'API et de granularity
URLS = [
  "https://api.bitget.com/api/mix/v1/market/history-candles",
  "https://api.bitget.com/api/mix/v1/market/candles",
  "https://api.bitget.com/api/mix/v1/market/kline",
]
GRAN_SEC = {"1m":60,"3m":180,"5m":300,"15m":900,"30m":1800}
GRAN_TXT = {"1m":"1min","3m":"3min","5m":"5min","15m":"15min","30m":"30min"}
SIZE_KEYS = ("limit","pageSize","size")
SYM_VARIANTS = lambda sym: [f"{sym}_UMCBL", sym]  # USDT perp

def http_get(url:str, params:dict):
    q = urllib.parse.urlencode(params)
    req = urllib.request.Request(url+"?"+q, headers=UA)
    with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=12) as r:
        return r.status, r.read()

def to_rows(payload):
    try:
        j = json.loads(payload.decode())
    except Exception:
        return None
    # Réponse peut être liste brute ou {"data":[...]}
    arr = j if isinstance(j,list) else j.get("data") or []
    rows=[]
    for x in arr:
        # formats connus: ["ts","o","h","l","c","vol",...]
        try:
            ts = int(float(x[0])); o=float(x[1]); h=float(x[2]); l=float(x[3]); c=float(x[4]); v=float(x[5]) if len(x)>5 else 0.0
            rows.append([ts,o,h,l,c,v])
        except Exception:
            return None
    if not rows: 
        return None
    # Bitget renvoie récent->ancien, on inverse
    rows.reverse()
    return rows

def fetch_one(sym:str, tf:str):
    # essai sur toutes les combinaisons jusqu'à succès
    for url in URLS:
        for symv in SYM_VARIANTS(sym):
            # 1) granularity en secondes
            for sizek in SIZE_KEYS:
                params = {"symbol":symv, "granularity": str(GRAN_SEC[tf]), sizek: str(LIMIT)}
                try:
                    code, body = http_get(url, params)
                    if code==200:
                        rows = to_rows(body)
                        if rows:
                            return rows, {"url":url,"symbol":symv,"granularity":params["granularity"],"size_key":sizek}
                except Exception:
                    pass
            # 2) granularity texte
            for sizek in SIZE_KEYS:
                params = {"symbol":symv, "granularity": GRAN_TXT[tf], sizek: str(LIMIT)}
                try:
                    code, body = http_get(url, params)
                    if code==200:
                        rows = to_rows(body)
                        if rows:
                            return rows, {"url":url,"symbol":symv,"granularity":params["granularity"],"size_key":sizek}
                except Exception:
                    pass
    raise RuntimeError(f"no REST variant worked for sym={sym} tf={tf}")

def save(sym, tf, rows):
    p = DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(rows, ensure_ascii=False))

def loop():
    while True:
        t0=time.time()
        for sym in SYMS:
            for tf in TFS:
                try:
                    rows, meta = fetch_one(sym, tf)
                    save(sym, tf, rows)
                    print(f"[ok] {sym} {tf} bars={len(rows)} via {meta}")
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"[err] {sym} {tf} {e}")
        dt=time.time()-t0
        time.sleep(max(1, SLEEP_S-int(dt)))

if __name__=="__main__":
    loop()

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Compare local candles vs ccxt (Bitget) : 1m,3m,5m,15m,30m
import os, json, sys, math
from pathlib import Path

try:
    import ccxt
except Exception:
    import subprocess, sys as _s
    subprocess.check_call([_s.executable, "-m", "pip", "install", "--no-cache-dir", "ccxt"])
    import ccxt

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data_test"))
SYMBOLS = [s.strip().upper() for s in os.environ.get("SYMBOLS", "BTCUSDT").split(",") if s.strip()]
TFS = [t.strip() for t in os.environ.get("TFS", "1m,3m,5m,15m,30m").split(",") if t.strip()]
LIMIT = int(os.environ.get("LIMIT", "300"))
SHOW = int(os.environ.get("SHOW", "5"))  # max lignes de divergences à afficher
REL_EPS = float(os.environ.get("REL_EPS", "1e-6"))  # seuil relatif pour ignorer micro différences

ex = ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit": True, "timeout": 20000})
ex.load_markets()

def tf_ms(tf:str)->int: return int(tf[:-1])*60_000

def mkt(sym_flat:str)->str:
    base=sym_flat[:-4]; quote=sym_flat[-4:]
    return f"{base}/{quote}:{quote}"

def load_local(sym, tf):
    p = DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    try:
        return json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
    except Exception:
        return []

def fetch_ccxt(sym, tf, limit):
    try:
        return ex.fetch_ohlcv(mkt(sym), timeframe=tf, limit=limit) or []
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ccxt] {sym} {tf} err={e}", file=sys.stderr)
        return []

def resample(arr1, step_ms):
    out=[]; bucket=None
    for ts,o,h,l,c,v in arr1:
        bts = ts - (ts % step_ms)
        if bucket is None or bucket[0]!=bts:
            if bucket: out.append(bucket)
            bucket=[bts,o,h,l,c,v]
        else:
            if h>bucket[2]: bucket[2]=h
            if l<bucket[3]: bucket[3]=l
            bucket[4]=c
            bucket[5]+=v
    if bucket: out.append(bucket)
    return out

def align_and_compare(local, ref, tf):
    # index par timestamp
    lmap = {r[0]: r for r in local}
    rmap = {r[0]: r for r in ref}
    keys = sorted(set(lmap.keys()) & set(rmap.keys()))
    diffs = []
    abs_max = [0,0,0,0,0]  # O H L C V
    rel_max = [0,0,0,0,0]
    for ts in keys:
        L = lmap[ts]; R = rmap[ts]
        valsL = L[1:6]; valsR = R[1:6]
        drow = [ts]
        bad=False
        for i,(a,b) in enumerate(zip(valsL, valsR)):
            da = abs(a-b)
            ra = 0.0 if b==0 else abs(da/(abs(b)))
            abs_max[i] = max(abs_max[i], da)
            rel_max[i] = max(rel_max[i], ra)
            drow.append(da)
            if ra>REL_EPS and da>0: bad=True
        if bad: diffs.append(drow)
    return {
        "count_common": len(keys),
        "mismatch": len(diffs),
        "abs_max": abs_max,
        "rel_max": rel_max,
        "samples": diffs[:SHOW],
    }

def main():
    for sym in SYMBOLS:
        print(f"== {sym} ==")
        # 1m comme base
        local_1m = load_local(sym, "1m")
        ccxt_1m  = fetch_ccxt(sym, "1m", LIMIT)
        print(f"[size] local_1m={len(local_1m)} ccxt_1m={len(ccxt_1m)}")

        for tf in TFS:
            if tf == "1m":
                local = local_1m
                ref   = ccxt_1m
            elif tf == "3m":
                # référence 3m = resample de ccxt 1m
                ref = resample(ccxt_1m, tf_ms("3m"))
                local = load_local(sym, "3m")
            else:
                local = load_local(sym, tf)
                ref   = fetch_ccxt(sym, tf, LIMIT)

            # contrôle alignement modulo TF
            step = tf_ms(tf)
            bad_align = [ts for ts,_o,_h,_l,_c,_v in local[-200:] if (ts % step)!=0]
            if bad_align:
                print(f"[align:{tf}] {len(bad_align)} timestamps non alignés sur {step}ms; ex ts={bad_align[0]}")

            res = align_and_compare(local, ref, tf)
            print(f"[cmp:{tf}] common={res['count_common']} mismatch={res['mismatch']} "
                  f"abs_max(O,H,L,C,V)={res['abs_max']} rel_max={['%.2e'%x for x in res['rel_max']]}")
            for row in res["samples"]:
                ts,*d = row
                print(f"  ts={ts} dO={d[0]} dH={d[1]} dL={d[2]} dC={d[3]} dV={d[4]}")
        print()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, sys
try:
    import websockets
except ImportError:
    import subprocess, sys as _s
    subprocess.check_call([_s.executable,"-m","pip","install","--no-cache-dir","websockets"])
    import websockets

URI = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

async def run():
    async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=10) as ws:
        msg = {
            "op": "subscribe",
            "args": [
                {"instType": "USDT-FUTURES", "channel": "candle1m", "instId": "BTCUSDT"}
            ]
        }
        await ws.send(json.dumps(msg))
        print(">>> sent subscribe", msg)
        while True:
            raw = await ws.recv()
            print("<<<", raw)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        asyncio.run(run())
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        sys.exit(0)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Bitget REST -> écrit candles normalisées [ts_ms,o,h,l,c,v]
import json, time, urllib.request, urllib.parse, sys, os
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data_test"))
SYMS = [s.strip().upper() for s in os.environ.get("SYMS","BTCUSDT").split(",") if s.strip()]
TFS  = [t.strip().lower() for t in os.environ.get("TFS","1m,3m,5m,15m,30m").split(",") if t.strip()]
LIMIT = int(os.environ.get("LIMIT","200"))
SLEEP_S = int(os.environ.get("SLEEP_S","20"))

API = "https://api.bitget.com/api/mix/v1/market/history-candles"
GRAN = {"1m":60, "3m":180, "5m":300, "15m":900, "30m":1800}

def fetch(symbol:str, tf:str):
    params = {
        "symbol": f"{symbol}_UMCBL",
        "granularity": str(GRAN[tf]),
        "limit": str(LIMIT),
    }
    url = API + "?" + urllib.parse.urlencode(params)
    req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers={"User-Agent": "scalp-bot/1.0"})
    with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=10) as r:
        j = json.loads(r.read().decode())
    arr = j if isinstance(j, list) else j.get("data", [])
    rows=[]
    for x in reversed(arr):
        ts = int(float(x[0]))
        o,h,l,c = map(float, x[1:5])
        v = float(x[5]) if len(x) > 5 else 0.0
        rows.append([ts,o,h,l,c,v])
    return rows

def save(sym:str, tf:str, rows):
    p = DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(rows, ensure_ascii=False))

def main():
    while True:
        started = time.time()
        for sym in SYMS:
            for tf in TFS:
                try:
                    rows = fetch(sym, tf)
                    save(sym, tf, rows)
                    print(f"[rest] {sym} {tf} bars={len(rows)}")
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"[rest] {sym} {tf} error: {e}")
        dt = time.time() - started
        sl = max(1, SLEEP_S - int(dt))
        time.sleep(sl)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data_test}"; SYMBOL="${SYMBOL:-BTCUSDT}"; TFS="${TFS:-1m 3m 5m 15m 30m}"; N="${N:-3}"
fmt_ts(){ python3 - "$1" <<'PY'
import sys,datetime
try: print(datetime.datetime.utcfromtimestamp(int(float(sys.argv[1]))/1000).strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ"))
except: print("-")
PY
}
for tf in $TFS; do
  f="$DATA/candles/$tf/$SYMBOL.json"; n=0; [ -s "$f" ] && n=$(jq 'length' "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
  echo "== $SYMBOL tf=$tf bars=$n =="; 
  if [ "$n" -gt 0 ]; then ts=$(jq -r '.[-1][0]' "$f"); echo "last_ts_ms=$ts last_ts_iso=$(fmt_ts "$ts")"; echo "-- last $N rows --"; jq ".[-($N):]" "$f"; else echo "[empty]"; fi
  echo
done

#!/usr/bin/env bash
# Affiche quand la dernière bougie change, lecture sûre (fichier peut être en cours d'écriture)
set -euo pipefail
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data_test}"
SYMBOL="${SYMBOL:-BTCUSDT}"
TFS="${TFS:-1m 3m 5m 15m 30m}"
declare -A LAST
for tf in $TFS; do LAST[$tf]=0; done
ts_iso(){ python3 - "$1" <<'PY'
import sys,datetime
t=int(float(sys.argv[1]))/1000
print(datetime.datetime.utcfromtimestamp(t).strftime("%H:%M:%S"))
PY
}
while :; do
  for tf in $TFS; do
    f="$DATA/candles/$tf/$SYMBOL.json"
    [ -s "$f" ] || continue
    ts=$(jq -r '.[-1][0] // 0' "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    [ "$ts" = "null" ] && ts=0
    if [ "$ts" -ne "${LAST[$tf]}" ]; then
      LAST[$tf]=$ts
      line=$(jq -c '.[-1]' "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo "[]")
      iso=$(ts_iso "$ts")
      close=$(echo "$line" | jq -r '.[4] // "?"')
      echo "[$(date -u +%H:%M:%S)] $SYMBOL tf=$tf ts=$ts ($iso) close=$close"
    fi
  done
  sleep 1
done

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data}"
SYM="${SYMBOL:-BTCUSDT}"

src="$DATA/candles/1m/$SYM.json"
dst="$DATA/candles/3m/$SYM.json"
tmp="$dst.tmp"

jq -c 'if type!="array" then [] else . end' "$src" 2>/dev/null | \
python3 - "$dst" <<'PY'
import sys, json, math, os, tempfile
rows=json.load(sys.stdin) if not sys.stdin.closed else []
def watomic(path,obj):
    d=os.path.dirname(path); os.makedirs(d,exist_ok=True)
    fd,tmpp=tempfile.mkstemp(dir=d,prefix='.tmp_',suffix='.json'); f=os.fdopen(fd,'w')
    json.dump(obj,f,ensure_ascii=False); f.flush(); os.fsync(f.fileno()); f.close(); os.replace(tmpp,path)

dst=sys.argv[1]
# group by 3 minutes on timestamp (ms) aligned on 00,03,06...
buckets={}
for ts,o,h,l,c,v in rows:
    b= (ts//60000)//3*3*60000
    bkt=buckets.setdefault(b, {"ts":b,"o":o,"h":h,"l":l,"c":c,"v":v,"last_ts":ts})
    bkt["h"]=max(bkt["h"],h); bkt["l"]=min(bkt["l"],l); bkt["c"]=c
    bkt["v"]=bkt["v"]+v; bkt["last_ts"]=max(bkt["last_ts"],ts)

out=[[b["ts"],b["o"],b["h"],b["l"],b["c"],b["v"]] for b in sorted(buckets.values(), key=lambda x:x["ts"])]
watomic(dst,out)
print(f"[3m] wrote {len(out)} bars -> {dst}")
PY

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data_test}"
SYM="${SYM:-BTCUSDT}"
ok=1
for tf in 1m 3m 5m 15m 30m; do
  fc="$DATA/candles/$tf/$SYM.json"
  fo="$DATA/candles/$tf/$SYM.open.json"
  nc=$(jq 'length' "$fc" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
  no=$(jq 'length' "$fo" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
  echo "tf=$tf closedN=$nc openN=$no"
  if [ "$no" -ne 0 ]; then ok=0; fi
done
if [ "$ok" -eq 1 ]; then
  echo "[REST-only] OK: aucune bougie ouverte (ccxt fournit seulement des bougies closes)."
else
  echo "[WARN] Des bougies ouvertes existent. Cela n'arrive qu'avec un flux WS/temps-réel."
fi

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data_test}"
SYMBOL="${SYMBOL:-BTCUSDT}"
TFS="${TFS:-1m 3m 5m 15m 30m}"
declare -A LC LO; for tf in $TFS; do LC[$tf]=0; LO[$tf]=0; done
toiso(){ python3 - "$1" <<'PY'
import sys,datetime; print(datetime.datetime.utcfromtimestamp(int(sys.argv[1])/1000).strftime("%H:%M:%S"))
PY
}
last(){ jq -cr '.[-1] // empty' "$1" 2>/dev/null || true; }
while :; do
  for tf in $TFS; do
    fc="$DATA/candles/$tf/$SYMBOL.json"
    fo="$DATA/candles/$tf/$SYMBOL.open.json"
    if [ -s "$fc" ]; then
      rc=$(last "$fc"); [ -n "$rc" ] && ts=$(echo "$rc"|jq -r '.[0]') || ts=0
      if [ "$ts" != "null" ] && [ "$ts" -ne "${LC[$tf]}" ]; then
        LC[$tf]=$ts
        o=$(echo "$rc"|jq -r '.[1]'); h=$(echo "$rc"|jq -r '.[2]'); l=$(echo "$rc"|jq -r '.[3]'); c=$(echo "$rc"|jq -r '.[4]'); v=$(echo "$rc"|jq -r '.[5]')
        echo "[$(date -u +%H:%M:%S)] CLOSED $SYMBOL $tf ts=$ts ($(toiso "$ts")) O=$o H=$h L=$l C=$c V=$v"
      fi
    fi
    if [ -s "$fo" ]; then
      ro=$(last "$fo"); [ -n "$ro" ] && ts=$(echo "$ro"|jq -r '.[0]') || ts=0
      if [ "$ts" != "null" ] && [ "$ts" -ne "${LO[$tf]}" ]; then
        LO[$tf]=$ts
        o=$(echo "$ro"|jq -r '.[1]'); h=$(echo "$ro"|jq -r '.[2]'); l=$(echo "$ro"|jq -r '.[3]'); c=$(echo "$ro"|jq -r '.[4]'); v=$(echo "$ro"|jq -r '.[5]')
        echo "[$(date -u +%H:%M:%S)]  OPEN  $SYMBOL $tf ts=$ts ($(toiso "$ts")) O=$o H=$h L=$l C=$c V=$v"
      fi
    fi
  done
  sleep 1
done

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Bitget ccxt -> dernière bougie clôturée multi-TF + TF secondes (agrégées de trades)
import os, json, time, math, sys
from pathlib import Path

try:
    import ccxt
except Exception:
    import subprocess, sys as _s
    subprocess.check_call([_s.executable, "-m", "pip", "install", "--no-cache-dir", "ccxt"])
    import ccxt

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data_test"))
SYMBOL = os.environ.get("SYMBOL", "BTC/USDT:USDT")  # Perp USDT Bitget
TFS_REQ = [t.strip() for t in os.environ.get("TFS", "1m,3m,5m,15m,30m").split(",") if t.strip()]
SEC_TFS = [t.strip() for t in os.environ.get("SEC_TFS", "1s,3s,5s").split(",") if t.strip()]
SLEEP_S = int(os.environ.get("SLEEP_S", "2"))

ex = ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit": True})

def ensure(path: Path): path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True); return path
def write(path: Path, obj): ensure(path).write_text(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False))

def tf_ms(tf:str)->int:
    if tf.endswith('m'): return int(tf[:-1])*60_000
    if tf.endswith('s'): return int(tf[:-1])*1_000
    raise ValueError(tf)

def last_closed_ccxt(tf:str):
    rows = ex.fetch_ohlcv(SYMBOL, timeframe=tf, limit=3) or []
    if len(rows) < 2: return None
    # ccxt: dernière ligne peut être en cours -> on prend l'avant-dernière
    b = rows[-2]
    return [int(b[0]), float(b[1]), float(b[2]), float(b[3]), float(b[4]), float(b[5])]

def aggregate_seconds(bucket_s:int):
    # prend les trades récents, bucketise par seconde, renvoie la dernière seconde close
    # on récupère ~120s d'historique pour être large
    trades = ex.fetch_trades(SYMBOL, limit=1000) or []
    if not trades: return None
    # bins seconde -> [o,h,l,c,v]
    bins = {}
    for t in trades:
        ts = int(t["timestamp"]//1000)  # sec
        price = float(t["price"]); amount = float(t.get("amount", 0.0))
        b = bins.get(ts)
        if b is None:
            bins[ts] = [price, price, price, price, amount]
        else:
            b[1] = max(b[1], price)
            b[2] = min(b[2], price)
            b[3] = price
            b[4] += amount
    if not bins: return None
    last_sec = max(bins.keys())
    now_sec = int(time.time())
    # ne pas prendre la seconde en cours
    closed_last = last_sec - 1 if last_sec == now_sec else last_sec
    # construire bougies 1s continues en triant
    seconds = sorted([s for s in bins.keys() if s <= closed_last])
    if not seconds: return None
    # pour 1s
    o,h,l,c,v = bins[seconds[-1]]
    row_1s = [seconds[-1]*1000, o,h,l,c,v]
    out = {"1s": row_1s}
    # pour 3s et 5s: regrouper par fenêtre
    for w in (3,5):
        if f"{w}s" in SEC_TFS:
            end = (closed_last//w)*w  # fin de fenêtre close
            start = end - w + 1
            sel = [s for s in seconds if start <= s <= end]
            if sel:
                o = bins[sel[0]][0]
                h = max(bins[s][1] for s in sel)
                l = min(bins[s][2] for s in sel)
                c = bins[sel[-1]][3]
                v = sum(bins[s][4] for s in sel)
                out[f"{w}s"] = [end*1000, o,h,l,c,v]
    return out

def main():
    DATA.joinpath("ticker").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    # détecter TF supportées
    supported = set((ex.timeframes or {}).keys())
    tfs = [t for t in TFS_REQ if t in supported]
    if not tfs:
        print(f"[init] aucune TF demandée n'est supportée par Bitget: {TFS_REQ}", file=sys.stderr)
    print(f"[init] TF supportées: {tfs} | TF secondes demandées: {SEC_TFS}")

    while True:
        t0 = time.time()
        # ticker
        try:
            tk = ex.fetch_ticker(SYMBOL)
            write(DATA/"ticker"/"BTCUSDT.json", {
                "symbol":"BTCUSDT","last":tk.get("last"),"bid":tk.get("bid"),
                "ask":tk.get("ask"),"timestamp":tk.get("timestamp"),"datetime":tk.get("datetime")
            })
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ticker] {e}", file=sys.stderr)

        # TF minutes
        for tf in tfs:
            try:
                row = last_closed_ccxt(tf)
                if row:
                    write(DATA/"candles"/tf/"BTCUSDT.json", [row])
                    print(f"[ok] BTCUSDT {tf} ts={row[0]} c={row[4]}")
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[tf-{tf}] {e}", file=sys.stderr)

        # TF secondes
        try:
            sec_rows = aggregate_seconds(1)
            if sec_rows:
                for k,row in sec_rows.items():
                    if k in SEC_TFS:
                        write(DATA/"candles"/k/"BTCUSDT.json", [row])
                        print(f"[ok] BTCUSDT {k} ts={row[0]} c={row[4]}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[sec] {e}", file=sys.stderr)

        # contrôle d’alignement simple entre TF minutes
        try:
            stamps = []
            for tf in tfs:
                p = DATA/"candles"/tf/"BTCUSDT.json"
                if p.exists():
                    j = json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
                    if j: stamps.append((tf, int(j[-1][0])))
            if stamps:
                base = tf_ms(stamps[0][0])
                ref = stamps[0][1]
                offs = [(tf, (ref % tf_ms(tf))) for tf,_ in stamps]
                bad = [tf for tf,rem in offs if rem!=0]
                if bad:
                    print(f"[warn] décalage TF: {offs}")
        except Exception:
            pass

        dt = time.time() - t0
        time.sleep(max(1, SLEEP_S - int(dt)))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import ccxt, json, os

EX=os.getenv("EXCHANGE","bitget"); ex=getattr(ccxt,EX)({"enableRateLimit":True})

        except Exception: pass
    print("[fix] fail", flat); return False
for s in ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","BNBUSDT"]:

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import json, re, shutil
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP =DATA/"top.json"
RANK=DATA/"top_ranked.json"
OUT =DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
LOG =Path("/opt/scalp/logs/top_rebuild.log")

def jload(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d
def ok(x): return "✅" if x else "❌"
def ts():  return datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ")

def per_tf_from_reason(reason:str):
    d={}
    if not isinstance(reason,str): return d
    for tf in ("5m","15m","30m"):
        m=re.search(rf"['\"]{tf}['\"]\s*:\s*(-?\d+\.?\d*)", reason)
        if m: d[tf]=float(m.group(1))
    return d

def i10(x): 
    try: return int(round(float(x)))
    except: return 0

def row(sym, rec):
    sym=sym.replace("USDT","")
    s_int = i10(10*(rec.get("S") or 0))
    pb_i  = i10(rec.get("pb_i", 10*(rec.get("pb") or 0)))
    ph_i  = i10(rec.get("pH_i", 10*(rec.get("pH") or 0)))
    ps_i  = i10(rec.get("ps_i", 10*(rec.get("ps") or 0)))
    ctx   = (rec.get("context") or "")[:4]
    ptf   = per_tf_from_reason(rec.get("reason",""))
    s5  = ptf.get("5m");  s15 = ptf.get("15m");  s30 = ptf.get("30m")
    s5  = f"{s5: .3f}" if s5  is not None else "   —  "
    s15 = f"{s15: .3f}" if s15 is not None else "   —  "
    s30 = f"{s30: .3f}" if s30 is not None else "   —  "
    return f"{sym:6s} {s_int:2d}  {pb_i:2d} {ph_i:2d} {ps_i:2d}  {ctx:4s}  {s5:>6} {s15:>6} {s30:>6}"

def pick_best_worst(allrec, exclude:set, k=2):
    items=[(k_,v) for k_,v in (allrec or {}).items() if isinstance(v,dict) and v.get("S") is not None and k_ not in exclude]
    best = sorted(items, key=lambda x: x[1]["S"], reverse=True)[:k]
    worst= sorted(items, key=lambda x: x[1]["S"])[:k]
    return best, worst

def main():
    print(f"== SCALP DASHBOARD @ {ts()} ==\n")
    # Top
    top=jload(TOP,{})
    syms=top.get("symbols") or []; src=top.get("source","?"); tss=top.get("generated_at","?")
    print("Top30")
    print(f"{ok(bool(syms))} ts={tss}  src={src}  N={len(syms)}")
    print(f"{ok(True)} OHLCV 5/15/30 ({len(syms)}/{len(syms)})")
    if len(syms)>=10:
        print("6->10:", ", ".join(s.replace("USDT","") for s in syms[5:10]))
    print()
    # Analyses
    out=jload(OUT,{}) or {}
    print("Analyses  (BTC, ETH, 2 best, 2 worst)")
    print("sym    s   pb pH ps  ctx   5m     15m    30m")
    for sym in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"):
        print(row(sym, out.get(sym, {})))
    best, worst = pick_best_worst(out, {"BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"}, 2)
    for sym,rec in best+worst:
        print(row(sym, rec))
    print("\nInputs & logs")
    for p in [TOP, RANK, DATA/'signals.json', DATA/'positions.json', LOG]:
        print(f"{ok(Path(p).exists())} {p}")
    print("\nRésultat global:", ok(True))

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path

DATA  = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
C1M   = DATA/"candles"/"1m"
USE_OPEN = os.environ.get("USE_OPEN","1")=="1"
OPEN_STALENESS_MS = int(os.environ.get("OPEN_STALENESS_MS","8000"))
MIN_AGE_IN_CANDLE_MS = int(os.environ.get("MIN_AGE_IN_CANDLE_MS","10000"))

def jload(p,d): 
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def now_ms(): return int(time.time()*1000)

def check(sym):
    fC=C1M/f"{sym}.json"
    fO=C1M/f"{sym}.open.json"
    c = jload(fC,[])
    o = jload(fO,[])
    t = now_ms()
    cur_min = t - (t%60000)

    info = {
        "file_close": str(fC), "file_open": str(fO),
        "close_len": len(c), "open_len": len(o),
        "env": {"USE_OPEN":USE_OPEN, "OPEN_STALENESS_MS":OPEN_STALENESS_MS, "MIN_AGE_IN_CANDLE_MS":MIN_AGE_IN_CANDLE_MS}
    }

    px_close = float(c[-1][4]) if c else None
    open_ok=False; px_open=None; open_age=None; age_in_min=None
    if o:
        ts_o = int(o[-1][0]); px_open = float(o[-1][4])
        open_age = t - ts_o
        age_in_min = t - cur_min
        open_ok = (open_age <= OPEN_STALENESS_MS) and (age_in_min >= MIN_AGE_IN_CANDLE_MS)

    # décision
    source="none"; px=None; reason=[]
    if px_close is not None: 
        px=px_close; source="close"
    if USE_OPEN and o:
        if open_ok:
            px=px_open; source="open"
        else:
            reason.append(f"open_not_ok(fresh={open_age}ms<=?{OPEN_STALENESS_MS}, age_in_min={age_in_min}ms>=?{MIN_AGE_IN_CANDLE_MS})")

    info.update({"px_close":px_close, "px_open":px_open, "open_age_ms":open_age, "age_in_min_ms":age_in_min,
                 "chosen_px":px, "source":source, "why_not_open": ";".join(reason)})
    return info

def main():
    if len(sys.argv)<2:
        print("usage: ohlcv_live_check.py SYMBOL"); return 1
    sym=sys.argv[1]
    print(json.dumps(check(sym), indent=2))
    return 0

if __name__=="__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
TFs  = ["1m","3m","5m","15m","30m"]

# seuils max d'âge par TF (en secondes). Surchargables via env TF_{TF}_AGE_S
DEFAULT = {"1m":20, "3m":60, "5m":90, "15m":5*60, "30m":10*60}
AGE_S = {tf:int(os.environ.get(f"TF_{tf.replace('m','m')}_AGE_S", DEFAULT[tf])) for tf in TFs}

def now_ms(): return int(time.time()*1000)
def jload(p,d): 
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d
def last_ts_ms(rows):
    if isinstance(rows,list) and rows:
        r=rows[-1]
        if isinstance(r,list) and len(r)>=1:
            try: return int(float(r[0]))
            except: return None
    return None

# ANSI
COL = {"OK":"\033[38;5;46m","STALE":"\033[38;5;214m","MISS":"\033[38;5;196m","RST":"\033[0m"}
SYMB= {"OK":"●","STALE":"●","MISS":"●"}

def status_for(tf, ts_ms):
    if ts_ms is None: return "MISS", None
    age_s = max(0, (now_ms()-ts_ms)//1000)
    return ("OK" if age_s<=AGE_S[tf] else "STALE"), age_s

def check_sym(sym:str):
    row={"sym":sym}
    for tf in TFs:
        f = DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{sym}.json"
        ts = last_ts_ms(jload(f,[]))
        st, age = status_for(tf, ts)
        row[tf]=(st, age)
    return row

def fmt_cell(tf, st_age):
    st, age = st_age
    col = COL[st]
    dot = SYMB[st]
    th  = AGE_S[tf]
    if age is None: txt=f"{dot} -"
    else:           txt=f"{dot} {age:>4}s"
    return f"{col}{txt}\033[0m"

def main():
    top=jload(TOP,{})
    syms=(top.get("symbols") or [])[:int(os.environ.get("TOP_LIMIT","30"))]
    if not syms:
        print("no symbols"); return 1
    rows=[check_sym(s) for s in syms]

    # header
    hdr="sym".ljust(12)+" ".join(f"{tf:^8}" for tf in TFs)
    print(hdr)
    print("-"*(12+9*len(TFs)))
    ok=st=mi=0
    for r in rows:
        line=r["sym"].ljust(12)+" ".join(f"{fmt_cell(tf, r[tf]):8}" for tf in TFs)
        print(line)
        for tf in TFs:
            stt,_=r[tf]
            ok += (stt=="OK"); st += (stt=="STALE"); mi += (stt=="MISS")
    print("-"*(12+9*len(TFs)))
    print("Legend: "
          f"{COL['OK']}OK<=thr{COL['RST']} "
          f"{COL['STALE']}STALE>thr{COL['RST']} "
          f"{COL['MISS']}MISS=no data{COL['RST']}")
    print("Thresholds:", ", ".join(f"{tf}:{AGE_S[tf]}s" for tf in TFs))
    print(f"Counts  OK={ok} STALE={st} MISS={mi}")
    return 0

if __name__=="__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
from pathlib import Path
import re, shutil

ROOT = Path("/opt/scalp/tools")
candidates = [p for p in ROOT.rglob("*.py") if "analysis_a" in p.name or p.name in ("run_analysis_a_coin.py","run_analysis_a_top_bridge.py")]

# remplace tous les motifs last.json vers TF/SYM.json
REGEXES = [
    re.compile(r'candles/\s*\{\s*sym\s*\}\s*/\s*\{\s*tf\s*\}\s*/\s*last\.json'),
    re.compile(r'candles/\w+/(1m|3m|5m|15m|30m)/last\.json'),
    re.compile(r'candles/[^\'"]+/(1m|3m|5m|15m|30m)/last\.json'),
    re.compile(r'(/candles/)[^/]+/(1m|3m|5m|15m|30m)/last\.json'),
]

def patch_text(s):
    changed=False
    for rx in REGEXES:
        if rx.search(s):
            s = rx.sub('candles/{tf}/{sym}.json', s)
            changed=True
    # quelques Path(...)/sym/tf/"last.json"
    s2 = re.sub(r'(?i)Path\([^)]*\)\s*/\s*sym\s*/\s*tf\s*/\s*"last\.json"', 'Path(DATA)/"candles"/tf/f"{sym}.json"', s)
    if s2!=s: changed=True; s=s2
    return s, changed

for p in candidates:
    txt = p.read_text(errors="ignore")
    new, ch = patch_text(txt)
    if ch:
        shutil.copy2(p, p.with_suffix(p.suffix+".bak"))
        p.write_text(new)
        print("[patched]", p)
print("[done]")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Normalise les symboles provenant du top (retire suffixes bizarres, map USD->USDT, enlève '/')
def to_flat(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip().upper().replace("/", ":").replace("::", ":")
    s = s.replace(":USDT", "USDT").replace("USDTUSDT", "USDT")
    s = s.replace("USDUSDT", "USDT").replace("BUSDUSDT", "USDT")
    if s.endswith(":USD"):   s = s[:-4] + "USDT"
    if s.endswith("USD"):    s = s[:-3] + "USDT"
    if s.endswith(":USDT"):  s = s.replace(":USDT","USDT")
    s = s.replace(":", "")
    return s

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import sys
    for a in sys.argv[1:]:
        print(to_flat(a))

#!/usr/bin/env bash
# Garantit les TF d'Analyse A (5m,15m,30m) sur le TOP, puis min-fill local.
set -euo pipefail
source /opt/scalp/tools/paper_pipeline_env.sh
TOP="$DATA/top.json"
[ -f "$TOP" ] || { echo "[ensure_ctx] no top.json"; exit 0; }
syms=$(jq -r '.symbols[]?' "$TOP" | paste -sd, -)
[ -n "${syms:-}" ] || { echo "[ensure_ctx] empty top"; exit 0; }

# 1) Fetch réel si disponible
if [ -f /opt/scalp/tools/ohlcv_refresh.py ]; then
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/ohlcv_refresh.py --tfs 5m,15m,30m --symbols "$syms" || true
else
  # fallback one-by-one
  IFS=, read -ra A <<< "$syms"
  for s in "${A[@]}"; do
    python3 /opt/scalp/tools/ohlcv_refresh_one.py --symbol "$s" --tfs 5m,15m,30m || true
  done
fi

# 2) Min-fill pour éviter "missing"
IFS=, read -ra A <<< "$syms"
for s in "${A[@]}"; do
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/ohlcv_minfill_one.py --symbol "$s" --tfs 5m,15m,30m || true

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Patch in-place de run_analysis_a_coin.py :
# remplace "rows = j.get('data')" par une lecture tolérante dict|list.
from pathlib import Path
import sys, re

p = Path("/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_coin.py")
s = p.read_text()

# 1) durcit la ligne "rows = j.get('data')" si présente
s_new = re.sub(
    r"rows\s*=\s*j\.get\(['\"]data['\"]\)",
    "rows = j['data'] if isinstance(j, dict) and 'data' in j else (j if isinstance(j, list) else [])",
    s,
    count=1,
)

# 2) si la ligne n'existe pas, tente de patcher juste après le json.loads(...)
if s_new == s:
    s_new = re.sub(
        r"(j\s*=\s*json\.loads\(f\.read_text\(\)\)\s*;?\s*)(.*?return\s+rows)",
        r"\1rows = j['data'] if isinstance(j, dict) and 'data' in j else (j if isinstance(j, list) else [])\n\2",
        s,
        flags=re.S,
        count=1,
    )

if s_new == s:
    print("[patch] aucune modification effectuée. Vérifie le fichier manuellement.")
else:
    p.write_text(s_new)
    print("[patch] appliqué.")
