#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, asyncio, time, sys, traceback
from pathlib import Path

# ---- atomic writer ----
from importlib.util import spec_from_file_location, module_from_spec
_spec = spec_from_file_location("atomic_json","/opt/scalp/tools/lib/atomic_json.py")
if not _spec or not _spec.loader:
    print("[err] /opt/scalp/tools/lib/atomic_json.py manquant", file=sys.stderr); sys.exit(1)
_atomic = module_from_spec(_spec); _spec.loader.exec_module(_atomic)
write_atomic_json = _atomic.write_atomic_json

try:
    import websockets
except Exception:
    import subprocess, sys as _s
    subprocess.check_call([_s.executable,"-m","pip","install","--no-cache-dir","websockets"])
    import websockets

DATA   = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data_test"))
SYMBOL = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT").upper()
KEEP   = int(os.environ.get("KEEP","1500"))
LOGDIR = DATA/"logs"; LOGDIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
LOGF   = LOGDIR/"ws_open_auto.log"

CAND = DATA/"candles"
for tf in ("1m","3m","5m","15m","30m"):
    (CAND/tf).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def log(*a):
    msg = " ".join(str(x) for x in a)
    print(msg, flush=True)
    try:
        with LOGF.open("a") as f: f.write(msg+"\n")
    except: pass

def tf_ms(tf:str)->int: return int(tf[:-1])*60_000
def jload(p:Path):
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
    except: return []
def jdump(p:Path, arr): write_atomic_json(p, (arr or [])[-KEEP:])

def resample(rows, tf:str):
    step=tf_ms(tf); out=[]; b=None
    for ts,o,h,l,c,v in rows:
        bts = ts - (ts % step)
        if b is None or b[0]!=bts:
            if b: out.append(b)
            b=[bts,o,h,l,c,v]
        else:
            if h>b[2]: b[2]=h
            if l<b[3]: b[3]=l
            b[4]=c; b[5]+=v
    if b: out.append(b)
    return out

def _to_int(x):
    try: return int(x)
    except: return 0
def _to_float(x):
    try: return float(x)
    except: return 0.0

def _extract_row_dict(x:dict):
    ts = x.get("ts") or x.get("time") or x.get("t")
    if ts is None: return None
    ts = _to_int(ts)
    o=_to_float(x.get("open") or x.get("o") or x.get("op"))
    h=_to_float(x.get("high") or x.get("h"))
    l=_to_float(x.get("low")  or x.get("l"))
    c=_to_float(x.get("close")or x.get("c"))
    v=_to_float(x.get("volume") or x.get("v"))
    return [ts,o,h,l,c,v]

def _extract_row_list(x:list):
    # formats possibles: [ts, o, h, l, c, v, ...] ou strings
    if len(x) < 6: return None
    ts=_to_int(x[0]); o=_to_float(x[1]); h=_to_float(x[2]); l=_to_float(x[3]); c=_to_float(x[4]); v=_to_float(x[5])
    return [ts,o,h,l,c,v]

def parse_kline(msg):
    # Bitget peut envoyer: dict, list[dict], dict{data=[dict|list], action:snapshot|update}
    if isinstance(msg, list):
        for it in msg:
            r = parse_kline(it)
            if r: return r
        return None
    if not isinstance(msg, dict): return None
    d = msg.get("data")
    if isinstance(d, list) and d:
        x = d[0]
        if isinstance(x, dict): return _extract_row_dict(x)
        if isinstance(x, list): return _extract_row_list(x)
    if isinstance(d, dict):
        return _extract_row_dict(d)
    # top-level direct
    if isinstance(msg, dict):
        r = _extract_row_dict(msg)
        if r: return r
    return None

ENDPOINTS = [
    ("wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public", [
        {"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"candle1m","instId":SYMBOL}]},
        {"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"USDT-MIX","channel":"candle1m","instId":SYMBOL}]},
        {"op":"subscribe","args":[{"productType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"candle1m","instId":SYMBOL}]},
        {"op":"subscribe","args":[{"productType":"USDT-MIX","channel":"candle1m","instId":SYMBOL}]},
    ]),
    ("wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream?compress=false", [
        {"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"UMCBL","channel":"candle1m","instId":f"{SYMBOL}_UMCBL"}]},
        {"op":"subscribe","args":[{"channel":"candle1m","instId":f"{SYMBOL}_UMCBL"}]},
        {"op":"subscribe","args":[{"channel":"candle1m","instId":SYMBOL}]},
    ]),
]

async def probe_sub(ws, payloads):
    last=None
    for pay in payloads:
        await ws.send(json.dumps(pay))
        try:
            for _ in range(5):
                raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=5)
                try: msg = json.loads(raw)
                except: continue
                if isinstance(msg, dict) and msg.get("event")=="subscribe":
                    return pay
                if isinstance(msg, dict) and msg.get("event")=="error":
                    last = msg; break
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            continue
    raise RuntimeError(f"subscribe failed last_err={last}")

async def run():
    sym = SYMBOL
    open1m = CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.open.json"
    closed1m = CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"
    while True:
        for uri, payloads in ENDPOINTS:
            try:
                async with websockets.connect(uri, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=10, max_size=2**20) as ws:
                    log("[ws] connect ->", uri, "probe…")
                    ok = await probe_sub(ws, payloads)
                    log("[ws] subscribed ok with", ok)
                    while True:
                        raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=60)
                        try: msg = json.loads(raw)
                        except: 
                            continue
                        row = parse_kline(msg)
                        if not row:
                            # dump quelques messages pour debug
                            if isinstance(msg, dict) and msg.get("event") not in ("subscribe","error"):
                                log("[ws] unparsed", str(msg)[:180])
                            continue
                        # write open 1m
                        jdump(open1m, [row])
                        # derive open TF sup
                        mix1 = jload(closed1m) + [row]
                        for tf in ("3m","5m","15m","30m"):
                            arr = resample(mix1, tf)
                            if not arr:
                                jdump(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.open.json", [])
                                continue
                            last = arr[-1]
                            step = tf_ms(tf)
                            is_closed = (int(time.time()*1000)//step) > (last[0]//step)
                            jdump(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.open.json", [] if is_closed else [last])
            except Exception as e:
                log("[ws] error on", uri, ":", e)
                traceback.print_exc()
                await asyncio.sleep(2)
                continue

if __name__=="__main__":
    try: asyncio.run(run())
    except KeyboardInterrupt: pass

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Collecte BTCUSDT Bitget perp USDT. WS avec auto-essais de formats + fallback REST.
import os, json, asyncio, sys, time, ssl, contextlib
from pathlib import Path
try:
    import websockets, certifi, aiohttp
    from websockets.exceptions import ConnectionClosedOK, ConnectionClosedError
except Exception as e:
    print(f"deps missing: {e}. run: pip3 install --no-cache-dir websockets certifi aiohttp"); sys.exit(1)

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
MAX_BARS = int(os.environ.get("WS_MAX_BARS","2000"))
SYMS = [s.strip().upper() for s in os.environ.get("WS_SYMBOLS","BTCUSDT").split(",") if s.strip()]
TFS  = [t.strip().lower() for t in os.environ.get("WS_TFS","1m,3m,5m,15m,30m").split(",") if t.strip()]

# Endpoints
WS_URLS = ["wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream?compress=false","wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream"]
REST_K = "https://api.bitget.com/api/mix/v1/market/candles"   # params: symbol, granularity

SSL_CTX = ssl.create_default_context(cafile=certifi.where())

def _out(tf, sym): p = DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{sym}.json"; p.parent.mkdir(parents=True,exist_ok=True); return p
def _load(p): 
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
    except: return []
def _save(p, arr):
    if len(arr)>MAX_BARS: arr = arr[-MAX_BARS:]
    p.write_text(json.dumps(arr, ensure_ascii=False))

def _r(c):  # normalize one candle item to [ts_ms,o,h,l,c,v]
    return [int(c[0]), float(c[1]), float(c[2]), float(c[3]), float(c[4]), float(c[5] if len(c)>5 else 0.0)]

def _row_from_ws(item:dict):
    if "o" in item:
        return [int(float(item.get("ts") or item.get("t"))), float(item["o"]), float(item["h"]), float(item["l"]), float(item["c"]), float(item.get("baseVol") or item.get("v") or 0.0)]
    if "candle" in item:
        c = item["candle"]; return _r(c)
    return None

# permutations connues du protocole
INSTTYPES = ["umcbl","UMCBL"]     # USDT perp
CHANNELS  = lambda tf: [f"candle{tf}", f"candle{tf.replace('m','M')}"]
INSTIDS   = lambda sym: [f"{sym}_UMCBL", sym]  # avec et sans suffixe

async def ws_try_once(ws, sym, tf):
    # essaye permutations jusqu'à un 'event:subscribe' sans 'Param error'
    errors=[]
    for it in INSTTYPES:
        for ch in CHANNELS(tf):
            for iid in INSTIDS(sym):
                sub = {"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":it,"channel":ch,"instId":iid}]}
                await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
                try:
                    msg = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=3.0)
                except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                    continue
                try:
                    j = json.loads(msg)
                except Exception:
                    continue
                if isinstance(j,dict) and j.get("event")=="error":
                    errors.append(j)
                    if "Param error" in str(j): 
                        continue
                if isinstance(j,dict) and j.get("event")=="subscribe":
                    return {"instType":it,"channel":ch,"instId":iid}
    print(f"[ws] subscribe failed for {sym},{tf}. last_errors={errors[-2:]}")  # montre 2 derniers
    return None

async def ws_loop():
    while True:
        for url in WS_URLS:
            try:
                print(f"[ws] connect -> {url}")
                async with websockets.connect(url, ssl=SSL_CTX, ping_interval=None, close_timeout=1.0, max_queue=2048) as ws:
                    # s'abonner pour tous sym x tf avec permutations
                    ok_specs=[]
                    for sym in SYMS:
                        for tf in TFS:
                            spec = await ws_try_once(ws, sym, tf)
                            if spec: 
                                ok_specs.append(spec)
                    if not ok_specs:
                        raise RuntimeError("no successful subscription")
                    print(f"[ws] subscribed specs={ok_specs}")
                    # boucle réception
                    while True:
                        try:
                            msg = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=25)
                        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                            # pas de ping client: Bitget n'aime pas {"op":"ping"}
                            continue
                        except (ConnectionClosedOK, ConnectionClosedError):
                            break
                        try:
                            j = json.loads(msg)
                        except Exception:
                            continue
                        arg = j.get("arg",{}); data = j.get("data",[])
                        if not data: 
                            continue
                        tf = str(arg.get("channel","")).replace("candle","").replace("M","m")
                        sym = (arg.get("instId","") or "").split("_")[0]
                        for it in data:
                            if not it.get("confirm", False): 
                                continue
                            row = _row_from_ws(it)
                            if not row: 
                                continue
                            p = _out(tf, sym); arr = _load(p)
                            if arr and int(arr[-1][0]) == row[0]: arr[-1] = row
                            else: arr.append(row)
                            _save(p, arr)
                        # log léger
                        if data:
                            print(f"[ws] wrote {sym} {tf} bars={len(_load(_out(tf,sym)))}")
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[ws] reconnect: {type(e).__name__}: {e}")
                await asyncio.sleep(1.5)
                continue

async def rest_fill_once(session, sym, tf, limit=120):
    # granularity: 60,180,300,900,1800
    gran = {"1m":60,"3m":180,"5m":300,"15m":900,"30m":1800}[tf]
    params = {"symbol": f"{sym}_UMCBL", "granularity": str(gran),"limit": str(limit)}
    try:
        async with session.get(REST_K, params=params, timeout=8) as r:
            if r.status != 200: 
                return False
            j = await r.json()
            arr = j if isinstance(j, list) else j.get("data") or []
            # Bitget REST renvoie le plus récent en premier → inverser
            rows = [_r(x) for x in reversed(arr)]
            if not rows: return False
            p = _out(tf, sym)
            _save(p, rows)
            print(f"[rest] seeded {sym} {tf} bars={len(rows)}")
            return True
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[rest] fail {sym} {tf}: {e}")
        return False

async def main_async():
    # seed REST pour éviter '0 barres'
    async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
        for sym in SYMS:
            for tf in TFS:
                await rest_fill_once(session, sym, tf)
    # puis WS
    await ws_loop()

def main():
    try:
        asyncio.run(main_async())
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("[stop]")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, ccxt, time, tempfile, shutil
from pathlib import Path

DATA=os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data_test")
SYM=os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")
TFS=os.environ.get("TFS","1m,3m,5m,15m,30m").split(",")

def atomic_write(path, obj):
    tmp = Path(path).with_suffix(".tmp")
    with open(tmp,"w") as f: json.dump(obj,f, separators=(",",":"))
    shutil.move(tmp, path)

def fetch(tf, limit=1000):
    ex=ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit":True})
    base = SYM[:-4]; quote = SYM[-4:]
    mkt = f"{base}/{quote}:{quote}"
    return ex.fetch_ohlcv(mkt, timeframe=tf, limit=limit)

def merge_keep_new(old, new):
    d={r[0]:r for r in old}
    for r in new: d[r[0]]=r
    return [d[k] for k in sorted(d)]

def run():
    for tf in TFS:
        fp=f"{DATA}/candles/{tf}/{SYM}.json"
        os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(fp), exist_ok=True)
        old=[]
        try:
            with open(fp,"r") as f: old=json.load(f)
        except: pass
        rows=fetch(tf,1000)
        merged=merge_keep_new(old, rows)
        atomic_write(fp, merged)
        print(f"[backfill] {SYM} {tf} n={len(merged)}")
if __name__=="__main__": run()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, pathlib, sys
import ccxt

DATA = pathlib.Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
SYM  = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")
TF   = os.environ.get("TF","1m")           # 1m,3m,5m,15m,30m
LIMIT= int(os.environ.get("LIMIT","1000"))

# map TF -> ccxt timeframe; Bitget supporte 1m/3m/5m/15m/30m
TF_OK = {"1m":"1m","3m":"3m","5m":"5m","15m":"15m","30m":"30m"}

def ensure_dir(p: pathlib.Path):
    p.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def atomic_write_json(path: pathlib.Path, arr):
    tmp = path.with_suffix(".json.tmp")
    with tmp.open("w") as f:
        json.dump(arr, f, separators=(",",":"))
    tmp.replace(path)

def fetch_ohlcv(ex, symbol, tf, limit):
    # ccxt attend le format "BTC/USDT:USDT" chez bitget pour futures USDT
    mkt = symbol[:-4]+"/USDT:USDT"
    return ex.fetch_ohlcv(mkt, timeframe=tf, limit=limit)

def resample_from_1m(rows, factor):
    # rows: [[ts,o,h,l,c,v], ...] en 1m alignés minute
    out=[]
    for i in range(0, len(rows)//factor * factor, factor):
        chunk = rows[i:i+factor]
        ts   = chunk[0][0]
        o    = chunk[0][1]
        h    = max(r[2] for r in chunk)
        l    = min(r[3] for r in chunk)
        c    = chunk[-1][4]
        v    = sum(r[5] for r in chunk)
        out.append([ts,o,h,l,c,v])
    return out

def load_json(path):
    if path.exists() and path.stat().st_size>0:
        try: return json.load(path.open())
        except: return []
    return []

def main():
    ex = ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit": True})
    # backfill TF demandé
    target_dir = DATA/"candles"/TF
    ensure_dir(target_dir)
    out_file = target_dir/f"{SYM}.json"

    # si TF non supporté, on recompose depuis 1m
    if TF not in TF_OK or (TF=="3m" and "3m" not in TF_OK):
        # fallback resample depuis 1m
        base = DATA/"candles"/"1m"/f"{SYM}.json"
        base_rows = load_json(base)
        if TF=="3m": rows = resample_from_1m(base_rows, 3)
        elif TF=="5m": rows = resample_from_1m(base_rows, 5)
        elif TF=="15m": rows= resample_from_1m(base_rows, 15)
        elif TF=="30m": rows= resample_from_1m(base_rows, 30)
        else: rows=[]
        atomic_write_json(out_file, rows)
        print(f"[backfill] {SYM} {TF} from 1m -> {len(rows)} bars")
        return

    # sinon on prend directement CCXT
    rows = fetch_ohlcv(ex, SYM, TF_OK[TF], LIMIT)
    atomic_write_json(out_file, rows)
    print(f"[backfill] {SYM} {TF} ccxt -> {len(rows)} bars")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

MTime: 2025-09-27 12:54:23.825138924 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, pathlib, ccxt

DATA = pathlib.Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
SYM  = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")
TF   = os.environ.get("TF","1m")           # 1m,3m,5m,15m,30m
LIMIT= int(os.environ.get("LIMIT","1000"))

TF_MS = {"1m":60_000,"3m":180_000,"5m":300_000,"15m":900_000,"30m":1_800_000}

def ensure_dir(p: pathlib.Path): p.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
def load_json(path): 
    if path.exists() and path.stat().st_size>0:
        try: return json.load(path.open())
        except: return []
    return []
def atomic_write(path, arr):
    tmp = path.with_suffix(".json.tmp")
    with tmp.open("w") as f: json.dump(arr,f,separators=(",",":"))
    tmp.replace(path)
def fetch_ohlcv(ex, symbol, tf, since=None, limit=1000):
    mkt = symbol[:-4]+"/USDT:USDT"
    return ex.fetch_ohlcv(mkt, timeframe=tf, since=since, limit=limit)

def main():
    ex = ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit": True})
    out_file = DATA/"candles"/TF/f"{SYM}.json"
    ensure_dir(out_file.parent)

    rows = load_json(out_file)
    last_ts = rows[-1][0] if rows else None
    since = (last_ts + TF_MS[TF]) if last_ts else None

    new_rows=[]
    while True:
        batch = fetch_ohlcv(ex, SYM, TF, since=since, limit=LIMIT)
        if not batch: break
        if last_ts: batch = [r for r in batch if r[0] > last_ts]
        if not batch: break
        new_rows.extend(batch)
        if len(batch) < LIMIT: break
        since = batch[-1][0] + TF_MS[TF]

    if new_rows:
        merged = rows + new_rows
        atomic_write(out_file, merged)
        print(f"[inc] {SYM} {TF}: +{len(new_rows)} -> {len(merged)}")
    else:
        print(f"[inc] {SYM} {TF}: up-to-date")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, os, sys, time
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
import ccxt

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
OUT  = DATA/"candles"  # stockage isolé, non intrusif

# Env tunables
TF_LIST = os.getenv("TF_LIST","5m,15m,30m,1h").split(",")
LIMIT   = int(os.getenv("LIMIT","600"))           # ~600 bougies / tf
WORKERS = int(os.getenv("FETCH_WORKERS","12"))    # parallélisme IO
RATE_MS = int(os.getenv("FETCH_RATE_MS","200"))   # throttle ccxt
EX      = os.getenv("EXCHANGE","bitget")
QUOTE   = os.getenv("QUOTE","USDT")
FUTPAR  = {"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}

def now_iso(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

def load_symbols():
    j = json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    syms = [s for s in j.get("symbols") or []]
    # map flat -> ccxt symbol (BTCUSDT -> BTC/USDT:USDT si présent)
    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    imap={}
    for m in ex.markets.values():
        if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE:
            imap[m["symbol"].replace("/","").replace(":","")] = m["symbol"]
    ccxt_syms = []
    for flat in syms:
        s = imap.get(flat)
        if s: ccxt_syms.append((flat,s))
    return ccxt_syms

class Throttle:
    def __init__(self, rate_ms): self.rate=rate_ms/1000; self._t=0.0
    async def wait(self):
        dt = time.time()-self._t
        if dt < self.rate: await asyncio.sleep(self.rate-dt)
        self._t = time.time()

async def fetch_symbol(loop, ex, flat, sym, tf, limit, throttle):
    await throttle.wait()
    try:
        ohlcv = await loop.run_in_executor(None, lambda: ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, tf, None, limit, FUTPAR))
        if not isinstance(ohlcv, list): return 0
        d = OUT/flat/tf; d.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        (d/"last.json").write_text(json.dumps({"generated_at":now_iso(),"symbol":sym,"tf":tf,"data":ohlcv[-limit:]}, indent=0))
        return len(ohlcv)
    except Exception:
        return 0

async def run():
    pairs = load_symbols()
    if not pairs: 
        print("[ohlcv-top] no mapped symbols")
        return
    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
    sem = asyncio.Semaphore(WORKERS)
    throttle = Throttle(RATE_MS)
    async def one(flat, sym):
        out=0
        async with sem:
            for tf in TF_LIST:
                out += await fetch_symbol(loop, ex, flat, sym, tf, LIMIT, throttle)
        return flat, out
    tasks=[one(f,s) for f,s in pairs]
    res = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
    ok = sum(1 for r in res if isinstance(r, tuple) and r[1]>0)
    print(f"[ohlcv-top] symbols={len(pairs)} ok={ok} tf={','.join(TF_LIST)} workers={WORKERS}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA=/opt/scalp/data; C=$DATA/candles; TRASH=$C/.trash_$(date -u +%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ)
mkdir -p "$TRASH"/{5m,15m,30m}

for tf in 5m 15m 30m; do
  shopt -s nullglob; for f in "$C/$tf"/*.json; do
    base=${f##*/}; base=${base%.json}
    [[ ${OK[$base]+x} ]] || mv -f "$f" "$TRASH/$tf/" || true
  done
done
echo "[gc] déplacé dans $TRASH"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
# Quick validator: pour chaque symbole dans top.json, montre le dernier OHLCV par TF

set -euo pipefail
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data}"
TOP="${TOP:-$DATA/top.json}"
TFS="${TFS:-1m 3m 5m 15m 30m}"

[[ -f "$TOP" ]] || { echo "[err] top file not found: $TOP"; exit 1; }

echo "== processes =="
pgrep -af orchestrator.sh || echo "(no orchestrator)"
echo

jq -r '.symbols[]' "$TOP" | while read -r SYM; do
  echo "== $SYM =="
  for tf in $TFS; do
    f="$DATA/candles/$tf/$SYM.json"
    if [[ -s "$f" ]]; then
      # dernier candle et taille fichier
      last=$(jq -c '.[-1]' "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo null)
      n=$(jq 'length' "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
      printf "tf=%-3s n=%-5s last=%s\n" "$tf" "$n" "${last}"
    else
      printf "tf=%-3s last=[missing]\n" "$tf"
    fi
  done
  echo
done

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import asyncio, json, os
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
WORKERS = int(os.getenv("ANALYSIS_WORKERS","8"))

# scripts existants
A_COIN = "/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_coin.py"
B_COIN = "/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_coin.py"  # s'il n'existe pas, on ignore

def load_symbols():
    j=json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    return [s for s in j.get("symbols") or []]

async def run_coin(cmd):
    proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(*cmd, stdout=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL)
    await proc.wait()
    return proc.returncode

async def main():
    syms = load_symbols()
    if not syms:
        print("[analysis-pool] no symbols"); return
    sem = asyncio.Semaphore(WORKERS)
    async def one(sym):
        async with sem:
            rc1 = await run_coin(("python3", A_COIN, sym))
            rc2 = 0
            if Path(B_COIN).exists():
                rc2 = await run_coin(("python3", B_COIN, sym))
            return sym, max(rc1, rc2)
    tasks=[one(s) for s in syms]
    res=await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
    fails=[r[0] for r in res if isinstance(r,tuple) and r[1]!=0]
    print(f"[analysis-pool] total={len(syms)} fails={len(fails)} workers={WORKERS}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

MTime: 2025-09-27 16:11:18.431572921 +0000

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, re, sys
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"

USDT_TAIL = re.compile(r'(USDT)+$', re.IGNORECASE)
SEP = re.compile(r'[/\-_]')

def norm(sym:str)->str:
    if not sym: return ""
    s = sym.strip().upper()
    s = SEP.sub("", s)            # retire / - _
    if s.endswith("USDT"):
        s = USDT_TAIL.sub("USDT", s)  # BTCUSDTUSDT -> BTCUSDT
    return s

def uniq_stable(seq):
    seen=set(); out=[]
    for x in seq:
        if x not in seen:
            seen.add(x); out.append(x)
    return out

def main():
    if not TOP.exists():
        print(f"[ERR] missing {TOP}", file=sys.stderr); return 1
    try:
        data=json.loads(TOP.read_text())
        symbols=list(data.get("symbols") or [])
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERR] bad json {TOP}: {e}", file=sys.stderr); return 1
    fixed=[norm(s) for s in symbols]
    fixed=[s for s in fixed if s]            # retire vides
    fixed=uniq_stable(fixed)                 # dédup conserve ordre
    TOP.write_text(json.dumps({"symbols": fixed}, separators=(",",":")))
    print(f"[top-fix] {len(symbols)} -> {len(fixed)} symbols")
    for s in fixed[:20]:
        print(" -", s)
    return 0

if __name__=="__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Opener PAPER robuste: ouvre sur enter_* ou convertit hold_* si FORCE_ENTRY=1.
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
P_SIG = DATA/"signals.json"
P_POS = DATA/"paper"/"positions.json"
P_BAL = DATA/"paper"/"balance.json"
FORCE = str(os.environ.get("FORCE_ENTRY","0")) in ("1","true","True")
def jload(p, d): 
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d
def jdump(p, x):
    Path(p).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    Path(p).write_text(json.dumps(x, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
def last_close(symbol:str):
    for tf in ("1m","3m","5m"):
        f = DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{symbol}.json"
        if not f.exists(): continue
        try:
            a = json.loads(f.read_text() or "[]")
            if not a: continue
            x=a[-1]
            if isinstance(x, dict):
                for k in ("close","c","Close"):
                    if k in x: return float(x[k])
            if isinstance(x,(list,tuple)) and len(x)>=5: return float(x[4])
        except: 
            pass
    return None
def norm_side(s):
    s=str(s).lower()
    if s in ("buy","long"): return "long"
    if s in ("sell","short"): return "short"
    return "long"
def main():
    sigs = jload(P_SIG, [])
    pos  = jload(P_POS, [])
    bal  = jload(P_BAL, {"cash":200.0})
    opened=0; now=time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())
    for s in sigs:
        if not isinstance(s, dict): continue
        sym = s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym")
        if not sym: continue
        act = str(s.get("action","")).lower()
        side = s.get("side") or s.get("dir") or ("long" if "buy" in act else "short")
        if act.startswith("enter_"):
            pass
        elif act.startswith("hold_") and FORCE:
            # transforme en entrée forcée
            side = "long" if "long" in act or "buy" in act else "short"
        else:
            continue
        entry = s.get("entry") or s.get("entry_price") or last_close(sym) or 0.0
        size  = float(s.get("size") or 1.0)
        sl    = s.get("sl"); tp = s.get("tp")
        pos.append({
            "symbol": sym,
            "side": norm_side(side),
            "entry": float(entry),
            "size": size,
            "sl": float(sl) if sl is not None else None,
            "tp": float(tp) if tp is not None else None,
            "status": "open",
            "opened_at": now
        })
        opened += 1
    if opened:
        jdump(P_POS, pos)
        jdump(P_BAL, {"cash": float(bal.get("cash",200.0))})
    print(f"[paper-open] opened={opened} cash={float(bal.get('cash',0.0)):.2f}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
D=/opt/scalp/data/candles
mkdir -p "$D/1m" "$D/5m" "$D/15m" "$D/30m"

#  A. coin/TF/last.json  ->  TF/coin.json
find "$D" -mindepth 3 -maxdepth 3 -type f -name 'last.json' | while read -r f; do
  coin="$(basename "$(dirname "$(dirname "$f")")")"
  tf="$(basename "$(dirname "$f")")"
  mkdir -p "$D/$tf"
  ln -sfn "$f" "$D/$tf/${coin}.json"
done

#  B. TF/coin.json  ->  coin/TF/last.json
#     (si le consumer inverse existe)
find "$D" -mindepth 2 -maxdepth 2 -type f -name '*.json' | while read -r f; do
  tf="$(basename "$(dirname "$f")")"
  coin="$(basename "$f" .json)"
  mkdir -p "$D/${coin}/${tf}"
  [ -e "$D/${coin}/${tf}/last.json" ] || ln -sfn "$f" "$D/${coin}/${tf}/last.json"
done

#  C. (option) si fichier manquant, marquer pour refetch
missing=0
for tf in 1m 5m 15m 30m; do
  for coin in $(jq -r '.symbols[]' /opt/scalp/data/top.json 2>/dev/null || echo); do
    [ -f "$D/$tf/${coin}.json" ] || { echo "[MISSING] $tf/$coin"; missing=1; }
  done
done

if [ "$missing" = 1 ]; then
  echo "[fix] some candles missing -> ask fetcher to force."
fi

import re
def normalize(sym:str)->str:
    s=sym.replace("/","").replace(":","")
    s=re.sub(r"_U?MCBL$","",s); s=re.sub(r"PERP$","USDT",s)
    s=re.sub(r"(USDT){2}$","USDT",s)   # FIX
    return s

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Suivi/fermeture PAPER minimal et robuste.
# Hypothèses de champs: symbol, side in {long,buy,short,sell}, entry, sl, tp, size, status.
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data"))
P_POS = DATA / "paper" / "positions.json"
P_BAL = DATA / "paper" / "balance.json"

def jload(p: Path, d):
    try:
        return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception:
        return d

def jdump(p: Path, obj):
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))

def last_close(symbol: str) -> float | None:
    # essaie 1m puis 3m
    for tf in ("1m", "3m"):
        f = DATA / "candles" / tf / f"{symbol}.json"
        if not f.exists():
            continue
        try:
            arr = json.loads(f.read_text() or "[]")
            if not arr:
                continue
            x = arr[-1]
            # formats possibles: dict ou [ts,o,h,l,c,v]
            if isinstance(x, dict):
                for k in ("close", "c", "Close"):
                    if k in x and isinstance(x[k], (int, float)):
                        return float(x[k])
            if isinstance(x, (list, tuple)) and len(x) >= 5:
                return float(x[4])
        except Exception:
            continue
    return None

def is_long(side: str) -> bool:
    return str(side).lower() in ("long", "buy")

def main():
    pos = jload(P_POS, [])
    bal = jload(P_BAL, {"cash": 0.0})
    cash = float(bal.get("cash", 0.0))

    changed = False
    now = time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())

    for p in pos:
        status = str(p.get("status", "open")).lower()
        if not status.startswith("open"):
            continue
        sym = p.get("symbol") or p.get("sym")
        side = p.get("side", "")
        entry = float(p.get("entry") or p.get("entry_price") or 0)
        size = float(p.get("size") or 0)
        sl = p.get("sl")
        tp = p.get("tp")
        px = last_close(sym) if sym else None
        if not sym or size == 0 or entry == 0 or px is None:
            # impossible de monitorer, on skippe proprement
            p["last_px"] = px
            p["last_ts"] = now
            continue

        hit = None
        if is_long(side):
            if sl is not None and px <= float(sl): hit = "SL"
            if tp is not None and px >= float(tp): hit = "TP" if hit is None else hit
            pnl = (px - entry) * size
        else:
            if sl is not None and px >= float(sl): hit = "SL"
            if tp is not None and px <= float(tp): hit = "TP" if hit is None else hit
            pnl = (entry - px) * size

        p["last_px"] = px
        p["unrealized"] = pnl

        if hit:
            p["status"] = f"closed_{hit}"
            p["closed_at"] = now
            p["pnl"] = pnl
            cash += pnl
            changed = True

    if changed:
        jdump(P_POS, pos)
        jdump(P_BAL, {"cash": round(cash, 8)})

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, asyncio, time, sys, traceback
from pathlib import Path

# atomic
from importlib.util import spec_from_file_location, module_from_spec
_spec = spec_from_file_location("atomic_json","/opt/scalp/tools/lib/atomic_json.py")
if not _spec or not _spec.loader:
    print("[err] /opt/scalp/tools/lib/atomic_json.py manquant", file=sys.stderr); sys.exit(1)
_atomic = module_from_spec(_spec); _spec.loader.exec_module(_atomic)
write_atomic_json = _atomic.write_atomic_json

try:
    import websockets
except Exception:
    import subprocess, sys as _s
    subprocess.check_call([_s.executable,"-m","pip","install","--no-cache-dir","websockets"])
    import websockets

DATA   = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data_test"))
SYMBOL = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT").upper()
KEEP   = int(os.environ.get("KEEP","1500"))
URI    = "wss://ws.bitget.com/mix/v1/stream?compress=false"  # mix (perp)

CAND = DATA/"candles"
for tf in ("1m","3m","5m","15m","30m"):
    (CAND/tf).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def tf_ms(tf:str)->int: return int(tf[:-1])*60_000
def jload(p:Path):
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
    except: return []
def jdump(p:Path, arr): write_atomic_json(p, (arr or [])[-KEEP:])

def resample(rows, tf:str):
    step=tf_ms(tf); out=[]; b=None
    for ts,o,h,l,c,v in rows:
        bts = ts - (ts % step)
        if b is None or b[0]!=bts:
            if b: out.append(b)
            b=[bts,o,h,l,c,v]
        else:
            if h>b[2]: b[2]=h
            if l<b[3]: b[3]=l
            b[4]=c; b[5]+=v
    if b: out.append(b)
    return out

def parse_kline(msg:dict):
    d = msg.get("data"); 
    if not d: return None
    x = d[0]
    # formats possibles
    ts = int(x.get("ts") or x.get("time") or x.get("t"))
    o  = float(x.get("open") or x.get("o") or x.get("op", 0))
    h  = float(x.get("high") or x.get("h", 0))
    l  = float(x.get("low")  or x.get("l", 0))
    c  = float(x.get("close")or x.get("c", 0))
    v  = float(x.get("volume") or x.get("v", 0))
    return [ts,o,h,l,c,v]

async def try_subscribe(ws, sym:str):
    # variantes connues (évite 30016)
    insts = [f"{sym}_UMCBL", sym, f"{sym}_SPBL"]
    chans = ["candle1m", "candle1M"]
    payloads = []
    for inst in insts:
        for ch in chans:
            payloads.append({"op":"subscribe","args":[{"channel":ch,"instId":inst}]})               # sans instType
            payloads.append({"op":"subscribe","args":[{"instType":"UMCBL","channel":ch,"instId":inst}]})
    last_err=None
    for pay in payloads:
        await ws.send(json.dumps(pay))
        try:
            # on lit 1-2 messages pour voir si "subscribe" ok ou "error"
            for _ in range(2):
                raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=5)
                try: msg = json.loads(raw)
                except: continue
                if msg.get("event")=="subscribe":
                    return pay  # succès
                if msg.get("event")=="error":
                    last_err = msg
                    break
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            continue
    raise RuntimeError(f"subscribe failed last_err={last_err}")

def merge_last(old, row):
    if not row: return old
    if not old: return [row]
    if old[-1][0]==row[0]: return (old[:-1]+[row])[-KEEP:]
    if old[-1][0] < row[0]: return (old+[row])[-KEEP:]
    m={r[0]:r for r in (old+[row])}; return [m[k] for k in sorted(m)][-KEEP:]

async def run():
    sym = SYMBOL
    open1m = CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.open.json"
    closed1m = CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"
    while True:
        try:
            async with websockets.connect(URI, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=10, max_size=2**20) as ws:
                print("[ws] connect ok, probing subscribe …")
                ok_pay = await try_subscribe(ws, sym)
                print(f"[ws] subscribed with {ok_pay}")
                while True:
                    raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.recv(), timeout=60)
                    # ignore heartbeats non JSON
                    try: msg = json.loads(raw)
                    except: continue
                    row = parse_kline(msg)
                    if not row: continue
                    # write open 1m
                    jdump(open1m, [row])
                    # compose opens TF sup
                    arr1 = jload(closed1m) + [row]
                    for tf in ("3m","5m","15m","30m"):
                        arr = resample(arr1, tf)
                        if not arr: 
                            jdump(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.open.json", [])
                            continue
                        last = arr[-1]
                        step = tf_ms(tf)
                        is_closed = (int(time.time()*1000)//step) > (last[0]//step)
                        jdump(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.open.json", [] if is_closed else [last])
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ws] loop error: {e}")
            traceback.print_exc()
            await asyncio.sleep(2)
            continue

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json
from pathlib import Path

BASE = Path("/opt/scalp/data/candles/1m")

def clean_file(path: Path):
    try:
        with open(path) as f:
            data = json.load(f)
        if not isinstance(data, list):
            print(f"[RESET] {path} (not a list)")
            data = []
        else:
            fixed = []
            for row in data:
                if (
                    isinstance(row, list) and
                    len(row) >= 5 and
                    all(isinstance(x,(int,float)) for x in row[1:5])
                ):
                    fixed.append(row)
                else:
                    print(f"[DROP] {path}: bad row -> {row}")
            data = fixed
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[RESET] {path} error: {e}")
        data = []
    with open(path,"w") as f:
        json.dump(data,f)
    return len(data)

def main():
    for f in BASE.glob("*.json"):
        n = clean_file(f)
        print(f"[OK] {f} => {n} rows valid")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA  = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
C1M   = DATA/"candles"/"1m"

OPEN_STALENESS_MS     = int(os.environ.get("OPEN_STALENESS_MS","20000"))
MIN_AGE_IN_CANDLE_MS  = int(os.environ.get("MIN_AGE_IN_CANDLE_MS","0"))
USE_OPEN              = os.environ.get("USE_OPEN","1") == "1"

def jload(p, d):
    try:
        with open(p) as f: return json.load(f)
    except:
        return d

def now_ms():
    return int(time.time()*1000)

def tail(a, n):
    """
    Renvoie la fin de la séquence 'a' sous forme de liste.
    Tolère les JSON corrompus (dict ou None).
    """
    try:
        seq = list(a)
    except Exception:
        return []
    L = len(seq)
    if L <= n:
        return seq
    else:
        return seq[L-n:]

def live_rows_1m(sym:str):
    """
    Retourne (closed_tail:list, row_open_last:list|None, cur_min_ts:int).
    """
    rows_c = jload(C1M/f"{sym}.json", []) or []
    rows_o = jload(C1M/f"{sym}.open.json", []) or []
    t = now_ms()
    cur_min = t - (t % 60000)
    row_open_last = rows_o[-1] if rows_o else None
    return tail(rows_c, 600), row_open_last, cur_min

def live_close(sym:str):
    rows_c, row_open, cur_min = live_rows_1m(sym)
    px = float(rows_c[-1][4]) if rows_c else None
    if USE_OPEN and row_open:
        ts_o = int(row_open[0])
        fresh = (now_ms() - ts_o) <= OPEN_STALENESS_MS
        age_ok = (now_ms() - cur_min) >= MIN_AGE_IN_CANDLE_MS
        if fresh and age_ok:
            px = float(row_open[4])
    return px

def live_atr(sym:str, n:int=14):
    rows_c, row_open, _ = live_rows_1m(sym)
    rows = tail(rows_c, n+1)
    if USE_OPEN and row_open:
        ts_o = int(row_open[0])
        if (now_ms() - ts_o) <= OPEN_STALENESS_MS:
            rows = rows + [row_open]
    if len(rows) < n+1:
        return None
    trs=[]; prev=float(rows[0][4])
    for r in rows[1:]:
        try:
            h,l,c = float(r[2]), float(r[3]), float(r[4])
        except:
            continue
        trs.append(max(h-l, abs(h-prev), abs(l-prev)))
        prev=c
    return (sum(trs)/len(trs)) if trs else None

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os, tempfile
from pathlib import Path

def jload(path, default=None):
    p = Path(path)
    try:
        txt = p.read_text()
        return json.loads(txt) if txt else (default if default is not None else [])
    except Exception:
        return default if default is not None else []

def jdump(path, obj):
    p = Path(path)
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    data = json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",",":"))
    fd, tmp = tempfile.mkstemp(prefix=".tmp-", dir=str(p.parent))
    try:
        with os.fdopen(fd, "w") as f: f.write(data)
        os.replace(tmp, p)   # atomic
    finally:
        try: os.unlink(tmp)
        except: pass

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, glob

DATA=os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data_test")
SYM=os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")
TFS=["1m","3m","5m","15m","30m"]

def tail(path):
    try:
        with open(path,"r") as f:
            j=json.load(f)
            return j[-1]
    except: return None

def tail_open(path):
    try:
        with open(path,"r") as f:
            j=json.load(f)
            return j[-1] if j else None
    except: return None

def main():
    rep={"sym":SYM, "ts":int(time.time()*1000), "per_tf":[]}
    for tf in TFS:
        fc=f"{DATA}/candles/{tf}/{SYM}.json"
        fo=f"{DATA}/candles/{tf}/{SYM}.open.json"
        last_c=tail(fc)
        last_o=tail_open(fo)
        rep["per_tf"].append({"tf":tf,"last_closed":last_c,"last_open":last_o})
    os.makedirs(f"{DATA}/status",exist_ok=True)
    with open(f"{DATA}/status/{SYM}_status.json","w") as f: json.dump(rep,f, indent=2)
    print(json.dumps(rep))
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, argparse, tempfile
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
CAND = DATA/"candles"
TOPF = DATA/"top.json"

DEF_MAX = {"1m":1800, "3m":1200, "5m":600, "15m":600, "30m":600}

def atomic_write(path:Path, obj):
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile("w", delete=False, dir=path.parent) as f:
        json.dump(obj, f)
        tmp = Path(f.name)
    tmp.replace(path)

def load_top():
    try:
        return set(json.loads(TOPF.read_text()).get("symbols",[]))
    except Exception:
        return set()

def valid_row(r):
    return isinstance(r,list) and len(r)>=6 and all(isinstance(x,(int,float)) for x in r[:6])

def trim_file(f:Path, maxbars:int)->tuple[int,int,str]:
    try:
        j = json.loads(f.read_text())
        data = j.get("data", [])
        if not isinstance(data, list) or not all(valid_row(r) for r in data):
            return (0,0,"bad")
        # tri par timestamp, dédoublonnage
        data.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])
        dedup = []
        last_ts = None
        for r in data:
            if r[0] != last_ts:
                dedup.append(r)
                last_ts = r[0]
        kept = dedup[-maxbars:] if len(dedup)>maxbars else dedup
        if kept != data:
            atomic_write(f, {"data": kept})
        return (len(dedup), len(kept), "ok")
    except Exception:
        return (0,0,"err")

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--max", default=",".join(f"{k}={v}" for k,v in DEF_MAX.items()),
                    help="ex: 1m=1800,3m=1200,5m=600,15m=600,30m=600")
    ap.add_argument("--prune-not-in-top", action="store_true")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    maxmap = DEF_MAX.copy()
    for kv in args.max.split(","):
        if "=" in kv:
            k,v = kv.split("="); maxmap[k.strip()] = int(v)

    top = load_top() if args.prune_not_in_top else None

    total_before=total_after=bad=removed=0
    for tf in maxmap.keys():
        d = CAND/tf
        if not d.exists(): continue
        for f in d.glob("*.json"):
            if top is not None:
                sym = f.stem
                if sym not in top:
                    f.unlink(missing_ok=True)
                    removed += 1
                    continue
            before, after, status = trim_file(f, maxmap[tf])
            if status in ("bad","err"):
                f.unlink(missing_ok=True); bad += 1
            total_before += before
            total_after  += after

    print(f"[trim] bars before={total_before} after={total_after} files_bad_deleted={bad} files_pruned_not_in_top={removed}")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import re

USDT = "USDT"

# patterns rapides pour gagner du temps
_rx_bad_chars = re.compile(r'[^A-Z0-9]')
_rx_usdt_tail  = re.compile(r'(USDT)+$')           # un ou plusieurs USDT à la fin
_rx_any_usdt   = re.compile(r'USDT')               # présence de USDT quelque part

def sanitize(sym: str) -> str:
    """
    Normalise un symbole en MAJ, supprime les caractères bizarres,
    élimine les suffixes USDT répétés (USDTUSDT, USDT…USDT), et
    s'assure qu'il finit par *exactement* un USDT.
    """
    if not sym:
        return sym

    s = sym.upper().strip()

    # remplace séparateurs suspects par rien (ex: 'FIL-USDT', 'FLOKI/USDT', 'FL O K IUSDT')
    s = _rx_bad_chars.sub('', s)

    # si on trouve USDT quelque part: on coupe tout ce qui suit le premier USDT
    m = _rx_any_usdt.search(s)
    if m:
        base = s[:m.start()]         # ce qu'il y a avant le 1er USDT
        # nettoie le base (au cas où il reste un USDT fragmenté)
        base = _rx_bad_chars.sub('', base)
        s = base + USDT
    else:
        # pas de USDT du tout -> on l'ajoute (nos quotes sont fixées à USDT)
        s = s + USDT

    # compresse tout suffixe USDT répété (sécurité)
    s = _rx_usdt_tail.sub(USDT, s)

    return s

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os, sys
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); TOP=DATA/"top.json"; C=DATA/"candles"
TFS=("5m","15m","30m")

def has(flat, tf):
    f=C/flat/tf/"last.json"
    if not f.exists(): return False
    try:
        j=json.loads(f.read_text()); return bool(j.get("data"))
    except: return False

def main():
    top=json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    syms=[s for s in top.get("symbols") or []][:30]
    missing={}
    for s in syms:
        miss=[tf for tf in TFS if not has(s, tf)]
        if miss: missing[s]=miss
    ok=len(missing)==0
    print(f"[ohlcv-check] ok={ok} missing={len(missing)}")
    for k,v in list(missing.items())[:20]:
        print(f" - {k}: {','.join(v)}")
    sys.exit(0 if ok else 1)
if __name__=="__main__": main()

MTime: 2025-09-27 08:46:48.899169292 +0000

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Bitget ccxt backfill (1m,5m,15m,30m) + resample 3m
# Suivi: 1 req/min (1m) -> resample 3/5/15/30, ÉCRITURE ATOMIQUE
import os, json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path
try:
    import ccxt
except Exception:
    import subprocess, sys as _s
    subprocess.check_call([_s.executable,"-m","pip","install","--no-cache-dir","ccxt"])
    import ccxt

# lib atomique
from importlib.util import spec_from_file_location, module_from_spec
_spec = spec_from_file_location("atomic_json","/opt/scalp/tools/lib/atomic_json.py")
_atomic = module_from_spec(_spec); _spec.loader.exec_module(_atomic)
write_atomic_json = _atomic.write_atomic_json

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data_test"))
CAND = DATA/"candles"
KEEP = int(os.environ.get("KEEP","1500"))
TFS  = ("1m","3m","5m","15m","30m")

ex = ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit": True, "timeout": 20000})
ex.load_markets()

def tf_ms(tf:str)->int: return int(tf[:-1])*60_000
def now_ms(): return int(time.time()*1000)
def mkt(sym_flat:str)->str:
    base=sym_flat[:-4]; quote=sym_flat[-4:]; return f"{base}/{quote}:{quote}"

def jload(p:Path):
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
    except: return []

def jdump_atomic(p:Path, arr):
    write_atomic_json(p, arr[-KEEP:])

def fetch(sym:str, tf:str, limit:int=200):
    try: return ex.fetch_ohlcv(mkt(sym), timeframe=tf, limit=limit) or []
    except Exception as e: print(f"[fetch] {sym} {tf} {e}", file=sys.stderr); return []

def resample(arr1, tf:str):
    step=tf_ms(tf); out=[]; bucket=None
    for ts,o,h,l,c,v in arr1:
        bts = ts - (ts % step)
        if bucket is None or bucket[0]!=bts:
            if bucket: out.append(bucket)
            bucket=[bts,o,h,l,c,v]
        else:
            bucket[2]=max(bucket[2],h); bucket[3]=min(bucket[3],l)
            bucket[4]=c; bucket[5]+=v
    if bucket: out.append(bucket)
    return out

def backfill(sym:str):
    # 1m/5m/15m/30m depuis ccxt
    for tf in ("1m","5m","15m","30m"):
        arr = fetch(sym, tf, KEEP)
        jdump_atomic(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json", arr)
        print(f"[backfill] {sym} {tf} n={len(arr)}")
    # 3m depuis 1m
    arr1 = jload(CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json")
    arr3 = resample(arr1, "3m")
    jdump_atomic(CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.json", arr3)
    print(f"[backfill] {sym} 3m n={len(arr3)}")

def follow(sym:str):
    # update 1m
    rows = fetch(sym, "1m", 3)
    if not rows: return
    p1 = CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"
    hist = jload(p1)
    merged = {r[0]:r for r in (hist+rows)}
    arr1m = [merged[k] for k in sorted(merged)][-KEEP:]
    jdump_atomic(p1, arr1m)
    print(f"[upd] {sym} 1m ts={arr1m[-1][0]} c={arr1m[-1][4]}")

    # resample à la bonne borne
    now = now_ms()
    for tf in ("3m","5m","15m","30m"):
        if now % tf_ms(tf) < 60_000:  # dans la 1re minute du nouveau slot
            arr = resample(arr1m, tf)
            jdump_atomic(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json", arr)
            print(f"[upd] {sym} {tf} ts={arr[-1][0]} c={arr[-1][4]}")

def main():
    sym = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")
    # répertoires
    for tf in TFS: (CAND/tf).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    backfill(sym)
    while True:
        t0=time.time()
        follow(sym)
        time.sleep(max(1, 60-(time.time()-t0)))

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

  | sed 's/,/, /g; s/^/6->10: /; s/$//' || true

  to_entries|map(select(.value.ctx!="none")|.key)

  | map( ( ( (input/0)? ) ) )

      && test -s "/opt/scalp/data/candles/3m/$s.json" \
      && test -s "/opt/scalp/data/candles/5m/$s.json" && c=$((c+1))
  done < <(jq -r "to_entries|map(select(.value.ctx!=\"none\")|.key)|.[]" '"$AOUT"')

    def sc: .value.S // 0;
    def row: {sym:.key, S:(.value.S//0), pb:(.value.pb//0), ph:(.value.ph//0), ps:(.value.ps//0), ctx:(.value.ctx//"none")};
    . as $A
    | [ "BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT" ]
    | map(select(IN($A|keys[]; .))) as $fixed
    | ($A|to_entries|sort_by(-(.value.S//0))|map(.key)) as $sorted
    | $fixed + ($sorted - $fixed)[0:2] + (($sorted|reverse) - $fixed)[0:2]
    | unique
    | .[]
  ' "$AOUT" 2>/dev/null

for s in $pick; do

    .[$k] // {}
    | [$k, (.S//0), (.pb//0), (.ph//0), (.ps//0), (.ctx//"none")]
    | @tsv
  ' "$AOUT" 2>/dev/null | awk -F'\t' '{

  }'

     to_entries|map(select(.value.ctx==$s)|.key)|map(sub("USDT$";"")|sub("USD$";""))|join(", ")
  ' "$AOUT" 2>/dev/null)
  [ -z "$line" ] && line="aucun"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Corrige proprement les entrées size=0 ou manquantes dans signals.json
import json
from pathlib import Path
import os

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data"))
P_SIG = DATA / "signals.json"

def main():
    try:
        arr = json.loads(P_SIG.read_text())
        if not isinstance(arr, list):
            return
    except Exception:
        return
    changed = False
    for s in arr:
        if not isinstance(s, dict):
            continue
        if str(s.get("action","")).startswith("enter"):
            qty = float(s.get("size") or 0)
            if qty <= 0:
                s["size"] = 1.0
                changed = True
            # normalise clés
            if "symbol" not in s and "sym" in s:
                s["symbol"] = s["sym"]
                changed = True
    if changed:
        P_SIG.write_text(json.dumps(arr, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, asyncio, websockets, time
from pathlib import Path
from lib.atomic_json import jload, jdump

DATA    = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
SYMBOL  = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")
WS_URL  = "wss://ws.bitget.com/v2/ws/public"

F_1M_CLOSED = DATA/"candles"/"1m"/f"{SYMBOL}.json"
F_1M_OPEN   = DATA/"candles"/"1m"/f"{SYMBOL}.open.json"

KEEP = int(os.environ.get("KEEP","1500"))
def trim(a): return (a or [])[-KEEP:]

def krow_to_ohlcv(row):
    # v2: [ts, o, h, l, c, vol, turnover]
    ts, o, h, l, c, v, *_ = row
    return [int(ts), float(o), float(h), float(l), float(c), float(v)]

async def run():
    sub = {
        "op":"subscribe",
        "args":[{"instType":"USDT-FUTURES","channel":"candle1m","instId":SYMBOL}]
    }
    async with websockets.connect(WS_URL, ping_interval=20, ping_timeout=20) as ws:
        await ws.send(json.dumps(sub))
        closed = jload(F_1M_CLOSED, [])
        open_c = jload(F_1M_OPEN, [])
        last_closed_ts = closed[-1][0] if closed else -1

        while True:
            msg = json.loads(await ws.recv())
            if msg.get("action")!="update":
                continue
            arg = msg.get("arg",{})
            if arg.get("channel")!="candle1m" or arg.get("instId")!=SYMBOL:
                continue
            for row in msg.get("data",[]):
                ts = int(row[0])
                ohlcv = krow_to_ohlcv(row)
                now_ms = int(time.time()*1000)
                cur_min = now_ms - (now_ms % 60000)
                if ts < cur_min:                      # CLOSED
                    if ts > last_closed_ts:
                        closed.append(ohlcv)
                        jdump(F_1M_CLOSED, trim(closed))
                        last_closed_ts = ts
                else:                                 # OPEN
                    open_c = [ohlcv]
                    jdump(F_1M_OPEN, open_c)

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(run())

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

# --- params ---
DATA="${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data}"
PRIMARY="${PRIMARY:-BTCUSDT}"
TFS="${TFS:-1m 3m 5m 15m 30m}"
SANITY_EVERY_MIN="${SANITY_EVERY_MIN:-120}"

# --- tiny logger (portable, pas de 'date %T') ---
log(){ printf '[%(%F %T)T] %s\n' -1 "$*"; }

# --- ensure exec bits ---
chmod +x /opt/scalp/tools/backfill/*.sh 2>/dev/null || true
chmod +x /opt/scalp/tools/test/*.sh     2>/dev/null || true

export DATA

log "orchestrator start DATA=${DATA} PRIMARY=${PRIMARY}"

# 1) backfill incrémental initial sur toutes les TF
SYMBOL="${PRIMARY}" /opt/scalp/tools/backfill/backfill_all_incremental.sh

# 2) démarrer WS + resampler (1m)
export SYMBOL="${PRIMARY}"
if ! pgrep -f ws_open_1m.py >/dev/null 2>&1 && ! pgrep -f ws_writer.py >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  log "WS live for ${PRIMARY}"
  /opt/scalp/tools/test/ws_start.sh
fi

# 3) boucle: sanity + resync périodique
i=0
while :; do
  ((i++))
  log "sanity round"
  # check cohérence, sans forcer backfill; on tolère les warnings
  BACKFILL=0 SYMBOL="${PRIMARY}" python3 -u /opt/scalp/tools/sanity/sanity_check_ccxt.py || true

  # toutes les SANITY_EVERY_MIN minutes: resync incrémental CCXT
  if (( i % SANITY_EVERY_MIN == 0 )); then
    log "periodic CCXT incremental sync"
    SYMBOL="${PRIMARY}" /opt/scalp/tools/backfill/backfill_all_incremental.sh
  fi

  sleep 60
done

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, math, glob
from pathlib import Path
from lib.ohlcv_live import live_close

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
SIG  = DATA/"signals.json"
POS  = DATA/"paper"/"positions.json"
BAL  = DATA/"paper"/"balance.json"
A_DIR= DATA/"analysis_a"
REFRESH = float(os.environ.get("WATCH_REFRESH","5"))
MAX_SIG_AGE_S = int(os.environ.get("MAX_SIG_AGE_S","600"))

def jload(p, d):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def ready_reasons(sig, positions, cash):
    r=[]; ok=True
    sym=sig.get("symbol"); side=(sig.get("side") or "").lower()
    entry=sig.get("entry"); sl=sig.get("sl"); tp=sig.get("tp")
    size=float(sig.get("size") or 0); margin=float(sig.get("margin") or 0)
    if side not in ("buy","sell"): ok=False; r.append("side?")
    if not(entry and entry>0): ok=False; r.append("entry?")
    if not(sl and sl>0): ok=False; r.append("sl?")
    if not(tp and tp>0): ok=False; r.append("tp?")
    if size<=0: ok=False; r.append("size=0")
    if margin>cash+1e-9: ok=False; r.append(f"cash<{margin:.2f}")
    if any(p.get("symbol")==sym for p in positions): ok=False; r.append("déjà ouvert")
    ts=sig.get("ts")
    if isinstance(ts,int) and (int(time.time()*1000)-ts>MAX_SIG_AGE_S*1000):
        ok=False; r.append(f"vieux>{MAX_SIG_AGE_S}s")
    if live_close(sym) is None: ok=False; r.append("ohlcv1m?")
    return ok,r

def print_table(rows, title):
    print(title)
    print("sym        side   qty        entry       sl          tp          margin$  status")
    print("-"*92)
    for r in rows:
        print("{sym:<10} {side:<5}  {qty:>8}  {entry:>10}  {sl:>10}  {tp:>10}  {marg:>8}  {status}".format(**r))
    print()

def load_analysis_a():
    out=[]
    for f in sorted(glob.glob(str(A_DIR/'*.json'))):
        try: d=jload(f,{}) or {}
        except: d={}
        sym=d.get("symbol") or Path(f).stem
        ctx=(d.get("ctx") or d.get("context") or "none").lower()
        out.append({"symbol":sym,"ctx":ctx})
    return out

def main():
    while True:
        os.system("clear")
        cash = float(jload(BAL,{"cash":0}).get("cash",0))
        positions = jload(POS, [])
        signals = jload(SIG, [])

        ready, blocked = [], []
        for s in signals:
            ok, reasons = ready_reasons(s, positions, cash)
            row = {
                "sym": s.get("symbol","?"),
                "side": (s.get("side") or "-")[:5],
                "qty": f"{float(s.get('size') or 0):.3f}",
                "entry": f"{float(s.get('entry') or 0):.6f}" if s.get("entry") else "-",
                "sl": f"{float(s.get('sl') or 0):.6f}" if s.get("sl") else "-",
                "tp": f"{float(s.get('tp') or 0):.6f}" if s.get("tp") else "-",
                "marg": f"{float(s.get('margin') or 0):.2f}",
                "status": "PRÊT" if ok else "NON: " + ",".join(reasons[:4])
            }
            (ready if ok else blocked).append(row)

        print("== WATCH DECISIONS ==")
        print(f"cash: {cash:.2f}   positions ouvertes: {len(positions)}   signaux: {len(signals)}\n")
        print_table(ready[:12], "OUVERTURE POSSIBLE" if ready else "OUVERTURE POSSIBLE (aucune)")
        if blocked: print_table(blocked[:20], "BLOQUÉS (raisons)")
        else: print("BLOQUÉS\n(aucun)\n")

        print("(maj auto %.0fs)  Ctrl-C pour quitter" % REFRESH)
        try: time.sleep(REFRESH)
        except KeyboardInterrupt: break

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os, re
from pathlib import Path
from sym_normalize import normalize

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
TFs  = ["1m","3m","5m","15m","30m"]

def rename_inside(dirp: Path):
    if not dirp.exists(): return
    for p in dirp.iterdir():
        if not p.is_file(): continue
        base = p.stem
        norm = normalize(base)
        if norm != base:
            p2 = p.with_name(norm + p.suffix)
            if not p2.exists():
                p.rename(p2)

def fix_top_json():
    f = DATA/"top.json"
    if not f.exists(): return
    t = json.loads(f.read_text())
    syms = t.get("symbols") or []
    fixed = []
    for s in syms:
        n = normalize(s)
        if n not in fixed:
            fixed.append(n)
    t["symbols"] = fixed
    f.write_text(json.dumps(t, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))

def main():
    # candles by TF
    for tf in TFs:
        rename_inside(CAND/tf)
    # historique compact éventuel
    for tf in TFs:
        d = CAND/f"{tf}_raw"
        if d.exists(): rename_inside(d)
    fix_top_json()
    print("OK: filenames & top.json normalisés.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import pathlib, re, shutil

ROOT = pathlib.Path("/opt/scalp/tools")
targets = [p for p in ROOT.rglob("*.py") if "analysis_a" in p.name]

pattern_old = re.compile(r'candles/[^/]+/[0-9]+m/last\.json')
pattern_tpl = re.compile(r'candles/\{sym\}/\{tf\}/last\.json')

def patch_file(p):
    txt = p.read_text()
    orig = txt
    txt = pattern_old.sub("candles/{tf}/{sym}.json", txt)
    txt = pattern_tpl.sub("candles/{tf}/{sym}.json", txt)
    if txt != orig:
        shutil.copy2(p, p.with_suffix(p.suffix+".bak"))
        p.write_text(txt)
        print("[patched]", p)

for f in targets:
    patch_file(f)

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

TOOLS=/opt/scalp/tools
ARCH="$TOOLS._archive_$(date -u +%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ)"
mkdir -p "$ARCH"

# Whitelist minimale à garder
keep=(
  "expand_top_ranked_light.py"  # Top futures, shortlist, depth optionnel
  "expand_top_fast_plus.py"     # Variante tickers-only + depth (fallback)
  "force_top5.sh"               # Noyau fixe d'urgence
  "show_top.py"                 # Affichage Top
  "snap_top.sh"                 # Snapshot top.*
  "diff_top.py"                 # Diff entre snapshots
)

# Crée fichiers vides si manquants pour éviter faux positifs
for f in "${keep[@]}"; do
  [ -e "$TOOLS/$f" ] || : > "$TOOLS/$f"
done

echo "[clean] Archiver tout sauf: ${keep[*]}"
shopt -s nullglob
moved=0
for f in "$TOOLS"/*; do
  base="$(basename "$f")"
  skip=0
  for k in "${keep[@]}"; do
    [[ "$base" == "$k" ]] && { skip=1; break; }
  done
  # Ne pas toucher au script courant
  [[ "$base" == "clean_tools.sh" ]] && skip=1
  if [[ $skip -eq 0 ]]; then
    mv -f "$f" "$ARCH/"
    ((moved++)) || true
  fi
done
shopt -u nullglob

echo "[clean] $moved éléments déplacés vers: $ARCH"
echo "[clean] Contenu conservé:"
printf ' - %s\n' "${keep[@]}" "clean_tools.sh"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
: "${DATA:=/opt/scalp/data}"
: "${LOOPS:=0}"        # 0 = infini
: "${SLEEP:=15}"
: "${DO_RESET:=0}"
: "${PAPER_BUDGET:=200.0}"
export DATA PAPER_BUDGET

LOGDIR="$DATA/logs"; mkdir -p "$LOGDIR" "$DATA/debug/bridge" "$DATA/paper" /opt/scalp/logs
ts(){ date -u +%FT%TZ; }

reset_state(){ [ "$DO_RESET" = "1" ] && /opt/scalp/tools/reset_signals_paper.sh || true; }
sanity(){ /opt/scalp/tools/paper_pipeline_sanity.sh || true; }

tick_once(){
  echo "=== TICK $(ts) ==="
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/fetch_A_then_B.py || true
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/top_fix_usdt.py || true     # <<< fixe BTCUSDTUSDT -> BTCUSDT
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_top_bridge.py || true
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/paper_open_from_signals.py || true
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/paper_monitor.py || true
  /opt/scalp/tools/paper_pipeline_dump.sh | tee -a "$LOGDIR/paper_dump.log" || true
  echo "--- signals (last 10) ---"; tail -n 10 "$DATA/signals.json" 2>/dev/null || true
  echo "--- bridge log (last 20) ---"; tail -n 20 /opt/scalp/logs/signals_bridge.log 2>/dev/null || true
}

echo "[pipe] start DATA=$DATA LOOPS=$LOOPS SLEEP=${SLEEP}s DO_RESET=$DO_RESET"
reset_state; sanity

if [ "$LOOPS" = "0" ]; then
  i=1
  while true; do
    echo; echo "--- boucle $i/∞ ---"
    tick_once
    sleep "$SLEEP"
    i=$((i+1))
  done
else
  for ((i=1;i<=LOOPS;i++)); do
    echo; echo "--- boucle $i/$LOOPS ---"
    tick_once
    (( i < LOOPS )) && sleep "$SLEEP" || true
  done
fi
echo "[pipe] done"

from pathlib import Path
import json, time

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"

def last_close_1m(sym:str)->float:
    """close de la dernière bougie 1m CLÔTURÉE pour sym."""
    p = CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"
    if not p.exists(): return 0.0
    try:
        rows = json.loads(p.read_text())
        if not rows: return 0.0
        now_ms = int(time.time()*1000)
        # période 1m
        per = 60_000
        last_ts = int(rows[-1][0])
        # si la dernière n'est pas close, on prend l'avant-dernière
        r = rows[-2] if last_ts + per > now_ms and len(rows) >= 2 else rows[-1]
        return float(r[4])  # close
    except Exception:
        return 0.0

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Wrapper minimal pour "un symbole / plusieurs TF".
# S'il trouve ohlcv_refresh.py, il le délègue. Sinon, no-op propre.
import argparse, os, sys, json, subprocess, shutil
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data"))
TOOLS = Path("/opt/scalp/tools")
REFRESH_ALL = TOOLS / "ohlcv_refresh.py"

def ensure_placeholder(symbol: str, tfs: list[str]):
    (DATA / "candles").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    for tf in tfs:
        d = DATA / "candles" / tf
        d.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        f = d / f"{symbol}.json"
        if not f.exists() or not f.read_text().strip():
            f.write_text("[]")

def main():
    p = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    p.add_argument("--symbol", required=True)
    p.add_argument("--tfs", default="1m")
    args = p.parse_args()
    symbol = args.symbol
    tfs = [t.strip() for t in args.tfs.split(",") if t.strip()]
    if REFRESH_ALL.exists():
        cmd = ["python3", str(REFRESH_ALL), "--symbols", symbol, "--tfs", ",".join(tfs)]
        try:
            subprocess.run(cmd, check=False)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ohlcv_refresh_one] delegate error: {e}")
            ensure_placeholder(symbol, tfs)
    else:
        print("[ohlcv_refresh_one] fallback no-op. Creating placeholders.")
        ensure_placeholder(symbol, tfs)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import json, time, shutil
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP   = DATA/"top.json"
AOUT1 = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
AOUT2 = DATA/"analysis_a_out.json"   # fallback
SIG   = DATA/"signals.json"
POS   = DATA/"positions.json"
HIST  = DATA/"history.json"
PBAL  = DATA/"paper_balance.json"    # {"balance": 200.0}

# ----- io -----
def jload(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def human_k(x):
    try:
        x=float(x)
        if x>=1e9: return f"{x/1e9:.1f}B"
        if x>=1e6: return f"{x/1e6:.1f}M"
        if x>=1e3: return f"{x/1e3:.1f}k"
        return f"{x:.0f}"
    except: return "—"

def bold(s): return f"\x1b[1m{s}\x1b[0m"

# ----- header -----
def show_top_and_balance():
    t=jload(TOP,{}) or {}
    ts=t.get("generated_at","—")
    src=t.get("source","—")
    syms=t.get("symbols") or []
    tail = [s.replace("USDT","") for s in syms[5:10]]
    bal = (jload(PBAL, {"balance":200.0}) or {}).get("balance", 200.0)
    print(bold(f"== SCALP DASHBOARD @ {time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ', time.gmtime())} =="))
    print(f"Top30  ts={ts}  src={src}  N={len(syms)}   Paper: ${bal:.2f}")
    if tail: print("6→10:", ", ".join(tail))

# ----- Analyses A: 1 ligne -----
def pick_best_worst(a, k=2):
    items=[(sym,v) for sym,v in (a or {}).items() if isinstance(v,dict)]
    items.sort(key=lambda x: float(x[1].get("S",0.0)), reverse=True)
    return items[:k], items[-k:]

def show_analyses_a():
    a = jload(AOUT1, None)
    if a is None: a = jload(AOUT2, {})
    if not a:
        print("Analyses A: —"); return
    want=[]
    for s in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"):
        if s in a: want.append((s,a[s]))
    best,worst = pick_best_worst(a,2)
    seen=set(x[0] for x in want)
    for t in best+worst:
        if t[0] not in seen:
            want.append(t); seen.add(t[0])
        if len(want)>=6: break
    print(bold("Analyses A  (S  pb pH ps  ctx)"))
    for sym,rec in want:
        name=sym.replace("USDT","")
        S   = float(rec.get("S",0.0))
        pbi = int(rec.get("pb_i",0)); pHi=int(rec.get("pH_i",0)); psi=int(rec.get("ps_i",0))
        ctx = rec.get("context","none")
        print(f"{name:5s}  S={S:0.4f}  pb={pbi:2d} pH={pHi:2d} ps={psi:2d}  {ctx:4s}")

# ----- Signaux regroupés -----
def derive_lev(n, m):
    try:
        n=float(n); m=float(m); return int(round(n/m)) if m>0 else 0
    except: return 0

def show_signals():
    data = jload(SIG, []) or []
    print(bold("\nSignaux récents"))
    if not data:
        print("  aucun"); return
    print("ts            sym side lev qty        notion  entry      tp         sl         why")
    for r in data[-10:][::-1]:
        ts   = (r.get("ts","") or "")[:16]
        sym  = (r.get("symbol","") or "").replace("USDT","")[:8]
        side = r.get("side","")
        lev  = derive_lev(r.get("notional",0), r.get("margin",0))
        qty  = float(r.get("qty",0.0))
        n    = human_k(r.get("notional",0.0))
        en   = r.get("entry","")
        tp   = r.get("tp","")
        sl   = r.get("sl","")
        why  = (r.get("why","") or "")[:28]
        print(f"{ts:16s} {sym:8s} {side:4s} {lev:3d} {qty:10.6f} {n:7s} {str(en):10s} {str(tp):10s} {str(sl):10s} {why}")

# ----- Positions / Historique -----
def show_positions():
    p = jload(POS, {}) or {}
    items = [p] if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("symbol") else (p if isinstance(p,list) else [])
    print(bold("\nPositions"))
    if not items:
        print("  aucune"); return
    print("sym   side  qty        entry      pnl     sl         tp")
    for r in items[:10]:
        sym=(r.get("symbol","") or "").replace("USDT","")
        print(f"{sym:6s} {r.get('side',''):4s} {r.get('qty',0.0):10.6f} {str(r.get('entry','')):10s} {str(r.get('pnl','')):7s} {str(r.get('sl','')):10s} {str(r.get('tp','')):10s}")

def show_history():
    h = jload(HIST, [])
    print(bold("\nHistorique récents"))
    if not h:
        print("  aucun"); return
    for r in h[-10:][::-1]:
        ts = (r.get("ts","") or "")[:16]
        sym= (r.get("symbol","") or "").replace("USDT","")
        act= r.get("action","")
        p  = r.get("price","")
        q  = r.get("qty","")
        print(f"{ts:16s} {sym:8s} {act:10s} p={p} q={q}")

def main():
    _ = shutil.get_terminal_size((100,40))  # reserve sizing if needed
    show_top_and_balance()
    show_analyses_a()
    show_signals()
    show_positions()
    show_history()

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

import json, os, sys, time
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA = os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = Path(DATA) / "candles"
TOPF = Path(DATA) / "top.json"

# mapping TF -> durée en ms
TF_MS = {
    "1m": 60_000,
    "3m": 180_000,
    "5m": 300_000,
    "15m": 900_000,
    "30m": 1_800_000,
}

def main():
    if not TOPF.exists():
        print(f"[ERR] top.json introuvable: {TOPF}")
        sys.exit(1)

    top = json.loads(TOPF.read_text())
    symbols = top.get("symbols") or []
    if not symbols:
        print("[ERR] Aucun symbole dans top.json")
        sys.exit(1)

    ex_name = top.get("exchange", "binance").lower()
    if ex_name not in ccxt.exchanges:
        print(f"[WARN] Exchange {ex_name} non supporté, fallback binance")
        ex_name = "binance"

    ex = getattr(ccxt, ex_name)()
    ex.load_markets()

    for sym in symbols:
        for tf, ms in TF_MS.items():
            try:
                ohlcv = ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, tf, limit=600)
                outdir = CAND / tf
                outdir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
                outf = outdir / f"{sym}.json"
                json.dump({"data": ohlcv}, open(outf, "w"))
                print(f"[OK] {sym} {tf} -> {outf}")
                time.sleep(ex.rateLimit/1000)
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[ERR] {sym} {tf}: {e}", file=sys.stderr)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Entrée: dict tf -> OHLCV [[ts,o,h,l,c,v],...]
# Sortie: features par tf et agrégés
from analysis_a_lib import ema, rsi, stdev, atr, logret, lastn, safe

def tf_features(rows):
    ts=[r[0] for r in rows]; o=[float(r[1]) for r in rows]
    h=[float(r[2]) for r in rows]; l=[float(r[3]) for r in rows]
    c=[float(r[4]) for r in rows]; v=[float(r[5]) for r in rows]
    # returns, vola
    lr=logret(c)
    vola=stdev([x or 0.0 for x in lr], period=48)  # ~2j en 5m
    # trend: ema fast/slow
    efast=ema(c, 2/(12+1))
    eslow=ema(c, 2/(48+1))
    trend=[(f/s-1.0) if s else 0.0 for f,s in zip(efast, eslow)]
    # rsi
    r = rsi(c, period=14)
    # atr %
    a = atr(h,l,c,period=14)
    atrp=[(x/c[i]) if (x and c[i]) else None for i,x in enumerate(a)]
    return dict(ts=ts, o=o,h=h,l=l,c=c,v=v, lr=lr, vola=vola, trend=trend, rsi=r, atrp=atrp)

def aggregate(fs5, fs15, fs30):
    # momentum récent = somme des 3 derniers ret sur chaque tf
    def mom_last(fs):
        lr=fs["lr"]; vals=[x for x in lr if x is not None][-3:]
        return sum(vals) if vals else 0.0
    mom = mom_last(fs5)+mom_last(fs15)+mom_last(fs30)
    # volatilité récente = moyenne des 24 dernières vola sur chaque tf
    def vola_last(fs):
        vv=[x for x in fs["vola"] if x is not None][-24:]
        return sum(vv)/len(vv) if vv else 0.0
    vola = sum([vola_last(fs5), vola_last(fs15), vola_last(fs30)])/3.0
    # pression acheteuse/vendeuse par RSI centrée
    def pressure(fs):
        r=[x for x in fs["rsi"] if x is not None][-12:]
        if not r: return 0.0
        import statistics as st
        return (st.mean(r)-50.0)/50.0  # [-1..+1]
    p5,p15,p30 = pressure(fs5), pressure(fs15), pressure(fs30)
    press = 0.5*p5 + 0.3*p15 + 0.2*p30
    # surchauffe via ATR%
    def heat(fs):
        a=[x for x in fs["atrp"] if x is not None][-12:]
        if not a: return 0.0
        import statistics as st
        return st.mean(a)
    heatp = sum([heat(fs5),heat(fs15),heat(fs30)])/3.0
    # trend multi-échelles
    def trend_last(fs):
        t=[x for x in fs["trend"] if x is not None][-6:]
        if not t: return 0.0
        import statistics as st
        return st.mean(t)
    tr = 0.5*trend_last(fs5)+0.3*trend_last(fs15)+0.2*trend_last(fs30)
    return dict(mom=mom, vola=vola, press=press, heat=heatp, trend=tr)

def compute_features(data):
    f5 = tf_features(data["5m"])
    f15 = tf_features(data["15m"])
    f30 = tf_features(data["30m"])
    agg = aggregate(f5,f15,f30)
    return {"5m":f5, "15m":f15, "30m":f30, "agg":agg}

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DATA=${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data}
TOP=${DATA}/top.json
INTERVAL=${INTERVAL:-5}   # secondes entre refresh

while true; do
  clear
  echo "[freshness-matrix] $(date -u +%FT%TZ)"
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/check_freshness_matrix.py | \
    awk '
      BEGIN { FS=" " }
      # Color rules enrichies
      {
        if ($1 == "sym" || $1 ~ /^---/) { print; next }
        sym=$1; stale=0; miss=0;
        for (i=2; i<=NF; i++) {
          if ($i ~ /STALE/) stale++;
          if ($i ~ /MISS/) miss++;
        }
        if (miss>0 || stale>5) {
          # trop de manques = rouge
          print "\033[38;5;196m"$0"\033[0m"
        }
        else if (stale>2) {
          # plusieurs stale = orange renforcé
          print "\033[38;5;214m"$0"\033[0m"
        }
        else {
          print $0
        }
      }
    '
  sleep "$INTERVAL"
done

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
from sym_norm import to_flat
from ctx_logic import compute_ctx, CtxState

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA / "candles"
TOP  = DATA / "top.json"
OUT  = DATA / "analyse_A_out.json"

def jload(p, d=None):
    p = Path(p)
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except: return d

def load_tf(sym, tf): return jload(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json", [])

def last_complete(arr, tf_s):
    if not arr: return []
    now = int(time.time())
    ts_last = int(arr[-1][0])//1000
    return arr[:-1] if (now - ts_last) < tf_s else arr

def mk_inputs(arr):
    if len(arr) < 60:
        return dict(ema12=0,ema26=0,atr14=1,macd_hist=0,macd_sigma100=1,
                    rsi14=50,adx14=20,obv_delta20=0,obv_medabs200=1,atr_pct=0.2)
    closes=[x[4] for x in arr]
    def ema(vals,n):
        k=2/(n+1); e=None
        for v in vals: e=v if e is None else e+k*(v-e)
        return e
    return dict(ema12=ema(closes,12),ema26=ema(closes,26),
                atr14=1,macd_hist=0,macd_sigma100=1,
                rsi14=50,adx14=20,obv_delta20=0,obv_medabs200=1,atr_pct=0.2)

def main():
    top = jload(TOP,{}) or {}
    syms = [to_flat(s) for s in top.get("symbols",[])[:30]]
    out={}
    for s in syms:
        m5=last_complete(load_tf(s,"5m"),5*60)
        m15=last_complete(load_tf(s,"15m"),15*60)
        m30=last_complete(load_tf(s,"30m"),30*60)
        if not (m5 and m15 and m30):
            out[s]=dict(ctx="none",pb=1/3,ph=1/3,ps=1/3,S=0.0,Sw=0.0); continue
        res=compute_ctx({"5m":mk_inputs(m5),"15m":mk_inputs(m15),"30m":mk_inputs(m30)},CtxState())
        out[s]=dict(ctx=res["ctx_state"].ctx,pb=float(res["pb"]),ph=float(res["ph"]),ps=float(res["ps"]),
                    S=float(res["agg"].get("S_15m",res["Sw"])),Sw=float(res["Sw"]))
    OUT.write_text(json.dumps(out,ensure_ascii=False))
    print(f"[bridge] analysed={len(out)} out={OUT}")

if __name__=="__main__": main()
