#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime
DATA=Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
SIGF=DATA/"signals.json"; POSF=DATA/"paper/positions.json"; BALF=DATA/"paper/balance.json"
CAND=DATA/"candles"; AOUT=DATA/"analysis_a"; BLAST=DATA/"debug/b_last"
N=20; FRESH=300; MIN_STRENGTH=float(os.environ.get("MIN_STRENGTH","1"))
def jload(p, d): 
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d
def hhmm(ts):
    if isinstance(ts,(int,float)): ts=int(ts/1000) if ts>1e12 else int(ts)
    try: return datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M")
    except: return "--:--"
def fresh(p:Path):
    try: return time.time()-p.stat().st_mtime <= FRESH
    except: return False
def budget():
    b=jload(BALF,{})
    for k in ("balance","equity","cash","budget"):
        if k in b:
            try: return float(b[k])
            except: pass
    return float(os.environ.get("PAPER_BUDGET","200"))
def is_open(sym):
    for p in jload(POSF,[]):
        if str(p.get("status","")).lower() in ("open","opened","running") and (p.get("symbol")==sym or p.get("sym")==sym):
            return True
    return False
def ctx(sym): return str(jload(AOUT/f"{sym}.json",{}).get("context","none")).lower()
def ohlcv_ok(sym):
    return all([
        (CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json").exists(),
        (CAND/"5m"/f"{sym}.json").exists(),
        fresh(CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"),
        fresh(CAND/"5m"/f"{sym}.json"),
    ])
def explain(sig):
    sym=sig.get("symbol") or sig.get("sym") or sig.get("coin") or "?"
    side=(sig.get("side") or sig.get("action") or "none").lower()
    action=(sig.get("action") or "none").lower()
    strength=float(sig.get("strength") or 0)
    margin=float(sig.get("margin") or sig.get("margin_usd") or sig.get("size_usd") or 0)
    bbal=budget()
    reasons=[]
    # infos brutes B
    b_last=jload(BLAST/f"{sym}.json",{})
    parsed=b_last.get("parsed",{})
    tp=parsed.get("tp"); sl=parsed.get("sl"); size=parsed.get("size") or 0; direction=parsed.get("direction") or side
    # règles
    if side=="none": reasons.append("side_none")
    if action in ("hold_long","hold_short","idle","wait"): reasons.append(f"action_{action}")
    if is_open(sym): reasons.append("already_open")
    if strength < MIN_STRENGTH: reasons.append(f"weak_strength<{MIN_STRENGTH}")
    if margin>0 and bbal < margin: reasons.append(f"insufficient_budget {bbal:.2f}<{margin:.2f}")
    if not ohlcv_ok(sym): reasons.append("stale_ohlcv")
    if ctx(sym)=="none": reasons.append("ctx_none")
    status = "WAIT" if reasons else "ACCEPTABLE"
    return {
        "t": hhmm(sig.get("ts") or sig.get("time") or sig.get("timestamp")),
        "sym": sym, "side": side, "action": action, "strength": strength,
        "margin": margin, "tp": tp, "sl": sl, "size": size, "dir": direction,
        "ctx": ctx(sym), "budget": bbal, "reasons": reasons or ["ok"]
    }, status
def main():
    sigs=jload(SIGF,[])
    if isinstance(sigs,dict): sigs=sigs.get("items") or sigs.get("signals") or []
    tail=sigs[-N:]
    print(f"== paper_debug_explain @ {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ')} ==")
    print(f"budget={budget():.2f}  open={len(jload(POSF,[]))}")
    for s in tail:
        res, st = explain(s)
        print(f"{res['t']} {res['sym']:<10} {res['side']:<5} str={res['strength']:<.1f} m={res['margin']:.2f} "
              f"tp={res['tp']} sl={res['sl']} sz={res['size']} dir={res['dir']} ctx={res['ctx']} -> {st} {','.join(res['reasons'])}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, json, subprocess, pathlib, time
DATA=pathlib.Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
ORIG="/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_coin.py"

def read_json_out(sym):
    p=subprocess.run(["python3", ORIG, sym], capture_output=True, text=True)
    out=(p.stdout or "").strip().splitlines()
    raw=out[-1] if out else "{}"
    try: j=json.loads(raw)
    except: j={"symbol":sym,"side":"none","action":"idle","strength":0,"reason":f"bad_json:{raw[:120]}"}
    j.setdefault("symbol", sym)
    # champs debug normalisés
    j.setdefault("direction", j.get("side","none"))
    j.setdefault("size", j.get("size") or j.get("qty") or j.get("amount") or 0)
    j.setdefault("margin", j.get("margin") or j.get("margin_usd") or j.get("size_usd") or 0)
    j.setdefault("tp", j.get("tp") or j.get("take_profit") or None)
    j.setdefault("sl", j.get("sl") or j.get("stop_loss") or None)
    j.setdefault("ts", int(time.time()))
    return j, p.stdout, p.stderr, p.returncode

def atomic_write(p, obj):
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    tmp=p.with_suffix(p.suffix+".tmp")
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(obj, indent=2))
    tmp.replace(p)

def main():
    if len(sys.argv)<2: sys.exit("usage: run_analysis_b_coin_debug.py SYMBOL")
    sym=sys.argv[1]
    j, out, err, rc = read_json_out(sym)
    # 1) trace debug
    dbg=DATA/"debug"/"b_last"/f"{sym}.json"
    atomic_write(dbg, {"stdout":out, "stderr":err, "rc":rc, "parsed":j})
    # 2) sortie coin pour l’agrégateur existant (ne rien casser)
    coin_out=DATA/"signals_coin"/f"{sym}.json"
    atomic_write(coin_out, j)
    # 3) echo pour logs
    print(json.dumps(j))
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import re, sys
from pathlib import Path
ROOT=Path("/opt/scalp/tools")
EXTS={".py",".sh",".bash",".zsh"}
SKIP=lambda p: any(s in p.name for s in (".bak",".backup","~")) or p.suffix not in EXTS
FILES=[p for p in ROOT.rglob("*") if p.is_file() and not SKIP(p)]

R=[
 # Python f-strings: f".../candles/{tf}/{sym}.json" -> f".../candles/{tf}/{sym}.json"
 (re.compile(r'candles/\s*\{\s*sym\s*\}\s*/\s*\{\s*tf\s*\}\s*/\s*last\.json'), r'candles/{tf}/{sym}.json'),
 # format %: "candles/%(tf)s/%(sym)s.json" -> "candles/%(tf)s/%(sym)s.json"
 (re.compile(r'candles/%\(sym\)s/%\(tf\)s/last\.json'), r'candles/%(tf)s/%(sym)s.json'),
 # .format: "candles/{tf}/{sym}.json".format(...) -> "candles/{tf}/{sym}.json"
 (re.compile(r'candles/\{sym\}/\{tf\}/last\.json'), r'candles/{tf}/{sym}.json'),
 # pathlib vars explicites: f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json" -> f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
 (re.compile(r'\bf\s*=\s*CAND\s*/\s*sym\s*/\s*tf\s*/\s*"?last\.json"?'), r'f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"'),
 # chaînes littérales coin/tf/last.json -> tf/coin.json
 (re.compile(r'candles/[A-Za-z0-9_]+/(1m|3m|5m|15m|30m)/last\.json'), r'candles/\1/{sym}.json'),
 # Bash: "$D/candles/${tf}/${sym}.json" -> "$D/candles/${tf}/${sym}.json"
 (re.compile(r'candles/\$\{sym\}/\$\{tf\}/last\.json'), r'candles/${tf}/${sym}.json'),
 (re.compile(r'candles/\$sym/\$tf/last\.json'), r'candles/$tf/$sym.json'),
]

def patch_text(s):
    changed=False
    for rx, rep in R:
        ns = rx.sub(rep, s)
        if ns!=s:
            s=ns; changed=True
    return s, changed

def main():
    touched=0
    for p in FILES:
        txt=p.read_text(errors="ignore")
        new, ch = patch_text(txt)
        if ch:
            p.with_suffix(p.suffix+".bak").write_text(txt)
            p.write_text(new)
            print("[patched]", p)
            touched+=1
    print(f"[done] {touched} fichiers modifiés")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, sys
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"

def norm(sym:str)->str:
    return sym.replace("/","").replace(":","").upper()

def main():
    top = json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    exn = (top.get("exchange") or "bitget").lower()
    ex  = getattr(ccxt, exn)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()

    ok = {norm(m["symbol"]) for m in ex.markets.values() if (m.get("quote") or "").upper()=="USDT"}
    syms = [s.upper() for s in (top.get("symbols") or [])]
    bad  = [s for s in syms if norm(s) not in ok]

    print(f"[map] exchange={exn} total={len(syms)} mapped={len(syms)-len(bad)} bad={len(bad)}")
    if bad:
        print("[map] bad:", ",".join(bad))
        top["symbols"] = [s for s in syms if s not in bad]
        TOP.write_text(json.dumps(top, indent=2))
        if len(top["symbols"]) < 5:
            print("[map] trop peu de symboles valides"); sys.exit(2)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
# Logic: S per TF -> softmax -> multi-TF aggregate -> 5m veto -> hysteresis+persist -> context

import math
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict

# ---------- Config ----------
W = dict(EMA=0.35, MACD=0.25, RSI=0.20, ADX=0.10, OBV=0.10)
TAU = {"30m": 0.35, "15m": 0.30, "5m": 0.25}
TF_W = {"30m": 0.50, "15m": 0.30, "5m": 0.20}
ATR_GATE = {"30m": 0.25, "15m": 0.18, "5m": 0.12}  # %

P_ENTER = 0.60
P_EXIT  = 0.45
RANGE_LOW, RANGE_HIGH = 0.40, 0.60
PERSIST_BARS = 2

# ---------- Helpers ----------
def clip(x, lo, hi): return hi if x>hi else lo if x<lo else x
def tanh(x): return math.tanh(x)

def softmax_triple(S, tau):
    e_pos = math.exp(S/tau); e_neg = math.exp(-S/tau); den = e_pos + 1.0 + e_neg
    return e_pos/den, 1.0/den, e_neg/den  # pb, ph, ps

# ---------- Score per TF ----------
def score_tf(inp: dict, tf: str):
    atr = max(inp.get("atr14", 0.0), 1e-12)
    s_ema  = tanh((inp.get("ema12",0.0)-inp.get("ema26",0.0))/(1.5*atr))
    sigma  = max(inp.get("macd_sigma100",1e-12), 1e-12)
    s_macd = tanh(inp.get("macd_hist",0.0)/sigma)
    s_rsi  = clip((inp.get("rsi14",50.0)-50.0)/50.0, -1.0, 1.0)
    s_adx  = clip((inp.get("adx14",20.0)-20.0)/20.0, -1.0, 1.0)
    medabs = max(inp.get("obv_medabs200",1e-12), 1e-12)
    s_obv  = tanh(inp.get("obv_delta20",0.0)/medabs)

    # ATR% gate (low vol -> damp EMA+MACD)
    atr_pct = float(inp.get("atr_pct", 0.0))  # %
    if atr_pct < ATR_GATE[tf]:
        s_ema *= 0.5; s_macd *= 0.5

    num = (W["EMA"]*s_ema + W["MACD"]*s_macd + W["RSI"]*s_rsi +
           W["ADX"]*s_adx + W["OBV"]*s_obv)
    S = clip(num/sum(W.values()), -1.0, 1.0)
    pb, ph, ps = softmax_triple(S, TAU[tf])
    return {"S": S, "pb": pb, "ph": ph, "ps": ps}

# ---------- Aggregation (expose per-TF for veto) ----------
def aggregate_probs(per_tf: dict):
    wsum = sum(TF_W.values())
    pb = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["pb"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf) / wsum
    ph = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ph"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf) / wsum
    ps = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ps"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf) / wsum
    Sw = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["S"]  for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf) / wsum
    tot = pb+ph+ps
    pb,ph,ps = (1/3,1/3,1/3) if tot<=0 else (pb/tot, ph/tot, ps/tot)
    out = {"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"Sw":Sw}
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        if tf in per_tf:
            out[f"pb_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["pb"]
            out[f"ps_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["ps"]
            out[f"S_{tf}"] =per_tf[tf]["S"]
    return out

# ---------- 5m veto ----------
def apply_veto_m5(agg: dict) -> dict:
    pb, ps = agg["pb"], agg["ps"]
    pb30, pb15 = agg.get("pb_30m",0.0), agg.get("pb_15m",0.0)
    ps30, ps15 = agg.get("ps_30m",0.0), agg.get("ps_15m",0.0)
    S5 = agg.get("S_5m", 0.0)

    bull_ok = (pb >= P_ENTER) and (pb30 >= 0.55) and (pb15 >= 0.55) and (S5 >= 0.0)
    bear_ok = (ps >= P_ENTER) and (ps30 >= 0.55) and (ps15 >= 0.55) and (S5 <= 0.0)

    if pb >= P_ENTER and not bull_ok:
        agg["pb"] = max(agg["pb"], P_EXIT - 1e-6)
    if ps >= P_ENTER and not bear_ok:
        agg["ps"] = max(agg["ps"], P_EXIT - 1e-6)

    tot = agg["pb"] + agg["ph"] + agg["ps"]
    if tot > 0:
        agg["pb"], agg["ph"], agg["ps"] = agg["pb"]/tot, agg["ph"]/tot, agg["ps"]/tot
    return agg

# ---------- Context state / decision ----------
from dataclasses import dataclass
@dataclass
class CtxState:
    ctx: str = "none"         # "buy"|"sell"|"hold"|"none"
    streak_ctx: str = "none"
    streak: int = 0
    bars_in_ctx: int = 0

def decide_next_ctx(prob, prev_ctx):
    pb, ph, ps = prob["pb"], prob["ph"], prob["ps"]
    buy_ok  = (pb >= P_ENTER) or (prev_ctx=="buy"  and pb >= P_EXIT)
    sell_ok = (ps >= P_ENTER) or (prev_ctx=="sell" and ps >= P_EXIT)
    range_ok = (RANGE_LOW <= ph <= RANGE_HIGH)
    if buy_ok  and pb >= ps and pb >= ph: return "buy"
    if sell_ok and ps >= pb and ps >= ph: return "sell"
    if range_ok: return "hold"
    return "none"

def update_context(state: CtxState, prob: dict, bar_closed: bool=True) -> CtxState:
    target = decide_next_ctx(prob, state.ctx)
    if target == state.ctx:
        return CtxState(ctx=state.ctx, streak_ctx=target,
                        streak=min(state.streak+1, PERSIST_BARS),
                        bars_in_ctx=state.bars_in_ctx + (1 if bar_closed else 0))
    streak = state.streak + 1 if target == state.streak_ctx else 1
    if streak >= PERSIST_BARS:
        return CtxState(ctx=target, streak_ctx=target, streak=streak,
                        bars_in_ctx=1 if bar_closed else 0)
    return CtxState(ctx=state.ctx, streak_ctx=target, streak=streak,
                    bars_in_ctx=state.bars_in_ctx + (1 if bar_closed else 0))

# ---------- Pipeline utilitaire ----------
def compute_ctx(per_tf_inputs: dict, prev_state: CtxState) -> dict:
    per_tf = {tf: score_tf(per_tf_inputs[tf], tf) for tf in per_tf_inputs}
    agg = aggregate_probs(per_tf)
    agg = apply_veto_m5(agg)
    new_state = update_context(prev_state, agg, bar_closed=True)
    ints = {k:int(round(10*agg[k])) for k in ("pb","ph","ps")}
    return {"pb":agg["pb"], "ph":agg["ph"], "ps":agg["ps"], "Sw":agg["Sw"],
            "ctx_state": new_state, "ints": ints, "per_tf": per_tf, "agg": agg}
----- FILE END -----

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/tools/indicators_tf.py
Size: 3247
MTime: 2025-09-26 11:56:47.233097382 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
from math import fabs
def ema(xs, n):
    if not xs: return []
    a = 2.0/(n+1.0); s = xs[0]; out=[s]
    for x in xs[1:]:
        s = a*x + (1-a)*s; out.append(s)
    return out
def rsi(cl, n=14):
    if len(cl)<n+1: return [None]*len(cl)
    gains=[]; losses=[]; out=[None]
    for a,b in zip(cl, cl[1:]):
        d=b-a; gains.append(max(d,0.0)); losses.append(max(-d,0.0)); out.append(None)
    ag=sum(gains[:n])/n; al=sum(losses[:n])/n
    vals=[]
    for g,l in zip(gains[n:], losses[n:]):
        ag=(ag*(n-1)+g)/n; al=(al*(n-1)+l)/n
        vals.append(100.0 - 100.0/(1.0 + (ag/(al+1e-12))))
    return [None]*(len(cl)-len(vals)) + vals
def macd_hist(cl, f=12, s=26, sig=9):
    ef=ema(cl,f); es=ema(cl,s); macd=[a-b for a,b in zip(ef,es)]
    sigl=ema(macd,sig); return [m-s for m,s in zip(macd,sigl)]
def adx(h,l,c,n=14):
    if len(h)<n+1: return [None]*len(h)
    tr=[None]; dmp=[None]; dmn=[None]
    for i in range(1,len(h)):
        tr.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-c[i-1]), abs(l[i]-c[i-1])))
        dmp.append(max(h[i]-h[i-1],0.0)); dmn.append(max(l[i-1]-l[i],0.0))
    atr=sum(tr[1:n+1])/n; pdi=sum(dmp[1:n+1])/n; ndi=sum(dmn[1:n+1])/n
    ax=[None]* (n+1)
    for i in range(n+1,len(h)):
        atr=(atr*(n-1)+tr[i])/n; pdi=(pdi*(n-1)+dmp[i])/n; ndi=(ndi*(n-1)+dmn[i])/n
        pd=100.0*(pdi/(atr+1e-12)); nd=100.0*(ndi/(atr+1e-12))
        dx=100.0*fabs(pd-nd)/max(pd+nd,1e-12)
        ax.append(dx if ax[-1] is None else ((ax[-1]*(n-1))+dx)/n)
    return ax[:len(h)]
def obv_deltas(cl, vol, win=20, medw=200):
    obv=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cl)):
        d=(1 if cl[i]>cl[i-1] else -1 if cl[i]<cl[i-1] else 0)*vol[i]
        obv.append(obv[-1]+d)
    d20=obv[-1] - (obv[-win-1] if len(obv)>win else 0.0)
    diffs=[abs(obv[i]-obv[i-1]) for i in range(1,len(obv))]
    import statistics as st
    med=st.median(diffs[-medw:]) if diffs else 1.0
    return d20, max(med,1.0)
def atr_pct(h,l,c,n=14):
    if len(c)<n+1: return [None]*len(c)
    tr=[None]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        tr.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-c[i-1]), abs(l[i]-c[i-1])))
    a=2.0/(n+1.0); s=sum(tr[1:n+1])/n; out=[None]*n+[s]
    for x in tr[n+1:]:
        s=a*x+(1-a)*s; out.append(s)
    return [ (out[i]/c[i])*100.0 if out[i] is not None and c[i]>0 else None for i in range(len(out))]
def indicators_from_ohlcv(rows):
    o=[float(r[1]) for r in rows]; h=[float(r[2]) for r in rows]
    l=[float(r[3]) for r in rows]; c=[float(r[4]) for r in rows]; v=[float(r[5]) for r in rows]
    ema12=ema(c,12)[-1]; ema26=ema(c,26)[-1]
    hist=macd_hist(c,12,26,9); import statistics as st
    macd_h=hist[-1] if hist else 0.0; macd_sigma=st.pstdev(hist[-100:]) if len(hist)>=2 else 1.0
    r=rsi(c,14); rsi14=r[-1] if r and r[-1] is not None else 50.0
    ad=adx(h,l,c,14); adx14=ad[-1] if ad and ad[-1] is not None else 20.0
    obv20, med=obv_deltas(c,v,20,200)
    atrp=atr_pct(h,l,c,14); atrp14=atrp[-1] if atrp and atrp[-1] is not None else 0.0
    return dict(ema12=ema12, ema26=ema26, atr14=max(abs(h[-1]-l[-1]),1e-9),
                macd_hist=macd_h, macd_sigma100=max(macd_sigma,1e-9),
                rsi14=rsi14, adx14=adx14, obv_delta20=obv20,
                obv_medabs200=max(med,1.0), atr_pct=atrp14)

from pathlib import Path
import json
from _lib_price import last_close_1m

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
SIG  = DATA/"signals.json"
DBG  = DATA/"debug"/"bridge"
DBG.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def jload(p:Path, dflt):
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception: return dflt

def main():
    items = jload(SIG, [])
    out = []
    for s in items:
        sym = s.get("symbol") or s.get("sym")
        if not sym: 
            out.append(s); 
            continue
        # normalise clé "price"
        px = s.get("price")
        if px in (None, 0, 0.0):
            px = last_close_1m(sym)
            if px: s["price"] = px
        # log léger par coin
        (DBG/f"{sym}.log").write_text(
            f'{sym} ctx={s.get("ctx")} str={s.get("strength")} '
            f'pb={s.get("pb")} ps={s.get("ps")} atr%={s.get("atr_pct",0)} '
            f'veto={s.get("veto",0)} action={s.get("action")} side={s.get("side")} '
            f'price={s.get("price")}\n'
        )
        out.append(s)
    SIG.write_text(json.dumps(out, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
    print(f"[bridge-enrich] signals={len(out)} updated")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

import os, json, time, tempfile
from pathlib import Path

DATA   = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data"))
SYMBOL = os.environ.get("SYMBOL", "BTCUSDT")
TFS    = ["1m","3m","5m","15m","30m"]

def read_last(path: Path):
    """Retourne le dernier array OHLCV ou None si fichier manquant/vide/incorrect."""
    try:
        with path.open("r") as f:
            arr = json.load(f)
        if isinstance(arr, list) and arr:
            last = arr[-1]
            return last if isinstance(last, list) else None
    except Exception:
        return None
    return None

def main():
    hub_dir = DATA / "hub"
    hub_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    per = []
    for tf in TFS:
        base = DATA / "candles" / tf
        closed = read_last(base / f"{SYMBOL}.json")
        opened = read_last(base / f"{SYMBOL}.open.json")
        per.append({
            "tf": tf,
            "last_closed": closed,
            "last_open": opened
        })

    out = {
        "symbol": SYMBOL,
        "updated_ms": int(time.time() * 1000),
        "per_tf": per
    }

    out_path = hub_dir / f"{SYMBOL}.json"
    tmp = tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile("w", delete=False, dir=str(hub_dir))
    json.dump(out, tmp, ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",", ":"))
    tmp.flush(); os.fsync(tmp.fileno()); tmp.close()
    os.replace(tmp.name, out_path)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math, asyncio, time, glob
from pathlib import Path
from lib.ohlcv_live import live_close, live_atr

DATA=Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
TOP =DATA/"top.json"
COIN_OUT=DATA/"signals_coin"
ALL =DATA/"signals.json"
A_DIR=DATA/"analysis_a"
RUN =Path("/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_coin.py")
LOGF=Path("/opt/scalp/logs/signals_bridge.log")

WORKERS=int(os.getenv("SIGNAL_WORKERS","10"))
TIMEOUT=int(os.getenv("SIGNAL_TIMEOUT_S","60"))

RISK_PCT=float(os.getenv("RISK_PCT","0.02"))
LEVERAGE=float(os.getenv("LEVERAGE","3"))
SLxATR=float(os.getenv("SLxATR","0.6"))
TPxATR=float(os.getenv("TPxATR","1.0"))
ATR_PER=int(os.getenv("ATR_PER","7"))
EASY_ATR_PCT=float(os.getenv("EASY_ATR_PCT","0.003"))
MIN_STOP_ABS_PCT=float(os.getenv("MIN_STOP_ABS_PCT","0.001"))
NOTIONAL_USD=float(os.getenv("NOTIONAL_USD","10"))
MIN_QTY=float(os.getenv("MIN_QTY","0.001"))
MIN_STRENGTH=float(os.getenv("MIN_STRENGTH","-1e9"))
PRICE_TRIGGER_PCT=float(os.getenv("PRICE_TRIGGER_PCT","0.0005"))  # 0.05% mouvement min

FALLBACK_A_TOP=int(os.getenv("FALLBACK_A_TOP","3"))
FALLBACK_A_MIN_CTX=os.getenv("FALLBACK_A_MIN_CTX","buy,sell").split(",")

BAL=DATA/"paper"/"balance.json"
C1M=DATA/"candles"/"1m"

def jload(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def wlog(msg):
    LOGF.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    with open(LOGF,"a") as fh:
        fh.write(f"{time.strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ', time.gmtime())} {msg}\n")

def detect_side(raw):
    s=(raw.get("side") or "").lower()
    a=(raw.get("action") or "").lower()
    ctx=(raw.get("context") or raw.get("ctx") or "").lower()
    why=(raw.get("reason") or raw.get("why") or "").lower()
    if s in ("buy","long"): return "buy"
    if s in ("sell","short"): return "sell"
    if a.startswith(("enter_long","hold_long")) or "buy" in a or ctx in ("buy","bullish") or "hold long" in why: return "buy"
    if a.startswith(("enter_short","hold_short")) or "sell" in a or ctx in ("sell","bearish") or "hold short" in why: return "sell"
    return None

def last_closed(sym):
    rows=jload(C1M/f"{sym}.json",[]) or []
    if not rows: return None
    try: return float(rows[-1][4])
    except: return None

async def run_one(sym):
    try:
        p=await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec("python3", str(RUN), sym,
                                               stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
                                               stderr=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL)
        await asyncio.wait_for(p.wait(), timeout=TIMEOUT)
    except asyncio.TimeoutError:
        try: p.kill()
        except: pass
        wlog(f"[TIMEOUT] {sym}")
    raw=jload(COIN_OUT/f"{sym}.json",{}) or {}
    return enrich_from_B(sym, raw)

def enrich_from_B(sym, raw):
    if not isinstance(raw,dict): wlog(f"[SKIP] {sym} raw-not-dict"); return None
    side=detect_side(raw)
    if not side: wlog(f"[SKIP] {sym} no-side B"); return None

    strength=float(raw.get("strength") or raw.get("S") or 0.0)
    if strength < MIN_STRENGTH: wlog(f"[SKIP] {sym} low-strength={strength}"); return None

    px_live = live_close(sym)
    px_close = last_closed(sym)
    px = px_live or px_close
    if not px: wlog(f"[SKIP] {sym} no-price"); return None

    # Déclencheur anti-bruit: exiger un écart min vs dernière close
    if px_close:
        move = abs(px - px_close)/px_close
        if move < PRICE_TRIGGER_PCT:
            wlog(f"[SKIP] {sym} move<{PRICE_TRIGGER_PCT} live_vs_close")
            return None

    atr = live_atr(sym, ATR_PER)
    if atr is None: atr = px*(EASY_ATR_PCT)

    stop=max(atr*SLxATR, px*MIN_STOP_ABS_PCT)
    take=max(atr*TPxATR, px*2*MIN_STOP_ABS_PCT)
    sl = px - stop if side=="buy" else px + stop
    tp = px + take if side=="buy" else px - take

    bal=float((jload(BAL,{"cash":200.0}) or {}).get("cash",200.0))
    risk_amt=max(0.0, bal*RISK_PCT)
    stop_dist=abs(px-sl)
    qty=0.0 if stop_dist<=0 else risk_amt/stop_dist
    if qty < MIN_QTY: qty=max(MIN_QTY, NOTIONAL_USD/px)

    order={
        "ts": int(time.time()*1000),
        "symbol": sym,
        "side": side,
        "entry": round(px,6),
        "sl": round(sl,6),
        "tp": round(tp,6),
        "size": round(qty,6),
        "margin": round(qty*px/(LEVERAGE if LEVERAGE>0 else 1),2),
        "why": raw.get("reason") or raw.get("why") or "B",
        "strength": strength,
        "source": "B"
    }
    wlog(f"[OK] {sym} {side} px={px:.6f} sl={sl:.6f} tp={tp:.6f} qty={qty:.3f} live={(px_live is not None)}")
    return order

def fallback_from_A():
    items=[]
    files=sorted(glob.glob(str(A_DIR/"*.json")))
    for f in files:
        d=jload(f,{}) or {}
        sym=d.get("symbol") or Path(f).stem
        ctx=(d.get("ctx") or d.get("context") or "none").lower()
        if ctx not in FALLBACK_A_MIN_CTX: 
            continue
        px = live_close(sym) or last_closed(sym)
        if not px: wlog(f"[A-FALLBACK SKIP] {sym} no price"); continue
        atr = live_atr(sym, ATR_PER) or px*(EASY_ATR_PCT)
        stop=max(atr*SLxATR, px*MIN_STOP_ABS_PCT)
        take=max(atr*TPxATR, px*2*MIN_STOP_ABS_PCT)
        side="buy" if ctx=="buy" else "sell"
        sl = px - stop if side=="buy" else px + stop
        tp = px + take if side=="buy" else px - take
        qty=max(MIN_QTY, NOTIONAL_USD/px)
        items.append({
            "ts": int(time.time()*1000),
            "symbol": sym,
            "side": side,
            "entry": round(px,6),
            "sl": round(sl,6),
            "tp": round(tp,6),
            "size": round(qty,6),
            "margin": round(NOTIONAL_USD/(LEVERAGE if LEVERAGE>0 else 1),2),
            "why": "A-fallback",
            "strength": float(d.get("S") or 0),
            "source": "A-fallback"
        })
    items.sort(key=lambda x: x.get("strength",0.0), reverse=True)
    sel=items[:FALLBACK_A_TOP]
    for it in sel:
        wlog(f"[A-FALLBACK OK] {it['symbol']} {it['side']} px={it['entry']} qty={it['size']}")
    return sel

async def main():
    top=jload(TOP,{}) or {}
    syms=[s for s in (top.get("symbols") or [])][:50]
    if not syms:
        ALL.write_text("[]"); wlog("[TOP] no symbols"); print("[signals] no symbols"); return

    sem=asyncio.Semaphore(WORKERS)
    async def one(s):
        async with sem: return await run_one(s)
    res=await asyncio.gather(*[one(s) for s in syms])

    out=[r for r in res if r]
    if not out:
        wlog("[INFO] 0 actionable from B → using A fallback")
        out=fallback_from_A()

    out=out[:60]
    ALL.write_text(json.dumps(out, separators=(",",":")))
    print(f"[signals] written {ALL} items={len(out)}")
    wlog(f"[DONE] signals={len(out)}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import json, sys
from pathlib import Path
from b_logic import jload, jsave, last_complete, analyze_symbol, PARAM as BPAR

DATA   = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND   = DATA/"candles"        # /candles/<tf>/<SYMBOL>.json  {"data":[[ts,o,h,l,c,v],...]}
A_OUT  = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
B_OUT  = DATA/"analyse_B_out.json"
SIGNALS= DATA/"signals.json"

TF_SEC = {"1m":60, "3m":180, "5m":300}

def load_tf(sym, tf):
    f = CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    try:
        j = json.loads(Path(f).read_text())
        arr = j.get("data") or []
    except:
        arr = []
    return last_complete(arr, TF_SEC[tf])

def write_signal(sig):
    if not sig: return
    # enrichissement standard
    sig.setdefault("lev", float(BPAR.get("leverage", 1)))
    sig.setdefault("risk_pct", float(BPAR.get("risk_pct", 0.0)))
    lst = (json.loads(SIGNALS.read_text()) if SIGNALS.exists() else []) or []
    lst.append(sig)
    lst = lst[-200:]
    SIGNALS.write_text(json.dumps(lst, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))

def main():
    if len(sys.argv)<2:
        print("usage: b_run_coin.py SYMBOL", file=sys.stderr); return 2
    sym = sys.argv[1]
    a    = (json.loads(A_OUT.read_text()) if A_OUT.exists() else {}) or {}
    arow = a.get(sym, {}) or {}
    ctxA = arow.get("context") or "none"

    m1 = load_tf(sym, "1m")
    m3 = load_tf(sym, "3m")
    m5 = load_tf(sym, "5m")
    if not (m1 and m3 and m5):
        print(json.dumps({"symbol":sym, "error":"missing_candles_1m/3m/5m"})); return 1

    res = analyze_symbol(sym, ctxA, m1, m3, m5)
    # persist analyse_B_out.json (dict par symbole)
    bout = (json.loads(B_OUT.read_text()) if B_OUT.exists() else {}) or {}
    bout[sym] = res
    B_OUT.write_text(json.dumps(bout, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
    # append signal si présent
    write_signal(res.get("signal"))
    print(json.dumps(res))
    return 0

if __name__=="__main__":
    import sys as _; _.exit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
C=/opt/scalp/data/candles
TS=$(date -u +%Y%m%dT%H%M%S)
TR=$C/.trash_$TS; mkdir -p "$TR"
mkdir -p "$C/1m" "$C/3m" "$C/5m"

is_tf(){ case "$1" in 1m|3m|5m|10m|15m|30m) return 0;; *) return 1;; esac; }

# 1) Si on a des dossiers SYMBOL contenant 1m.json/3m.json/5m.json → on range
find "$C" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d | while read -r d; do
  bn=$(basename "$d")
  is_tf "$bn" && continue
  # si le dossier contient des JSON par TF, on les dépose dans C/TF/SYMBOL.json
  for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
    f="$d/${tf}.json"
    [ -s "$f" ] && mv -f "$f" "$C/$tf/${bn}.json"
  done
  # si vide → poubelle
  rmdir "$d" 2>/dev/null || true
done

# 2) Fichiers égarés à la racine → poubelle
find "$C" -maxdepth 1 -type f -name '*.json' -exec mv -f {} "$TR"/ \;

# 3) Corriger *USD -> *USDT (fichiers)
for tf in 1m 3m 5m; do
  find "$C/$tf" -maxdepth 1 -type f -name '*USD.json' ! -name '*USDT.json' | while read -r f; do
    base=$(basename "$f")
    mv -f "$f" "$C/$tf/${base%.json}T.json"
  done
done

# 4) Supprimer TF non supportés
for bad in 10m 15m 30m; do
  [ -d "$C/$bad" ] && mv "$C/$bad" "$TR/${bad}_$TS" || true
done

echo "[repair] layout OK. Trash -> $TR"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
from math import isfinite, log
def safe(x, d=0.0):
    try:
        return float(x) if isfinite(float(x)) else d
    except: return d

def ema(series, alpha):
    out=[]; s=None
    for x in series:
        x=safe(x,0.0)
        s = x if s is None else (alpha*x + (1-alpha)*s)
        out.append(s)
    return out

def rsi(closes, period=14):
    if not closes: return []
    gains=[]; losses=[]
    prev=closes[0]
    rsis=[None]
    for c in closes[1:]:
        d=c-prev; prev=c
        gains.append(max(d,0.0)); losses.append(max(-d,0.0))
    if len(gains)<period: return [None]*len(closes)
    import itertools
    ag=sum(gains[:period])/period; al=sum(losses[:period])/period
    rs=[ag/(al+1e-12)]
    for g,l in zip(gains[period:], losses[period:]):
        ag=(ag*(period-1)+g)/period; al=(al*(period-1)+l)/period
        rs.append(ag/(al+1e-12))
    vals=[None]*(len(closes)-len(rs)-1)
    vals += [100.0 - 100.0/(1.0+r) for r in rs]
    return [None]+vals

def stdev(series, period):
    out=[None]*len(series)
    if period<=1 or len(series)<period: return out
    from statistics import pstdev
    for i in range(period-1, len(series)):
        window=series[i-period+1:i+1]
        out[i]=pstdev(window)
    return out

def atr(h, l, c, period=14):
    trs=[None]; prev=c[0]
    for hi,lo,cl in zip(h[1:],l[1:],c[1:]):
        tr=max(hi-lo, abs(hi-prev), abs(lo-prev))
        trs.append(tr); prev=cl
    return stdev(trs, period)

def logret(closes):
    out=[None]
    for a,b in zip(closes, closes[1:]):
        try: out.append(log(b/a))
        except: out.append(None)
    return out

def lastn(xs, n=1, default=None):
    return [x for x in xs if x is not None][-n:] or [default]

def norm01(x, lo, hi):
    if hi<=lo: return 0.0
    v=(x-lo)/(hi-lo)
    return 0.0 if v<0 else 1.0 if v>1 else v

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, sys
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone

def now_iso(): 
    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

# ---- Params
EX="bitget"; QUOTE="USDT"
TOP_N = int(os.getenv("TOP_N", "30"))
MIN_QV = float(os.getenv("MIN_QV", "1000000"))       # 1M
MAX_SP = float(os.getenv("MAX_SP_BPS", "60"))        # 0.60%
USE_DEPTH = os.getenv("USE_DEPTH", "0") == "1"
MIN_DEPTH = float(os.getenv("MIN_DEPTH_USD", "200000"))  # gate si USE_DEPTH=1
BAND_BPS = int(os.getenv("DEPTH_BAND_BPS", "50"))    # ±0.5%
FUT = {"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}

BAD_KW=("UP","DOWN","BULL","BEAR","3L","3S","5L","5S")
BAD_BASES={"USDT","USDC","FDUSD","TUSD","DAI","EUR","TRY","USD"}

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
TOP=DATA/"top.json"; RANK=DATA/"top_ranked.json"; MAP=DATA/"symbol_map.json"
INACT=DATA/"coins_90d.json"

def load_inactive():
    try:
        j=json.loads(INACT.read_text())
        return set(j.get("inactive_symbols", []))
    except: 
        return set()

def load_seed():
    if TOP.exists():
        try:
            j=json.loads(TOP.read_text()); s=j.get("symbols") or []
            s=[x for x in s if isinstance(x,str)]
            if s: return s
        except: pass
    return ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","BNBUSDT"]

def clamp(x,a,b): 
    return a if x<a else b if x>b else x

def depth_usd(ex, sym, band_bps):
    try:
        ob = ex.fetch_order_book(sym, 100, {**FUT})
        if not ob.get("bids") or not ob.get("asks"): return 0.0
        bb=ob["bids"][0][0]; ba=ob["asks"][0][0]; mid=0.5*(bb+ba)
        lo,hi = mid*(1-band_bps/10000.0), mid*(1+band_bps/10000.0)
        q=0.0
        for p,a in ob["bids"]:
            if p<lo: break
            q += p*a
        for p,a in ob["asks"]:
            if p>hi: break
            q += p*a
        return float(q)
    except:
        return 0.0

def main():
    import ccxt
    seeds = load_seed()
    inactive = load_inactive()    # persistance inactifs 90j
    
    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    mkts=[m for m in ex.markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE and m.get("active") is not False]
    symbols=[m["symbol"] for m in mkts]
    bases={m["symbol"]: m["base"] for m in mkts}
    sym_map = {m["symbol"].replace("/","").replace(":",""): m["symbol"] for m in mkts}
    MAP.write_text(json.dumps(sym_map, indent=2))

    # tickers bulk + fallback par symbole si besoin
    tickers={}
    try:
        tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols, {**FUT})
    except Exception:
        for s in symbols:
            try: tickers[s]=ex.fetch_ticker(s,{**FUT})
            except Exception: tickers[s]={}

    pool=[]
    for s in symbols:
        flat = s.replace("/","").replace(":","")
        if flat in inactive: 
            continue
        b=bases[s]
        if any(k in b for k in BAD_KW): 
            continue
        if b in BAD_BASES:
            continue

        t = tickers.get(s, {})
        # quoteVolume fallback (Bitget/ccxt)
        qv = t.get("quoteVolume")
        if not qv:
            info = t.get("info", {})
            qv = info.get("quoteVolume") or info.get("quoteVolume24h") or info.get("baseVolume") # au cas où
        qv = float(qv or 0.0)

        bid,ask = t.get("bid"), t.get("ask")
        if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0:
            continue
        mid = 0.5*(bid+ask)
        sp_bps = clamp(10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid, 0.0, 200.0)  # clamp spread [0,200] bps

        if qv < MIN_QV or sp_bps > MAX_SP:
            continue

        # Depth gate optionnel
        d_q = 0.0
        if USE_DEPTH:
            try:
                d_q = depth_usd(ex, s, BAND_BPS)
            except:
                d_q = 0.0
            if d_q < MIN_DEPTH:
                continue

        pool.append({"symbol": s, "flat": flat, "qv": qv, "sp_bps": sp_bps, "depth_q": d_q})

    # tri par volume 24h
    pool.sort(key=lambda x: x["qv"], reverse=True)

    # compose résultat: noyau fixe d'abord, puis complétion
    seed_set=set(seeds)
    out=list(seeds)
    details=[]
    # ajouter d'abord les seeds avec métriques si dispo
    for e in pool:
        if e["flat"] in seed_set:
            details.append({"symbol": e["flat"], "score": 1.0, "volume24h_quote": e["qv"], "spread_bps": e["sp_bps"], "depth_quote": e["depth_q"]})
    # compléter
    for e in pool:
        if e["flat"] in seed_set:
            continue
        out.append(e["flat"]); seed_set.add(e["flat"])
        details.append({"symbol": e["flat"], "score": 0.0, "volume24h_quote": e["qv"], "spread_bps": e["sp_bps"], "depth_quote": e["depth_q"]})
        if len(out) >= TOP_N:
            break

    meta={"generated_at": now_iso(), "source":"futures-tickers-fast+options", "exchange":EX, "quote":QUOTE}
    (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({**meta, "symbols": out[:TOP_N]}, indent=2))
    (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({"generated_at": meta["generated_at"], "n": len(out[:TOP_N]), "items": details[:TOP_N]}, indent=2))
    print(f"[expand+fast] seeds={len(seeds)} pool={len(pool)} use_depth={USE_DEPTH} top={len(out[:TOP_N])}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
C1   = DATA/"candles"/"1m"

def jload(p,d):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def jsave(p, rows):
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(rows, separators=(",",":")))

def last_ts(rows):
    if isinstance(rows,list) and rows:
        try: return int(rows[-1][0])
        except: return None
    return None

def run_one(sym):
    fo = C1/f"{sym}.open.json"
    fc = C1/f"{sym}.json"
    rows_o = jload(fo, [])
    if not rows_o: return False
    row_o  = rows_o[-1]
    ts_o   = int(row_o[0])
    now_ms = int(time.time()*1000)
    curmin = now_ms - (now_ms % 60000)
    # on clôture l'open si elle appartient à la minute passée
    if ts_o < curmin:
        rows_c = jload(fc, [])
        ts_last = last_ts(rows_c) or -1
        if ts_o > ts_last:
            rows_c.append(row_o)
            jsave(fc, rows_c)
            return True
    return False

def main():
    syms = (jload(TOP, {}).get("symbols") or [])[:int(os.environ.get("TOP_LIMIT","50"))]
    n=0
    for s in syms:
        try:
            if run_one(s): n+=1
        except Exception: pass
    print(f"[closer] closed={n}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
from pathlib import Path
import json, sys
from sanitize_symbol import sanitize

TOP = Path("/opt/scalp/data/top.json")
BAK = Path("/opt/scalp/data/top.json.bak")

def main():
    if not TOP.exists():
        print(f"[ERR] {TOP} introuvable", file=sys.stderr)
        sys.exit(1)

    raw = json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    # on gère les 2 structures possibles: objet {"symbols":[...]} ou liste brute [...]
    if isinstance(raw, dict):
        symbols = raw.get("symbols", [])
        changed, out = normalize_list(symbols)
        raw["symbols"] = out
        # si présent, on tente aussi de nettoyer d'autres champs potentiels
        for k in ("seeds", "pool", "bad", "mapped"):
            if isinstance(raw.get(k), list):
                _, cleaned = normalize_list(raw[k])
                raw[k] = cleaned
        if changed: write(raw)
        print(f"[top-fix] total={len(out)}  changed={changed}")
    elif isinstance(raw, list):
        changed, out = normalize_list(raw)
        if changed: write(out)
        print(f"[top-fix] total={len(out)}  changed={changed}")
    else:
        print("[WARN] format inconnu pour top.json (ni dict ni list)")

def normalize_list(lst):
    seen = set()
    out  = []
    changed = False
    for sym in lst:
        s0 = str(sym)
        s1 = sanitize(s0)
        if s1 != s0:
            changed = True
        if s1 not in seen:
            seen.add(s1)
            out.append(s1)
        else:
            changed = True
    # tri stable par ordre alpha pour reproductibilité
    out = sorted(out)
    return changed, out

def write(obj):
    if TOP.exists():
        BAK.write_text(TOP.read_text())
    TOP.write_text(json.dumps(obj, indent=2))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, time, json, pathlib, math
import ccxt

DATA   = pathlib.Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
SYMBOL = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")

# NB: Bitget futures USDT
ex = ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit": True})

# mapping TF -> ccxt timeframe
TFS = ["1m","5m","15m","30m"]
LIMIT = int(os.environ.get("LIMIT","1000"))

def ensure_dirs():
    for tf in TFS + ["3m"]:
        (DATA/"candles"/tf).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def fetch_tf(tf):
    m = ex.fetch_ohlcv(SYMBOL[:-4]+"/"+SYMBOL[-4:]+":"+SYMBOL[-4:], timeframe=tf, limit=LIMIT)
    return m

def write_atomic(path: pathlib.Path, arr):
    tmp = path.with_suffix(".json.tmp")
    with tmp.open("w") as f:
        json.dump(arr, f, separators=(",",":"))
    tmp.replace(path)

def resample_3m_from_1m(c1m):
    out = []
    for i in range(0, len(c1m), 3):
        chunk = c1m[i:i+3]
        if len(chunk) < 3: break
        ts = (chunk[0][0]//60000)*60000  # align début minute
        o  = chunk[0][1]
        h  = max(x[2] for x in chunk)
        l  = min(x[3] for x in chunk)
        c  = chunk[-1][4]
        v  = sum(float(x[5]) for x in chunk)
        out.append([ts,o,h,l,c,v])
    return out

def main():
    ensure_dirs()

    # 1m
    one = fetch_tf("1m")
    write_atomic(DATA/"candles"/"1m"/f"{SYMBOL}.json", one)

    # 5/15/30m via CCXT direct
    for tf in ["5m","15m","30m"]:
        arr = fetch_tf(tf)
        write_atomic(DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{SYMBOL}.json", arr)

    # 3m local depuis 1m
    three = resample_3m_from_1m(one)
    write_atomic(DATA/"candles"/"3m"/f"{SYMBOL}.json", three)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

Size: 4085
MTime: 2025-09-27 09:03:02.448344914 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path
try:
    import ccxt
except Exception:
    import subprocess, sys as _s
    subprocess.check_call([_s.executable,"-m","pip","install","--no-cache-dir","ccxt"])
    import ccxt
from importlib.util import spec_from_file_location, module_from_spec
_spec = spec_from_file_location("atomic_json","/opt/scalp/tools/lib/atomic_json.py")
if not _spec or not _spec.loader:
    print("[err] atomic_json.py introuvable", file=sys.stderr); sys.exit(1)
_atomic = module_from_spec(_spec); _spec.loader.exec_module(_atomic)
write_atomic_json = _atomic.write_atomic_json

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data_test"))
CAND = DATA/"candles"
KEEP = int(os.environ.get("KEEP","1500"))
SYMBOL = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")
TFS = ("1m","3m","5m","15m","30m")

ex = ccxt.bitget({"enableRateLimit": True, "timeout": 20000})
ex.load_markets()

def tf_ms(tf:str)->int: return int(tf[:-1])*60_000
def now_ms(): return int(time.time()*1000)
def mkt(sym_flat:str)->str:
    base=sym_flat[:-4]; quote=sym_flat[-4:]; return f"{base}/{quote}:{quote}"

def jload(p:Path):
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text() or "[]")
    except: return []

def jdump_closed(p:Path, arr): write_atomic_json(p, arr[-KEEP:])
def jdump_open(p:Path, arr_or_empty): write_atomic_json(p, arr_or_empty if isinstance(arr_or_empty, list) else [])

def fetch(sym:str, tf:str, limit:int=200):
    try: return ex.fetch_ohlcv(mkt(sym), timeframe=tf, limit=limit) or []
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[fetch] {sym} {tf} {e}", file=sys.stderr); return []

def is_closed(ts:int, tf:str)->bool:
    return (now_ms() // tf_ms(tf)) > (ts // tf_ms(tf))

def split_closed_open(rows, tf):
    if not rows: return [], []
    rows = sorted(rows, key=lambda r:r[0])
    closed = rows[:]
    openp = []
    if not is_closed(rows[-1][0], tf):
        openp = [rows[-1]]
        closed = rows[:-1]
    return closed, openp

def resample_from_1m(arr1, tf:str):
    step=tf_ms(tf); out=[]; bucket=None
    for ts,o,h,l,c,v in arr1:
        bts=ts - (ts % step)
        if bucket is None or bucket[0]!=bts:
            if bucket: out.append(bucket)
            bucket=[bts,o,h,l,c,v]
        else:
            if h>bucket[2]: bucket[2]=h
            if l<bucket[3]: bucket[3]=l
            bucket[4]=c; bucket[5]+=v
    if bucket: out.append(bucket)
    return out

def backfill(sym:str):
    for tf in ("1m","5m","15m","30m"):
        arr = fetch(sym, tf, KEEP)
        closed, openp = split_closed_open(arr, tf)
        jdump_closed(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json", closed)
        jdump_open  (CAND/tf/f"{sym}.open.json", openp)
        print(f"[backfill] {sym} {tf} close={len(closed)} open={(1 if openp else 0)}")
    arr1 = jload(CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json")
    arr3 = resample_from_1m(arr1, "3m")
    jdump_closed(CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.json", arr3)
    jdump_open  (CAND/"3m"/f"{sym}.open.json", [])
    print(f"[backfill] {sym} 3m close={len(arr3)} open=0")

def merge_closed(old, new_closed):
    merged = {r[0]:r for r in (old+new_closed)}
    return [merged[k] for k in sorted(merged)][-KEEP:]

def follow_once(sym:str):
    rows = fetch(sym, "1m", 4)
    rows_c, row_o = split_closed_open(rows, "1m")
    p1c = CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.json"
    p1o = CAND/"1m"/f"{sym}.open.json"
    hist = jload(p1c)
    arr1c = merge_closed(hist, rows_c)
    jdump_closed(p1c, arr1c)
    jdump_open  (p1o, row_o)
    print(f"[upd] {sym} 1m closeN={len(arr1c)} openN={len(row_o)}")
    for tf in ("3m","5m","15m","30m"):
        arr = resample_from_1m(arr1c, tf)
        closed_tf, open_tf = split_closed_open(arr, tf)
        jdump_closed(CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json", closed_tf)
        jdump_open  (CAND/tf/f"{sym}.open.json", open_tf)
        print(f"[resample] {sym} {tf} closeN={len(closed_tf)} openN={len(open_tf)}")

def main():
    for tf in TFS: (CAND/tf).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    sym = SYMBOL
    backfill(sym)
    while True:
        t0=time.time()
        follow_once(sym)
        time.sleep(max(1, 60-(time.time()-t0)))

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

Size: 1484
MTime: 2025-09-27 14:39:54.816781396 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, json
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
CAND = DATA/"candles"

# TF requis pour A
REQ = ("5m","15m","30m")

def jload(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def load_tf(sym,tf):
    f=CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    rows=jload(f,[])
    if not rows:
        # au lieu de ValueError → retourne []
        sys.stderr.write(f"[A] WARN: empty {f}, fallback ctx=none\n")
        return []
    return rows

def indicators_from_ohlcv(rows):
    if not rows: return {}
    closes=[float(r[4]) for r in rows if len(r)>=5]
    if not closes: return {}
    ma= sum(closes[-20:])/min(20,len(closes))
    last= closes[-1]
    return {"ma20":ma,"last":last}

def main():
    if len(sys.argv)<2:
        print("usage: run_analysis_a_coin.py SYMBOL"); return 1
    sym=sys.argv[1]
    per_tf_inputs={tf: indicators_from_ohlcv(load_tf(sym,tf)) for tf in REQ}
    # si aucun TF dispo → ctx=none
    if not any(per_tf_inputs.values()):
        out={"symbol":sym,"ctx":"none","reason":"A-empty"}
    else:
        ctx="buy" if per_tf_inputs["5m"].get("last",0)>per_tf_inputs["5m"].get("ma20",0) else "sell"
        out={"symbol":sym,"ctx":ctx,"reason":"ma20 rule"}
    fout=DATA/"analysis_a"/f"{sym}.json"
    fout.parent.mkdir(parents=True,exist_ok=True)
    fout.write_text(json.dumps(out))
    print(json.dumps(out))
    return 0

if __name__=="__main__":
    sys.exit(main())

# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from typing import Dict, Any

# Seuils en "dixièmes" (alignés avec pb_i, pH_i, ps_i = int(10*proba))
PB_ENTER = 7   # >=0.70
PS_ENTER = 7
PB_EXIT  = 4   # <=0.40
PS_EXIT  = 4

# Garde ATR% 5m
ATR5_MIN = 0.10   # %
ATR5_MAX = 3.00   # %

COOLDOWN_BARS = 2  # 2 bougies 5m

@dataclass
class PosState:
    pos: str = "flat"        # flat|long|short
    cooldown: int = 0
    last_ctx: str = "none"

def _ok_atr5(atrp5: float) -> bool:
    try:
        a = float(atrp5)
    except:
        return False
    return (ATR5_MIN <= a <= ATR5_MAX)

def decide_signal(a_rec: Dict[str,Any], feats: Dict[str,Any], state: PosState):
    """
    a_rec: ligne issue de analyse_A (keys: S, pb_i, pH_i, ps_i, context, reason)
    feats: dict avec 'atrp5' (ATR% 5m)
    state: PosState persistant
    Return: dict(side, action, strength, reason, new_state)
    """
    ctx = (a_rec.get("context") or "none")
    pb_i = int(a_rec.get("pb_i", 0))
    ph_i = int(a_rec.get("pH_i", 0))
    ps_i = int(a_rec.get("ps_i", 0))
    atr_ok = _ok_atr5(feats.get("atrp5", 0.0))

    # Cooldown
    if state.cooldown > 0:
        ns = PosState(pos="flat", cooldown=state.cooldown-1, last_ctx=ctx)
        return dict(side="none", action="cooldown", strength=0,
                    reason=f"cooldown={state.cooldown}", new_state=ns)

    # Entrées
    if state.pos == "flat" and atr_ok:
        if ctx == "buy"  and pb_i >= PB_ENTER:
            ns = PosState(pos="long", cooldown=0, last_ctx=ctx)
            return dict(side="buy", action="enter_long", strength=pb_i,
                        reason=f"ctx=buy pb_i={pb_i} atr5={feats.get('atrp5'):.3f}%", new_state=ns)
        if ctx == "sell" and ps_i >= PS_ENTER:
            ns = PosState(pos="short", cooldown=0, last_ctx=ctx)
            return dict(side="sell", action="enter_short", strength=ps_i,
                        reason=f"ctx=sell ps_i={ps_i} atr5={feats.get('atrp5'):.3f}%", new_state=ns)

    # Sorties
    if state.pos == "long":
        if (ctx != "buy") or (pb_i <= PB_EXIT) or (ps_i >= PS_ENTER):
            ns = PosState(pos="flat", cooldown=COOLDOWN_BARS, last_ctx=ctx)
            return dict(side="sell", action="exit_long", strength=max(10-ps_i, 1),
                        reason=f"exit_long ctx={ctx} pb_i={pb_i} ps_i={ps_i}", new_state=ns)
        return dict(side="none", action="hold_long", strength=pb_i,
                    reason=f"hold_long ctx={ctx} pb_i={pb_i}", new_state=state)

    if state.pos == "short":
        if (ctx != "sell") or (ps_i <= PS_EXIT) or (pb_i >= PB_ENTER):
            ns = PosState(pos="flat", cooldown=COOLDOWN_BARS, last_ctx=ctx)
            return dict(side="buy", action="exit_short", strength=max(10-pb_i, 1),
                        reason=f"exit_short ctx={ctx} ps_i={ps_i} pb_i={pb_i}", new_state=ns)
        return dict(side="none", action="hold_short", strength=ps_i,
                    reason=f"hold_short ctx={ctx} ps_i={ps_i}", new_state=state)

    # Flat par défaut
    return dict(side="none", action="idle", strength=0,
                reason=f"no-entry atr_ok={atr_ok} ctx={ctx} pb_i={pb_i} ps_i={ps_i}",
                new_state=PosState(pos="flat", cooldown=0, last_ctx=ctx))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import os, json, asyncio
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
RUN  = Path("/opt/scalp/tools/b_run_coin.py")

WORKERS = int(os.getenv("B_WORKERS", "12"))
TIMEOUT = int(os.getenv("B_TIMEOUT_S", "90"))

def jload(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

async def run_one(sym, sem):
    async with sem:
        try:
            p = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
                "python3", str(RUN), sym,
                stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE, stderr=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL
            )
            await asyncio.wait_for(p.wait(), timeout=TIMEOUT)
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            try: p.kill()
            except: pass

async def main():
    top=jload(TOP,{}) or {}
    syms=[s for s in (top.get("symbols") or [])][:30]
    if not syms: 
        print("[b] no symbols"); return
    sem=asyncio.Semaphore(WORKERS)
    await asyncio.gather(*[run_one(s, sem) for s in syms])
    print(f"[b] done symbols={len(syms)}")

if __name__=="__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, sys, time, subprocess, shutil
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
RANK = DATA/"top_ranked.json"
SIGS = DATA/"signals.json"
POS  = DATA/"positions.json"
AOUT = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
LOG  = Path("/opt/scalp/logs/top_rebuild.log")
SERVICE="scalp-top-lite.service"
TIMER="scalp-top-lite.timer"

def jload(p, d=None):
    try:
        return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception:
        return d

def age_sec(iso):
    try:
        dt = datetime.fromisoformat(iso.replace("Z","+00:00"))
        return max(0, (datetime.now(timezone.utc)-dt).total_seconds())
    except Exception:
        return 9e9

def box(ok=None):  # None -> pending
    return "✅" if ok is True else ("❌" if ok is False else "⏳")

def is_active(unit):
    try:
        r = subprocess.run(["systemctl","is-active","--quiet",unit])
        return r.returncode==0
    except Exception:
        return False

def short(txt, n=80):
    s=str(txt or "")
    return s if len(s)<=n else s[:n-1]+"…"

def pick_best_worst(rank_items, k=2):
    if not rank_items: return [], []
    items = sorted(rank_items, key=lambda x: float(x.get("score",0.0)), reverse=True)
    best = items[:k]
    worst = items[-k:][::-1]
    return best, worst

def get_metrics_for(sym):
    flat = sym
    # from analyse_A_out.json -> { "BTCUSDT": {"pb":..,"pH":..,"ps":..,"context":..,"reason":..}, ...}
    a = jload(AOUT, {})
    m = a.get(flat) or {}
    # fallback from signals.json last matching
    if not m and SIGS.exists():
        sj = jload(SIGS, [])
        for it in reversed(sj if isinstance(sj,list) else sj.get("items",[])):
            if (it.get("symbol") or it.get("sym") or "").replace("/","").replace(":","")==flat:
                m = {k:it.get(k) for k in ("pb","pH","ps","context","reason")}
                break
    # coercion
    def f(x): 
        try: return float(x)
        except: return 0.0
    pb, pH, ps = f(m.get("pb")), f(m.get("pH")), f(m.get("ps"))
    ctx = m.get("context") or m.get("ctx") or ""
    reason = m.get("reason") or m.get("why") or ""
    return pb, pH, ps, ctx, reason

def main():
    top = jload(TOP, {})
    rank = jload(RANK, {})
    symbols = top.get("symbols") or []
    items = rank.get("items") or []
    gen = top.get("generated_at")
    fresh_ok = gen is not None and age_sec(gen) <= 3*3600 and len(symbols)>=5
    svc_ok = is_active(SERVICE)
    tmr_ok = is_active(TIMER)

    # sections
    print("=== Services ===")
    print(f"{box(tmr_ok)} timer: {TIMER}")
    print(f"{box(svc_ok)} service: {SERVICE}\n")

    print("=== Top30 ===")
    src = top.get("source") or "?"
    print(f"{box(fresh_ok)} ts={gen or 'n/a'}  src={src}  N={len(symbols)}")
    # aperçu top 10
    for i,it in enumerate(items[:10],1):
        s = it.get("symbol","?")
        sc = it.get("score",0.0)
        d = int(float(it.get("depth_quote_band",0))/1000)
        print(f"{i:02d}. {s:>10}  S={sc:0.4f}  depth≈{d}k")
    print()

    # Analyses: BTC, ETH + 2 best/2 worst
    best, worst = pick_best_worst(items, 2)
    focus = []
    for sym in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT"):
        if sym in [it.get("symbol") for it in items] or sym in symbols:
            focus.append({"symbol": sym, "score": next((it.get('score') for it in items if it.get('symbol')==sym), 1.0)})
    focus += best + worst
    # de-dup en gardant ordre
    seen=set(); f2=[]
    for it in focus:
        sym = it.get("symbol","")
        if sym and sym not in seen:
            seen.add(sym); f2.append(it)

    print("=== Analyses (BTC, ETH, 2 best, 2 worst) ===")
    if not f2:
        print(f"{box(False)} aucune donnée d'analyse")
    else:
        for it in f2:
            s = it.get("symbol")
            sc = float(it.get("score",0.0))
            pb,pH,ps,ctx,why = get_metrics_for(s)
            P = int(10*pb); H = int(10*pH); S = int(10*ps)
            print(f"{box(True)} {s:>10}  S={sc:0.4f}  pb={P} pH={H} ps={S}  ctx={short(ctx,40)}  reason={short(why,60)}")
    print()

    # Données nécessaires / inputs
    need_ok = TOP.exists() and RANK.exists()
    print("=== Inputs ===")
    print(f"{box(TOP.exists())} {TOP}")
    print(f"{box(RANK.exists())} {RANK}")
    print(f"{box(SIGS.exists())} {SIGS}")
    print(f"{box(POS.exists())} {POS}")
    print(f"{box(LOG.exists())} {LOG}")
    print()

    # Derniers 5 signaux
    print("=== 5 derniers signaux ===")
    sj = jload(SIGS, [])
    sigs = sj if isinstance(sj,list) else sj.get("items",[])
    # heuristique d'ordre par timestamp/ts
    def ts_of(x):
        for k in ("ts","timestamp","time","at"): 
            if k in x: 
                try: return float(x[k])
                except: pass
        return 0.0
    sigs = sorted(sigs, key=ts_of, reverse=True)[:5]
    if not sigs:
        print("⏳ aucun")
    else:
        for it in sigs:
            sym = (it.get("symbol") or it.get("sym") or "").replace("/","").replace(":","")
            side = (it.get("side") or it.get("action") or "?").upper()
            px = it.get("price") or it.get("px") or 0
            print(f"• {sym:>10}  {side:>4}  @ {px}")
    print()

    # Positions / historique bref
    print("=== Positions / historique bref ===")
    pj = jload(POS, {})
    poss = pj.get("positions") or pj.get("open") or []
    if poss:
        for it in poss[:5]:
            sym = (it.get("symbol") or "").replace("/","").replace(":","")
            side = it.get("side") or it.get("direction") or "?"
            sz = it.get("size") or it.get("qty") or 0
            upnl = it.get("unrealizedPnl") or it.get("uPnL") or 0
            print(f"• {sym:>10} {side:>4} sz={sz} uPnL={upnl}")
    else:
        print("⏳ aucune position détectée")
    print()

    # Résumé final
    all_ok = fresh_ok and svc_ok and need_ok
    print(f"=== Résultat global: {box(all_ok)} ===")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math
from pathlib import Path

BASE = Path(os.environ.get("DATA", "/opt/scalp/data")) / "candles" / "1m"

def is_num(x):
    try: float(x); return True
    except: return False

def fix_row(row):
    # attend [ts, o, h, l, c, v] au minimum [ts,o,h,l,c]
    if not isinstance(row, list): return None
    if len(row) < 5: return None
    ts, o, h, l, c = row[:5]
    if not (is_num(ts) and is_num(o) and is_num(h) and is_num(l) and is_num(c)):
        return None
    v = float(row[5]) if len(row) > 5 and is_num(row[5]) else 0.0
    return [int(float(ts)), float(o), float(h), float(l), float(c), v]

def load_json(p):
    try:
        with open(p) as f: return json.load(f)
    except: return None

def save_json(p, data):
    tmp = p.with_suffix(p.suffix + ".tmp")
    with open(tmp, "w") as f: json.dump(data, f, separators=(",",":"))
    os.replace(tmp, p)

def clean_file(path: Path):
    data = load_json(path)
    out = []
    if isinstance(data, list):
        # certains fichiers ont plusieurs lignes -> ne garder que la DERNIÈRE valide
        for row in (data[-10:]):  # limite parsing
            fr = fix_row(row)
            if fr: out.append(fr)
        out = out[-1:]  # au plus 1 ligne
    elif isinstance(data, dict) or data is None:
        out = []
    else:
        out = []
    save_json(path, out)
    return len(out)

def main():
    base = BASE
    if not base.exists():
        print(f"[ERR] base not found: {base}")
        return 1
    files = sorted(base.glob("*.open.json"))
    if not files:
        print(f"[INFO] no *.open.json in {base}")
        return 0
    ok=0
    for f in files:
        n = clean_file(f)
        ok += 1
        print(f"[OK] {f.name:<20} rows_kept={n}")
    print(f"[DONE] cleaned {ok} files in {base}")
    return 0

if __name__=="__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3
from pathlib import Path
import json, time, sys, math, datetime as dt

D = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP = D/"top.json"                      # liste des symbols
CAND = D/"candles"

# TFs à inspecter (mins)
TFS = [1,5,15,30]

def read_top():
    p = TOP
    if not p.exists():
        print("ERR: top.json introuvable", file=sys.stderr); return []
    try:
        j = json.loads(p.read_text())
        syms = j.get("symbols") or j.get("items") or []
        # items peut être dicts {'symbol': 'BTCUSDT'}
        if syms and isinstance(syms[0], dict):
            syms = [x.get("symbol") for x in syms if x.get("symbol")]
        return syms
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"ERR top.json: {e}", file=sys.stderr); return []

def load_last(sym, tfm):
    """
    essaie plusieurs chemins:
    - /candles/SYM/TF/last.json
    - /candles/TF/SYM.json
    - /candles/SYM/TF.json
    retourne (ts_ms, close) ou (None, None)
    """
    tf = f"{tfm}m"
    candidates = [
        CAND/sym/tf/"last.json",
        CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json",
        CAND/sym/f"{tf}.json",
    ]
    for p in candidates:
        if p.exists():
            try:
                j = json.loads(p.read_text())
                # format attendu: liste de bougies [t,o,h,l,c,v]
                if isinstance(j, list) and j and isinstance(j[-1], list):
                    t, *_rest, c = j[-1][0], *j[-1][1:-1], j[-1][-2]
                    return int(t), float(c)
                # ou objet {"data": [...]} 
                if isinstance(j, dict) and "data" in j and j["data"]:
                    row = j["data"][-1]
                    t, c = int(row[0]), float(row[4])
                    return t, c
            except Exception:
                pass
    return None, None

def fmt_age(s):
    m, s = divmod(int(s), 60)
    h, m = divmod(m, 60)
    if h: return f"{h}h{m:02d}m"
    if m: return f"{m}m{s:02d}s"
    return f"{s}s"

def due_status(now, last_ts_ms, tfm):
    tf_sec = tfm*60
    # "due" quand la bougie (close) est attendue au prochain multiple de tf
    # et que l'âge dépasse ~90% du tf (proche clôture)
    if last_ts_ms is None: return "MISSING"
    last_close_sec = last_ts_ms//1000
    age = now - last_close_sec
    nxt = (last_close_sec//tf_sec + 1)*tf_sec
    secs_to_next = max(0, nxt - now)
    # statut
    if age < tf_sec*0.1:
        return f"fresh -{fmt_age(tf_sec-age)}"
    # align info “not due / due soon”
    tag = "due" if secs_to_next==0 else "not_due"
    return f"{tag} T-{secs_to_next}s"

def main():
    syms = read_top()
    if not syms:
        print("Aucun symbole dans top.json"); return
    now = int(time.time())
    print("== TF LOAD VISU ==")
    print("ts_now:", dt.datetime.utcfromtimestamp(now).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%SZ"))
    print(f"symbols={len(syms)}   tfs={TFS}\n")
    header = f"{'coin':10} {'tf':>4} {'last(UTC)':>19} {'age':>8} {'status':>12} {'close':>12}"
    print(header)
    print("-"*len(header))
    miss=0
    for sym in syms:
        for tfm in TFS:
            ts_ms, close = load_last(sym, tfm)
            if ts_ms is None:
                miss+=1
                print(f"{sym:10} {tfm:>4} {'-':>19} {'-':>8} {'MISSING':>12} {'-':>12}")
                continue
            last = ts_ms//1000
            age = now - last
            status = due_status(now, ts_ms, tfm)
            iso = dt.datetime.utcfromtimestamp(last).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
            print(f"{sym:10} {tfm:>4} {iso:>19} {fmt_age(age):>8} {status:>12} {close:12.6f}")
    print("\nMISSING files:", miss)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

MTime: 2025-09-27 14:20:50.983396745 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time
from pathlib import Path
from lib.atomic_json import jload, jdump

DATA   = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
SYM    = os.environ.get("SYMBOL","BTCUSDT")

BASE_C = DATA/"candles"/"1m"/f"{SYM}.json"
BASE_O = DATA/"candles"/"1m"/f"{SYM}.open.json"

TFS = {"3m":3,"5m":5,"15m":15,"30m":30}

KEEP = int(os.environ.get("KEEP","1500"))
def trim(a): return (a or [])[-KEEP:]

def bkt(ts, m): return ts - (ts % (60000*m))

def compose(rows):
    # rows: liste 1m sur un bucket
    if not rows: return None
    ts = bkt(rows[0][0], max(1, (rows[-1][0]-rows[0][0])//60000 + 1))
    o = rows[0][1]
    h = max(r[2] for r in rows)
    l = min(r[3] for r in rows)
    c = rows[-1][4]
    v = sum(r[5] for r in rows)
    return [ts, o, h, l, c, v]

def resample_tf(mult, base_closed, open1):
    now = int(time.time()*1000)
    cur1 = now - (now % 60000)
    last_closed_boundary = bkt(cur1, mult) - (60000*mult)

    # CLOSED strict par bucket
    part_closed = [r for r in base_closed if bkt(r[0], mult) <= last_closed_boundary]

    # Candidats pour l'OPEN courant
    bucket_start = bkt(cur1, mult)
    candidates = [r for r in base_closed if r[0] >= bucket_start]
    if open1: candidates += open1

    # Agrège CLOSED
    buckets={}
    for r in part_closed:
        buckets.setdefault(bkt(r[0], mult), []).append(r)
    out_closed=[]
    for tsB in sorted(buckets):
        if tsB <= last_closed_boundary:
            row = compose(sorted(buckets[tsB], key=lambda x:x[0]))
            if row: out_closed.append(row)

    # Agrège OPEN
    out_open=[]
    if candidates:
        rows = sorted(candidates, key=lambda x:x[0])
        row = compose(rows)
        if row: out_open=[row]

    return out_closed, out_open

def main():
    # boucle continue
    while True:
        base = jload(BASE_C, [])
        open1 = jload(BASE_O, [])
        for tf, mult in TFS.items():
            closed, open_c = resample_tf(mult, base, open1)
            fC = DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{SYM}.json"
            fO = DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{SYM}.open.json"
            curC = jload(fC, [])
            if closed and (not curC or closed[-1][0] > (curC[-1][0] if curC else -1) or len(closed)>len(curC)):
                jdump(fC, trim(closed))
            jdump(fO, trim(open_c))
        time.sleep(1.5)

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

Size: 2667
MTime: 2025-09-27 16:14:40.671834918 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
C1   = DATA/"candles"/"1m"

# Seuils
CLOSE_MAX_AGE_S = int(os.environ.get("CLOSE_MAX_AGE_S","180"))   # 3 min
OPEN_MAX_AGE_MS = int(os.environ.get("OPEN_MAX_AGE_MS","20000")) # 20 s
LIMIT = int(os.environ.get("TOP_LIMIT","30"))

def now_ms(): return int(time.time()*1000)

def jload(p, d):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d

def last_ts(rows):
    if not isinstance(rows,list) or not rows: return None
    r = rows[-1]
    if isinstance(r,list) and len(r)>=1:
        try: return int(float(r[0]))
        except: return None
    return None

def age_s(ts_ms):
    if ts_ms is None: return None
    return max(0, (now_ms()-int(ts_ms))//1000)

def check_sym(sym:str):
    fc = C1/f"{sym}.json"
    fo = C1/f"{sym}.open.json"
    rows_c = jload(fc, [])
    rows_o = jload(fo, [])
    ts_c = last_ts(rows_c)
    ts_o = last_ts(rows_o)
    a_c  = age_s(ts_c)
    a_o  = None if ts_o is None else (now_ms()-ts_o)
    # Statut
    if ts_c is None and ts_o is None:
        status = "MISSING"
    elif ts_c is not None and a_c <= CLOSE_MAX_AGE_S:
        status = "OK"
    elif ts_o is not None and a_o <= OPEN_MAX_AGE_MS:
        status = "OK(open)"
    else:
        status = "STALE"
    return {
        "sym": sym,
        "close_age_s": a_c,
        "open_age_ms": a_o,
        "status": status,
        "have_close": int(ts_c is not None),
        "have_open":  int(ts_o is not None),
    }

def fmt(v, none="-"):
    return str(v) if v is not None else none

def main():
    top = jload(TOP, {})
    syms = (top.get("symbols") or [])[:LIMIT]
    if not syms:
        print("no symbols in top.json"); return 1
    rows=[check_sym(s) for s in syms]
    ok=sum(1 for r in rows if r["status"].startswith("OK"))
    stale=sum(1 for r in rows if r["status"]=="STALE")
    miss=sum(1 for r in rows if r["status"]=="MISSING")
    print(f"== FRESHNESS TOP{len(rows)} ==")
    print(f"thresholds: CLOSE_MAX_AGE_S={CLOSE_MAX_AGE_S} OPEN_MAX_AGE_MS={OPEN_MAX_AGE_MS}")
    print("sym         close  open   have  status")
    print("            age_s  age_ms close/open")
    print("-------------------------------------------")
    for r in rows:
        print(f"{r['sym']:<11} {fmt(r['close_age_s']):>6}  {fmt(r['open_age_ms']):>7}   {r['have_close']}/{r['have_open']}   {r['status']}")
    print("-------------------------------------------")
    print(f"OK={ok}  STALE={stale}  MISSING={miss}")
    return 0 if stale==0 and miss==0 else 2

if __name__=="__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
: "${DATA:=/opt/scalp/data_test}"
: "${SYMBOL:=BTCUSDT}"
: "${LOOKBACK:=-300}"
: "${TOL_PCT:=0.002}"
: "${TOL_VOL_P:=0.05}"
: "${CHECK_EVERY_S:=60}"       # cadence sanity
: "${BF_ON_MISM:=1}"           # 1=backfill auto si mismatch>0

mkdir -p "$DATA/logs"

# 1) start WS + resampler
bash /opt/scalp/tools/ws/ws_start.sh || true

while true; do
  # 2) sanity check
  DATA="$DATA" SYMBOL="$SYMBOL" LOOKBACK="$LOOKBACK" TOL_PCT="$TOL_PCT" TOL_VOL_P="$TOL_VOL_P" \
    python3 -u /opt/scalp/tools/sanity/sanity_check_ccxt.py \
    > "$DATA/logs/sanity_last.json" 2>/dev/null || true

  # 3) décision et éventuel backfill
  mism_total=$(jq '[.per_tf[].mismatchN]|add' "$DATA/logs/sanity_last.json" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
  if [ "${mism_total:-0}" -gt 0 ] && [ "$BF_ON_MISM" = "1" ]; then
    # backfill ciblé: ne recharge que les TF en écart
    tfs=$(jq -r '.per_tf[] | select(.mismatchN>0)|.tf' "$DATA/logs/sanity_last.json")
    if [ -n "$tfs" ]; then
      list=$(echo "$tfs" | paste -sd, -)
      DATA="$DATA" SYMBOL="$SYMBOL" TFS="$list" python3 -u /opt/scalp/tools/backfill/backfill_ccxt.py \
        >> "$DATA/logs/orchestrator.log" 2>&1 || true
    fi
  fi

  # 4) status JSON pour le bot
  DATA="$DATA" SYMBOL="$SYMBOL" python3 -u /opt/scalp/tools/lib/status_writer.py \
    > "$DATA/status/${SYMBOL}_status.json" 2>/dev/null || true

  # 5) log court
  ts=$(date -u +%FT%TZ)
  echo "[$ts] mism_total=${mism_total:-0}" >> "$DATA/logs/orchestrator.log"

  sleep "$CHECK_EVERY_S"
done

Size: 1286
MTime: 2025-09-27 16:57:57.451107183 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
C1   = DATA/"candles"/"1m"
TFS  = {"3m":3,"5m":5,"15m":15,"30m":30}

def jload(p,d):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d
def jsave(p, rows):
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(rows, separators=(",",":")))

def roll(rows, n):
    out=[]
    buckets={}
    for r in rows:
        ts=int(r[0]); o,h,l,c = map(float, r[1:5])
        v = float(r[5]) if len(r)>5 else 0.0
        k = ts - (ts % (60000*n))
        b = buckets.get(k)
        if not b:
            buckets[k] = [k, o, h, l, c, v]
        else:
            b[2] = max(b[2], h)
            b[3] = min(b[3], l)
            b[4] = c
            b[5] += v
    for k in sorted(buckets):
        out.append(buckets[k])
    return out

def main():
    syms = (jload(TOP, {}).get("symbols") or [])[:int(os.environ.get("TOP_LIMIT","50"))]
    for s in syms:
        rows1 = jload(C1/f"{s}.json", [])
        if not rows1: continue
        for tf, n in TFS.items():
            dst = DATA/"candles"/tf/f"{s}.json"
            jsave(dst, roll(rows1, n))
    print("[rollup] done")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3

    S=float(j.get("S") or 0)

from collections import Counter

print("A files:", tot, " | ", " ".join(f"{k}={cnt.get(k,0)}" for k in ("buy","sell","hold","none")))
rows.sort(key=lambda x:x[1], reverse=True)

print("\nNON-NONE:")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os, time
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path(os.environ.get("DATA","/opt/scalp/data"))
C1=DATA/"candles"/"1m"
def j(p,d): 
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return d
def age_ms(ts): return int(time.time()*1000)-int(ts)
def info(sym):
    c=j(C1/f"{sym}.json",[])
    o=j(C1/f"{sym}.open.json",[])
    c_ok=len(c)>0
    o_ok=len(o)>0
    a=age_ms(o[-1][0]) if o_ok else None
    return {"sym":sym,"close":c_ok,"open":o_ok,"open_age_ms":a}

bad=[info(s) for s in syms]
bad.sort(key=lambda x:(not x["close"], not x["open"]))

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

BASE="/opt/scalp/data/candles"
# TF autorisés
TF=(1m 3m 5m 10m 15m 30m)

echo "[1/4] Vérif dossiers TF"
mkdir -p "$BASE"
for t in "${TF[@]}"; do
  mkdir -p "$BASE/$t"
done

echo "[2/4] Suppression de tous les JSON (y compris noms corrompus avec retours à la ligne)"
# -print0 gère les noms bizarres, xargs -0 supprime sans erreur
find "$BASE" -type f -name '*.json' -print0 | xargs -0r rm -f --

echo "[3/4] Suppression des dossiers au niveau racine qui ne sont pas des TF"
# liste blanche -> tout le reste est supprimé
shopt -s nullglob
for d in "$BASE"/*/; do
  name="$(basename "$d")"
  keep=0
  for t in "${TF[@]}"; do
    [[ "$name" == "$t" ]] && keep=1 && break
  done
  if [[ $keep -eq 0 ]]; then
    echo "  - rm -rf $d"
    rm -rf -- "$d"
  fi
done
shopt -u nullglob

echo "[4/4] Nettoyage des sous-dossiers vides restants"
find "$BASE" -type d -empty -mindepth 1 -delete

echo "OK. Structure cible à utiliser: $BASE/<TF>/<COIN>.json"
printf 'TF présents: '; ls -1 "$BASE" | paste -sd',' -
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA=/opt/scalp/data; TOOLS=/opt/scalp/tools
mkdir -p "$DATA"/{candles,logs}

mapfile -t SYMS < <(jq -r '.symbols[]' "$DATA/top.json")
((${#SYMS[@]})) || { echo "[quick] top.json vide"; exit 1; }

python3 "$TOOLS/ohlcv_refresh.py" --tfs 1m,5m,15m,30m --symbols "$(IFS=,; echo "${SYMS[*]}")"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
: "${DATA:=/opt/scalp/data}"
: "${TOP_LIMIT:=30}"
: "${OPEN_MAX_AGE_MS:=20000}"   # 20s
: "${CLOSE_MAX_AGE_S:=180}"     # 3min
: "${WS:=/opt/scalp/tools/ws_candle_futures_writer.py}"

jq -r '.symbols[]' "$DATA/top.json" | head -n "$TOP_LIMIT" | while read -r sym; do
  [ -n "$sym" ] || continue
  fo="$DATA/candles/1m/${sym}.open.json"
  fc="$DATA/candles/1m/${sym}.json"
  now=$(date +%s%3N)

  # ages
  ts_o=$(jq -r '.[-1][0] // empty' "$fo" 2>/dev/null || true)
  ts_c=$(jq -r '.[-1][0] // empty' "$fc" 2>/dev/null || true)
  age_o=$([ -n "$ts_o" ] && echo $((now-ts_o)) || echo -1)
  age_c_s=$([ -n "$ts_c" ] && echo $(( (now-ts_c)/1000 )) || echo -1)

  need=0
  if [ "$ts_o" = "" ] && [ "$ts_c" = "" ]; then need=1; fi
  if [ "$age_o" -ge 0 ] && [ "$age_o" -gt "$OPEN_MAX_AGE_MS" ]; then need=1; fi
  if [ "$age_c_s" -ge 0 ] && [ "$age_c_s" -gt "$CLOSE_MAX_AGE_S" ]; then need=1; fi

  if [ "$need" = "1" ]; then
    pkill -f "ws_candle_futures_writer.py.*$sym" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    nohup /opt/scalp/tools/ws_run_symbol.sh "$sym" >/dev/null 2>&1 &
    echo "[wd] restart $sym  o_age_ms=${age_o} c_age_s=${age_c_s}"
  else
    echo "[wd] ok      $sym  o_age_ms=${age_o} c_age_s=${age_c_s}"
  fi
done

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, json, asyncio
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP  = DATA/"top.json"
A_CMD = "python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_coin.py {sym}"
B_CMD = "python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_coin.py {sym}"
LIMIT = int(os.environ.get("LIMIT","600"))

# --- planification TF dues en fonction de l'horloge UTC ---
def due_tfs():
    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
    m = now.minute
    return {"1m":True, "3m":(m%3==0), "5m":(m%5==0), "15m":(m%15==0), "30m":(m%30==0)}

# --- fetch OHLCV pour un symbole et une TF ---
async def fetch_tf(sym:str, tf:str):
    from subprocess import run
    try:
        # SUPPRESSION de --limit (erreur argparse observée)
        cmd = ["python3","/opt/scalp/tools/ohlcv_refresh_one.py","--sym",sym,"--tf",tf]
        r = run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
        if r.returncode==0:
            print(f"[OK] {sym} {tf}")
        else:
            sys.stderr.write(f"[ERR] {sym} {tf} {r.returncode} {r.stderr.strip()}\n")
    except FileNotFoundError:
        print(f"[SKIP-FETCH] no fetcher for {sym} {tf}")

# --- pipeline A puis B pour un symbole ---
async def run_sym(sym:str, tfdue:dict):
    tasks=[]
    for tf in ("5m","15m","30m"):
        if tfdue.get(tf, False):
            tasks.append(fetch_tf(sym, tf))
    if tasks: await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
    os.system(A_CMD.format(sym=sym))
    os.system(B_CMD.format(sym=sym))

async def main():
    tfdue = due_tfs()
    print(f"=== fetch_A_then_B @ {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ')}  due: 5m={int(tfdue['5m'])} 15m={int(tfdue['15m'])} 30m={int(tfdue['30m'])} ===")
    top = json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    symbols = top.get("symbols", [])
    sem = asyncio.Semaphore(int(os.environ.get("MAX_PAR", "6")))
    async def guard(s):
        async with sem: await run_sym(s, tfdue)
    await asyncio.gather(*(guard(s) for s in symbols))
if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA=${DATA:-/opt/scalp/data}
PAPER="$DATA/paper"
BRDBG="$DATA/debug/bridge"
TS=$(date -u +%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ)
CASH=${PAPER_BUDGET:-200.0}

mkdir -p "$PAPER" "$BRDBG" "$DATA/signals_coin"

# backups si présents
for f in "$DATA/signals.json" "$PAPER/positions.json" "$PAPER/balance.json"; do
  [[ -s "${f:-}" ]] && cp -a "$f" "$f.bak.$TS" || true
done

# reset des états
printf '[]\n' > "$DATA/signals.json"
printf '[]\n' > "$PAPER/positions.json"
printf '{ "cash": %.2f }\n' "$CASH" > "$PAPER/balance.json"
: > "$PAPER/cooldown.json" 2>/dev/null || true

# purge debug/anciennes sorties
rm -f "$BRDBG"/*.log 2>/dev/null || true
rm -f "$DATA/signals_coin"/*.json 2>/dev/null || true

# sanity rapide (sans jq requis)
echo "[reset] OK  -> cash=$(sed -n 's/.*"cash":[[:space:]]*\([0-9.]\+\).*/\1/p' "$PAPER/balance.json")"
echo "signals=$(wc -c <"$DATA/signals.json") bytes, positions=$(wc -c <"$PAPER/positions.json") bytes"
