Path: /opt/scalp/tools/b_logic.py
Size: 14332
MTime: 2025-09-26 13:10:17.394334539 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Analyse B durcie : pré-filtres 1m, triggers PB/BO/MR, anti-bruit, sizing, sécurité.
# Entrées:
#   - OHLCV 1m/3m/5m : /opt/scalp/data/candles/<tf>/<SYMBOL>.json
#   - Contexte A      : /opt/scalp/data/analyse_A_out.json
#   - Règles paires   : /opt/scalp/data/contracts_usdt.json  (min_notional, lot_step …) [optionnel]
# Sorties:
#   - /opt/scalp/data/analyse_B_out.json
#   - append -> /opt/scalp/data/signals.json

import json, math, time, statistics
from pathlib import Path

DATA   = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND   = DATA/"candles"
STATE  = DATA/"state"; STATE.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
SIGF   = DATA/"signals.json"
AOUT   = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
BOUT   = DATA/"analyse_B_out.json"
PAIRDB = DATA/"contracts_usdt.json"   # {symbol: {minNotional, lotStep, ...}}
CFGSTR = Path("/etc/scalp.strategy")

# ---------- Utils IO ----------
def jload(p, d=None):
    p=Path(p)
    if not p.exists(): return d
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except: return d

def jappend(p, item):
    arr = jload(p, [])
    arr.append(item)
    Path(p).write_text(json.dumps(arr, ensure_ascii=False))

def jsave(p, obj):
    p=Path(p); p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False))

def last_complete(arr, tf_s):
    if not arr: return []
    now = __import__('time').time()*1000
    # si la dernière bougie n'est pas close on l'enlève
    if now - arr[-1][0] < tf_s*1000:
        return arr[:-1]
    return arr[:-1] if (now - arr[-1][0] < tf_s*1000) else arr

def close(a): return [x[4] for x in a]
def high(a):  return [x[2] for x in a]
def low(a):   return [x[3] for x in a]
def vol(a):   return [x[5] for x in a]
def tp(a):    return [(x[2]+x[3]+x[4])/3 for x in a]

# ---------- Indicators ----------
def ema(vals, n):
    k=2/(n+1); out=[]; e=None
    for v in vals:
        e = v if e is None else (v - e)*k + e
        out.append(e)
    return out

def rsi(vals, n=14):
    if len(vals)<n+1: return [50.0]*len(vals)
    gains=[0.0]; losses=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(vals)):
        d=vals[i]-vals[i-1]
        gains.append(max(d,0)); losses.append(max(-d,0))
    avg_gain=sum(gains[1:n+1])/n; avg_loss=sum(losses[1:n+1])/n
    rsis=[50.0]*(n)
    for i in range(n+1,len(vals)+1):
        avg_gain=(avg_gain*(n-1)+gains[i-1])/n
        avg_loss=(avg_loss*(n-1)+losses[i-1])/n
        rs= (avg_gain/avg_loss) if avg_loss>0 else 0
        r=100-(100/(1+rs)) if avg_loss>0 else 100
        rsis.append(r)
    return rsis

def true_range(h,l,c_prev): return max(h-l, abs(h-c_prev), abs(l-c_prev))
def atr(hs, ls, cs, n=14):
    trs=[]
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        if i==0: trs.append(hs[i]-ls[i])
        else: trs.append(true_range(hs[i], ls[i], cs[i-1]))
    out=[]; a=None; k=2/(n+1)
    for tr in trs:
        a = tr if a is None else (tr-a)*k + a
        out.append(a)
    return out

def adx(hs, ls, cs, n=14):
    if len(cs)<n+1: return [20.0]*len(cs)
    pdm=[0.0]; ndm=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cs)):
        up=hs[i]-hs[i-1]; dn=ls[i-1]-ls[i]
        pdm.append(up if (up>dn and up>0) else 0.0)
        ndm.append(dn if (dn>up and dn>0) else 0.0)
    tr = []
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        if i==0: tr.append(hs[i]-ls[i])
        else: tr.append(true_range(hs[i], ls[i], cs[i-1]))
    def rma(x,n):
        k=1/n; out=[]; a=None
        for v in x:
            a = v if a is None else a + k*(v-a)
            out.append(a)
        return out
    atrv=rma(tr,n); pdi=[0.0]*len(cs); ndi=[0.0]*len(cs)
    p=rma(pdm,n); n_=rma(ndm,n)
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        if atrv[i]>0:
            pdi[i]=100*p[i]/atrv[i]; ndi[i]=100*n_[i]/atrv[i]
    dx=[0.0]*len(cs)
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        s=pdi[i]+ndi[i]; dx[i]= (100*abs(pdi[i]-ndi[i])/s) if s>0 else 0.0
    return rma(dx,n)

def macd_hist(vals, f=12, s=26, sig=9):
    e1=ema(vals,f); e2=ema(vals,s)
    macd=[e1[i]-e2[i] for i in range(len(vals))]
    sigl=ema(macd,sig)
    return [macd[i]-sigl[i] for i in range(len(vals))]

def bb(vals, n=20, k=2.0):
    if len(vals)<n: return [None]*len(vals), [None]*len(vals), [None]*len(vals)
    ma=[]; dev=[]
    for i in range(len(vals)):
        if i<n-1:
            ma.append(None); dev.append(None)
        else:
            w=vals[i-n+1:i+1]
            m=sum(w)/n
            v=(sum((x-m)**2 for x in w)/n)**0.5
            ma.append(m); dev.append(v)
    upper=[(ma[i]+k*dev[i]) if ma[i] is not None else None for i in range(len(vals))]
    lower=[(ma[i]-k*dev[i]) if ma[i] is not None else None for i in range(len(vals))]
    return upper, lower, ma

def keltner(hs, ls, cs, n=20, k=1.5):
    ema_c=ema(cs,n)
    atrv=atr(hs,ls,cs,n)
    upper=[ema_c[i]+k*atrv[i] for i in range(len(cs))]
    lower=[ema_c[i]-k*atrv[i] for i in range(len(cs))]
    return upper, lower, ema_c

def obv(cl, vo):
    o=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cl)):
        if cl[i]>cl[i-1]: o.append(o[-1]+vo[i])
        elif cl[i]<cl[i-1]: o.append(o[-1]-vo[i])
        else: o.append(o[-1])
    return o

def vwap(arr, n=20):
    tpv=tp(arr); v=vol(arr)
    out=[]; num=0.0; den=0.0
    for i in range(len(arr)):
        num += tpv[i]*v[i]; den += v[i]
        out.append(num/den if den>0 else tpv[i])
        if i>=n:
            num -= tpv[i-n]*v[i-n]; den -= v[i-n]
    return out

# ---------- Strategy params (override via /etc/scalp.strategy) ----------
PARAM = {
  "risk_pct": 0.003,           # 0.3%
  "leverage": 5,
  "min_notional": 5.0,
  "max_pair_expo_pct": 0.25,
  "lot_step": 0.0001,
  "cooldown_1m": 5,            # 5×1m
  "N_breakout": 20,
  "vol_mult_pullback": 1.3
}
if CFGSTR.exists():
    for ln in CFGSTR.read_text().splitlines():
        ln=ln.strip()
        if not ln or ln.startswith("#"): continue
        k,v = ln.split("=",1)
        try: PARAM[k]=float(v) if "." in v or v.isdigit() else v
        except: PARAM[k]=v

# ---------- Pair rules ----------
def get_pair_rules(sym):
    d = jload(PAIRDB, {})
    r = (d or {}).get(sym, {})
    return {
        "min_notional": float(r.get("minNotional", PARAM["min_notional"])),
        "lot_step":    float(r.get("lotStep",    PARAM["lot_step"]))
    }

# ---------- Préfiltres durcis ----------
def median_spread_1m(m1, k=5):
    """Médiane sur k dernières 1m du (H-L)/C ; supprime bruit bougie unique."""
    if not m1: return 1.0
    k = min(k, len(m1))
    cs = close(m1); hs=high(m1); ls=low(m1)
    arr=[]
    for i in range(len(cs)-k, len(cs)):
        if cs[i] <= 0: continue
        arr.append( (hs[i]-ls[i]) / cs[i] )
    return statistics.median(arr) if arr else 1.0

def prefilters(sym, m1, m3, m5):
    # Vol 1m
    c1=close(m1); h1=high(m1); l1=low(m1)
    atr1=atr(h1,l1,c1,14)
    atrpct1 = (atr1[-1]/c1[-1])*100 if c1 and atr1[-1] else 0.0
    if atrpct1 < 0.10: return False, "atr1%<0.10"

    # Cooldown
    cd=jload(STATE/"cooldown.json", {}).get(sym, 0)
    if int(time.time()) < cd: return False, "cooldown"

    # Spread médian 3–5 bougies
    spr = median_spread_1m(m1, k=5)
    if spr > 0.010: return False, "spread>1%"

    return True, "ok"

# ---------- Evidences (0/1) ----------
def macd_accel(vals):
    h=macd_hist(vals)
    if len(h)<4: return 0.0
    return 1.0 if (h[-1]>h[-2]>h[-3]) else 0.0

def squeeze_ok(hs,ls,cs):
    bu,bl,_ = bb(cs,20,2.0); ku,kl,_ = keltner(hs,ls,cs,20,1.5)
    if bu[-1] is None: return 0.0
    return 1.0 if (bu[-1]-bl[-1]) < (ku[-1]-kl[-1]) else 0.0

def evidence_breakout(ctx, m3, m5):
    # N=20 en 3m => ~60m de range ; ADX(14) sur 5m
    c3=close(m3)
    if len(c3)<22: return 0.0
    N=int(PARAM["N_breakout"])
    hh=max(c3[-N-1:-1]); ll=min(c3[-N-1:-1])
    adx5 = adx(high(m5), low(m5), close(m5), 14)[-1] if m5 else 0.0
    accel = macd_accel(c3)
    sq = squeeze_ok(high(m3),low(m3),c3)
    if ctx=="buy"  and c3[-1]>hh and adx5>=20 and accel and sq: return 1.0
    if ctx=="sell" and c3[-1]<ll and adx5>=20 and accel and sq: return 1.0
    return 0.0

def evidence_pullback(ctx, m1, m3):
    c1=close(m1); v1=vol(m1); e20=ema(c1,20)
    up,lo,_ = bb(c1,20,2.0); vw= vwap(m1,20)
    rsi7=rsi(c1,7); vavg20=sum(v1[-20:])/max(1,len(v1[-20:]))
    if ctx=="buy":
        touch = ((lo[-1] is not None and c1[-1]<=lo[-1]) or c1[-1]<=e20[-1] or c1[-1]<=vw[-1])
        side  = rsi7[-1]<=45
    elif ctx=="sell":
        touch = ((up[-1] is not None and c1[-1]>=up[-1]) or c1[-1]>=e20[-1] or c1[-1]>=vw[-1])
        side  = rsi7[-1]>=55
    else:
        return 0.0
    volok = (v1[-1] >= PARAM["vol_mult_pullback"]*vavg20)
    return 1.0 if (touch and side and volok) else 0.0

def candle_reversal(c):
    if len(c)<3: return False
    b2,b1,c0 = c[-3],c[-2],c[-1]
    return (c0<b1 and b1>b2) or (c0>b1 and b1<b2)

def evidence_meanrev(ctx, m1):
    # Un seul sens par bougie: priorité au côté touché
    c1=close(m1); up,lo,_ = bb(c1,20,2.0); r7=rsi(c1,7)
    if up[-1] is None: return 0.0
    touched_up   = c1[-1]>=up[-1]
    touched_low  = c1[-1]<=lo[-1]
    if ctx!="hold": return 0.0
    if touched_up and not touched_low:
        return 1.0 if (r7[-1]>=60 and candle_reversal(c1)) else 0.0
    if touched_low and not touched_up:
        return 1.0 if (r7[-1]<=40 and candle_reversal(c1)) else 0.0
    # Si les deux ou aucun: pas d’ordre MR pour éviter double-sens
    return 0.0

# ---------- Entry scoring ----------
def entry_score(m1, m3, m5, ctx):
    if not (m1 and m3 and m5): return 0.0
    e1 = evidence_meanrev(ctx, m1)
    e3 = evidence_breakout(ctx, m3, m5)
    e5 = evidence_pullback(ctx, m1, m3)
    return 0.5*e5 + 0.3*e3 + 0.2*e1

# ---------- Sizing ----------
def round_step(q, step):
    if step<=0: return q
    return math.floor(q/step)*step

def size_order(sym, price, sl, balance, risk_pct, leverage, max_pair_expo_pct):
    rules = get_pair_rules(sym)
    min_notional = rules["min_notional"]
    lot_step     = rules["lot_step"]

    D = abs(price - sl)
    if D<=0: return 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0
    risk_usd = balance * risk_pct
    qty = risk_usd / D
    notional = qty * price

    if notional < min_notional:
        qty = min_notional / price
        notional = min_notional

    max_notional = balance * max_pair_expo_pct * leverage
    if notional > max_notional:
        qty = max_notional / price
        notional = max_notional

    qty = round_step(qty, lot_step)
    margin = notional / leverage
    return qty, notional, margin, risk_usd

# ---------- Mapping contexte A -> B ----------
def map_ctx_a_to_b(ctx_a):
    m = {"bullish":"buy", "bearish":"sell", "range":"hold"}
    return m.get(ctx_a, "none")

# ---------- Main per-symbol ----------
def analyze_symbol(sym, ctx_a, m1, m3, m5, balance=200.0):
    ok, why = prefilters(sym, m1, m3, m5)
    if not ok: return {"symbol": sym, "ctx": "none", "why": why}

    ctx = map_ctx_a_to_b(ctx_a)

    score = entry_score(m1, m3, m5, ctx)

    # Veto 5m directionnel (EMA9-21)
    e9=ema(close(m5),9); e21=ema(close(m5),21)
    S5 = (e9[-1]-e21[-1])
    if ctx=="buy" and S5<0:  score = min(score, 0.59)
    if ctx=="sell" and S5>0: score = min(score, 0.59)

    # Persistance 2×1m
    pst=jload(STATE/"persist_B.json", {})
    st=pst.get(sym, {"score_ge":0})
    st["score_ge"] = st.get("score_ge",0)+1 if score>=0.60 else 0
    pst[sym]=st; jsave(STATE/"persist_B.json", pst)

    signal=None
    if st["score_ge"]>=2:
        c1=close(m1); h1=high(m1); l1=low(m1)
        atr1 = atr(h1,l1,c1,14)[-1]
        entry = c1[-1]
        if ctx=="buy":
            sl = entry - 1.2*atr1
            tp = entry + 1.8*atr1
        elif ctx=="sell":
            sl = entry + 1.2*atr1
            tp = entry - 1.8*atr1
        else:
            # MR: pas d’ordre sans contexte clair -> garder neutre
            sl = entry; tp = entry

        qty, notion, margin, risk_usd = size_order(
            sym, entry, sl, balance,
            risk_pct=PARAM["risk_pct"],
            leverage=PARAM["leverage"],
            max_pair_expo_pct=PARAM["max_pair_expo_pct"]
        )

        if qty>0 and ctx in ("buy","sell"):
            signal = {
                "ts": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S", time.gmtime()),
                "symbol": sym,
                "side": "buy" if ctx=="buy" else "sell",
                "entry": round(entry,6),
                "sl": round(sl,6),
                "tp": round(tp,6),
                "qty": qty,
                "notional": round(notion,2),
                "margin": round(margin,2),
                "risk_usd": round(risk_usd,2),
                "why": f"B:score>=0.60x2|ctxA={ctx_a}",
                "sl_type": "stop-market",        # exécution hard côté exchange
                "timeout_s": 25*60,              # 25×1m
                "trail_arm_at": round(1.0*atr1,6),
                "trail_step_atr": 1.0            # trailing 1×ATR après +1×ATR
            }
            # cooldown
            cd=jload(STATE/"cooldown.json", {})
            cd[sym] = int(time.time()) + int(PARAM["cooldown_1m"])*60
            jsave(STATE/"cooldown.json", cd)
            # reset persistence
            st["score_ge"]=0; pst[sym]=st; jsave(STATE/"persist_B.json", pst)
            # append signal
            jappend(SIGF, signal)

    return {"symbol": sym, "ctxA": ctx_a, "ctx": ctx, "score": round(score,3), "signal": signal}

# ---------- Batch runner ----------
def load_tf(sym, tf):
    from pathlib import Path, PurePath as PP; import json
    DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
    tfsec={'1m':60,'3m':180,'5m':300,'15m':900,'30m':1800}.get(tf,60)
    f=C/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    if not f.exists(): return []
    a=json.loads(f.read_text())
    return last_complete(a, tfsec) 60)
    elif tf=="3m":  return last_complete(a, 180)
    elif tf=="5m":  return last_complete(a, 300)
    else: return a

def run_for_top(top_syms, balance=200.0):
    ctxA = jload(AOUT, {})
    out=[]
    for sym in top_syms:
        rec = ctxA.get(sym, {})
        ctxa = rec.get("context") or rec.get("ctx") or rec.get("trend") or "none"
        m1 = load_tf(sym,"1m"); m3 = load_tf(sym,"3m"); m5 = load_tf(sym,"5m")
        out.append(analyze_symbol(sym, ctxa, m1, m3, m5, balance=balance))
    jsave(BOUT, out)
    return out

if __name__ == "__main__":
    top = (jload(DATA/"top.json", {}) or {}).get("symbols", []) or []
    run_for_top(top[:30], balance=(jload(DATA/"paper_balance.json",{"balance":200.0})["balance"]))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
TOP=json.loads((DATA/"top.json").read_text())["symbols"][:30]

def last_ts(p):
    try:
        a=json.loads(p.read_text()); return int(a[-1][0]) if a else 0
    except Exception: return 0

def age(ts): 
    return max(0,int(time.time()*1000-ts)//1000)

def fmt(a): 
    return f"{a//3600:02d}:{(a%3600)//60:02d}"

print(f"{'symbol':6s} {'5m':>5s} {'15m':>5s} {'30m':>5s}  (âge en mm:ss)")
for s in TOP:
    a5=age(last_ts(C/'5m'/f"{s}.json"))
    a15=age(last_ts(C/'15m'/f"{s}.json"))
    a30=age(last_ts(C/'30m'/f"{s}.json"))
    print(f"{s.replace('USDT',''):6s} {fmt(a5):>5s} {fmt(a15):>5s} {fmt(a30):>5s}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, math
from urllib.request import urlopen, Request
from urllib.parse import urlencode
from urllib.error import URLError, HTTPError

BASE="https://api.bitget.com"

def _http_json(path, params=None, tries=3, timeout=10):
    if params: path += ("?" + urlencode(params))
    for i in range(tries):
        try:
            with urlopen(Request(BASE+path, headers={"User-Agent":"scalp/1"}), timeout=timeout) as r:
                raw=r.read().decode("utf-8")
                return json.loads(raw)
        except (URLError, HTTPError):
            if i+1>=tries: raise
            time.sleep(0.6*(2**i))

def ticker_last(symbol:str)->float|None:
    # v2
    j=_http_json("/api/v2/mix/market/ticker", {"symbol":symbol})
    data=j.get("data") or {}
    p=data.get("lastPr") or data.get("last") or data.get("close")
    try: return float(p)
    except: return None

def klines(symbol:str, granularity:int, limit:int=300):
    # try v2 first
    j=_http_json("/api/v2/mix/market/candles", {"symbol":symbol,"granularity":granularity,"limit":limit})
    data=j.get("data")
    if not data:
        j=_http_json("/api/mix/v1/market/candles", {"symbol":symbol,"granularity":granularity,"limit":limit})
        data=j.get("data")
    rows=[]
    # Bitget renvoie récents→anciens sous forme ["ts","open","high","low","close","volume"]
    for r in (data or []):
        try:
            ts=int(r[0])
            o,h,l,c=map(float,(r[1],r[2],r[3],r[4]))
            rows.append((ts,o,h,l,c))
        except: continue
    rows.sort(key=lambda x:x[0])  # ancien→récent
    return rows

# util
def tf_to_seconds(tf:str)->int:
    m={"1m":60,"5m":300,"15m":900,"30m":1800,"1h":3600}
    return m.get(tf,60)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, ccxt, hashlib
from pathlib import Path
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
F_OK=DATA/"coins_90d.json"
F_PEN=DATA/"coins_pending.json"
F_TOP=DATA/"top.json"
F_FIX=Path("/etc/scalp.fixed_top.json")

RUN=Path("/opt/scalp/run"); RUN.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
CACHE_DIR=RUN/"ohlcv_cache"; CACHE_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

LIMIT=int(os.getenv("TUNE_TOP_OHLCV_LIMIT","48"))      # nb bougies 1h stockées
WORKERS=int(os.getenv("TUNE_TOP_WORKERS","6"))         # parallélisme

def ex():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })
EX=ex()

def load_list(p):
    try:
        j=json.loads(Path(p).read_text() or "{}")
        return j if isinstance(j,list) else (j.get("symbols") or [])
    except: return []

def load_fixed():
    try:
        j=json.loads(F_FIX.read_text()); lst=j.get("symbols",[])
        return [s for s in lst if isinstance(s,str)]
    except: return []

def universe():
    seen=set(); out=[]
    for s in load_fixed()+load_list(F_OK)+load_list(F_TOP)+load_list(F_PEN):
        if s and s not in seen:
            out.append(s); seen.add(s)
    return out

def ccxt_symbol(bitget_id:str)->str:
    return bitget_id.replace("_UMCBL","/USDT:USDT")

def cache_path(sym:str)->Path:
    h=hashlib.sha1(sym.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]
    return CACHE_DIR/f"{h}.json"

def refresh_one(sym:str)->bool:
    try:
        ohlcv=EX.fetch_ohlcv(ccxt_symbol(sym), timeframe="1h", limit=LIMIT)
        cache_path(sym).write_text(json.dumps({"ts":time.time(),"data":ohlcv}))
        return True
    except Exception:
        return False

def main():
    U=universe()
    ok=0
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS) as tp:
        fut={tp.submit(refresh_one,s):s for s in U}
        for f in as_completed(fut):
            ok += 1 if f.result() else 0
    print(f"[ohlcv_refresh] universe={len(U)} updated={ok} limit={LIMIT} workers={WORKERS}")
    (RUN/"ohlcv_refresh.stamp").write_text(str(int(time.time())))
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
from concurrent.futures import ProcessPoolExecutor, as_completed

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
DEBUG = DATA/"debug"
RUN = Path("/opt/scalp/run")
LOCKDIR = RUN/"locks"
DEBUG.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
LOCKDIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

def load_top_symbols():
    top_path = DATA/"top.json"
    if not top_path.exists():
        return []
    try:
        j = json.loads(top_path.read_text())
        return (j.get("symbols") or [])[:30]
    except Exception:
        return []

def lock_path(sym): 
    return LOCKDIR/f"A_{sym}.lock"

def safe_run(sym:str)->tuple[str,bool,str]:
    p = lock_path(sym)
    try:
        fd = os.open(p, os.O_CREAT|os.O_EXCL|os.O_RDWR)
    except FileExistsError:
        return (sym, False, "locked")
    try:
        rc = os.system(f"/usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_coin.py {sym} >/dev/null 2>&1")
        ok = (os.WEXITSTATUS(rc)==0)
        return (sym, ok, "done")
    finally:
        try: os.close(fd); os.unlink(p)
        except: pass

def main():
    symbols = load_top_symbols()
    if not symbols:
        Path(DEBUG/"a_pool.json").write_text(json.dumps({"ts":int(time.time()),"ok":0,"err":0,"skipped":0,"note":"empty top.json"}, indent=2))
        print("[A-pool] empty top.json")
        return
    workers = max(1, min(os.cpu_count() or 2, 6))
    stats={"ok":0,"err":0,"skipped":0}
    with ProcessPoolExecutor(max_workers=workers) as px:
        fut = {px.submit(safe_run, s): s for s in symbols}
        for f in as_completed(fut):
            sym, ok, why = f.result()
            if why=="locked": stats["skipped"]+=1
            elif ok: stats["ok"]+=1
            else: stats["err"]+=1
    tmp = DEBUG/".a_pool.tmp"
    final = DEBUG/"a_pool.json"
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps({"ts":int(time.time()),**stats}, indent=2))
    tmp.replace(final)
    print(f"[A-pool] {stats}")

if __name__=="__main__": 
    main()

import time, math
TF_SEC = {"5m":300,"15m":900,"30m":1800}

def last_closed_epoch(tf:str)->int:
    step = TF_SEC[tf]
    now  = int(time.time())
    return (now//step - 1)*step  # dernière bougie FERMÉE

def ttl_left(tf:str)->int:
    step = TF_SEC[tf]
    now  = int(time.time())
    next_close = (now//step + 0)*step  # fin de la bougie courante
    return max(0, next_close - now)

def since_for(tf:str, bars:int)->int:
    end = last_closed_epoch(tf)
    return (end - (bars-1)*TF_SEC[tf])

import json, time
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
TTL={"30m":1800,"15m":900,"5m":300}
def last_ts(tf):
    latest=0
    for f in (C/tf).glob("*.json"):
        try:
            arr=json.loads(f.read_text())
            if isinstance(arr,list) and arr:
                ts=int(arr[-1][0])//1000
                if ts>latest: latest=ts
        except: pass
    return latest
def probe(tf):
    ts=last_ts(tf)
    age=int(time.time())-ts if ts else 1_000_000_000
    return {"tf":tf,"age_s":age,"ok":age<TTL[tf],"last_ts":ts}
out={"ts":int(time.time()),"fresh":[probe(tf) for tf in ("30m","15m","5m")]}
print(json.dumps(out, indent=2))

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
LOG=/opt/scalp/logs/a_parallel.log
mkdir -p /opt/scalp/logs

{
  date -Is; echo "A:parallel start"

  ( /usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_tf.py 30m ) &
  pid30=$!
  ( /usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_tf.py 15m ) &
  pid15=$!
  ( /usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_tf.py 5m )  &
  pid5=$!

  wait "$pid30" || true
  wait "$pid15" || true
  wait "$pid5"  || true

  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/a_sanity.py >/dev/null 2>&1 || true

    exit 0
  fi

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path

DATA   = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND   = DATA/"candles"
TOP    = (DATA/"top.json").read_text()
SYMS   = json.loads(TOP).get("symbols", [])[:30]  # top strict

PERIOD = {"5m":300, "15m":900, "30m":1800}

def worst(tf, syms):
    now = int(time.time())
    stale, bad = 0, []
    for s in syms:
        p = CAND/tf/f"{s}.json"
        if not p.exists():
            bad.append((s,"missing")); stale += 1; continue
        try:
            a = json.loads(p.read_text())
            ts = a[-1][0]//1000 if a else 0
        except Exception:
            bad.append((s,"corrupt")); stale += 1; continue
        lag = max(0, now - ts)
        if lag > PERIOD[tf] + 30:
            bad.append((s, lag)); stale += 1
    worst_lag = max([v for _,v in bad if isinstance(v,int)] or [0])
    return {"tf":tf, "worst_lag":worst_lag, "stale":stale, "bad":bad}

def main():
    out = {"ts": int(time.time()), "checks": []}
    ok = True
    for tf in ("5m","15m","30m"):
        r = worst(tf, SYMS)
        out["checks"].append(r)
        if r["stale"]>0: ok = False
    print(json.dumps(out, indent=2))
    sys.exit(0 if ok else 1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import asyncio, time, random
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# Config: adapte selon la rateLimit de l’exchange (en ms)
RATE_LIMIT_MS = 200
MAX_INFLIGHT  = max(1, 1000//RATE_LIMIT_MS)
FETCH_WORKERS = min(8, MAX_INFLIGHT)

_executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=FETCH_WORKERS)
_sem = asyncio.Semaphore(MAX_INFLIGHT)

async def throttled_call(loop, func, *args, **kwargs):
    async with _sem:
        t0 = time.time()
        res = await loop.run_in_executor(_executor, lambda: func(*args, **kwargs))
        # respect rate-limit + jitter
        delay = max(0, RATE_LIMIT_MS/1000 - (time.time()-t0))
        if delay>0: await asyncio.sleep(delay + random.uniform(0,0.05))
        return res

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOPF=DATA/"top.json"
AOUT=DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
CAND=DATA/"candles"

TTL={"30m":1800,"15m":900,"5m":300}
SAFETY=60   # on exige au moins 60s de validité restante pour ✅

def j(p,d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception: return d

def last_ts_tf(tf, symbols):
    mx=0; missing=[]
    for s in symbols:
        f=CAND/f"{tf}/{s}.json"
        try:
            arr=json.loads(f.read_text())
            if arr: mx=max(mx, arr[-1][0]//1000)
            else: missing.append(s)
        except Exception:
            missing.append(s)
    return mx, missing

def left_str(sec):
    sec=max(0,int(sec))
    return f"{sec//60:02d}m{sec%60:02d}s"

def main():
    top=j(TOPF, {"symbols":[]})
    syms=top.get("symbols",[])[:30]
    n=len(syms)

    now=int(time.time())
    # Data freshness per TF
    lefts={}
    oks={}
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        ts,_=last_ts_tf(tf, syms)
        left = TTL[tf] - (now - ts)
        lefts[tf]=max(0,left)
        oks[tf] = lefts[tf] >= SAFETY

    # Analyse A freshness vs data
    a=j(AOUT, {"generated_at":"", "max_data_ts":0, "results":[]})
    try:
        ats=int(time.mktime(time.strptime(a["generated_at"], "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ")))
    except Exception:
        ats=0
    a_left = max(0, TTL["5m"] - (now - ats))
    # ok seulement si data 5/15/30 sont OK et analyse >= max_data_ts
    a_ok = all(oks.values()) and (ats >= a.get("max_data_ts",0))

    # lignes header
    print("# Dashboard")
    print(f"Top>90j {left_str(  (90*24*3600) ):>s} ✅ | Top30 {left_str(max(0,int(top.get('keep',30))*3600 - (now - 0)))} ✅  n={n:>2d} ✅")
    print(f"Data :  30m {left_str(lefts['30m'])} {'✅' if oks['30m'] else '❌'}  |  15m {left_str(lefts['15m'])} {'✅' if oks['15m'] else '❌'}  |  5m  {left_str(lefts['5m'])} {'✅' if oks['5m'] else '❌'}")
    print(f"Analyse: {left_str(a_left)} {'✅' if a_ok else '❌'}  |  b:{sum(r['pb']>r['ph'] and r['pb']>r['ps'] for r in a['results'])} h:{sum(r['ph']>r['pb'] and r['ph']>r['ps'] for r in a['results'])} s:{sum(r['ps']>r['pb'] and r['ps']>r['ph'] for r in a['results'])} none:{n - len(a['results']) if n else 0} {'✅' if len(a['results'])==n else '❌'}")

    # table : BTC, ETH, + 2 best/2 worst S
    rows=[r for r in a.get("results",[]) if r["symbol"] in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT")]
    rest=[r for r in a.get("results",[]) if r["symbol"] not in ("BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT")]
    rest=sorted(rest, key=lambda x:x["S"])
    rows += rest[:2] + (list(reversed(rest))[:2] if rest else [])
    # distinct 5 lignes max
    seen=set(); out=[]
    for r in rows:
        k=r["symbol"]
        if k in seen: continue
        seen.add(k); out.append(r)
        if len(out)>=6: break

    print("-"*70)
    print("symbol Sx10  ctx   pb  ph  ps  reason")
    for r in out:
        print(f"{r['symbol'][:-4]:<5} {int(round(10*r['S'])):>3}  {r['ctx']:<5} {int(round(10*r['pb'])):>3} {int(round(10*r['ph'])):>3} {int(round(10*r['ps'])):>3} {r.get('reason','')}")
    print("-"*70)
    print("Derniers signaux: (aucun)")
    print("Positions ouvertes: (aucune)")
    print("Historique récent: (vide)")

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time, json, ccxt
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
F_CON = DATA/"contracts_usdt.json"     # liste lisible humaine (BTCUSDT, …)
F_OK  = DATA/"coins_90d.json"          # whitelist >=90j (ids: BTCUSDT_UMCBL, …)
F_PEN = DATA/"coins_pending.json"      # 80–90j, à rechecker
F_DBG = DATA/"debug/coins_scan_ccxt.json"

def ex():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })

def main():
    e = ex()
    markets = e.load_markets()
    # USDT linear swaps uniquement
    mlist = [m for m in markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("settle")=="USDT"]
    ids   = sorted({ m["id"] for m in mlist })            # ex: BTCUSDT_UMCBL
    F_CON.write_text(json.dumps([i.replace("_UMCBL","USDT") for i in ids], indent=2))

    now = int(time.time()*1000)
    need90 = now - 90*24*3600*1000
    need80 = now - 80*24*3600*1000

    ok, pen, details = [], [], []
    since = now - 130*24*3600*1000
    for m in mlist:
        sym = m["symbol"]      # ex: BTC/USDT:USDT
        mid = m["id"]          # ex: BTCUSDT_UMCBL
        try:
            rows = e.fetch_ohlcv(sym, timeframe="1d", since=since, limit=130)
            if not rows:
                pen.append(mid); details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"nodata"}); continue
            first_ts = rows[0][0]
            if first_ts <= need90:
                ok.append(mid); details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"ok90","rows":len(rows),"first":first_ts})
            elif first_ts <= need80:
                pen.append(mid); details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"pending80","rows":len(rows),"first":first_ts})
            else:
                details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"too_young","rows":len(rows),"first":first_ts})
        except Exception as err:
            pen.append(mid); details.append({"id":mid,"sym":sym,"st":"error","err":str(err)[:140]})

    ts = time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())
    F_OK.write_text(json.dumps({"symbols":ok,"generated_at":ts,"source":"ccxt-1d-90d"}, indent=2))
    F_PEN.write_text(json.dumps({"symbols":pen,"generated_at":ts,"note":"check next run (>=80d)"}, indent=2))
    F_DBG.write_text(json.dumps({"ts":ts,"contracts":len(ids),"ok90":len(ok),"pending":len(pen),"details":details[:60]}, indent=2))
    print(f"[ccxt usdt 1d] markets={len(ids)} ok90={len(ok)} pending={len(pen)}")
if __name__ == "__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"

Path: /opt/scalp/tools._archive_20250926T100937Z/rebuild_top_v2_async.py

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math, time, asyncio, statistics as stats
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# ====== Config ======
DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
PARAMS = Path("/opt/scalp/tools/top_params.json")
WORKERS = int(os.getenv("TOP_WORKERS", "10"))
RATE_LIMIT_MS = int(os.getenv("TOP_RATE_LIMIT_MS", "200"))
MAX_INFLIGHT = max(1, 1000 // RATE_LIMIT_MS)
FUT = {"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}  # Bitget futures USDT

# ====== Helpers ======
def now_iso(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")
def load_params(): return json.loads(PARAMS.read_text())

def rank_norm(d):
    if not d: return {}
    it = sorted(d.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1])
    n = max(1, len(it)-1)
    return {k:i/n for i,(k,_) in enumerate(it)}

def ema(vals, p):
    if not vals: return 0.0
    a=2/(p+1); e=float(vals[0])
    for v in vals[1:]: e=a*float(v)+(1-a)*e
    return float(e)

def winsorize(vals, p=0.01):
    if not vals: return vals
    s=sorted(vals); n=len(s)
    lo=s[max(0,int(n*p)-1)]; hi=s[min(n-1,int(n*(1-p)))]
    return [min(max(v,lo),hi) for v in vals]

def spread_bps_from_ticker(t):
    bid, ask = t.get("bid"), t.get("ask")
    if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0: return 1e9
    mid = 0.5*(bid+ask); return 10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid

def depth_quote_in_band(ob, band_bps=50):
    if not ob or not ob.get("bids") or not ob.get("asks"): return 0.0
    bb=ob["bids"][0][0]; ba=ob["asks"][0][0]; mid=0.5*(bb+ba)
    lo=mid*(1-band_bps/10000.0); hi=mid*(1+band_bps/10000.0)
    q=0.0
    for p,a in ob["bids"]:
        if p<lo: break
        q+=p*a
    for p,a in ob["asks"]:
        if p>hi: break
        q+=p*a
    return float(q)

def spread_bps_median_proxy(o1h24):
    vals=[]
    for k in (o1h24 or []):
        _,_,h,l,_,_=k
        if h and l:
            mid=0.5*(h+l)
            if mid>0: vals.append(10000.0*(h-l)/mid)
    return float(stats.median(vals)) if vals else 1e9

# ====== Throttle async ======
_executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS)
_sem = asyncio.Semaphore(MAX_INFLIGHT)
async def throttled(loop, func, *args, **kw):
    async with _sem:
        t0=time.time()
        try:
            res = await loop.run_in_executor(_executor, lambda: func(*args, **kw))
        except Exception:
            res = None
        dt=time.time()-t0
        sl=max(0.0, RATE_LIMIT_MS/1000 - dt)
        if sl: await asyncio.sleep(sl)
        return res

# ====== Per-symbol job (Futures only) ======
async def fetch_bundle(loop, ex, sym, band_bps, funding_since_ms):
    # 1D pour activité + âge
    o1d = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_ohlcv, sym, "1d", 400, FUT)
    if not isinstance(o1d, list) or not o1d:
        return {"skip": True}  # pas d'info fiable
    last_ts = o1d[-1][0]; first_ts = o1d[0][0]

    # 1H pour turnover EMA, vola, spread proxy
    o1h = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_ohlcv, sym, "1h", 24*7+1, FUT)
    turnover_vals=[]; rets=[]
    o1h24 = o1h[-24:] if isinstance(o1h,list) else []
    spr_med = spread_bps_median_proxy(o1h24)
    if isinstance(o1h, list) and len(o1h)>10:
        prev=o1h[0][4]
        for _,_,_,_,c,v in o1h[1:]:
            turnover_vals.append(float(v)*float(c))
            if prev>0 and c>0: rets.append(math.log(c/prev))
            prev=c
    turn_ema = float(ema(turnover_vals, 24))
    vola7d = float(stats.pstdev(rets)) if rets else 0.0

    # Order book depth
    ob = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_order_book, sym, 100, FUT)
    depth_q = depth_quote_in_band(ob, band_bps)

    # Funding 7j
    fund_abs = 0.0
    if hasattr(ex, "fetchFundingRateHistory"):
        hist = await throttled(loop, ex.fetchFundingRateHistory, sym, funding_since_ms, None, {**FUT})
        vals=[]
        if isinstance(hist, list):
            for it in hist:
                fr = it.get("fundingRate") or it.get("fundingRateDaily") or 0.0
                try: vals.append(abs(float(fr)))
                except: pass
        if vals: fund_abs = float(sum(vals)/len(vals))

    return {
        "skip": False,
        "last_ts": last_ts, "first_ts": first_ts,
        "turnover_ema7d": turn_ema, "vola7d": vola7d,
        "spread_bps_med": spr_med, "depth_quote": depth_q,
        "funding_abs_mean": fund_abs
    }

# ====== Main ======
def main():
    import ccxt
    p = load_params()
    EX, QUOTE, N = p["exchange"], p["quote"], p["top_n"]
    flt, dep, W = p["filters"], p["depth"], p["scoring"]

    NOW = datetime.now(timezone.utc); NOW_ISO = now_iso()
    cutoff_90d_ms = int((NOW - timedelta(days=90)).timestamp()*1000)
    listing_cut_ms = int((NOW - timedelta(days=int(flt.get("min_listing_days",180)))).timestamp()*1000)
    funding_since_ms = int((NOW - timedelta(days=7)).timestamp()*1000)
    band_bps = int(dep.get("band_bps",50))
    min_depth_q = float(dep.get("min_quote_depth",0.0))
    min_qv = float(flt["min_quote_vol_24h"])
    max_sp = float(flt["max_spread_bps"])

    ex0 = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex0.load_markets()

    # Univers: SWAP linéaire USDT
    mkts = [m for m in ex0.markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE and m.get("active") is not False]
    symbols = [m["symbol"] for m in mkts]
    bases = {m["symbol"]: m["base"] for m in mkts}

    # Tickers avec params (certains exchanges ignorent params sur fetch_tickers → fallback par symbole)
    tickers = {}
    try:
        tickers = ex0.fetch_tickers(symbols, {**FUT})
    except Exception:
        for s in symbols:
            try: tickers[s] = ex0.fetch_ticker(s, {**FUT})
            except Exception: tickers[s] = {}

    # Pré-filtre rapide
    bad_kw = tuple(flt["exclude_leveraged_keywords"])
    bad_bases = set(flt["exclude_bases"])
    pre=[]; vol24={}
    for s in symbols:
        b=bases[s]
        if any(k in b for k in bad_kw): continue
        if b in bad_bases: continue
        t=tickers.get(s,{})
        qv=float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        sp=spread_bps_from_ticker(t)
        if qv < min_qv or sp > max_sp: continue
        pre.append(s); vol24[s]=qv

    # Pool de clients
    def ex_factory():
        e = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
        try: e.load_markets()
        except Exception: pass
        return e
    clients = [ex_factory() for _ in range(max(1, min(WORKERS, len(pre))))]

    async def run_all():
        loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
        tasks=[]
        for i,s in enumerate(pre):
            ex = clients[i % len(clients)]
            tasks.append(fetch_bundle(loop, ex, s, band_bps, funding_since_ms))
        res = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
        return {s:r for s,r in zip(pre,res)}

    results = asyncio.run(run_all())

    # Gates et métriques
    inactive_90d=[]; too_young=[]; depth_fail=[]; metrics={}
    for s,r in results.items():
        if isinstance(r,Exception) or r is None or r.get("skip"):  # pas de data fiable → ignore
            continue
        if r["last_ts"] < cutoff_90d_ms:
            inactive_90d.append(s.replace("/","")); continue
        if r["first_ts"] and r["first_ts"] > listing_cut_ms:
            too_young.append(s.replace("/","")); continue
        if r["depth_quote"] < min_depth_q:
            depth_fail.append(s.replace("/","")); continue
        metrics[s]=r

    # coins_90d.json
    DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    (DATA/"coins_90d.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "source": "ccxt-1d-90d",
        "exchange": EX, "quote": QUOTE, "cutoff_days": 90,
        "inactive_symbols": sorted(inactive_90d)
    }, indent=2))

    if not metrics:
        # pas de top possible
        (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({
            "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "source": "futures-only+advanced-async-v2",
            "exchange": EX, "quote": QUOTE, "symbols": []
        }, indent=2))
        (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({
            "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "n": 0,
            "gates": {"inactive_90d": len(inactive_90d), "too_young": len(too_young), "depth_fail": len(depth_fail)},
            "items": []
        }, indent=2))
        print(f"[top-v2-futures] pre={len(pre)} active=0 top=0 inactive90d={len(inactive_90d)} tooyoung={len(too_young)} depthfail={len(depth_fail)}")
        return

    # Winsor + log-scale
    vvals=[vol24.get(s,0.0) for s in metrics]
    tvals=[metrics[s]["turnover_ema7d"] for s in metrics]
    vvals=winsorize(vvals,0.01) if len(vvals)>10 else vvals
    tvals=winsorize(tvals,0.01) if len(tvals)>10 else tvals
    vmap={s: math.log1p(v) for s,v in zip(metrics.keys(), vvals)}
    tmap={s: math.log1p(v) for s,v in zip(metrics.keys(), tvals)}
    volmap={s: metrics[s]["vola7d"] for s in metrics}
    dmap  ={s: metrics[s]["depth_quote"] for s in metrics}
    spmap ={s: metrics[s]["spread_bps_med"] for s in metrics}
    fmap  ={s: metrics[s]["funding_abs_mean"] for s in metrics}

    Rv,Rt,Rvol,Rd,Rs,Rf = map(rank_norm,(vmap,tmap,volmap,dmap,spmap,fmap))
    W = p["scoring"]

    score={}
    for s in metrics:
        score[s] = (
            W["w_volume24h"]       * Rv.get(s,0.0) +
            W["w_turnover7d_ema"]  * Rt.get(s,0.0) +
            W["w_volatility7d"]    * Rvol.get(s,0.0) +
            W["w_depth"]           * Rd.get(s,0.0) +
            W["w_spread_med"]      * Rs.get(s,0.0) +
            W.get("w_funding",-0.05)*Rf.get(s,0.0)
        )

    ranked = sorted(score.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1], reverse=True)
    top_syms = [s.replace("/","") for s,_ in ranked[:p["top_n"]]]

    (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "source": "futures-only+advanced-async-v2",
        "exchange": EX, "quote": QUOTE, "symbols": top_syms
    }, indent=2))

    out=[]
    for s,sc in ranked[:p["top_n"]]:
        t=tickers.get(s,{})
        m=metrics[s]
        out.append({
            "symbol": s.replace("/",""),
            "score": round(float(sc),6),
            "volume24h_quote": float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0),
            "turnover7d_ema": float(m["turnover_ema7d"]),
            "volatility7d": float(m["vola7d"]),
            "depth_quote_band": float(m["depth_quote"]),
            "spread_bps_median": float(m["spread_bps_med"]),
            "funding_abs_mean": float(m["funding_abs_mean"])
        })

    (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "n": len(top_syms),
        "gates": {"inactive_90d": len(inactive_90d), "too_young": len(too_young), "depth_fail": len(depth_fail)},
        "items": out
    }, indent=2))

    print(f"[top-v2-futures] pre={len(pre)} active={len(metrics)} top={len(top_syms)} "
          f"inactive90d={len(inactive_90d)} tooyoung={len(too_young)} depthfail={len(depth_fail)} "
          f"workers={WORKERS} inflight={MAX_INFLIGHT}")
if __name__ == "__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
ts(){ date -Is; }

DATA=/opt/scalp/data

# TTL (validité)
TTL_COINS90=$((2*24*3600))   # 2 jours
TTL_TOP=$((2*3600))          # 2 h
TTL_AOUT=$((5*60))           # 5 min

fresh(){ # fresh file ttl
  f=$1; ttl=$2
  [ -s "$f" ] || return 1
  ts=$(jq -r '.generated_at // empty' "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo "")
  [ -n "$ts" ] || return 1
  now=$(date +%s)
  ft=$(date -d "$ts" +%s 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
  age=$(( now - ft ))
  [ $age -lt $ttl ]
}

echo "[INIT] $(ts) start"

# Solde initial si absent
[ -s $DATA/paper_balance.json ] || echo '{"equity":200,"ts":"'"$(ts)"'"}' > $DATA/paper_balance.json
[ -s $DATA/signals.json ] || echo '[]' > $DATA/signals.json
[ -s $DATA/history.json ] || echo '[]' > $DATA/history.json
[ -s $DATA/positions.json ] || echo '{"positions":[]}' > $DATA/positions.json

# 1) Univers
if ! fresh $DATA/coins_90d.json $TTL_COINS90; then
  echo "[INIT] coins_90d refresh"
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/filter_contracts_usdt_ccxt.py || true
fi

# 2) Top
if ! fresh $DATA/top.json $TTL_TOP; then
  echo "[INIT] top.json refresh"
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/filter_top.py || true
fi

# 3) Analyse A (si expiré)
if ! fresh $DATA/analyse_A_out.json $TTL_AOUT; then
  echo "[INIT] Analyse A refresh"
  python3 /opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_tf.py || true
  bash /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_guard.sh || true
fi

# 4) Analyse B (toujours 1m → ctx dépendant)
echo "[INIT] Analyse B run"
python3 /opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_1m3m_subset.py || true
bash /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_guard.sh || true

echo "[INIT] $(ts) done"

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TOP=/opt/scalp/data/top.json
[ -s "$TOP" ] || { echo "[data-guard] no top.json"; exit 0; }
# calc retard maxi via python (pire des top30)
python3 - <<'PY'
import json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path
DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=DATA/"candles"
def last(s,tf):
    p=C/tf/(s+".json")
    if not p.exists(): return 0
    try:
        a=json.loads(p.read_text()); return int(a[-1][0])//1000 if a else 0
    except: return 0
top=json.loads(Path("/opt/scalp/data/top.json").read_text()); syms=top.get("symbols",[])[:30]
now=int(time.time()); bad=[]
for tf,period in [("5m",300),("15m",900),("30m",1800)]:
    left=min([period-(now-last(s,tf)) if last(s,tf)>0 else 0 for s in syms] or [0])
    if left<=0: bad.append(tf)
if bad:
    print("[data-guard] refresh TF:", ",".join(bad)); sys.stdout.flush()
    import subprocess as sp
    for tf in bad: sp.call(["python3","/opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_tf.py", tf])
else:
    print("[data-guard] OK")
PY

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
pos_f=D/"positions.json"; bal_f=D/"paper_balance.json"

now=int(time.time()); closed=0
for p in positions:
    if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("status")=="open" and now-int(p.get("ts",now))>20:
        p["status"]="closed"; p["close_ts"]=now; p["pnl"]=1 if int(str(p.get("id",""))[-1])%2 else -1; closed+=1
pos_f.write_text(json.dumps(positions,indent=2))
equity=sum(p.get("pnl",0) for p in positions if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("status")=="closed")
bal={"equity":equity,"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())}
bal_f.write_text(json.dumps(bal,indent=2))
print(f"[monitor] closed={closed} equity={equity}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import argparse, json, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
NOW  = int(time.time())

TF_REQ = [("5m",300), ("15m",900), ("30m",1800)]
STALE = 2*3600  # on considère "frais" si dernière bougie < 2h

def load_universe(p):
    p = Path(p)
    if not p.exists(): return []
    try: j = json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception: return []
    syms = j.get("symbols") or j.get("Symbols") or []
    return [s for s in syms if isinstance(s,str)]

def score_symbol(sym:str)->tuple:
    """score = nb de TF présents et frais, puis inverse de staleness."""
    ok = 0
    worst_left = -10**9
    for tf,period in TF_REQ:
        f = CAND/tf/f"{sym}.json"
        if not f.exists(): continue
        try:
            a = json.loads(f.read_text())
            ts = int(a[-1][0])//1000 if a else 0
        except Exception:
            ts = 0
        left = max(0, (ts + period) - NOW)  # validité restante
        age = period - left
        if age <= STALE: ok += 1
        worst_left = max(worst_left, left)
    return (ok, worst_left)  # tri décroissant

def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--universe", required=True)
    ap.add_argument("--keep", type=int, default=30)
    ap.add_argument("--fixed", default="BTCUSDT,ETHUSDT,XRPUSDT,SOLUSDT,BNBUSDT")
    ap.add_argument("--out", required=True)
    args = ap.parse_args()

    uni = load_universe(args.universe)
    fixed = [s.strip() for s in (args.fixed or "").split(",") if s.strip()]
    fixed = [s for s in fixed if s in uni]

    rest = [s for s in uni if s not in fixed]
    scored = sorted(rest, key=score_symbol, reverse=True)

    pick = list(dict.fromkeys(fixed + scored))[:args.keep]

    out = {
        "symbols": pick,
        "generated_at": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()),
        "source": "coins_90d->local_candles",
        "keep": args.keep,
        "fixed": fixed,
    }
    Path(args.out).write_text(json.dumps(out, indent=2))
    print(f"[top] n={len(pick)} fixed={len(fixed)} -> {args.out}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, json, time, shutil
from pathlib import Path
OK=True; msgs=[]
def need(p,t="f"):
    global OK
    P=Path(p); ex=(P.is_file() if t=="f" else P.is_dir())
    if not ex: OK=False; msgs.append(f"missing:{t}:{p}")
def touch(p): Path(p).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True); Path(p).touch()
for f in ("/etc/scalp.env","/etc/scalp.app","/etc/scalp.tuning"): need(f,"f")
for d in ("/opt/scalp/tools","/opt/scalp/logs","/opt/scalp/data","/opt/scalp/data/debug","/opt/scalp/run"): need(d,"d")
need("/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_minutely.sh","f")
for f in ("contracts_usdt.json","coins_90d.json","top.json"): touch(f"/opt/scalp/data/{f}")
st=shutil.disk_usage("/opt/scalp"); OK = OK and st.free >= 500*1024*1024 or False
out={"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ",time.gmtime()),"ok":OK,"issues":msgs}
Path("/opt/scalp/data/debug/preflight.json").write_text(json.dumps(out,indent=2))
print(json.dumps(out)); sys.exit(0 if OK else 2)
PY

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); IN=D/"coins_90d.json"; OUT=D/"top.json"; DBG=D/"debug/top_debug.json"
ts=time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())
syms=[]
try:
    j=json.loads(IN.read_text() or "{}")
    syms=j.get("symbols") if isinstance(j,dict) else (j if isinstance(j,list) else [])
except Exception as e:
    DBG.write_text(json.dumps({"ok":False,"err":str(e),"ts":ts},indent=2)); syms=[]
OUT.write_text(json.dumps({"symbols":syms,"generated_at":ts,"source":"coins_90d"},indent=2))
DBG.write_text(json.dumps({"ok":True,"count":len(syms),"ts":ts},indent=2))
print(f"[quality] {len(syms)}")
PY

cat >/opt/scalp/tools/drain_symbol_queue.sh <<'SHH'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
Q="/opt/scalp/run/symbol_queue.txt"; MAX="${QUEUE_MAX_PER_TICK:-10}"
[ -f "$Q" ] || exit 0
mapfile -t ALL < <(grep -E '^[A-Z0-9]+' "$Q" 2>/dev/null || true); [ ${#ALL[@]} -eq 0 ] && { rm -f "$Q"; exit 0; }
KEEP=(); cnt=0
for S in "${ALL[@]}"; do
  if [ "$cnt" -lt "$MAX" ]; then /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_for_symbol_hint.sh "$S" || true; cnt=$((cnt+1)); else KEEP+=("$S"); fi
done
( [ ${#KEEP[@]} -gt 0 ] && printf "%s\n" "${KEEP[@]}" > "$Q" ) || rm -f "$Q"
echo "[drain] processed=$cnt remaining=${#KEEP[@]}"
SHH

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, os, time
from pathlib import Path
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
T=float(os.environ.get("TUNE_S_THRESHOLD","0.6"))
A=json.loads((D/"analyse_A_out.json").read_text() or "[]")
A=[A] if isinstance(A,dict) else A
signals=[]
now=int(time.time())
for r in A:
    if not isinstance(r,dict): continue
    ctx=str(r.get("context","none")).lower(); S=float(r.get("S",0) or 0)
    if ctx in ("buy","sell") and S>=T:
        signals.append({"symbol":r.get("symbol"),"side":ctx,"score":S,"ts":now,"source":"B"})
(D/"signals.json").write_text(json.dumps(signals,indent=2))
print(f"[B] signals={len(signals)} T={T}")
PY

cat >/opt/scalp/tools/signal_router.py <<'PY'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, random
from pathlib import Path
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
signals=json.loads((D/"signals.json").read_text() or "[]") if (D/"signals.json").exists() else []
positions=json.loads((D/"positions.json").read_text() or "[]") if (D/"positions.json").exists() else []
if isinstance(positions,dict) and "positions" in positions: positions=positions["positions"]
orders=[]; now=int(time.time())
for s in signals:
    if not isinstance(s,dict): continue
    sym=s.get("symbol"); side=s.get("side")
    if not sym or side not in ("buy","sell"): continue
    oid=f"paper-{now}-{random.randint(1000,9999)}"
    entry={"id":oid,"symbol":sym,"side":side,"qty":1.0,"price":100.0,"ts":now,"status":"open"}
    positions.append(entry); orders.append(entry)
(D/"positions.json").write_text(json.dumps(positions,indent=2))
(D/"orders.log").touch(exist_ok=True)
if orders:
    with (D/"orders.log").open("a") as f:
        for o in orders: f.write(f"{o['ts']} NEW {o['side']} {o['symbol']} {o['id']}\n")
if signals: (D/"signals.json").write_text("[]")
if not (D/"paper_balance.json").exists(): (D/"paper_balance.json").write_text(json.dumps({"equity":0,"ts":"1970-01-01T00:00:00Z"},indent=2))
print(f"[router] routed={len(orders)} positions_total={len(positions)}")
PY

cat >/opt/scalp/tools/paper_monitor.py <<'PY'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
pos_f=D/"positions.json"; bal_f=D/"paper_balance.json"
positions=json.loads(pos_f.read_text() or "[]") if pos_f.exists() else []
if isinstance(positions,dict) and "positions" in positions: positions=positions["positions"]
now=int(time.time()); closed=0
for p in positions:
    if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("status")=="open" and now-int(p.get("ts",now))>20:
        p["status"]="closed"; p["close_ts"]=now; p["pnl"]=1 if int(str(p.get("id",""))[-1])%2 else -1; closed+=1
pos_f.write_text(json.dumps(positions,indent=2))
equity=sum(p.get("pnl",0) for p in positions if isinstance(p,dict) and p.get("status")=="closed")
bal={"equity":equity,"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())}
bal_f.write_text(json.dumps(bal,indent=2))
print(f"[monitor] closed={closed} equity={equity}")
PY

cat >/opt/scalp/tools/metrics_export.py <<'PY'
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path
RUN=Path("/opt/scalp/run"); RUN.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
M=RUN/"metrics.prom"; D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DD=D/"debug"
def J(p,default=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except: return default
pf=J(DD/"preflight.json",{}); ae=J(DD/"a_export_check.json",{}); bs=J(DD/"b_status.json",{})
top=J(D/"top.json",{}); coins=J(D/"coins_90d.json",{}); sig=J(D/"signals.json",[])
now=int(time.time()); L=[]
def g(n,v,l=None):
    if v is None: return
    if isinstance(v,bool): v=1 if v else 0
    lbl="" if not l else "{"+",".join([f'{k}=\"{str(x)}\"' for k,x in l.items()])+"}"
    L.append(f"{n}{lbl} {v}")
g("scalp_ok", pf.get("ok",0), {"comp":"preflight"})
g("scalp_ok", ae.get("ok",0), {"comp":"analyse_a_export"})
g("scalp_ok", bs.get("ok",0), {"comp":"analyse_b"})
g("scalp_counts", len((top or {}).get("symbols",[])), {"name":"top"})
g("scalp_counts", len((coins or {}).get("symbols",[])), {"name":"coins90"})
g("scalp_counts", len(sig if isinstance(sig,list) else []), {"name":"signals"})
g("scalp_timestamp", now, {"name":"export"})
M.write_text("\n".join(L)+"\n"); print(f"[metrics] wrote {M}")
PY
chmod +x /opt/scalp/tools/metrics_export.py

# 8) Runner + boucle paper
cat >/opt/scalp/tools/priority_runner.sh <<'RUN'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
/opt/scalp/tools/env_compat.sh >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
source /etc/scalp.app 2>/dev/null || true
source /etc/scalp.tuning 2>/dev/null || true
LOCK="/tmp/scalp.prio.lock"; exec 9>"$LOCK"; flock -n 9 || { echo "busy"; exit 0; }
LOG="${LOG_DIR:-/opt/scalp/logs}/priority_runner.log"; RUN="${RUN_DIR:-/opt/scalp/run}"
mkdir -p "$(dirname "$LOG")" "$RUN" /opt/scalp/data/debug
TS(){ date -Iseconds; }; echo "$(TS) tick:start pid=$$" >>"$LOG"
if ! /usr/bin/env ${PYTHON_BIN:-python3} /opt/scalp/tools/preflight.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1; then
  echo "$(TS) preflight:not-ok -> skip tick" >>"$LOG"; /opt/scalp/tools/alert_eval.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; /opt/scalp/tools/metrics_export.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; /opt/scalp/tools/events_notify.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; echo "$(TS) tick:end" >>"$LOG"; exit 0; fi
if [ -x /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_minutely.sh ]; then echo "$(TS) B:minutely start" >>"$LOG"; /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_minutely.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; echo "$(TS) B:minutely end" >>"$LOG"; fi
MIN=$(date +%M)
if [ $((10#${MIN} % 5)) -eq 0 ]; then
  echo "$(TS) A:sync start" >>"$LOG"
  TF_ORDER="${SYNC_TF_ORDER:-1m,5m,15m,30m}" FORCE_CATCHUP=1 TARGET_ROWS="${A_TARGET_ROWS:-600}" /usr/bin/env ${PYTHON_BIN:-python3} /opt/scalp/tools/sync_candles_safe.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  echo "$(TS) A:sync end" >>"$LOG"
  /opt/scalp/tools/detect_fresh_symbols.sh "${FRESH_AGE_SEC:-180}" >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  /opt/scalp/tools/drain_symbol_queue.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  if [ "${APPEND_GLOBAL_A_ON_5MIN:-1}" = "1" ]; then /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_5min.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; fi
fi
if [ "$(date +%M)" = "00" ] && [ $((10#$(date +%H) % ${QUALITY_EVERY_HOURS:-2})) -eq 0 ]; then echo "$(TS) quality:start" >>"$LOG"; /usr/bin/env ${PYTHON_BIN:-python3} /opt/scalp/tools/run_quality_only.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; echo "$(TS) quality:end" >>"$LOG"; fi
PERIOD_H="${CONTRACTS_PERIOD_H:-48}"; ST="$RUN/contracts.stamp"; now=$(date +%s); last=0; [ -f "$ST" ] && last=$(cat "$ST"||echo 0)
if [ $(( now - last )) -ge $(( PERIOD_H*3600 )) ]; then echo "$(TS) contracts:start" >>"$LOG"; [ -f /opt/scalp/tools/refresh_contracts.py ] && /usr/bin/env ${PYTHON_BIN:-python3} /opt/scalp/tools/refresh_contracts.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; [ -f /opt/scalp/tools/rebuild_coins_90d_light.py ] && /usr/bin/env ${PYTHON_BIN:-python3} /opt/scalp/tools/rebuild_coins_90d_light.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; date +%s > "$ST"; echo "$(TS) contracts:end" >>"$LOG"; fi
[ -x /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b.sh ] && /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
/opt/scalp/tools/alert_eval.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; /opt/scalp/tools/metrics_export.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true; /opt/scalp/tools/events_notify.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
echo "$(TS) tick:end" >>"$LOG"; exit 0
RUN
chmod +x /opt/scalp/tools/priority_runner.sh

----- FILE BEGIN -----
Path: /opt/scalp/tools._archive_20250926T100937Z/ohlcv.py
Size: 549
MTime: 2025-09-25 08:17:21.450631419 +0000
----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
def ema(vals,n):
    if not vals: return []
    k=2/(n+1); out=[vals[0]]
    for x in vals[1:]: out.append(out[-1]+k*(x-out[-1]))
    return out
def minmax_pos(vals,win):
    out=[]
    for i in range(len(vals)):
        a=max(0,i-win+1); w=vals[a:i+1]
        lo=min(w); hi=max(w); rng=(hi-lo) or 1e-9
        out.append((vals[i]-lo)/rng)
    return out
def slope(vals,step=5):
    out=[0]*len(vals)
    for i in range(step,len(vals)):
        prev=vals[i-step] or 1e-9
        out[i]=(vals[i]-prev)/abs(prev)
    return out

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path
BASE=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); C=BASE/"candles"
TOP=json.loads((BASE/"top.json").read_text()) if (BASE/"top.json").exists() else {"symbols":[]}
now=int(time.time())

def load(sym, tf):
    p=C/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    if not p.exists(): return None, f"missing:{tf}"
    try:
        j=json.loads(p.read_text()); k=j.get("data",[])
        if not k: return None, f"empty:{tf}"
        # drop bougie incomplète
        tf_s={"30m":1800,"15m":900,"5m":300}[tf]
        if now - int(k[-1][0]//1000) < int(0.9*tf_s): k=k[:-1]
        if len(k)<500: return None, f"bars<{500}:{tf}"
        age= now - int(k[-1][0]//1000)
        if age>tf_s*2: return None, f"stale:{tf} age={age}s"
        return k, "ok"
    except Exception as e:
        return None, f"readerr:{tf}:{e}"

issues=[]
ok=0
syms=list(TOP.get("symbols",[]))
for sym in syms:
    row={"symbol":sym}
    bad=[]
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        k,st=load(sym, tf)
        row[f"{tf}_status"]=st
        if st!="ok": bad.append(st)
    if bad: issues.append({**row,"fail":bad})
    else: ok+=1

out={"ts":now,"checked":len(syms),"ok":ok,"fail":len(issues),"issues":issues[:20]}
print(json.dumps(out, indent=2))
# dump complet pour inspection
DEBUG=BASE/"debug"; DEBUG.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
(DEBUG/"a_sanity.json").write_text(json.dumps({**out,"issues_full":issues}, indent=2))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, math, statistics as st
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
TOPF = DATA/"top.json"
OUTF = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
HIST_DIR = DATA/"history/A"
HIST_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

TF_STEPS = {"30m":1800, "15m":900, "5m":300}
TF_W = {"30m":0.5, "15m":0.3, "5m":0.2}
TAU = {"30m":0.35, "15m":0.30, "5m":0.25}
ATR_GATE = {"30m":0.0025, "15m":0.0018, "5m":0.0012}  # en ratio

P_ENTER, P_EXIT = 0.60, 0.45

def jload(p, d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception: return d

def ema(arr, n):
    k = 2/(n+1)
    out=[]
    s=None
    for x in arr:
        s = x if s is None else (x*k + s*(1-k))
        out.append(s)
    return out

def atr(h,l,c,n=14):
    tr=[]
    prev=c[0]
    for i in range(len(c)):
        if i==0: tr.append(h[i]-l[i])
        else: tr.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-prev), abs(l[i]-prev)))
        prev=c[i]
    return ema(tr,n)

def macd_hist(c, f=12, s=26, sig=9):
    e1=ema(c,f); e2=ema(c,s)
    macd=[e1[i]-e2[i] for i in range(len(c))]
    es=ema(macd, sig)
    return [macd[i]-es[i] for i in range(len(c))]

def rsi(c, n=14):
    gains=[]; losses=[]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        d=c[i]-c[i-1]
        gains.append(max(d,0)); losses.append(max(-d,0))
    def rma(x, n):
        if not x: return []
        a=[sum(x[:n])/n]+[0]*(len(x)-n)
        for i in range(n,len(x)):
            a[i-n+1] = (a[i-n]*(n-1)+x[i])/n
        return [0]* (len(x)-len(a)) + a
    rg=rma(gains,n); rl=rma(losses,n)
    out=[50]*len(c)
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        avg_g=rg[i-1]; avg_l=rl[i-1]
        if avg_l==0 and avg_g==0: out[i]=50
        elif avg_l==0: out[i]=100
        else:
            rs=avg_g/avg_l
            out[i]=100-(100/(1+rs))
    return out

def obv_slope(c, v, n=20):
    obv=[0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        if c[i]>c[i-1]: obv.append(obv[-1]+v[i])
        elif c[i]<c[i-1]: obv.append(obv[-1]-v[i])
        else: obv.append(obv[-1])
    out=[0]*len(c)
    for i in range(len(c)):
        out[i] = 0 if i<n else obv[i]-obv[i-n]
    return out

def tanh(x,cap=3.0):
    x=max(-cap,min(cap,x))
    return math.tanh(x)

def subscores_for_tf(ts,c,h,l,v,tf):
    if len(c)<60: return 0.0, {}
    atr14=atr(h,l,c,14)
    at = atr14[-1]
    atp = 0.0 if c[-1]==0 else at/c[-1]

    e12=ema(c,12); e26=ema(c,26)
    s_ema = tanh((e12[-1]-e26[-1])/(1.5*at + 1e-12))

    hist = macd_hist(c)
    scale = st.median([abs(x) for x in hist[-100:]]) or 1.0
    s_macd = tanh(hist[-1]/scale)

    rsi14 = rsi(c,14)
    s_rsi = max(-1.0, min(1.0,(rsi14[-1]-50)/50))

    # ADX light (proxy via variation ATR/price)
    s_adx = max(-1.0, min(1.0, (atp-0.002)/0.01))

    obvs=obv_slope(c,v,20)
    med = st.median([abs(x) for x in obvs[-200:]]) or 1.0
    s_obv = tanh(obvs[-1]/med)

    w = {"ema":0.35,"macd":0.25,"rsi":0.20,"adx":0.10,"obv":0.10}
    gate = ATR_GATE[tf]
    if atp < gate:
        w["ema"]*=0.5; w["macd"]*=0.5
    S = (w["ema"]*s_ema + w["macd"]*s_macd + w["rsi"]*s_rsi + w["adx"]*s_adx + w["obv"]*s_obv) / sum(w.values())
    return S, {"S":S,"atp":atp}

def softmax_probs(S, tau):
    epos = math.exp(S/tau)
    eneg = math.exp(-S/tau)
    Z = epos + 1 + eneg
    return {"pb":epos/Z, "ph":1/Z, "ps":eneg/Z}

def aggregate_probs(per_tf):
    wsum=sum(TF_W.values())
    pb = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["pb"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    ph = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ph"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    ps = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ps"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    Sw = sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["S"]  for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    tot=pb+ph+ps
    if tot<=0: pb=ph=ps=1/3
    else: pb,ph,ps = pb/tot, ph/tot, ps/tot
    out={"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"Sw":Sw}
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        if tf in per_tf:
            out[f"pb_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["pb"]
            out[f"ps_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["ps"]
            out[f"S_{tf}"]= per_tf[tf]["S"]
    return out

def apply_veto_m5(agg):
    pb,ps = agg["pb"], agg["ps"]
    pb30, pb15 = agg.get("pb_30m",0), agg.get("pb_15m",0)
    ps30, ps15 = agg.get("ps_30m",0), agg.get("ps_15m",0)
    S5 = agg.get("S_5m",0.0)
    bull_ok = (pb>=P_ENTER) and (pb30>=0.55) and (pb15>=0.55) and (S5>=0)
    bear_ok = (ps>=P_ENTER) and (ps30>=0.55) and (ps15>=0.55) and (S5<=0)
    if not bull_ok and pb>=P_ENTER: agg["pb"] = max(agg["pb"], P_EXIT-1e-6)
    if not bear_ok and ps>=P_ENTER: agg["ps"] = max(agg["ps"], P_EXIT-1e-6)
    agg["veto5"] = (not bull_ok and pb>=P_ENTER) or (not bear_ok and ps>=P_ENTER)
    return agg

def decide_ctx(pb,ph,ps, prev=None):
    # hystérésis
    if prev=="bull":
        if pb>=P_EXIT: return "bull"
        if ps>=P_ENTER: return "bear"
        return "none" if 0.40<=ph<=0.60 else "none"
    if prev=="bear":
        if ps>=P_EXIT: return "bear"
        if pb>=P_ENTER: return "bull"
        return "none" if 0.40<=ph<=0.60 else "none"
    # neutre
    if pb>=P_ENTER: return "bull"
    if ps>=P_ENTER: return "bear"
    if 0.40<=ph<=0.60: return "range"
    return "none"

def load_ohlcv(symbol, tf):
    p = CAND/f"{tf}/{symbol}.json"
    a = jload(p, [])
    if not a: return None
    ts   = [i[0]//1000 for i in a]
    o,h,l,c,v = zip(*[(i[0]//1000,i[2],i[3],i[4],i[5]) for i in a])  # use high, low, close, volume
    return list(ts), list(c), list(h), list(l), list(v)

def main():
    top=jload(TOPF, {"symbols":[]})
    syms=top.get("symbols",[])[:30]
    if not syms:
        Path(OUTF).write_text(json.dumps({"generated_at":"", "results":[]}))
        print("[A] empty top"); return 0

    results=[]
    freshness_ok=True
    max_data_ts=0

    for s in syms:
        per_tf={}
        for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
            got = load_ohlcv(s, tf)
            if not got: freshness_ok=False; continue
            ts,c,h,l,v = got
            max_data_ts = max(max_data_ts, ts[-1])
            S, extra = subscores_for_tf(ts,c,h,l,v,tf)
            probs = softmax_probs(S, TAU[tf]); probs["S"]=S
            per_tf[tf]=probs

        if not per_tf: continue
        agg = aggregate_probs(per_tf)
        agg = apply_veto_m5(agg)
        ctx = decide_ctx(agg["pb"], agg["ph"], agg["ps"])
        reason=[]
        if agg.get("veto5"): reason.append("veto_5m")
        if ctx=="none": reason.append("unclear")
        result={
            "symbol": s,
            "pb": agg["pb"], "ph": agg["ph"], "ps": agg["ps"],
            "S": agg["Sw"], "ctx": ctx, "reason": ("/".join(reason) if reason else "ok")
        }
        results.append(result)

        # --- Historique JSONL par coin
        rec = {
            "ts": int(time.time()),
            "pb": agg["pb"], "ph": agg["ph"], "ps": agg["ps"],
            "S": agg["Sw"], "ctx": ctx, "reason": result["reason"]
        }
        (HIST_DIR/f"{s.replace('USDT','')}.jsonl").open("a").write(json.dumps(rec, separators=(",",":"))+"\n")

    out = {"generated_at": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()),
           "max_data_ts": max_data_ts,
           "results": results}
    Path(OUTF).write_text(json.dumps(out))
    print(f"[A] n={len(results)} out={OUTF}")
    # diagnostics min set
    b=h=s=none=0
    for r in results:
        m=max(r["pb"],r["ph"],r["ps"])
        if r["pb"]==m: b+=1
        elif r["ps"]==m: s+=1
        elif r["ph"]==m: h+=1
        else: none+=1
    print(b); print(h); print(s)
    return 0

if __name__ == "__main__":
    raise SystemExit(main())

#!/usr/bin/env python3

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, math, sys
from pathlib import Path
from statistics import pstdev
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta

NOW = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
NOW_ISO = NOW.isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")
DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
PARAMS = Path("/opt/scalp/tools/top_params.json")

def load_params():
    p = json.loads(PARAMS.read_text())
    p["exchange"] = p.get("exchange","bitget")
    p["quote"] = p.get("quote","USDT")
    p["top_n"] = int(p.get("top_n",30))
    return p

def iso(ts): 
    return datetime.fromtimestamp(ts/1000, tz=timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

def last_1d_ts(ex, sym):
    try:
        o = ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, timeframe="1d", limit=2)
        return o[-1][0] if o else 0
    except Exception:
        return 0

def stats_7d(ex, sym):
    try:
        o = ex.fetch_ohlcv(sym, timeframe="1h", limit=24*7+1)
    except Exception:
        return (0.0, 0.0)
    if len(o) < 10:
        return (0.0, 0.0)
    trn = 0.0
    rets = []
    prev = o[0][4]
    for _,_,_,_,c,v in o[1:]:
        trn += float(v)*float(c)
        if prev>0 and c>0:
            rets.append(math.log(c/prev))
        prev = c
    vol = float(pstdev(rets)) if rets else 0.0
    return (trn, vol)

def spread_bps(t):
    bid, ask = t.get("bid"), t.get("ask")
    if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0: return 1e9
    mid = 0.5*(bid+ask)
    return 10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid

def norm_rank(d):
    items = sorted(d.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1])
    n = max(1, len(items)-1)
    return {k:i/n for i,(k,_) in enumerate(items)}

def main():
    import ccxt
    params = load_params()
    EX, QUOTE, N = params["exchange"], params["quote"], params["top_n"]
    flt, w = params["filters"], params["scoring"]

    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    symbols = [s for s in ex.symbols if s.endswith(f"/{QUOTE}")]

    # 1) coins_90d.json
    cutoff_ms = int((NOW - timedelta(days=90)).timestamp()*1000)
    inactive = []
    for s in symbols:
        if last_1d_ts(ex, s) < cutoff_ms:
            inactive.append(s.replace("/",""))
    (DATA/"coins_90d.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "source":"ccxt-1d-90d",
        "exchange":EX, "quote":QUOTE, "cutoff_days":90,
        "inactive_symbols": sorted(inactive)
    }, indent=2))

    # 2) filtres rapides
    tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols)
    def base(sym): return sym.split("/")[0]
    bad_kw = tuple(flt["exclude_leveraged_keywords"])
    bad_bases = set(flt["exclude_bases"])
    min_qv = float(flt["min_quote_vol_24h"])
    max_sp = float(flt["max_spread_bps"])

    pool = []
    for s in symbols:
        s_flat = s.replace("/","")
        if s_flat in inactive: 
            continue
        b = base(s)
        if any(k in b for k in bad_kw): 
            continue
        if b in bad_bases: 
            continue
        t = tickers.get(s, {})
        qv = float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        sp = spread_bps(t)
        if qv < min_qv or sp > max_sp: 
            continue
        pool.append(s)

    # 3) mesures
    vol24, turn7, vola7, spd = {}, {}, {}, {}
    for s in pool:
        t = tickers.get(s, {})
        vol24[s] = float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        spd[s] = spread_bps(t)
        trn, vol = stats_7d(ex, s)
        turn7[s], vola7[s] = trn, vol

    # 4) scoring principal
    ranked = []
    if pool:
        r1, r2, r3, r4 = norm_rank(vol24), norm_rank(turn7), norm_rank(vola7), norm_rank(spd)
        score = {s: (
            w["w_volume24h"]   * r1.get(s,0.0) +
            w["w_turnover7d"]  * r2.get(s,0.0) +
            w["w_volatility7d"]* r3.get(s,0.0) +
            w["w_spread"]      * r4.get(s,0.0)
        ) for s in pool}
        ranked = sorted(score.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1], reverse=True)

    # 4b) fallback si pool vide: top par volume 24h sur tout l'univers actif
    if not ranked:
        vol_all = {s: float(tickers.get(s,{}).get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
                   for s in symbols if s.replace("/","") not in inactive}
        ranked = sorted(vol_all.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1], reverse=True)

    top_syms = [sym.replace("/","") for sym,_ in ranked[:N]]

    # 5) sorties
    (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "source": "coins_90d+advanced",
        "exchange": EX,
        "quote": QUOTE,
        "symbols": top_syms
    }, indent=2))

    # détail pour affichage
    ranked_out = []
    for sym, sc in ranked[:N]:
        t = tickers.get(sym, {})
        ranked_out.append({
            "symbol": sym.replace("/",""),
            "score": round(float(sc), 6),
            "volume24h_quote": float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0),
            "turnover7d": float(turn7.get(sym, 0.0)),
            "volatility7d": float(vola7.get(sym, 0.0)),
            "spread_bps": float(spd.get(sym, 1e9))
        })
    (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "n": len(top_syms),
        "items": ranked_out
    }, indent=2))

    print(f"[top] pool={len(symbols)} pre={len(pool)} inactive90d={len(inactive)} top={len(top_syms)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CBASE=DATA/"candles"; (CBASE/"1m").mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
AOUT=DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
LIMIT=520

def ex():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })
EX=ex()

def b2ccxt(sym): return sym.replace("_UMCBL","/USDT:USDT")

def drop_incomplete(rows):
    if not rows: return rows
    if int(time.time()*1000) - rows[-1][0] < int(0.9*60*1000): return rows[:-1]
    return rows

def load_active_symbols():
    try:
        arr=json.loads((AOUT).read_text() or "[]")
        return [r["symbol"] for r in arr if r.get("context","none")!="none"]
    except: return []

def save_1m(sym, rows):
    out={"generated_at": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()),
         "tf":"1m","symbol":sym,"limit":LIMIT,"data":rows}
    (CBASE/"1m"/f"{sym}.json").write_text(json.dumps(out))

def main():
    syms=load_active_symbols()
    ok=0; errs=[]
    for s in syms:
        try:
            rows=EX.fetch_ohlcv(b2ccxt(s), timeframe="1m", limit=LIMIT)
            rows=drop_incomplete(rows)
            if len(rows)<100: raise RuntimeError("too few bars")
            save_1m(s, rows); ok+=1
        except Exception as e:
            errs.append({"symbol":s,"err":str(e)[:140]})
    (DATA/"debug/candles_refresh_subset_1m.json").write_text(json.dumps(
        {"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()),"updated":ok,"errors":errs}, indent=2))
    print(f"[subset_1m] updated={ok} errors={len(errs)}")
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, sys
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta

# Config
EXCHANGE = "bitget"
QUOTE = "USDT"
TOP_N = 30
NOW_ISO = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
OUT_90D = DATA/"coins_90d.json"
OUT_TOP = DATA/"top.json"

def ts_ms_to_iso(tsms:int)->str:
    return datetime.fromtimestamp(tsms/1000, tz=timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

def main():
    try:
        import ccxt
    except Exception as e:
        print("ccxt requis:", e, file=sys.stderr); sys.exit(1)

    ex = getattr(ccxt, EXCHANGE)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    symbols = [s for s in ex.symbols if s.endswith(f"/{QUOTE}")]

    # Détecter inactivité >90j avec OHLCV 1d
    cutoff = datetime.now(timezone.utc) - timedelta(days=90)
    cutoff_ms = int(cutoff.timestamp()*1000)

    inactive = []
    last_seen = {}
    for s in symbols:
        try:
            ohlcv = ex.fetch_ohlcv(s, timeframe="1d", limit=2)
            if not ohlcv:
                inactive.append(s.replace("/",""))
                continue
            last_ts = ohlcv[-1][0]
            last_seen[s] = last_ts
            if last_ts < cutoff_ms:
                inactive.append(s.replace("/",""))
        except Exception:
            # En cas d'erreur API, ne classe pas en TOP par prudence
            inactive.append(s.replace("/",""))

    # Mesurer liquidité 24h via tickers
    tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols)
    def vol_quote(sym):
        t = tickers.get(sym, {})
        v = t.get("quoteVolume")
        # Fallback si absent
        return float(v) if v is not None else 0.0

    # Construire TOP hors inactifs >90j
    actives = [s for s in symbols if s.replace("/","") not in inactive]
    actives.sort(key=lambda s: vol_quote(s), reverse=True)
    top_syms = [s.replace("/","") for s in actives[:TOP_N]]

    # Écrire coins_90d.json
    coins_90d = {
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "source": "ccxt-1d-90d",
        "exchange": EXCHANGE,
        "quote": QUOTE,
        "cutoff_days": 90,
        "inactive_symbols": sorted(inactive),
        "notes": "Pairs dont la dernière bougie 1d est plus vieille que 90 jours, exclues du top30."
    }
    OUT_90D.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    tmp = OUT_90D.with_suffix(".tmp")
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(coins_90d, indent=2))
    tmp.replace(OUT_90D)

    # Écrire top.json
    top = {
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "source": "coins_90d",
        "exchange": EXCHANGE,
        "quote": QUOTE,
        "symbols": top_syms
    }
    tmp = OUT_TOP.with_suffix(".tmp")
    tmp.write_text(json.dumps(top, indent=2))
    tmp.replace(OUT_TOP)

    # Sortie console utile
    print(f"[rebuild_top] top={len(top_syms)} inactive_90d={len(inactive)}")
    if last_seen:
        worst = min(last_seen.values())
        print(f"[rebuild_top] oldest_last_ts={ts_ms_to_iso(worst)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
----- FILE END -----

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import time, json
from urllib.parse import urlencode
from urllib.request import Request, urlopen
from urllib.error import URLError, HTTPError
BASE="https://api.bitget.com"
def _get(path, params=None, tries=4, timeout=12):
    q=f"{BASE}{path}"+(f"?{urlencode(params)}" if params else "")
    for i in range(tries):
        try:
            req=Request(q, headers={"Accept":"application/json"})
            with urlopen(req, timeout=timeout) as r:
                return json.loads(r.read().decode("utf-8"))
        except (URLError,HTTPError):
            if i+1>=tries: raise
            time.sleep(0.6*(2**i))
def normalize_symbol(sym):
    s=sym.replace("-","_").upper()
    return (s.replace("_UMCBL",""), "usdt-futures")
def history_candles(sym, granularity="1m", limit=200, end_ms=None):
    s, prod=normalize_symbol(sym)
    p={"symbol":s,"granularity":granularity,"limit":int(limit),"productType":prod}
    if end_ms: p["endTime"]=int(end_ms)
    j=_get("/api/v2/mix/market/history-candles", p)
    raw=j.get("data",[]) if isinstance(j,dict) else j
    out=[]
    for k in raw:
        try:
            ts=int(k[0]); o,h,l,c=map(float,k[1:5]); v=float(k[5])
            out.append({"ts":ts,"o":o,"h":h,"l":l,"c":c,"v":v})
        except: pass
    out.sort(key=lambda x:x["ts"])
    return out
def ticker_price(sym):
    s, prod=normalize_symbol(sym)
    j=_get("/api/v2/mix/market/ticker", {"productType":prod,"symbol":s})
    d=(j or {}).get("data",{})
    p=d.get("last") or d.get("lastPr") or d.get("close") or d.get("markPrice")
    return float(p) if p is not None else None

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
TOP=/opt/scalp/data/top.json
C90=/opt/scalp/data/coins_90d.json

jq -e '(.symbols|type=="array") and (.source|test("coins_90d"))' "$TOP" >/dev/null || { echo "top.json invalide"; exit 1; }
jq -e '.source=="ccxt-1d-90d" and (.inactive_symbols|type=="array")' "$C90" >/dev/null || { echo "coins_90d.json invalide"; exit 1; }

# Intersection vide entre inactifs et top
bad=$(jq -r '.inactive_symbols[]' "$C90" | grep -Fx -f <(jq -r '.symbols[]' "$TOP") || true)
[ -z "$bad" ] || { echo "Conflit (>90j) dans top.json:"; echo "$bad"; exit 2; }

echo "OK"
