#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); CAND=DATA/"candles"
AOUT=DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"; TOP=DATA/"top.json"
LIMIT=600
TF_LIST=["1m","3m"]               # pour Analyse B

def ex():
    import ccxt
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })

def norm_symbol(mkts, base):
    if base in mkts: return base
    if base.endswith("_UMCBL"):
        q=base.split("_")[0].replace("USDT","/USDT:USDT")
        if q in mkts: return q
    if base.endswith("USDT"):
        q=base.replace("USDT","/USDT:USDT")
        if q in mkts: return q
        q=base.replace("USDT","/USDT")
        if q in mkts: return q
    for k in mkts:
        if k.replace(":USDT","").replace("/","").upper()==base.replace("_UMCBL","").upper():
            return k
    return None

def drop_incomplete(rows, tf):
    tf_s={"1m":60,"3m":180}[tf]; now=int(time.time()); last=int(rows[-1][0]//1000)
    if now-last < int(0.9*tf_s): rows=rows[:-1]
    return rows

def save_json(path, rows):
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    path.write_text(json.dumps({"ts":int(time.time()),"data":rows}))

def subset_symbols():
    syms=[]
    try:
        a=json.loads(AOUT.read_text())
        syms=[r.get("symbol") for r in a if r.get("context") in ("buy","sell","hold")]
    except: pass
    if not syms:
        try:
            t=json.loads(TOP.read_text()); syms=t.get("symbols",[])[:30]
        except: pass
    return list(dict.fromkeys(syms))  # unique et ordre conservé

def main():
    e=ex(); mkts=e.load_markets()
    syms=subset_symbols()
    ok=wrote=0
    for base in syms:
        sid=norm_symbol(mkts, base)
        if not sid: continue
        for tf in TF_LIST:
            try:
                rows=e.fetch_ohlcv(sid, timeframe=tf, limit=LIMIT)
                rows=drop_incomplete(rows, tf)
                if len(rows)<200: continue
                save_json(CAND/tf/f"{base}.json", rows)
                wrote+=1
            except: pass
        ok+=1
    print(f"[candles_refresh_1m3m_subset] in={len(syms)} ok={ok} wrote={wrote}")
if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time
from pathlib import Path

def g(n,v,l=None):
    if v is None: return
    if isinstance(v,bool): v=1 if v else 0
    lbl="" if not l else "{"+",".join([f'{k}=\"{str(x)}\"' for k,x in l.items()])+"}"
    L.append(f"{n}{lbl} {v}")

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, os
from pathlib import Path
from urllib.parse import urlencode
from urllib.request import Request, urlopen
from bitget_http import history_candles

BASE="https://api.bitget.com"
D=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); D.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
F_CON=D/"contracts_usdt.json"
F_OK =D/"coins_90d.json"
F_PENDING=D/"coins_pending.json"
F_DBG=D/"debug/coins_scan_1d.json"

SEED=["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","XRPUSDT","SOLUSDT","BNBUSDT","ADAUSDT","DOGEUSDT","LTCUSDT","LINKUSDT","DOTUSDT"]

def http_get(path, params=None, tries=4, timeout=12):
    q=f"{BASE}{path}"+(f"?{urlencode(params)}" if params else "")
    hdr={"Accept":"application/json","User-Agent":"scalp-bot/1.0"}
    last=None
    for i in range(tries):
        try:
            with urlopen(Request(q, headers=hdr), timeout=timeout) as r:
                import json as _j; return _j.loads(r.read().decode("utf-8"))
        except Exception as e:
            last=e; time.sleep(0.5*(2**i))
    raise last

def list_usdt_contracts():
    try:
        j=http_get("/api/v2/mix/market/contracts", {"productType":"umcbl"})
        data=(j or {}).get("data",[]) if isinstance(j,dict) else (j or [])
        s=sorted({str(d.get("symbol","")).upper() for d in data if str(d.get("symbol","")).upper().endswith("USDT")})
        return s or SEED
    except Exception:
        return SEED

def atomic_write(path: Path, obj):
    tmp=path.with_suffix(".tmp"); tmp.write_text(json.dumps(obj,indent=2)+"\n"); os.replace(tmp, path)

def main():
    now_ms=int(time.time()*1000)
    need90=now_ms-90*24*3600*1000
    need80=now_ms-80*24*3600*1000

    syms=list_usdt_contracts()
    atomic_write(F_CON, syms)

    ok=[]; pending=[]; meta=[]
    for s in syms:
        try:
            k=history_candles(s,"1d",limit=120)  # 1 appel par coin
            if not k:
                # pas de données -> garder en pending pour recheck
                pending.append(f"{s}_UMCBL"); meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"nodata"})
                continue
            first_ts=k[0]["ts"]
            if first_ts<=need90:
                ok.append(f"{s}_UMCBL"); meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"ok90","first_ts":first_ts,"rows":len(k)})
            elif first_ts<=need80:
                pending.append(f"{s}_UMCBL"); meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"pending80","first_ts":first_ts,"rows":len(k)})
            else:
                meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"too_young","first_ts":first_ts,"rows":len(k)})
        except Exception as e:
            pending.append(f"{s}_UMCBL"); meta.append({"symbol":s,"status":"error","err":str(e)})

    ts=time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())
    atomic_write(F_OK, {"symbols":ok,"generated_at":ts,"source":"bitget-1d-90d"})
    atomic_write(F_PENDING, {"symbols":pending,"generated_at":ts,"note":"check next run (>=80d)"})
    atomic_write(F_DBG, {"ts":ts,"total":len(syms),"ok90":len(ok),"pending80_or_err":len(pending),"details":meta})
    print(f"[usdt 1d] total={len(syms)} ok90={len(ok)} pending={len(pending)}")
if __name__=="__main__": main()

import math
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
W=dict(EMA=0.35,MACD=0.25,RSI=0.20,ADX=0.10,OBV=0.10)
TAU={"30m":0.35,"15m":0.30,"5m":0.25}
TF_W={"30m":0.50,"15m":0.30,"5m":0.20}
ATR_GATE={"30m":0.25,"15m":0.18,"5m":0.12}
P_ENTER=0.60
P_EXIT=0.45
RANGE_LOW,RANGE_HIGH=0.40,0.60
PERSIST_BARS=2
def clip(x,lo,hi):return hi if x>hi else lo if x<lo else x
def tanh(x):return math.tanh(x)
def softmax_triple(S,tau):
    e1=math.exp(S/tau); e2=math.exp(-S/tau); d=e1+1.0+e2
    return e1/d,1.0/d,e2/d
def score_tf(inp,tf):
    atr=max(inp.get("atr14",0.0),1e-12)
    s_ema=tanh((inp.get("ema12",0.0)-inp.get("ema26",0.0))/(1.5*atr))
    sigma=max(inp.get("macd_sigma100",1e-12),1e-12)
    s_macd=tanh(inp.get("macd_hist",0.0)/sigma)
    s_rsi=clip((inp.get("rsi14",50.0)-50.0)/50.0,-1.0,1.0)
    s_adx=clip((inp.get("adx14",20.0)-20.0)/20.0,-1.0,1.0)
    med=max(inp.get("obv_medabs200",1e-12),1e-12)
    s_obv=tanh(inp.get("obv_delta20",0.0)/med)
    reasons=[]
    atr_pct=float(inp.get("atr_pct",0.0))
    if atr_pct<ATR_GATE[tf]:
        s_ema*=0.5; s_macd*=0.5; reasons.append(f"gate_atr_{tf}")
    num=(W["EMA"]*s_ema+W["MACD"]*s_macd+W["RSI"]*s_rsi+W["ADX"]*s_adx+W["OBV"]*s_obv)
    S=clip(num/sum(W.values()),-1.0,1.0)
    pb,ph,ps=softmax_triple(S,TAU[tf])
    return {"S":S,"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"reasons":reasons}
def aggregate_probs(per_tf):
    wsum=sum(TF_W.values())
    pb=sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["pb"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    ph=sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ph"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    ps=sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["ps"] for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    Sw=sum(TF_W[tf]*per_tf[tf]["S"]  for tf in TF_W if tf in per_tf)/wsum
    tot=pb+ph+ps
    pb,ph,ps=(1/3,1/3,1/3) if tot<=0 else (pb/tot,ph/tot,ps/tot)
    out={"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"Sw":Sw}
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        if tf in per_tf:
            out[f"pb_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["pb"]; out[f"ps_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["ps"]; out[f"S_{tf}"]=per_tf[tf]["S"]
    return out
def apply_veto_m5(agg,reasons):
    pb,ps=agg["pb"],agg["ps"]
    pb30,pb15=agg.get("pb_30m",0.0),agg.get("pb_15m",0.0)
    ps30,ps15=agg.get("ps_30m",0.0),agg.get("ps_15m",0.0)
    S5=agg.get("S_5m",0.0)
    bull_ok=(pb>=P_ENTER) and (pb30>=0.55) and (pb15>=0.55) and (S5>=0.0)
    bear_ok=(ps>=P_ENTER) and (ps30>=0.55) and (ps15>=0.55) and (S5<=0.0)
    if pb>=P_ENTER and not bull_ok: reasons.append("veto5_buy"); agg["pb"]=max(agg["pb"],P_EXIT-1e-6)
    if ps>=P_ENTER and not bear_ok: reasons.append("veto5_sell"); agg["ps"]=max(agg["ps"],P_EXIT-1e-6)
    tot=agg["pb"]+agg["ph"]+agg["ps"]
    if tot>0: agg["pb"],agg["ph"],agg["ps"]=agg["pb"]/tot,agg["ph"]/tot,agg["ps"]/tot
    return agg
@dataclass
class CtxState:
    ctx:str="none"; streak_ctx:str="none"; streak:int=0; bars_in_ctx:int=0
def decide_next_ctx(prob,prev_ctx,reasons):
    pb,ph,ps=prob["pb"],prob["ph"],prob["ps"]
    buy_ok=(pb>=P_ENTER) or (prev_ctx=="buy" and pb>=P_EXIT)
    sell_ok=(ps>=P_ENTER) or (prev_ctx=="sell" and ps>=P_EXIT)
    range_ok=(RANGE_LOW<=ph<=RANGE_HIGH)
    if buy_ok and pb>=ps and pb>=ph: reasons.append("enter_buy" if pb>=P_ENTER else "hold_buy"); return "buy"
    if sell_ok and ps>=pb and ps>=ph: reasons.append("enter_sell" if ps>=P_ENTER else "hold_sell"); return "sell"
    if range_ok: reasons.append("range_band"); return "hold"
    reasons.append("under_thresholds"); return "none"
def update_context(state,prob,reasons,bar_closed=True):
    target=decide_next_ctx(prob,state.ctx,reasons)
    if target==state.ctx:
        if state.streak>=PERSIST_BARS: reasons.append("persistence_ok")
        return CtxState(ctx=state.ctx,streak_ctx=target,streak=min(state.streak+1,PERSIST_BARS),bars_in_ctx=state.bars_in_ctx+(1 if bar_closed else 0))
    streak=state.streak+1 if target==state.streak_ctx else 1
    if streak>=PERSIST_BARS:
        reasons.append("persistence_ok")
        return CtxState(ctx=target,streak_ctx=target,streak=streak,bars_in_ctx=1 if bar_closed else 0)
    else:
        reasons.append("persistence_wait")
        return CtxState(ctx=state.ctx,streak_ctx=target,streak=streak,bars_in_ctx=state.bars_in_ctx+(1 if bar_closed else 0))
def compute_ctx(per_tf_inputs,prev_state):
    per_tf={tf:score_tf(per_tf_inputs[tf],tf) for tf in per_tf_inputs}
    agg=aggregate_probs(per_tf)
    reasons=[]
    for tf in per_tf: reasons+=per_tf[tf].get("reasons",[])
    agg=apply_veto_m5(agg,reasons)
    new_state=update_context(prev_state,agg,reasons,bar_closed=True)
    ints={k:int(round(10*agg[k])) for k in ("pb","ph","ps")}
    return {"pb":agg["pb"],"ph":agg["ph"],"ps":agg["ps"],"Sw":agg["Sw"],"ctx_state":new_state,"ints":ints,"per_tf":per_tf,"agg":agg,"reasons":reasons[:8]}

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, math, sys
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
TOPF = DATA/"top.json"

TF_CFG = {"5m":300, "15m":900, "30m":1800}
SAFETY_LAG = 5        # secondes post close avant d'accepter la bougie
MAX_PER_SYMBOL = 400  # profondeur locale max par TF

def now_s(): return int(time.time())
def read_json(p, d=None):
    try: return json.loads(Path(p).read_text())
    except Exception: return d

def bitget():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "enableRateLimit": True,
        "options": {"defaultType": "swap"},
    })

def tf_to_ccxt(tf): return tf   # ccxt accepte '5m','15m','30m'

def fp(symbol, tf): 
    return CAND/f"{tf}/{symbol}.json"

def load_local(symbol, tf):
    p = fp(symbol, tf)
    if not p.exists(): return []
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except Exception: return []

def save_local(symbol, tf, arr):
    p = fp(symbol, tf)
    p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(arr, separators=(",",":")))

def last_ts(arr): 
    return 0 if not arr else int(arr[-1][0])//1000

def aligned_floor(ts, step):  # floor(ts to step)
    return (ts//step)*step

def fetch_append(ex, symbol, tf, limit_keep):
    step = TF_CFG[tf]
    local = load_local(symbol, tf)
    last = last_ts(local)

    # on ne demande une nouvelle bougie QUE si la bougie vient d’être close + SAFETY_LAG
    t = now_s()
    last_close = aligned_floor(t, step)
    if t < last_close + SAFETY_LAG:
        # dernière bougie pas encore «finalisée» : on ne touche à rien
        return local, False

    # since : on repart un peu avant la dernière pour éviter trous
    since = (last - 3*step) * 1000 if last else (t - limit_keep*step)*1000
    try:
        ohlcv = ex.fetch_ohlcv(symbol, tf_to_ccxt(tf), since=since, limit=limit_keep+10)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[fetch] {symbol} {tf} error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
        return local, False

    # dédoublonnage (ts croissants, millis)
    merged = {int(a[0]):a for a in local}
    for a in ohlcv:
        merged[int(a[0])] = a
    out = [merged[k] for k in sorted(merged.keys())]
    # bornage mémoire (MAX_PER_SYMBOL)
    out = out[-MAX_PER_SYMBOL:]

    # validité : ne garder que bougies <= last_close (donc closes)
    out = [a for a in out if int(a[0])//1000 <= last_close]

    changed = (len(out) != len(local)) or (last_ts(out) != last)
    if changed:
        save_local(symbol, tf, out)
    return out, changed

def main():
    top = read_json(TOPF, {"symbols":[]})
    syms = top.get("symbols", [])
    if not syms:
        print("top.json vide, skip"); return 0

    ex = bitget()
    ok=skip=err=0
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        for s in syms:
            try:
                _, changed = fetch_append(ex, s, tf, MAX_PER_SYMBOL)
                ok += 1 if changed else 0
                skip += 0 if changed else 1
            except Exception as e:
                err += 1
                print(f"[{s} {tf}] EXC {e}", file=sys.stderr)
    print(json.dumps({"ok":ok,"skip":skip,"err":err,"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())}))
    return 0

if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())

    jsave(sigf, arr)

print(json.dumps({"n":len(out), "signals":len(signals)}))

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, time, hmac, hashlib, base64, requests

BASE = "https://api.bitget.com"

def sign(message: str, secret: str) -> str:
    return base64.b64encode(
        hmac.new(secret.encode(), message.encode(), hashlib.sha256).digest()
    ).decode()

def auth_headers(path: str, method="GET", body="") -> dict:
    api_key     = os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY")
    api_secret  = os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET")
    passphrase  = os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE")
    ts          = str(int(time.time() * 1000))
    prehash     = ts + method.upper() + path + body
    sig         = sign(prehash, api_secret)
    return {
        "ACCESS-KEY": api_key,
        "ACCESS-SIGN": sig,
        "ACCESS-TIMESTAMP": ts,
        "ACCESS-PASSPHRASE": passphrase,
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    }

def main():
    # --- public check (no auth needed) ---
    r = requests.get(BASE + "/api/v2/mix/market/contracts", params={"productType":"usdt-futures"})
    print("[PUBLIC]", r.status_code, r.text[:200])

    # --- private check (auth required) ---
    path = "/api/v2/user/fee/query"
    url  = BASE + path
    r = requests.get(url, headers=auth_headers(path))
    print("[PRIVATE]", r.status_code, r.text[:200])

if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import requests

BASE = "https://api.bitget.com"

def get_ohlcv(symbol="BTCUSDT_UMCBL", granularity="1day", limit=5):
    """
    Récupère les bougies OHLCV pour un symbole donné
    granularity: "1min", "5min", "15min", "1hour", "4hour", "1day", "1week"
    limit: nombre de bougies à récupérer
    """
    path = "/api/v2/mix/market/candles"
    params = {
        "symbol": symbol,
        "granularity": granularity,
        "limit": limit
    }
    try:
        r = requests.get(BASE + path, params=params, timeout=10)
        r.raise_for_status()
        return r.status_code, r.json()
    except Exception as e:
        return 500, {"error": str(e)}

if __name__ == "__main__":
    code, data = get_ohlcv()
    print("[OHLCV]", code)
    print(data)

#!/usr/bin/env bash

import os, time, ccxt, math
ex=ccxt.bitget({
  "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
  "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
  "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
  "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
  "enableRateLimit": True,
})
# temps serveur Bitget en ms
srv_ms = ex.milliseconds()
loc_ms = int(time.time()*1000)
offset = srv_ms - loc_ms  # positif si serveur "en avance"
# calcul du prochain top de minute côté serveur
next_min = ((srv_ms//60000)+1)*60000
sleep_ms = (next_min - srv_ms) + 800  # +0.8s de marge
if sleep_ms>0:
    time.sleep(sleep_ms/1000.0)
print(f"[sync] offset_ms={offset} slept_ms={sleep_ms}")

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
LOG="/opt/scalp/logs/priority_runner.log"; mkdir -p /opt/scalp/logs
now_s=$(date +%s)

jget_ts() {
  # lit .generated_at sinon mtime
  local f="$1" ; local ttl="$2"
  if [ ! -s "$f" ]; then echo "0"; return; fi
  if command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    local ts
    ts=$(jq -r '.generated_at // empty' "$f" 2>/dev/null || true)
    if [ -n "$ts" ]; then date -d "$ts" +%s 2>/dev/null || echo "0"; return; fi
  fi
  stat -c %Y "$f" 2>/dev/null || echo "0"
}

fresh() {
  # fresh <file> <ttl_seconds>
  local f="$1" ttl="$2"
  local ft; ft=$(jget_ts "$f" "$ttl")
  [ "$ft" -gt 0 ] && [ $(( now_s - ft )) -lt "$ttl" ]
}

echo "$(date -Is) tick:start" >>"$LOG"

# TTL
TTL_COINS90=$((48*3600))
TTL_TOP=$((2*3600))
TTL_A=$((5*60))

F_COINS="/opt/scalp/data/coins_90d.json"
F_TOP="/opt/scalp/data/top.json"
F_A="/opt/scalp/data/analyse_A_out.json"

# 1) Univers USDT >=90j (48h)
if ! fresh "$F_COINS" "$TTL_COINS90"; then
  echo "$(date -Is) refresh coins_90d" >>"$LOG"
  /usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/filter_contracts_usdt_ccxt.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
fi

# 2) Top (2h)
if ! fresh "$F_TOP" "$TTL_TOP"; then
  echo "$(date -Is) refresh OHLCV only (top.json protected)" >>"$LOG"
  /usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/filter_top.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
fi

# 3) Analyse A (5min) -> ne rafraîchit TF que si A expiré
if ! fresh "$F_A" "$TTL_A"; then
  echo "$(date -Is) refresh A (TF 30/15/5 + A)" >>"$LOG"
  /usr/bin/env python3 /opt/scalp/tools/candles_refresh_tf.py >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
  /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_a_guard.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true
fi

# 4) Analyse B chaque minute, sync 1m (coins ctx != none) puis B
/opt/scalp/tools/run_b_synced.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || /opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_guard.sh >>"$LOG" 2>&1 || true

echo "$(date -Is) tick:end" >>"$LOG"

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, math, argparse, statistics as stats
from pathlib import Path

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CBASE=DATA/"candles"
OUT =DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
STATE=Path("/opt/scalp/run/a_state.json")

# Tuning
W_EMA,W_MACD,W_RSI,W_ADX,W_OBV = 0.35,0.25,0.20,0.10,0.10
TAU = {"30m":0.35,"15m":0.30,"5m":0.25}
ALPHA={"30m":0.5,"15m":0.3,"5m":0.2}
ATR_GATE={"30m":0.0025,"15m":0.0018,"5m":0.0012}

def ema(x,n):
    if not x: return []
    k=2/(n+1); o=[x[0]]
    for v in x[1:]: o.append(o[-1]+k*(v-o[-1]))
    return o
def stdev(x):
    if len(x)<2: return 0.0
    mu=sum(x)/len(x)
    return (sum((v-mu)**2 for v in x)/len(x))**0.5
def atr(h,l,c,n=14):
    trs=[]; prev=c[0]
    for i in range(len(c)):
        trs.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-prev), abs(l[i]-prev))); prev=c[i]
    return ema(trs,n)
def macd_hist(c, fast=12, slow=26, sig=9):
    m=[a-b for a,b in zip(ema(c,fast), ema(c,slow))]
    s=ema(m,sig); n=min(len(m),len(s))
    return [m[-n+i]-s[-n+i] for i in range(n)]
def rsi(c,n=14):
    if len(c)<n+1: return [50.0]*len(c)
    g=[0.0]; d=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        ch=c[i]-c[i-1]; g.append(max(ch,0.0)); d.append(max(-ch,0.0))
    ag=ema(g,n); ad=ema(d,n)
    out=[]
    for x,y in zip(ag,ad):
        rs=x/(y+1e-12); out.append(100-100/(1+rs))
    return out
def adx(h,l,c,n=14):
    if len(c)<n+1: return [20.0]*len(c)
    pd=[0.0]; md=[0.0]; TR=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        up=h[i]-h[i-1]; dn=l[i-1]-l[i]
        pd.append(up if (up>dn and up>0) else 0.0)
        md.append(dn if (dn>up and dn>0) else 0.0)
        TR.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-c[i-1]), abs(l[i]-c[i-1])))
    pdi=[100*(x/(y+1e-12)) for x,y in zip(ema(pd,n), ema(TR,n))]
    mdi=[100*(x/(y+1e-12)) for x,y in zip(ema(md,n), ema(TR,n))]
    DX=[100*abs(a-b)/(a+b+1e-12) for a,b in zip(pdi,mdi)]
    return ema(DX,n)
def obv(c,v):
    o=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        o.append(o[-1] + (v[i] if c[i]>c[i-1] else (-v[i] if c[i]<c[i-1] else 0.0)))
    return o

def load_tf(sym, tf):
    p=CBASE/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    j=json.loads(p.read_text())
    k=j["data"]
    if len(k)<500: raise RuntimeError(f"{sym} {tf} <500 bars")
    # colonnes
    o=[r[1] for r in k]; h=[r[2] for r in k]; l=[r[3] for r in k]; c=[r[4] for r in k]; v=[r[5] for r in k]
    return o,h,l,c,v,k[-1][0]

def subscores_tf(o,h,l,c,v, tf):
    # EMA spread / ATR gate
    atr14 = atr(h,l,c,14)[-1]
    base = max(1.5*atr14,1e-9)
    s_ema = math.tanh( (ema(c,12)[-1] - ema(c,26)[-1]) / base )

    # MACD hist / sigma100
    hist = macd_hist(c)
    sigma = stdev(hist[-100:]) if len(hist)>=100 else stdev(hist)
    s_macd = math.tanh( (hist[-1])/(sigma+1e-12) )

    # RSI
    s_rsi = max(-1.0,min(1.0,(rsi(c,14)[-1]-50.0)/50.0))

    # ADX
    s_adx = max(-1.0,min(1.0,(adx(h,l,c,14)[-1]-20.0)/20.0))

    # OBV slope(20)/median(|OBV|_200)
    ob = obv(c,v)
    slope = ob[-1]-ob[-21] if len(ob)>=21 else 0.0
    denom = stats.median([abs(x) for x in (ob[-200:] if len(ob)>=200 else ob)]) or 1.0
    s_obv = math.tanh(slope/denom)

    # ATR% gate
    gate = (atr14 / c[-1]) < ATR_GATE[tf]
    w_ema = W_EMA*0.5 if gate else W_EMA
    w_macd= W_MACD*0.5 if gate else W_MACD
    num = w_ema*s_ema + w_macd*s_macd + W_RSI*s_rsi + W_ADX*s_adx + W_OBV*s_obv
    den = (w_ema + w_macd + W_RSI + W_ADX + W_OBV)
    S = num/den if den>0 else 0.0

    # Softmax tri-state
    t=TAU[tf]
    epos=math.exp(S/t); eneg=math.exp(-S/t); den3=epos+1+eneg
    pb=epos/den3; ph=1/den3; ps=eneg/den3

    return {"S":S,"pb":pb,"ph":ph,"ps":ps,"atrpct":atr14/c[-1]}

def persist(symbol, candidate, bar_ts):
    try: st=json.loads(STATE.read_text() or "{}")
    except: st={}
    rec=st.get(symbol, {"last":"none","streak":0,"ts":0})
    if candidate!="none":
        if rec["last"]==candidate and rec.get("ts")!=bar_ts:
            rec["streak"]=min(2, rec.get("streak",0)+1)
        else:
            rec["streak"]=1
        rec["last"]=candidate; rec["ts"]=bar_ts
    else:
        if rec.get("ts")!=bar_ts:
            rec={"last":"none","streak":0,"ts":bar_ts}
    st[symbol]=rec
    STATE.write_text(json.dumps(st))
    return candidate if rec["streak"]>=2 else "none"

def decide_context(pb,ph,ps,res):
    bull = pb>=0.60 and (res["30m"]["pb"]>=0.55) and (res["15m"]["pb"]>=0.55)
    bear = ps>=0.60 and (res["30m"]["ps"]>=0.55) and (res["15m"]["ps"]>=0.55)
    veto_buy = res["5m"]["S"]<0
    veto_sell= res["5m"]["S"]>0
    if bull and not veto_buy: return "buy"
    if bear and not veto_sell: return "sell"
    if 0.40 <= res["30m"]["ph"] <= 0.60: return "hold"
    return "none"

def upsert_out(rec):
    try: arr=json.loads(OUT.read_text() or "[]")
    except: arr=[]
    m={r["symbol"]:i for i,r in enumerate(arr) if isinstance(r,dict) and "symbol" in r}
    if rec["symbol"] in m:
        arr[m[rec["symbol"]]]=rec
    else:
        arr.append(rec)
    OUT.write_text(json.dumps(arr, indent=2))

def main():
    ap=argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--symbol", required=True)
    a=ap.parse_args()
    sym=a.symbol

    # load TFs
    o30,h30,l30,c30,v30,ts30 = load_tf(sym,"30m")
    o15,h15,l15,c15,v15,ts15 = load_tf(sym,"15m")
    o5 ,h5 ,l5 ,c5 ,v5 ,ts5  = load_tf(sym,"5m")

    r30=subscores_tf(o30,h30,l30,c30,v30,"30m")
    r15=subscores_tf(o15,h15,l15,c15,v15,"15m")
    r5 =subscores_tf(o5 ,h5 ,l5 ,c5 ,v5 ,"5m")

    # agrégation
    S = ALPHA["30m"]*r30["S"] + ALPHA["15m"]*r15["S"] + ALPHA["5m"]*r5["S"]
    pb= ALPHA["30m"]*r30["pb"]+ ALPHA["15m"]*r15["pb"]+ ALPHA["5m"]*r5["pb"]
    ph= ALPHA["30m"]*r30["ph"]+ ALPHA["15m"]*r15["ph"]+ ALPHA["5m"]*r5["ph"]
    ps= ALPHA["30m"]*r30["ps"]+ ALPHA["15m"]*r15["ps"]+ ALPHA["5m"]*r5["ps"]
    s=pb+ph+ps; 
    if s>0: pb,ph,ps = pb/s, ph/s, ps/s

    ctx_cand=decide_context(pb,ph,ps, {"30m":r30,"15m":r15,"5m":r5})
    ctx = persist(sym, ctx_cand, ts5)

    rec={"symbol":sym,"S":round(S,6),"pb":round(pb,6),"ph":round(ph,6),"ps":round(ps,6),
         "context":ctx,"ts":int(ts5//1000)}
    upsert_out(rec)
    print(f"[A-coin] {sym} ctx={ctx} S={rec['S']}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, sys
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
def now_iso(): return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

# Params
EX="bitget"; QUOTE="USDT"; N=int(os.getenv("TOP_N","30"))
BAD_KW=("UP","DOWN","BULL","BEAR","3L","3S","5L","5S")
BAD_BASES={"USDT","USDC","FDUSD","TUSD","DAI","EUR","TRY","USD"}
MIN_QV=float(os.getenv("MIN_QV","1000000"))  # 1M
MAX_SP=float(os.getenv("MAX_SP_BPS","50"))   # 0.5%
FUT={"type":"swap","productType":"USDT-FUTURES"}

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
TOP=DATA/"top.json"; RANK=DATA/"top_ranked.json"

# noyau fixe lu de top.json existant, sinon BTC/ETH/SOL/XRP/BNB
def load_seed():
    if TOP.exists():
        try:
            j=json.loads(TOP.read_text()); s=j.get("symbols") or []
            return [x for x in s if isinstance(x,str)]
        except: pass
    return ["BTCUSDT","ETHUSDT","SOLUSDT","XRPUSDT","BNBUSDT"]

def main():
    import ccxt
    seeds = load_seed()
    ex = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex.load_markets()
    # Univers futures USDT
    mkts=[m for m in ex.markets.values() if m.get("type")=="swap" and m.get("linear") and m.get("quote")==QUOTE and m.get("active") is not False]
    symbols=[m["symbol"] for m in mkts]
    bases={m["symbol"]: m["base"] for m in mkts}

    # Tickers bulk (fallback par symbole si besoin)
    tickers={}
    try: tickers = ex.fetch_tickers(symbols, {**FUT})
    except Exception:
        for s in symbols:
            try: tickers[s]=ex.fetch_ticker(s,{**FUT})
            except Exception: tickers[s]={}

    # Préfiltre rapide
    pool=[]
    for s in symbols:
        b=bases[s]
        if any(k in b for k in BAD_KW): continue
        if b in BAD_BASES: continue
        t=tickers.get(s,{})
        qv=float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        bid,ask=t.get("bid"),t.get("ask")
        if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0: continue
        mid=0.5*(bid+ask); sp_bps=10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid
        if qv<MIN_QV or sp_bps>MAX_SP: continue
        pool.append((s,qv,sp_bps))

    # Tri volume desc et complétion
    pool.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
    seed_set=set(seeds)
    out=list(seeds)
    details=[]
    for s,qv,sp in pool:
        flat=s.replace("/","")
        if flat in seed_set: 
            details.append({"symbol":flat,"score":1.0,"volume24h_quote":qv,"spread_bps":sp})
            continue
        out.append(flat); seed_set.add(flat)
        details.append({"symbol":flat,"score":0.0,"volume24h_quote":qv,"spread_bps":sp})
        if len(out)>=N: break

    # Écritures
    meta={"generated_at":now_iso(),"source":"futures-tickers-fast","exchange":EX,"quote":QUOTE}
    (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({**meta,"symbols":out[:N]}, indent=2))
    (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": meta["generated_at"],
        "n": len(out[:N]),
        "items": details[:N]
    }, indent=2))
    print(f"[expand] seeds={len(seeds)} pool={len(pool)} top={len(out[:N])}")

if __name__=="__main__": main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, math, hashlib, statistics as stats
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

# --------- Paths / I/O ----------
DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
RUN  = Path("/opt/scalp/run");  RUN.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
STATE = RUN/"a_state.json"                # persistance 2 barres
OUT   = DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"         # sortie

# univers
TOP = DATA/"top.json"

# cache OHLCV par TF (compact et TTL court)
C_DIR = RUN/"ohlcv_cache_tf"; C_DIR.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
TTL = {"30m":1800, "15m":1200, "5m":900}  # secondes
LIMIT = 520                               # >= 500, marge pour EMA/ATR

# --------- Tuning ----------
W_EMA, W_MACD, W_RSI, W_ADX, W_OBV = 0.35, 0.25, 0.20, 0.10, 0.10
TAU   = {"30m":0.35, "15m":0.30, "5m":0.25}           # softmax temp
ALPHA = {"30m":0.5, "15m":0.3, "5m":0.2}             # poids TF
ATR_GATE = {"30m":0.0025, "15m":0.0018, "5m":0.0012} # ATR% seuils

# --------- CCXT ----------
def ex():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })
EX = ex()

def b2ccxt(s):  # BTCUSDT_UMCBL -> BTC/USDT:USDT
    return s.replace("_UMCBL","/USDT:USDT")

# --------- Utils ----------
def ema(series, n):
    if not series: return []
    k = 2/(n+1)
    out=[series[0]]
    for x in series[1:]:
        out.append(out[-1] + k*(x-out[-1]))
    return out
def stdev(xs):
    if len(xs)<2: return 0.0
    mu = sum(xs)/len(xs)
    return math.sqrt(sum((x-mu)**2 for x in xs)/len(xs))

def atr_ohlc(h,l,c,n=14):
    trs=[]; prev=c[0]
    for i in range(len(c)):
        hi,lo,cl=h[i],l[i],c[i]
        tr=max(hi-lo, abs(hi-prev), abs(lo-prev))
        trs.append(tr); prev=cl
    return ema(trs, n)

def macd_hist(cl, fast=12, slow=26, sig=9):
    macd_line=[a-b for a,b in zip(ema(cl,fast), ema(cl,slow))]
    signal = ema(macd_line, sig)
    # aligne
    n=min(len(macd_line), len(signal))
    return [macd_line[-n+i]-signal[-n+i] for i in range(n)]

def rsi14(cl, n=14):
    if len(cl)<n+1: return [50.0]*len(cl)
    gains=[0.0]; losses=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cl)):
        ch=cl[i]-cl[i-1]
        gains.append(max(ch,0.0)); losses.append(max(-ch,0.0))
    avgG=ema(gains,n); avgL=ema(losses,n)
    out=[]
    for g,l in zip(avgG,avgL):
        rs = g/(l+1e-12)
        out.append(100.0 - 100.0/(1.0+rs))
    return out

def adx14(h,l,c,n=14):
    # DM+/DM-, TR; DX=100*|+DI - -DI|/(+DI + -DI); ADX=EMA(DX,n)
    if len(c)<n+1: return [20.0]*len(c)
    plusDM=[0.0]; minusDM=[0.0]; TR=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        up=h[i]-h[i-1]; dn=l[i-1]-l[i]
        plusDM.append( up if (up>dn and up>0) else 0.0 )
        minusDM.append( dn if (dn>up and dn>0) else 0.0 )
        TR.append( max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-c[i-1]), abs(l[i]-c[i-1])) )
    plusDI   = [100*(x/(y+1e-12)) for x,y in zip(ema(plusDM,n), ema(TR,n))]
    minusDI  = [100*(x/(y+1e-12)) for x,y in zip(ema(minusDM,n), ema(TR,n))]
    DX = [100*abs(p-m)/(p+m+1e-12) for p,m in zip(plusDI, minusDI)]
    return ema(DX, n)

def obv(cl, vol):
    out=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cl)):
        if cl[i]>cl[i-1]: out.append(out[-1]+vol[i])
        elif cl[i]<cl[i-1]: out.append(out[-1]-vol[i])
        else: out.append(out[-1])
    return out

def cache_key(sym, tf):
    h = hashlib.sha1((sym+"|"+tf).encode()).hexdigest()[:16]
    return C_DIR/f"{h}.json"

def fetch_ohlcv(sym, tf):
    """Retourne OHLCV fermé (bougie incomplète retirée)."""
    p=cache_key(sym, tf)
    ttl=TTL[tf]
    now=time.time()
    if p.exists():
        try:
            j=json.loads(p.read_text())
            if now - j.get("ts",0) <= ttl: 
                o=j.get("data",[])
                if o: 
                    # drop last if incomplète
                    ms = {"30m":30, "15m":15, "5m":5}[tf]*60*1000
                    if int(time.time()*1000) - o[-1][0] < 0.9*ms: o=o[:-1]
                return o
        except: pass
    raw = EX.fetch_ohlcv(b2ccxt(sym), timeframe=tf, limit=LIMIT)
    if raw:
        ms = {"30m":30, "15m":15, "5m":5}[tf]*60*1000
        if int(time.time()*1000) - raw[-1][0] < 0.9*ms: raw=raw[:-1]
    p.write_text(json.dumps({"ts":now,"data":raw}))
    return raw

# --------- Sous-score par TF ----------
def subscores_tf(ohlcv, tf):
    # colonnes
    o=[r[1] for r in ohlcv]; h=[r[2] for r in ohlcv]; l=[r[3] for r in ohlcv]
    c=[r[4] for r in ohlcv]; v=[r[5] for r in ohlcv]
    if len(c)<500: return None

    # EMA spread / ATR gate
    atr = atr_ohlc(h,l,c,14)
    ema12 = ema(c,12); ema26 = ema(c,26)
    n=min(len(atr),len(ema12),len(ema26))
    atr14=atr[-1]; base=max(1.5*atr14,1e-9)
    s_ema = math.tanh( (ema12[-1]-ema26[-1]) / base )

    # MACD hist normalisé par sigma_100
    hist = macd_hist(c)
    sigma = stdev(hist[-100:]) if len(hist)>=100 else stdev(hist)
    s_macd = math.tanh( (hist[-1])/(sigma+1e-12) )

    # RSI
    r = rsi14(c)
    r_last = r[-1] if r else 50.0
    s_rsi = max(-1.0, min(1.0, (r_last-50.0)/50.0 ))

    # ADX
    adx = adx14(h,l,c,14)
    a_last = adx[-1] if adx else 20.0
    s_adx = max(-1.0, min(1.0, (a_last-20.0)/20.0 ))

    # OBV slope(20) / median(|OBV|_200)
    ob = obv(c,v)
    if len(ob)>=220:
        slope = ob[-1]-ob[-21]
        denom = stats.median([abs(x) for x in ob[-200:]]) or 1.0
    else:
        slope = ob[-1]-ob[-min(21,len(ob)-1)]
        denom = stats.median([abs(x) for x in ob]) or 1.0
    s_obv = math.tanh(slope/denom)

    # ATR% gate: si trop faible → demi-poids sur EMA+MACD
    gate = (atr14 / c[-1]) < ATR_GATE[tf]
    w_ema = W_EMA*0.5 if gate else W_EMA
    w_macd= W_MACD*0.5 if gate else W_MACD

    # Score TF ∈ [-1,1]
    num = w_ema*s_ema + w_macd*s_macd + W_RSI*s_rsi + W_ADX*s_adx + W_OBV*s_obv
    den = (w_ema + w_macd + W_RSI + W_ADX + W_OBV)
    S = num/den if den>0 else 0.0

    # Softmax tri-state
    t = TAU[tf]
    epos = math.exp(S/t); eneg = math.exp(-S/t); den3 = epos + 1.0 + eneg
    pb = epos/den3; ph = 1.0/den3; ps = eneg/den3

    return {
        "S": S, "pb": pb, "ph": ph, "ps": ps,
        "gate": gate, "atrpct": atr14/c[-1],
        "last_ts": ohlcv[-1][0]
    }

# --------- Agrégation multi-TF + contexte ----------
def aggregate(tf_res):
    # pondération et renormalisation
    S = sum(ALPHA[k]*tf_res[k]["S"] for k in tf_res)
    pb= sum(ALPHA[k]*tf_res[k]["pb"] for k in tf_res)
    ph= sum(ALPHA[k]*tf_res[k]["ph"] for k in tf_res)
    ps= sum(ALPHA[k]*tf_res[k]["ps"] for k in tf_res)
    s = pb+ph+ps
    if s>0: pb,ph,ps = pb/s, ph/s, ps/s
    return S, pb, ph, ps

def veto_context(tf_res, S5):
    # util pour veto 5m
    return (S5<0), (S5>0)

def decide_context(pb,ph,ps, tf_res):
    # candidats
    bull = pb>=0.60 and (tf_res["30m"]["pb"]>=0.55) and (tf_res["15m"]["pb"]>=0.55)
    bear = ps>=0.60 and (tf_res["30m"]["ps"]>=0.55) and (tf_res["15m"]["ps"]>=0.55)
    veto_buy, veto_sell = veto_context(tf_res, tf_res["5m"]["S"])
    if bull and not veto_buy: return "buy"
    if bear and not veto_sell: return "sell"
    if 0.40 <= ph <= 0.60: return "hold"
    return "none"

def persist(symbol, candidate, bar_ts):
    # persistance sur 2 barres: on exige 2 occurrences consécutives du même candidat
    try:
        st=json.loads(STATE.read_text() or "{}")
    except: st={}
    s=st.get(symbol, {"last":"none","streak":0,"ts":0})
    if candidate!="none":
        if s.get("last")==candidate and s.get("ts")!=bar_ts:
            s["streak"]=min(2, s.get("streak",0)+1)
        else:
            s["streak"]=1
        s["last"]=candidate; s["ts"]=bar_ts
    else:
        # reset seulement si on change de barre
        if s.get("ts")!=bar_ts:
            s["streak"]=0; s["last"]="none"; s["ts"]=bar_ts
    st[symbol]=s
    STATE.write_text(json.dumps(st))
    return candidate if st[symbol]["streak"]>=2 else "none"

# --------- Main ----------
def run_symbol(sym):
    # fetch trois TF
    res={}
    for tf in ("30m","15m","5m"):
        k = fetch_ohlcv(sym, tf)
        if not k or len(k)<500: return None
        r = subscores_tf(k, tf)
        if not r: return None
        res[tf]=r
    S,pb,ph,ps = aggregate(res)
    # contexte + persistance
    cand = decide_context(pb,ph,ps,res)
    final = persist(sym, cand, res["5m"]["last_ts"])
    return {
        "symbol": sym,
        "S": round(S,6),
        "pb": round(pb,6),
        "ph": round(ph,6),
        "ps": round(ps,6),
        "context": final,
        "ts": int(res["5m"]["last_ts"]//1000)
    }

def main():
    try:
        syms = (json.loads(TOP.read_text()).get("symbols")) or []
    except: syms=[]
    out=[]
    for s in syms:
        try:
            r=run_symbol(s)
            if r: out.append(r)
        except Exception as e:
            # silencieux pour robustesse en prod
            pass
    OUT.write_text(json.dumps(out, indent=2))
    print(f"[A] analysed={len(out)}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, math, time, asyncio
from pathlib import Path
from statistics import pstdev
from datetime import datetime, timezone, timedelta
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

# ---------- Params ----------
DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
PARAMS = Path("/opt/scalp/tools/top_params.json")
WORKERS = int(os.getenv("TOP_WORKERS", "8"))             # threads pour appels ccxt
RATE_LIMIT_MS = int(os.getenv("TOP_RATE_LIMIT_MS", "250"))
MAX_INFLIGHT = max(1, 1000 // RATE_LIMIT_MS)

# ---------- Helpers ----------
def now_iso():
    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

def load_params():
    p = json.loads(PARAMS.read_text())
    p["exchange"] = p.get("exchange","bitget")
    p["quote"] = p.get("quote","USDT")
    p["top_n"] = int(p.get("top_n",30))
    return p

def spread_bps(t):
    bid, ask = t.get("bid"), t.get("ask")
    if not bid or not ask or bid<=0 or ask<=0: return 1e9
    mid = 0.5*(bid+ask)
    return 10000.0*(ask-bid)/mid

def norm_rank(d):
    items = sorted(d.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1])
    n = max(1, len(items)-1)
    return {k:i/n for i,(k,_) in enumerate(items)}

# ---------- Async throttle ----------
_executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=WORKERS)
_sem = asyncio.Semaphore(MAX_INFLIGHT)

async def throttled(loop, func, *args, **kwargs):
    async with _sem:
        t0 = time.time()
        try:
            res = await loop.run_in_executor(_executor, lambda: func(*args, **kwargs))
        except Exception:
            res = None
        dt = time.time() - t0
        sleep_need = max(0.0, RATE_LIMIT_MS/1000 - dt)
        if sleep_need: await asyncio.sleep(sleep_need)
        return res

# ---------- Per-symbol workers ----------
def compute_turnover_vola_7d(ohlcv_1h):
    if not ohlcv_1h or len(ohlcv_1h) < 10: return 0.0, 0.0
    trn = 0.0
    rets=[]
    prev = ohlcv_1h[0][4]
    for _,_,_,_,c,v in ohlcv_1h[1:]:
        trn += float(v)*float(c)
        if prev>0 and c>0:
            rets.append(math.log(c/prev))
        prev=c
    vola = float(pstdev(rets)) if rets else 0.0
    return trn, vola

async def fetch_symbol_bundle(loop, ex, sym, cutoff_ms):
    # 1d last ts
    o1d = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_ohlcv, sym, "1d", 2)
    last_ts = o1d[-1][0] if isinstance(o1d, list) and o1d else 0
    # 1h x 7j
    o1h = await throttled(loop, ex.fetch_ohlcv, sym, "1h", 24*7+1)
    trn, vola = compute_turnover_vola_7d(o1h if isinstance(o1h, list) else [])
    inactive = last_ts < cutoff_ms
    return inactive, trn, vola

# ---------- Main ----------
def main():
    import ccxt
    params = load_params()
    EX, QUOTE, N = params["exchange"], params["quote"], params["top_n"]
    flt, w = params["filters"], params["scoring"]
    NOW = datetime.now(timezone.utc); NOW_ISO = now_iso()
    cutoff_ms = int((NOW - timedelta(days=90)).timestamp()*1000)

    # Client maître
    ex0 = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
    ex0.load_markets()
    symbols = [s for s in ex0.symbols if s.endswith(f"/{QUOTE}")]
    tickers = ex0.fetch_tickers(symbols)

    def base(sym): return sym.split("/")[0]
    bad_kw = tuple(flt["exclude_leveraged_keywords"])
    bad_bases = set(flt["exclude_bases"])
    min_qv = float(flt["min_quote_vol_24h"])
    max_sp = float(flt["max_spread_bps"])

    # Pré-filtre rapide
    pre = []
    vol24 = {}
    spd = {}
    for s in symbols:
        b = base(s)
        if any(k in b for k in bad_kw): continue
        if b in bad_bases: continue
        t = tickers.get(s, {})
        qv = float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0)
        sp = spread_bps(t)
        if qv < min_qv or sp > max_sp: continue
        pre.append(s); vol24[s]=qv; spd[s]=sp

    # Répartir la charge ccxt: petits clients par thread
    def ex_factory():
        e = getattr(ccxt, EX)({"enableRateLimit": True})
        try: e.load_markets()
        except Exception: pass
        return e
    # Pré-crée un pool de clients pour limiter les coûts d’init
    clients = [ex_factory() for _ in range(max(1, min(WORKERS, len(pre))))]

    async def run_all():
        loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
        turn7, vola7, inactive = {}, {}, []
        # round-robin des clients
        tasks=[]
        for i, s in enumerate(pre):
            ex = clients[i % len(clients)]
            tasks.append(fetch_symbol_bundle(loop, ex, s, cutoff_ms))
        results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
        for s, r in zip(pre, results):
            if isinstance(r, Exception) or r is None: 
                inactive.append(s.replace("/","")); continue
            is_inactive, trn, vol = r
            if is_inactive:
                inactive.append(s.replace("/",""))
            else:
                turn7[s]=trn; vola7[s]=vol
        return turn7, vola7, inactive

    turn7, vola7, inactive_list = asyncio.run(run_all())

    # Écrit coins_90d.json
    DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    (DATA/"coins_90d.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "source": "ccxt-1d-90d",
        "exchange": EX,
        "quote": QUOTE,
        "cutoff_days": 90,
        "inactive_symbols": sorted([x.replace("/","") for x in inactive_list])
    }, indent=2))

    # Scoring
    candidates = [s for s in pre if s not in inactive_list]
    ranked=[]
    if candidates:
        r1 = norm_rank({k:vol24[k] for k in candidates})
        r2 = norm_rank({k:turn7.get(k,0.0) for k in candidates})
        r3 = norm_rank({k:vola7.get(k,0.0) for k in candidates})
        r4 = norm_rank({k:spd.get(k,1e9) for k in candidates})
        score = {s: (
            w["w_volume24h"]   * r1.get(s,0.0) +
            w["w_turnover7d"]  * r2.get(s,0.0) +
            w["w_volatility7d"]* r3.get(s,0.0) +
            w["w_spread"]      * r4.get(s,0.0)
        ) for s in candidates}
        ranked = sorted(score.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1], reverse=True)

    if not ranked:
        # Fallback volume 24h si vide
        ranked = sorted(vol24.items(), key=lambda kv: kv[1], reverse=True)

    top_syms = [sym.replace("/","") for sym,_ in ranked[:N]]

    # Sorties
    (DATA/"top.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO,
        "source": "coins_90d+advanced-async",
        "exchange": EX,
        "quote": QUOTE,
        "symbols": top_syms
    }, indent=2))

    ranked_out=[]
    for sym, sc in ranked[:N]:
        t = tickers.get(sym, {})
        ranked_out.append({
            "symbol": sym.replace("/",""),
            "score": round(float(sc),6),
            "volume24h_quote": float(t.get("quoteVolume") or 0.0),
            "turnover7d": float(turn7.get(sym,0.0)),
            "volatility7d": float(vola7.get(sym,0.0)),
            "spread_bps": float(spd.get(sym,1e9))
        })
    (DATA/"top_ranked.json").write_text(json.dumps({
        "generated_at": NOW_ISO, "n": len(top_syms), "items": ranked_out
    }, indent=2))

    print(f"[top-async] pre={len(pre)} inactive90d={len(inactive_list)} top={len(top_syms)} workers={WORKERS} inflight={MAX_INFLIGHT}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Utilitaire de REPARATION: relit /opt/scalp/data/coins_90d.json
# et filtre /opt/scalp/data/top.json si par erreur il contient des coins >90j.
import json, sys
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
TOP = DATA/"top.json"
C90 = DATA/"coins_90d.json"

def now_iso():
    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec="seconds").replace("+00:00","Z")

def main():
    if not TOP.exists() or not C90.exists():
        print("Fichiers manquants", file=sys.stderr); sys.exit(1)
    top = json.loads(TOP.read_text())
    c90 = json.loads(C90.read_text())
    bad = set(c90.get("inactive_symbols", []))
    syms = [s for s in top.get("symbols", []) if s not in bad]
    changed = (syms != top.get("symbols", []))
    if changed:
        top["symbols"] = syms
        top["generated_at"] = now_iso()
        top["source"] = "coins_90d"
        tmp = TOP.with_suffix(".tmp")
        tmp.write_text(json.dumps(top, indent=2))
        tmp.replace(TOP)
        print(f"[repair_top] removed {len(bad)} inactive; new len={len(syms)}")
    else:
        print("[repair_top] no change")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import json, time, datetime as dt
from pathlib import Path

DATA = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND = DATA/"candles"
TOPF = DATA/"top.json"
TFS = [("5m", 300), ("15m", 900), ("30m", 1800)]

def load_top():
    try:
        j = json.loads(TOPF.read_text())
        syms = j.get("symbols", [])
        return [s for s in syms if isinstance(s, str)]
    except Exception:
        return []

def last_ts(sym, tf):
    f = CAND/tf/(sym + ".json")
    if not f.exists():
        return None
    try:
        a = json.loads(f.read_text())
        if not a:
            return None
        return int(a[-1][0]//1000)
    except Exception:
        return None

def hhmm(ts):
    if ts is None:
        return "—"
    # system is set to UTC; display HH:MM
    return dt.datetime.utcfromtimestamp(ts).strftime("%H:%M")

def main():
    syms = load_top()
    if not syms:
        print("top.json: aucun symbole trouvé")
        return
    # header
    print("# Top updates (UTC)")
    header = ["symbol","5m","15m","30m","lag(max)"]
    colw = [max(6, max(len(s.replace("USDT","")) for s in syms)), 5, 5, 5, 8]
    print(f"{header[0]:<{colw[0]}}  {header[1]:^{colw[1]}}  {header[2]:^{colw[2]}}  {header[3]:^{colw[3]}}  {header[4]:>{colw[4]}}")
    now = int(time.time())
    worst_lag = 0
    rows = []
    for s in syms:
        ts5  = last_ts(s, "5m")
        ts15 = last_ts(s, "15m")
        ts30 = last_ts(s, "30m")
        # compute lag
        lags = [x for x in [now-(ts5 or 0), now-(ts15 or 0), now-(ts30 or 0)] if x>0]
        lag = max(lags) if lags else 0
        worst_lag = max(worst_lag, lag)
        rows.append((s.replace("USDT",""), hhmm(ts5), hhmm(ts15), hhmm(ts30), lag))

    for sym, t5, t15, t30, lag in rows:
        print(f"{sym:<{colw[0]}}  {t5:^{colw[1]}}  {t15:^{colw[2]}}  {t30:^{colw[3]}}  {lag/60:>{colw[4]}.0f}m")

    print(f"\nMax retard: {worst_lag//60}m {worst_lag%60}s")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, json, time, math, statistics as stats
from pathlib import Path
import ccxt

DATA=Path("/opt/scalp/data"); DATA.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
CBASE=DATA/"candles"
A_OUT=DATA/"analyse_A_out.json"
SIG=DATA/"signals.json"
STATE=Path("/opt/scalp/run/b_state.json")
DBG_REJ=DATA/"debug/b_rejects.json"

RISK_PCT=float(os.getenv("B_RISK_PCT","0.003"))
MAX_EXPO=float(os.getenv("B_MAX_PAIR_PCT","0.10"))
LEV=int(os.getenv("B_LEVERAGE","10"))
MIN_NOTIONAL=float(os.getenv("B_MIN_NOTIONAL","5"))
LOT_STEP=float(os.getenv("B_LOT_STEP","0.001"))

def ex():
    return ccxt.bitget({
        "apiKey": os.getenv("BITGET_API_KEY",""),
        "secret": os.getenv("BITGET_API_SECRET",""),
        "password": os.getenv("BITGET_PASSPHRASE",""),
        "options": {"defaultType":"swap","defaultSubType":"linear"},
        "enableRateLimit": True,
    })
EX=ex()

def ema(x,n):
    if not x: return []
    k=2/(n+1); o=[x[0]]
    for v in x[1:]: o.append(o[-1]+k*(v-o[-1]))
    return o
def atr(h,l,c,n=14):
    trs=[]; prev=c[0]
    for i in range(len(c)):
        trs.append(max(h[i]-l[i], abs(h[i]-prev), abs(l[i]-prev))); prev=c[i]
    return ema(trs,n)
def macd_hist(c, fast=12, slow=26, sig=9):
    m=[a-b for a,b in zip(ema(c,fast), ema(c,slow))]
    s=ema(m,sig); n=min(len(m),len(s))
    return [m[-n+i]-s[-n+i] for i in range(n)]
def rsi(c,n=7):
    if len(c)<n+1: return [50.0]*len(c)
    g=[0.0]; d=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(c)):
        ch=c[i]-c[i-1]; g.append(max(ch,0.0)); d.append(max(-ch,0.0))
    ag=ema(g,n); ad=ema(d,n)
    out=[]
    for x,y in zip(ag,ad):
        rs=x/(y+1e-12); out.append(100-100/(1+rs))
    return out

def load_tf(sym, tf):
    p=CBASE/tf/f"{sym}.json"
    if not p.exists(): return None
    j=json.loads(p.read_text()); k=j["data"]
    if len(k)<100: return None
    ms={"1m":60,"3m":180,"5m":300}[tf]*1000
    if int(time.time()*1000)-k[-1][0] < 0.9*ms: k=k[:-1]
    o=[r[1] for r in k]; h=[r[2] for r in k]; l=[r[3] for r in k]; c=[r[4] for r in k]; v=[r[5] for r in k]
    return {"o":o,"h":h,"l":l,"c":c,"v":v,"ts":k[-1][0]}

def prefilters(sym, ctx, d1):
    reasons=[]
    if not d1:
        return False,["no-1m"]
    c,h,l=d1["c"],d1["h"],d1["l"]
    atr14=atr(h,l,c,14)[-1]; atrpct=atr14/c[-1]
    if atrpct<0.001: reasons.append("atr%<0.10%")
    # cooldown
    try: st=json.loads(STATE.read_text() or "{}")
    except: st={}
    last=st.get(sym,0)
    if time.time()-last<5*60: reasons.append("cooldown")
    # spread
    try:
        t=EX.fetch_ticker(sym.replace("_UMCBL","/USDT:USDT"))
        if (t["ask"]-t["bid"])/t["bid"]>0.002: reasons.append("spread>0.2%")
    except: pass
    return (len(reasons)==0, reasons if reasons else ["ok"])

def detect_pullback(sym, ctx, d1):
    c,h,l,v=d1["c"],d1["h"],d1["l"],d1["v"]
    ema20=ema(c,20)[-1]; last=c[-1]; rsi7=rsi(c,7)[-1]
    ma20=sum(v[-20:])/20; vol=v[-1]
    if ctx=="buy" and last<=ema20 and rsi7>=60 and vol>1.3*ma20:
        atr14=atr(h,l,c,14)[-1]; sl=last-1.2*atr14; tp=last+1.8*atr14
        return {"trigger":"pullback","side":"buy","entry":last,"sl":sl,"tp":tp,
                "why":["ema20-touch","rsi>=60","vol>1.3x20"]}
    if ctx=="sell" and last>=ema20 and rsi7<=40 and vol>1.3*ma20:
        atr14=atr(h,l,c,14)[-1]; sl=last+1.2*atr14; tp=last-1.8*atr14
        return {"trigger":"pullback","side":"sell","entry":last,"sl":sl,"tp":tp,
                "why":["ema20-touch","rsi<=40","vol>1.3x20"]}
    return None

def detect_breakout(sym, ctx, d1,d5):
    if not d5: return None
    c,h,l=d1["c"],d1["h"],d1["l"]
    # ADX 5m simple
    def _adx5(d5):
        ch=d5["c"]; hh=max(d5["h"][-15:]); ll=min(d5["l"][-15:])
        rng=hh-ll
        return 25.0 if rng>0 and (ch[-1]-ch[-6])>0 else 15.0
    adx5=_adx5(d5)
    if adx5<20: return None
    hh=max(h[-20:]); ll=min(l[-20:])
    last=c[-1]; macd_acc=macd_hist(c)[-1]>0
    if ctx=="buy" and last>hh and macd_acc:
        sl=ll; tp=last+(hh-ll)*1.5
        return {"trigger":"breakout","side":"buy","entry":last,"sl":sl,"tp":tp,
                "why":["HH20-break","macd-accel","ADX5>=20"]}
    if ctx=="sell" and last<ll and macd_acc:
        sl=hh; tp=last-(hh-ll)*1.5
        return {"trigger":"breakout","side":"sell","entry":last,"sl":sl,"tp":tp,
                "why":["LL20-break","macd-accel","ADX5>=20"]}
    return None

def detect_mr(sym, ctx, d1):
    if ctx!="hold": return None
    c=d1["c"]; rsi7=rsi(c,7)[-1]; last=c[-1]
    mid=sum(c[-20:])/20; std=stats.pstdev(c[-20:])
    up=mid+2*std; dn=mid-2*std
    if last>up and rsi7<60:
        return {"trigger":"meanrev","side":"sell","entry":last,"sl":last-std,"tp":mid,
                "why":["BB2sigma-touch","RSI<60","reversal"]}
    if last<dn and rsi7>40:
        return {"trigger":"meanrev","side":"buy","entry":last,"sl":last+std,"tp":mid,
                "why":["BB2sigma-touch","RSI>40","reversal"]}
    return None

def size_trade(balance, entry, sl):
    D=abs(entry-sl)
    R=balance*RISK_PCT
    if D<=0: return 0
    qty=R/D
    notional=qty*entry
    if notional<MIN_NOTIONAL: qty=MIN_NOTIONAL/entry
    max_notional=balance*MAX_EXPO*LEV
    if qty*entry>max_notional: qty=max_notional/entry
    step=LOT_STEP
    qty=math.floor(qty/step)*step
    return qty

def main():
    try: arrA=json.loads(A_OUT.read_text())
    except: arrA=[]
    try: sigs=json.loads(SIG.read_text())
    except: sigs=[]
    balance=float(os.getenv("B_BALANCE","100"))
    rejects=[]
    added=[]
    for r in arrA:
        sym,ctx=r.get("symbol"),r.get("context")
        if ctx=="none": 
            rejects.append({"symbol":sym,"ctx":"none","reasons":["ctx-none"]}); 
            continue
        d1=load_tf(sym,"1m"); d5=load_tf(sym,"5m")
        ok,pre=prefilters(sym,ctx,d1)
        if not ok:
            rejects.append({"symbol":sym,"ctx":ctx,"reasons":pre}); 
            continue
        cand=detect_pullback(sym,ctx,d1) or detect_breakout(sym,ctx,d1,d5) or detect_mr(sym,ctx,d1)
        if not cand:
            rejects.append({"symbol":sym,"ctx":ctx,"reasons":["no-trigger"]}); 
            continue
        entry=cand["entry"]; sl=cand["sl"]; qty=size_trade(balance, entry, sl)
        if qty<=0:
            rejects.append({"symbol":sym,"ctx":ctx,"reasons":["qty<=0"]}); 
            continue
        sig={"symbol":sym,"side":cand["side"],"type":cand["trigger"],
             "entry":entry,"sl":sl,"tp":cand["tp"],"qty":qty,"leverage":LEV,
             "timestamp":int(time.time()),"expires":int(time.time()+1500),
             "reasons":cand.get("why",[])}
        sigs.append(sig); added.append(sig)
        # cooldown
        try: st=json.loads(STATE.read_text() or "{}")
        except: st={}
        st[sym]=time.time(); STATE.write_text(json.dumps(st))
    SIG.write_text(json.dumps(sigs, indent=2))
    DBG_REJ.write_text(json.dumps({"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime()),
                                   "added":len(added),"rejects":rejects}, indent=2))
    print(f"[B] added={len(added)} total={len(sigs)}")
if __name__=="__main__":
    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, json, time, shutil
from pathlib import Path
OK=True; msgs=[]
def need(p,t="f"):
    global OK
    P=Path(p); ex=(P.is_file() if t=="f" else P.is_dir())
    if not ex: OK=False; msgs.append(f"missing:{t}:{p}")
def touch(p): Path(p).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True); Path(p).touch()
for f in ("/etc/scalp.env","/etc/scalp.app","/etc/scalp.tuning"): need(f,"f")
for d in ("/opt/scalp/tools","/opt/scalp/logs","/opt/scalp/data","/opt/scalp/data/debug","/opt/scalp/run"): need(d,"d")
need("/opt/scalp/tools/run_analysis_b_minutely.sh","f")
for f in ("contracts_usdt.json","coins_90d.json","top.json"): touch(f"/opt/scalp/data/{f}")
st=shutil.disk_usage("/opt/scalp"); OK = OK and st.free >= 500*1024*1024 or False
out={"ts":time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ",time.gmtime()),"ok":OK,"issues":msgs}
Path("/opt/scalp/data/debug/preflight.json").write_text(json.dumps(out,indent=2))
print(json.dumps(out)); sys.exit(0 if OK else 2)

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
DATA=/opt/scalp/data
TOP=$DATA/top.json

ttl() { python3 - "$@" <<'PY'
import sys, json, time
tf, path = sys.argv[1], sys.argv[2]
try:
  j=json.load(open(path))
  ts=j.get("generated_at") or j.get("ts") or ""
  if not ts: raise SystemExit(9999)
  # accepte ISO ou epoch s
  if isinstance(ts,str) and ts.endswith("Z"):
    import datetime as dt
    t=int(dt.datetime.fromisoformat(ts.replace("Z","+00:00")).timestamp())
  else:
    t=int(ts)
  step={"5m":300,"15m":900,"30m":1800}[tf]
  now=int(time.time())
  # temps restant avant fermeture de la bougie courante du TF
  left = (now//step + 1)*step - now
  print(left)
except: print(0)
PY
}

ok_tf() {
  tf=$1; f="/opt/scalp/data/candles/${tf}.json"
  test -s "$f" || return 1
  left=$(ttl "$tf" "$f")
  # on accepte vert si on a au moins 2/5/10 min de "validité" restante pour 5/15/30
  min_left=$([ "$tf" = "5m" ] && echo 120 || ([ "$tf" = "15m" ] && echo 300 || echo 600))
  [ "$left" -ge "$min_left" ]
}

jq -e '.symbols|length==30' "$TOP" >/dev/null || { echo "[A-guard] bad TOP"; exit 0; }
ok_tf 5m && ok_tf 15m && ok_tf 30m || { echo "[A-guard] TF not fresh"; exit 0; }
echo "[A-guard] run A"
python3 /opt/scalp/tools/analysis_a.py || true

----- CONTENT -----
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Analyse B : pré-filtres 1m, triggers Pullback/Breakout/MeanReversion, anti-bruit, sizing paper.
# Lit OHLCV 1m/3m/5m depuis /opt/scalp/data/candles/<tf>/<SYMBOL>.json
# Contexte A lu dans /opt/scalp/data/analyse_A_out.json
# Ecrit /opt/scalp/data/analyse_B_out.json et append dans /opt/scalp/data/signals.json

import json, math, time
from pathlib import Path

DATA   = Path("/opt/scalp/data")
CAND   = DATA/"candles"
STATE  = DATA/"state"; STATE.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
CFGSTR = Path("/etc/scalp.strategy")  # paramètres ajustables (si présent)

# ---------- Utils IO ----------
def jload(p, d=None):
    p=Path(p)
    if not p.exists(): return d
    try: return json.loads(p.read_text())
    except: return d

def jsave(p, obj):
    p=Path(p); p.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    p.write_text(json.dumps(obj, ensure_ascii=False))

def last_complete(arr, tf_s):
    """retire la bougie incomplète si nécessaire, renvoie liste propre"""
    if not arr: return []
    now = int(time.time()*1000)
    if now - arr[-1][0] < tf_s*1000:  # bougie courante non close
        return arr[:-1]
    return arr

def close(a): return [x[4] for x in a]
def high(a):  return [x[2] for x in a]
def low(a):   return [x[3] for x in a]
def vol(a):   return [x[5] for x in a]
def tp(a):    return [(x[2]+x[3]+x[4])/3 for x in a]

# ---------- Indicators ----------
def ema(vals, n):
    k=2/(n+1); out=[]; e=None
    for v in vals:
        e = v if e is None else (v - e)*k + e
        out.append(e)
    return out

def rsi(vals, n=14):
    if len(vals)<n+1: return [50.0]*len(vals)
    gains=[0.0]; losses=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(vals)):
        d=vals[i]-vals[i-1]
        gains.append(max(d,0)); losses.append(max(-d,0))
    avg_gain=sum(gains[1:n+1])/n; avg_loss=sum(losses[1:n+1])/n
    rsis=[50.0]*(n)
    for i in range(n+1,len(vals)+1):
        avg_gain=(avg_gain*(n-1)+gains[i-1])/n
        avg_loss=(avg_loss*(n-1)+losses[i-1])/n
        rs= (avg_gain/avg_loss) if avg_loss>0 else 0
        r=100-(100/(1+rs)) if avg_loss>0 else 100
        rsis.append(r)
    return rsis

def true_range(h,l,c_prev): return max(h-l, abs(h-c_prev), abs(l-c_prev))
def atr(hs, ls, cs, n=14):
    trs=[]
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        if i==0: trs.append(hs[i]-ls[i])
        else: trs.append(true_range(hs[i], ls[i], cs[i-1]))
    out=[]; a=None; k=2/(n+1)
    for tr in trs:
        a = tr if a is None else (tr-a)*k + a
        out.append(a)
    return out

def adx(hs, ls, cs, n=14):
    # simple Wilder
    if len(cs)<n+1: return [20.0]*len(cs)
    pdm=[0.0]; ndm=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cs)):
        up=hs[i]-hs[i-1]; dn=ls[i-1]-ls[i]
        pdm.append(up if (up>dn and up>0) else 0.0)
        ndm.append(dn if (dn>up and dn>0) else 0.0)
    tr = []
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        if i==0: tr.append(hs[i]-ls[i])
        else: tr.append(true_range(hs[i], ls[i], cs[i-1]))
    def rma(x,n):
        k=1/n; out=[]; a=None
        for v in x:
            a = v if a is None else a + k*(v-a)
            out.append(a)
        return out
    atrv=rma(tr,n); pdi=[0.0]*len(cs); ndi=[0.0]*len(cs)
    p=rma(pdm,n); n_=rma(ndm,n)
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        if atrv[i]>0:
            pdi[i]=100*p[i]/atrv[i]; ndi[i]=100*n_[i]/atrv[i]
    dx=[0.0]*len(cs)
    for i in range(len(cs)):
        s=pdi[i]+ndi[i]; dx[i]= (100*abs(pdi[i]-ndi[i])/s) if s>0 else 0.0
    return rma(dx,n)

def macd_hist(vals, f=12, s=26, sig=9):
    e1=ema(vals,f); e2=ema(vals,s)
    macd=[e1[i]-e2[i] for i in range(len(vals))]
    sigl=ema(macd,sig)
    return [macd[i]-sigl[i] for i in range(len(vals))]

def bb(vals, n=20, k=2.0):
    if len(vals)<n: return [None]*len(vals), [None]*len(vals)
    ma=[]; dev=[]
    for i in range(len(vals)):
        if i<n-1:
            ma.append(None); dev.append(None)
        else:
            w=vals[i-n+1:i+1]
            m=sum(w)/n
            v=(sum((x-m)**2 for x in w)/n)**0.5
            ma.append(m); dev.append(v)
    upper=[(ma[i]+k*dev[i]) if ma[i] is not None else None for i in range(len(vals))]
    lower=[(ma[i]-k*dev[i]) if ma[i] is not None else None for i in range(len(vals))]
    return upper, lower, ma

def keltner(hs, ls, cs, n=20, k=1.5):
    ema_c=ema(cs,n)
    atrv=atr(hs,ls,cs,n)
    upper=[ema_c[i]+k*atrv[i] for i in range(len(cs))]
    lower=[ema_c[i]-k*atrv[i] for i in range(len(cs))]
    return upper, lower, ema_c

def obv(cl, vo):
    o=[0.0]
    for i in range(1,len(cl)):
        if cl[i]>cl[i-1]: o.append(o[-1]+vo[i])
        elif cl[i]<cl[i-1]: o.append(o[-1]-vo[i])
        else: o.append(o[-1])
    return o

# ---------- Strategy params ----------
PARAM = {
  "risk_pct": 0.003,           # 0.3%
  "leverage": 5,
  "min_notional": 5.0,
  "max_pair_expo_pct": 0.25,
  "lot_step": 0.0001,
  "cooldown_1m": 5,            # 5×1m
  "N_breakout": 20,
  "vol_mult_pullback": 1.3
}
if CFGSTR.exists():
    for ln in CFGSTR.read_text().splitlines():
        ln=ln.strip()
        if not ln or ln.startswith("#"): continue
        k,v = ln.split("=",1)
        try:
            PARAM[k]=float(v) if "." in v or v.isdigit() else v
        except: PARAM[k]=v

# ---------- Prefilters ----------
def prefilters(sym, m1, m3, m5):
    # ATR% 1m ≥ 0.10%
    c1=close(m1); h1=high(m1); l1=low(m1)
    atr1=atr(h1,l1,c1,14)
    atrpct1 = (atr1[-1]/c1[-1])*100 if c1 and atr1[-1] else 0.0
    if atrpct1 < 0.10: return False, "atr1%<0.10"
    # pas de bougie incomplète (déjà nettoyé par last_complete)
    # cooldown
    cd=jload(STATE/"cooldown.json", {}).get(sym, 0)
    if int(time.time()) < cd: return False, "cooldown"
    # spread ok (approx: range/close < 1.0% sur 1m)
    rng = (h1[-1]-l1[-1])/c1[-1] if c1 else 1.0
    if rng > 0.01: return False, "spread>1%"
    return True, "ok"

# ---------- Evidence helpers (0..1) ----------
def norm01(x, a, b):
    if b==a: return 0.0
    t=(x-a)/(b-a); return max(0.0, min(1.0, t))

def evidence_pullback(ctx, m1, m3):
    c1=close(m1); v1=vol(m1); e20=ema(c1,20)
    up,lo,ma = bb(c1,20,2.0); vw= vwap(m1,20)
    rsi7=rsi(c1,7); vavg20=sum(v1[-20:])/max(1,len(v1[-20:]))
    if ctx=="buy":
        touch = (c1[-1]<=lo[-1] if lo[-1] is not None else False) or (c1[-1]<=e20[-1]) or (c1[-1]<=vw[-1])
        side  = rsi7[-1]<=45
    elif ctx=="sell":
        touch = (c1[-1]>=up[-1] if up[-1] is not None else False) or (c1[-1]>=e20[-1]) or (c1[-1]>=vw[-1])
        side  = rsi7[-1]>=55
    else:
        return 0.0
    volok = (v1[-1] >= PARAM["vol_mult_pullback"]*vavg20)
    return 1.0 if (touch and side and volok) else 0.0

def macd_accel(vals):
    h=macd_hist(vals); 
    if len(h)<4: return 0.0
    return 1.0 if (h[-1]>h[-2]>h[-3]) else 0.0

def squeeze_ok(hs,ls,cs):
    bu,bl,ma = bb(cs,20,2.0); ku,kl,ema20 = keltner(hs,ls,cs,20,1.5)
    if bu[-1] is None: return 0.0
    return 1.0 if (bu[-1]-bl[-1]) < (ku[-1]-kl[-1]) else 0.0

def evidence_breakout(ctx, m3, m5):
    c3=close(m3); h3=high(m3); l3=low(m3)
    adx5 = adx(high(m5), low(m5), close(m5), 14)[-1] if m5 else 0.0
    N=int(PARAM["N_breakout"])
    if len(c3)<N+2: return 0.0
    hh=max(c3[-N-1:-1]); ll=min(c3[-N-1:-1])
    accel = macd_accel(c3)
    sq = squeeze_ok(high(m3),low(m3),c3)
    if ctx=="buy" and c3[-1]>hh and adx5>=20 and accel and sq: return 1.0
    if ctx=="sell" and c3[-1]<ll and adx5>=20 and accel and sq: return 1.0
    return 0.0

def candle_reversal(c):
    if len(c)<3: return False
    b2,b1,c0 = c[-3],c[-2],c[-1]
    # simple: engulfing / hammer-ish
    return (c0<b1 and b1>b2) or (c0>b1 and b1<b2)

def evidence_meanrev(ctx, m1):
    c1=close(m1); h1=high(m1); l1=low(m1)
    up,lo,ma = bb(c1,20,2.0); r7=rsi(c1,7)
    if up[-1] is None: return 0.0
    if ctx=="hold":
        if c1[-1]>=up[-1] and r7[-1]>=60 and candle_reversal(c1): return 1.0
        if c1[-1]<=lo[-1] and r7[-1]<=40 and candle_reversal(c1): return 1.0
    return 0.0

def vwap(arr, n=20):
    tpv=tp(arr); v=vol(arr)
    out=[]; num=0.0; den=0.0
    for i in range(len(arr)):
        num += tpv[i]*v[i]; den += v[i]
        out.append(num/den if den>0 else tpv[i])
        if i>=n:
            num -= tpv[i-n]*v[i-n]; den -= v[i-n]
    return out

# ---------- Entry scoring ----------
def entry_score(m1, m3, m5, ctx):
    c1=close(m1); c3=close(m3); c5=close(m5)
    if not c1 or not c3 or not c5: return 0.0
    e1 = evidence_meanrev(ctx, m1)
    e3 = evidence_breakout(ctx, m3, m5)
    e5 = evidence_pullback(ctx, m1, m3)
    score = 0.5*e5 + 0.3*e3 + 0.2*e1
    return score

# ---------- Sizing ----------
def round_step(q, step):
    if step<=0: return q
    return math.floor(q/step)*step

def size_order(price, sl, balance, risk_pct, leverage, min_notional, max_pair_expo_pct, lot_step):
    D = abs(price - sl)
    if D<=0: return 0.0, 0.0, 0.0
    R = balance * risk_pct
    qty = R / D
    notional = qty * price
    # constraints
    if notional < min_notional:
        qty = min_notional / price
        notional = min_notional
    max_notional = balance * max_pair_expo_pct * leverage
    if notional > max_notional:
        qty = max_notional / price
        notional = max_notional
    qty = round_step(qty, lot_step)
    margin = notional / leverage
    return qty, notional, margin

# ---------- Main per-symbol ----------
def analyze_symbol(sym, ctx_a, m1, m3, m5, balance=200.0):
    # Prefilters
    ok, why = prefilters(sym, m1, m3, m5)
    if not ok: return {"symbol": sym, "ctx": "none", "why": why}

    # Trend direction from A
    ctx = ctx_a if ctx_a in ("buy","sell","hold") else "none"
    # Entry evidence
    score = entry_score(m1, m3, m5, ctx)
    # veto 5m opposé (simple: EMA9-21 signe)
    e9=ema(close(m5),9); e21=ema(close(m5),21)
    S5 = (e9[-1]-e21[-1])
    if ctx=="buy" and S5<0: score = min(score, 0.59)
    if ctx=="sell" and S5>0: score = min(score, 0.59)

    # persistance 2×1m
    pst=jload(STATE/"persist_B.json", {})
    st=pst.get(sym, {"score_ge":0})
    if score>=0.60:
        st["score_ge"] = st.get("score_ge",0)+1
    else:
        st["score_ge"] = 0
    pst[sym]=st; jsave(STATE/"persist_B.json", pst)

    signal=None
    if st["score_ge"]>=2:
        # Build trade params
        c1=close(m1); h1=high(m1); l1=low(m1)
        atr1 = atr(h1,l1,c1,14)[-1]
        entry = c1[-1]
        if ctx=="buy":
            sl = entry - 1.2*atr1
            tp = entry + 1.8*atr1
        elif ctx=="sell":
            sl = entry + 1.2*atr1
            tp = entry - 1.8*atr1
        else:
            # mean-reversion en hold: utiliser BB mid ou VWAP
            mid = ema(c1,20)[-1]
            if c1[-1] >= (bb(c1,20,2.0)[0][-1] or c1[-1]):  # short MR
                sl = entry + 1.0*atr1; tp = mid
                ctx = "sell"
            else:  # long MR
                sl = entry - 1.0*atr1; tp = mid
                ctx = "buy"
        # sizing
        qty, notion, margin = size_order(entry, sl, balance, PARAM["risk_pct"], PARAM["leverage"],
                                         PARAM["min_notional"], PARAM["max_pair_expo_pct"], PARAM["lot_step"])
        if qty>0:
            signal = {
                "ts": time.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S", time.gmtime()),
                "symbol": sym,
                "side": "buy" if ctx=="buy" else "sell",
                "entry": round(entry,6),
                "sl": round(sl,6),
                "tp": round(tp,6),
                "qty": qty,
                "notional": round(notion,2),
                "margin": round(margin,2),
                "why": "B:score>=0.60x2|ctx="+ctx_a,
                "trail": round(atr1,6),
                "timeout_s": 25*60
            }
            # cooldown
            cd=jload(STATE/"cooldown.json", {})
            cd[sym] = int(time.time()) + int(PARAM["cooldown_1m"])*60
            jsave(STATE/"cooldown.json", cd)
            # reset persistence
            st["score_ge"]=0; pst[sym]=st; jsave(STATE/"persist_B.json", pst)

    return {"symbol": sym, "ctx": ctx_a, "score": round(score,3), "signal": signal}
